MAT 1:1 Ina ndazhazhana kǝ tugwa mbǝrt Yasu Kristu, zǝr Dod, zǝr Brakhim.
MAT 1:2 Brakhim kǝ yiga Ishaku, Ishaku kǝ yiga Yakub, Yakub kǝ yiga Yakhud zǝ zarbabakh sar,
MAT 1:3 Yakhud kǝ yiga Perez zǝ Zera ai yiga Tamar, Perez kǝ yiga Khezron, Khezron kǝ yiga Ram,
MAT 1:4 Ram kǝ yiga Aminadab, Aminadab kǝ yiga Nakhshon, Nakhshon kǝ yiga Salmon,
MAT 1:5 Salmon kǝ yiga Boaz, bab sara Rakhab, Boaz kǝ yiga Obed bab sara Rutl, Obed kǝ yiga Yese,
MAT 1:6 Yese kǝ yiga Dod shik. Dod kǝ yiga Sulemanu ai yiga nus Uri.
MAT 1:7 Sulemanu kǝ yiga Rekhobom, Rekhobom kǝ yiga Abij. Abij kǝ yiga Asa,
MAT 1:8 As kǝ yiga Jekhoshafat. Jekhoshafat kǝ yiga Joram, Joram kǝ yiga Uzi.
MAT 1:9 Uzi kǝ yiga Jotlam, Jotlam kǝ yiga Ahaz. Ahaz kǝ yiga Khezikay,
MAT 1:10 Khezikay kǝ yiga Manas. Manas kǝ yiga Amon, Amon kǝ yiga Yosi.
MAT 1:11 Yosi kǝ yiga Yekoni, zǝ zarbabakh sar ǝn tǝ sarte tsa khutsalud udakh ya Yakhud da man vǝɓ ǝn Khay ya Babil.
MAT 1:12 Ən tǝ khal kǝ ɓǝtral ɓa tsud da khaya Babil. Ka yiga Yekoni ad Sheyaltiyal. Sheyaltiyal kǝ yiga Zerobabel,
MAT 1:13 Zerobabel kǝ yiga Abikhud. Abikhud kǝ yiga Eliyakim. Eliyakim kǝ yiga Azor,
MAT 1:14 Azor kǝ yiga Zadok, Zadok kǝ yiga Akim, Akim kǝ yiga Eliyud
MAT 1:15 Eliyud kǝ yiga Eliyazar, Eliyazar kǝ yiga Matan, Matan kǝ yiga Yakub,
MAT 1:16 Yakub kǝ yiga Yusuvu zil Maryam, Maryam tsuguna ka yigan ad Yasu ai ɗakhdud dǝ Kristu.
MAT 1:17 Tsiyif ǝnt Brakhim kakh da tǝ Dod, a nala kǝ kǝlgwidz klatǝm ufaɗ. Tsiyif ǝn tǝ Dod, tsa kǝlgwidz klatǝm ufaɗ ǝn sarte a dzǝtrarud ak Izrailakh da man vǝɓ ǝn Babil. Tsiyif ǝn tǝ sarte tsǝn manud vǝɓ ǝn Babil da tǝ sarte yigdud Kristu tsa kǝlgwidz klatǝm ufaɗ.
MAT 1:18 Auna ɗule a yigdud Yasu Kristu. Ən sarta sǝb Maryam bab Yasu kǝ Jisav, kǝda nguɗatra sǝba tsuda, ka dzoghǝr khuɗ tsin tǝ dǝva dǝ ndzǝɗa Sǝɗikw Chuwaɗaɗan.
MAT 1:19 Jambu sar Jisava ud charan, nagh ba dǝ kǝɗara zhiru ǝn tatak udakh bi. Ka ɗayanan ad ghǝr kǝ tǝkaghera tsitar ɓǝghanyan.
MAT 1:20 Madvin ǝn ɗaya ghǝra, dzagwdlam ǝmdlawala zǝrɓǝla Yazhigǝl tsin ǝn suwan. Niya tsin, “Jisav zǝr Dod, a ɗuwa gǝdza kǝ zǝɓ Maryam kǝ nǝga kǝ nusagh, wirva khuɗsarna a sa tǝdǝva dǝ ndzǝɗa Siɗikw Chuwaɗaɗan.
MAT 1:21 Da yigayiga dǝ zǝr dǝɗungw, da barva bǝg kha ɗakha Yasu. Wirva in da kat yakhtar ǝn khaipakh tar.”
MAT 1:22 Daghan ina a dzoghǝr kǝ righada dǝge a kwarga Dadzikan tǝ dǝva dǝ tlayang kwarne,
MAT 1:23 “Da dlǝgh khuɗ dughmbǝl, da yiga yiga ad zer. Ka da barva ɗakhud Manuwel.” Dǝge tuku Manuwel na in kwarne “Dagha kǝnda zǝ Yazhigǝl.”
MAT 1:24 Tsiyif kǝ Yusuvu ǝn khara, ka gatars kǝ lave a kwararkhe zǝrɓǝla Yazhigǝl. Yusuvu tsuguna ka ɓǝf ad Maryam kǝ nǝga kǝ nus sar.
MAT 1:25 A khǝnarghǝr bi, ba yiga tsin zǝr sar. Ka barva Yusuvu ad ɗakha Yasu.
MAT 2:1 A yava Yasu ǝn kǝs ya Baitalkhami ǝn ǝntla khay ya Yakhudi ǝn kwarga shik Khiridus. Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sart, ka sosǝg kǝ li tsatsǝg ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ kwadladlakh sǝgo ǝn mbǝrt kǝs, da wurshalim. Ka ndiɗa tsitar
MAT 2:2 kwarne, “Ən vara fitl na yavan ai da nǝga kǝ shik Yakhudakh ni? Wirva a nǝgha tsǝkǝnda kwadladl sar sǝgo ǝn mbǝrt kǝs, wirva yana a so da ɗabaɗaba kǝnd.”
MAT 2:3 Tsǝna kǝ Khiridus Shik ad yan, ka tsiyif mǝkǝn sar zǝva udakh daghan ǝn Wurshalim.
MAT 2:4 Ka dzakhanǝf ad zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus. Ka ndiɗatǝrwal ad vake da yigdud Kristu.
MAT 2:5 Ka nǝv itar tsin, “Ən kǝs ya Baitalkhami, ǝn ǝntla khay ya Yakhudi. Wirva a vindzga ndǝk yan tlayangen ad dǝge a kwarga Yazhigǝl kwarne,
MAT 2:6 “ ‘Ghǝra tsugun Baitalkhami ǝntla khay ya Yakhud, Khǝɗikan bakhǝn li man tlǝkǝs ǝn Yakhud bi; Wirva da sǝgawal ǝn tǝb tsǝkur dadake da man tlǝks, Dadake da zighw udakhar ya Israil.’ ”
MAT 2:7 Ka ɗakhga Khiridus ad li tsatsǝgen ɓǝghanyan, ki nǝghda tsatsǝg tsin ad sarte tsa ǝmdlawala kwadladlen.
MAT 2:8 Ka ɓǝlatǝral dǝgal da Baitalkhami, ka ni, “Dam da nǝghamako ndǝghǝr nǝgh ad fitlen ɗussa nikur. Da tlarghǝr kur, ka kwara ke kur ki dǝgal kǝ ghǝrar da ɗabaɗab.”
MAT 2:9 Udzala tsitar ǝn tsǝn lav shika, ka dal itar. Kwadladle tsa nǝgha itar ǝn mbǝrtǝ kǝsena ǝn tǝ vuk tar. Ka gatars gata tsitar tlǝm sa tsin da tǝghǝr kǝ vake dǝ fitlen.
MAT 2:10 Nǝgha tsitar ad kwadladlen ka righǝf itar dǝ khwaɗǝga char.
MAT 2:11 Da tsitar da mǝghen, ka nǝgha tsitar fitlen zǝ Maryam bab sar, kalga itar juguv ǝn tǝ vuksar, ka ɗabanǝf itar. Ka vadana itar mbǝl jilaɗakh tar ka bara itar ad dawan zǝ tǝrshin ɗiz ai manavadal sǝgawal ǝn uf ai ɗakhdud frankinsens, zǝ ai ɗakhud Mir ǝn tlerna uf.
MAT 2:12 Ka gwiyagh itar ǝn tǝ tlǝrna ɗul da kǝstar, wirva tsa tǝkhatǝranud ǝn suwan kwarne, a ɗuwa itar gwiya daks da vak Khiridus.
MAT 2:13 Ən tǝ khal kǝ daldǝg tsitar, ka tlarghǝr zǝrɓǝla Yazhigǝl kǝ Yusuvu ǝn suwan, avin, “Tsiya, zǝɓa ad fitl na zǝ bab sar khwaya dǝgal da Masar. Giɗam giɗǝn vin kwa kwara kurkhai ka saks, wirva da gatagata Khiridus ad zǝrna kǝ kǝɗakǝɗ.”
MAT 2:14 Ka tsiyǝf Yusuvu ɓǝf ad fitlen zǝ babsar kǝviɗ, ka dal da khay Masar.
MAT 2:15 Ka nndzǝgan ǝn vin da tǝ sarte a ǝmtsǝga Khiridus. Ina kǝ digit a dzaughǝr ki zǝɗa righada dǝge a kwarga Dadzikan ǝn tǝ dǝva dǝ ghay tlayangen kwarne, “A ɗakhadǝghǝr ǝn Masar ka zǝrar.”
MAT 2:16 Katlga kǝ Khiridus kwarne raja kharghǝra liye tsa digit ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ kwadladlen, ka nguɗǝrǝv tsin char. Ka ɓǝlanǝf ad udakh kǝ khadzga ɗeghwa zǝr dǝɗungw ǝn Baitalkhami zai ǝn gǝdzar kǝsakhe tǝvǝgh, tsiyif ǝn tǝ vǝg mits da tǝ vunj, kalkala sarte tsa kwararkhai li tsatsǝgen ǝn tǝ ghǝr kǝ zǝren.
MAT 2:17 A righif lave tsa kwarga Irimi tlayang;
MAT 2:18 “Ka tsǝna tsena tsud ad kwind ǝn dlǝgh tsits. Kwinda tuwa ziwaziw, Rakhil ǝn tuwa wirva zarsar. A piyarwala kitlandagh rǝv. Wirva a ruga zar sar.”
MAT 2:19 Tǝkhal kǝ ǝmtsa Khiridus, ka tlarghǝr zǝrɓǝla Yazhigǝl kǝ Yusuvu ǝn suwan ǝn Masar
MAT 2:20 ni, “Tsiya ɓǝf ɓa dǝ fitlǝn zǝ bab sar gwiya daks da Izrail, wirva liye gat kǝɗ fitl na a ruwargan.”
MAT 2:21 Ka tsiyif, ɓǝf ad fitlen zǝ babsar ka gwiya da khay ya Izrail.
MAT 2:22 Ai tsǝna tsin kwarne zǝr Khiridus, ai dakhdud Arkilayus kǝ chauga tlǝksa dad sar, ǝn man tlǝks ǝn khay ya Yakhudi, ka gǝdza tsin dǝgal da vinen. Wirva tsa tǝkhatǝranud ǝn suwana, ka khutsval da ǝntla khaya Galili.
MAT 2:23 Ka dal da giɗǝn tlǝrna kǝsen ǝn ɗakhdud dǝ Nazarat. “Ki righada dǝge tsa kwarga tlayang kwarne, Zǝrna da ɗakha dǝ zil Nazarat ud.”
MAT 3:1 Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sart, a sawal Yukhan dadak para ud da kwardu lav Yazhigǝl ǝn tǝghal ǝntla khay ya Yakhudi.
MAT 3:2 Ni, “Pǝlam pǝla ghǝr, wirva tlǝksa Yazhigǝla a khǝrzgan.”
MAT 3:3 Tsa Yukhan dadake tsǝn kwara Ishay tlayang ad laven tǝghǝr tsin kwarne, “Kwinda ud ǝn tlǝkh ǝn tǝghal kwarne, ‘Ɗikamarna ɗul kǝ Dadzikan, Andz ger nǝv ɗulsar.’ ”
MAT 3:4 Gabage talǝm Yukhan na a manava dǝ guj tlǝgwam. Nguɗan sambal ǝn tǝ khukw tsin. Dǝg zuwa sara tsǝvakwa zǝ mam tǝghal.
MAT 3:5 Tǝkǝna udakh ya Wurshalim zǝ ǝntla Yakhudi daghan, zǝ daghan ǝntla khay zagh Urdun, ka sakhgawal itar da vaksar,
MAT 3:6 ka kwarakh khaipakhtar itar, ka paratǝra para tsin ǝn zagh Urdun.
MAT 3:7 Ai vazga kǝ Yukhan ad Farisakh zǝ Sadukiyakh zikǝn sǝgawal da vaksar kǝ paratǝrapar, ka niya tsitar, “Kur zar ya pushakh. War kǝ khiɗakurf kǝ ngikh kuba rǝvakhuɗ Yazhigǝl nǝn saksi?
MAT 3:8 Manam giɗe da ǝmdla kwarne a palga kur ghǝr ǝn khaipakhur.
MAT 3:9 Dzamam ba ǝn khuɗur kwarne, ‘Dadǝnda Brakhim bi,’ Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ. Tǝkha Yazhigǝl kǝ vǝrɗarkhai zara kǝ Brakhim sǝgawal ǝn kurakhan.
MAT 3:10 Audzalud ǝn bars khil kǝ mbǝrt uf. Itsera kǝ ufe kwal yig zar charan ka ǝntlarsud kǝɗaghud da kar.
MAT 3:11 “Ni ka ǝn para kura dǝ yu kǝ, kǝ mǝtlada kwarne a palga kur ghǝr, ude ndanga tǝghǝr tsǝka da saks ǝn tǝ khal tsǝk, ude itsa kimbak sar tǝkh ba ka kǝ ɓanǝf bi. In da para kuran dǝ Sǝɗikw Chuwaɗaɗan, zǝ kar tsugun.
MAT 3:12 Khutan ad kwat kava sar, kǝ kav khi sar ǝn tǝ ghwuzay, ka dzanǝf ad khi, ɗidagh ǝn kuvur sar, ka ndǝghanan ad tlitl dǝ kare kwal tǝkha tsud kǝ kǝɗgan.”
MAT 3:13 Ən tǝ khalak yan ka sagha Yasu ǝn Galili, da vak Yukhan kǝ parapara tsud ǝn zagha Urdun.
MAT 3:14 Tsǝn na Yukhan ad gadlara gadl. Ka niya tsin, “Ka tsǝn nagha paraka para tsǝkha ka kha kǝ sagha da vakara?”
MAT 3:15 Ka ngawarkhai Yasu kwarne, “nalnǝgin ndǝk yan, wirva ndǝk yan khwaran kǝ righada dǝge ǝn nagha Yazhigǝl.” Khal kǝ yana ka khayanǝf Yukhan.
MAT 3:16 Ən tǝ khal kǝ Parandal tsud Yasu, madvin ǝn sǝgawal ǝn yu, tǝvin tǝvina ka ngurǝf garazhigǝl, ka nǝghan ad sǝɗikw Yazhigǝl ǝn sǝgadagh ndǝk kakur, sodagh da tǝghǝr tsin.
MAT 3:17 Ka tsǝnud lava sǝgadagh ǝn gharazhigǝl kwarne, “Ina zǝrare ǝn waya kǝ, ǝn tsǝn zǝɗa sar ka char.”
MAT 4:1 Ka fiwandal Sǝɗikw Chuwaɗaɗan ad Yasu da tǝghal kǝ kurakura kǝ wurdu.
MAT 4:2 A zǝɓga Yasu ad ndǝl khǝna kul ufaɗ viɗa zǝ fatsi. Kǝ khala ka ndzikǝnǝf way.
MAT 4:3 Ka sa wurdu niya tsin, “Da zǝr Yazhigǝl kha, kwarara kwara kǝ kurakhan nalnǝg itar kǝ dǝg zu.”
MAT 4:4 Ka ngawarkhe Yasu kwarne, “Vindzan ǝn kaɗkaɗ Yazhigǝl kwarne, ‘Uk ǝn safǝn tǝ dǝg zuwa kitakul bud bi, khekwa dǝ itsera kǝ lave ǝn sǝgawal ǝn ghay kǝ Yazhigǝl.’ ”
MAT 4:5 Ka ɓala wurdu da dlǝmdla kǝs Chuwaɗaɗan ǝn Wurshalim, ka ɓoɓa tsin da tǝ ghǝr kǝ beɗem fǝta Yazhigǝl.
MAT 4:6 Niya tsin, “Da zǝr Yazhigǝl kha,” ghǝdzǝvdagh ghǝdzǝva dǝg dagh da khay, wirva vindzan kwarne, “ ‘Da batra bǝg Yazhigǝl ad ndzǝɗa kǝ zarɓǝlakh sar kǝ kat kha kat. Ka da chau kha chawa itar dǝ dǝv tar. Khek kǝɗkhe kǝ kur ǝn tǝ sig.’ ”
MAT 4:7 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Vindzan tsugun kwarne, ‘Kura ba dǝ Dad zikan Yazhigǝla bi.’ ”
MAT 4:8 Ka gwidǝn wurdu ad ɓoɓa dǝgo da tǝ tsǝɓan na kǝ ghay ghuɓ, ka mǝdlaran ad tlǝksakh lard zǝ zika khwara sar daghan.
MAT 4:9 Ka niya tsin, “Da kǝla ke kha juguv ɗaba ke kh. Daghan dǝgakhana da bakha bǝg kǝ.”
MAT 4:10 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, Tsiya dǝgal ǝn van kha shatan, wirva vindzan kwarne, “ ‘Ɗabaɗaba Dad zikan Yazhigǝlakh, tsuguna in kitakul da manara kha tlǝr.’ ”
MAT 4:11 Khalak yana ka ɗuwars wurdu, ka sǝgdagh kǝ zarɓǝlakh Yazhigǝl da nǝgharu nǝgh.
MAT 4:12 Tsǝna kǝ Yasu kwarne a viyava Yukhan da sal, ka tsiya tsin dǝgal da Nazarat ǝn Galili.
MAT 4:13 Ka ɗuwars ad Nazarat, dal da giɗǝn Kafarnakhum, ai tǝvai ǝn tuk dǝlv ǝn tǝ ghala ǝntla khaya Zǝbulun zǝ Naftali.
MAT 4:14 Ki da righada lave kwarga Yazhigǝl ǝn tǝ dǝva dǝ Ishay tlayang kwarne,
MAT 4:15 “Əntla khay mbǝrt Zebulun, zǝ dǝg Naftali ǝn Galili. Ən tǝ ɗul dǝlva Madateri, tangw da tǝ ǝntla khay zagha Urdun, Galili vake ǝn giɗda liye kwal Yakhudakh.
MAT 4:16 Liye ǝn giɗǝn gurtl. Nǝgha tsitar kǝs kheɗaɗ char. Liye giɗǝn kǝs sǝɗikw fayam ǝmtsa. A mǝdlawala kheɗaɗa kes da vak tar.”
MAT 4:17 Tsif tǝ yanen kǝ sart, a farsa Yasu ad kwardu lav Yazhigǝl, ǝn kwar kwarne, “Pǝlam pǝla ghǝr, wirva tlǝksa Yazhigǝl a khǝrzǝgan.”
MAT 4:18 Madǝv Yasu ǝn dǝgal ǝn tǝ kalam dǝlva Galili ma, ka nǝghanǝgha tsin zarbabakh mits, Simane ɗakhdud dǝ Bitrus zǝ zer bab sar Ndros. Ən ɗay sika vay kilf itar da dǝlv, wirva li vay kilf itar.
MAT 4:19 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Gatamakǝs gat, da nakurar nǝg ka kǝ li khutsado ud ndǝkve ǝn vaya kur kilf.”
MAT 4:20 Tǝvin tǝvina ka ɗuwars itar ad sikakh tar, ka gatars itar.
MAT 4:21 Din ǝn zu vuk dǝ dǝga, ka nǝghan ad yakhaya kǝ zarbabakh mits tsugun, ai Yakub zǝr Zabadi zǝ zer bab sar Yukhan. Ən peryu itar zǝ dad tar Zabadi, ǝn ɗika sikakh tar itar. Ka ɗakh tǝrkhai.
MAT 4:22 Tǝvin tǝvina ka ɗuda itar peryu tar zǝ dad tar, ka gatars itar.
MAT 4:23 A gwayafkhai Yasu ǝn kǝs Galili daghan, ǝn tsagakhdu lav Yazhigǝl ǝn gud dzakhav Yakhudakh. Ka kwardu lav zǝɗǝn tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝksa yazhigǝl. Ən mbakha itsera kǝ khulf kuz, zǝ liye kwal yang kǝ udakh.
MAT 4:24 A tsa tǝ dǝva dǝ yan kǝ tlǝr ud ad Yasu ǝn khay ya Suri daghan. Ka zaɓardo li kwal yang ud zǝ liye ǝn tuk kuzakh sikh sikh sikh zǝ li khǝɓ dlaɗ, zǝ li sǝɗikw bǝzan, zǝ liye tlavarghǝr wurdu zǝ li ǝmtsa kalam vǝgh, a mbakhatru daghan.
MAT 4:25 A gatars dzakhava udakh zikǝn sǝgawal ǝn Galili, zǝ ǝntla khaya kǝsakh kǝlɗǝk, zǝ Wurshalim, zǝ ǝntla khaya Yakhudi, zǝva liye ǝn ghǝdzǝva zagha Urdun.
MAT 5:1 Vazga kǝ Yasu a dzafkhai udakh zikǝn, do da tǝ gil, ka nndzǝgan. Ka saks kǝ furakh sar da vak sar,
MAT 5:2 ka farsa tsagatǝra lava tsin kwarne;
MAT 5:3 A batǝrghǝr Yazhigǝl ad bark kǝ liye ǝn tsa khǝtsala khǝtsa tar ǝn dǝgakhe ǝn nagha Yazhigǝl, Wirva tlǝksa gharazhigǝla da dǝg tar.
MAT 5:4 Nǝg bark kǝ liye bazan rǝvakhuɗ. Wirva da kitla tǝra rǝvud.
MAT 5:5 Nǝg bark kǝ liye gulandagh ghǝrtar, Da wurawura itar ad dǝgakhe manga Yazhigǝl ad lanji sar.
MAT 5:6 Nǝg bark kǝ liye way man dǝgakhe ǝn nagha Yazhigǝl. Wirva da bagha tǝra bagh.
MAT 5:7 Nǝg bark kǝ liye mǝdla kwiɗkwiɗǝrǝv. Wirva da mǝdla tǝra mǝdla Yazhigǝl ad kwiɗkwiɗǝrǝv.
MAT 5:8 Nǝg bark kǝ liye chuwaɗaɗ rǝva tar. Da nǝghanǝgha itar Yazhigǝl.
MAT 5:9 Nǝg bark kǝ liye matla giɗa khwiɗ. Da ɗakh tǝr dǝ zar Yazhigǝl ud.
MAT 5:10 Nǝg bark kǝ liye ǝn batǝrud dlaɗ wirvǝn man dǝgakhe ǝn nagha Yazhigǝl itar. Wirva tlǝksa Yazhigǝla dǝg tar.
MAT 5:11 Nǝg bark tsǝkur, madǝv udakh ǝn lakh kur lakh, zǝ bakura dlaɗ, zǝ ngatla filakh ǝn teghǝr tsǝkur sikh sikh sikh, wirva li gataks gata kur.
MAT 5:12 Kwam khwaɗǝg zǝ panakha rǝv char, wirva da gǝmadu gǝma kur dǝg sigur zikǝn ǝn ghǝrazhigǝl, wirva a batra ndǝk yan ud dlaɗ ak tlayangakh Yazhigǝl liye tsa soghǝr chak tǝghǝr tsǝkur.
MAT 5:13 Kuram tlǝgul lard. Da tǝkaghǝra tlǝgul zǝ nashnash sar, da wurondǝghǝr ndarud zǝɗa sari? Aghba dla dǝge ǝn tukuwin bi akwa ɗiduwud, ghǝdlapakh gud.
MAT 5:14 Kuram kheɗaɗ lard. Afke dlǝmdla kǝs ai khavǝn tǝ bǝɗar ǝn ɓǝghafǝkhai bi.
MAT 5:15 Na bud ǝn vǝdzanǝf kara kazaz ka khǝmbarghǝrud gagay bi, akwa bugud ǝn tǝ vak ghitsa sar vake da mǝdlaradin ɗul kǝ li mǝgh kheɗeɗ.
MAT 5:16 Ndǝk yan tsugun, namal nǝg kheɗeɗ tsi kǝ udakh, wirva da nǝgha tsitar ad tlǝr khwarane manakur, da farghǝrafǝg itar kǝ Dadure ǝn ghǝrazhigǝl.
MAT 5:17 Dzamamba kwarne a sodagh da kala ndzikhandzikh Mus zǝ dǝge vindzan ǝn kaɗkaɗ tlayangakh ba ka bi. A so da kala kala ba ka bi, a so kǝ regharegha kǝ.
MAT 5:18 Kaɗi ǝn kwara kura kǝ, akwa mbasu ghǝrazhighǝl zǝ khay, nga itsa khǝɗikana kǝ lav ai da ɓǝlal ǝn dǝge a tsagdu Mus bi, kwa reghanaud itsauɗ.
MAT 5:19 Wirva yan ɗaga ude kǝlanǝm itsa kitakul ǝn khǝɗikan nak ndzikha ndzikha khan, zǝ tsagardu kǝ udakh ad kǝla ndzikha ndzikha khan, da ɗakha dǝ khǝɗikan kǝ udud ǝn tlǝksa Yazhigǝl. Ude gatars, ka tsagardu kǝ udakh tsugun, da ɗakha dǝ zikan kǝ udud ǝn tlǝksa Yazhigǝl.
MAT 5:20 Ən kwara kura kwara kǝ, da malga ba kur liye tsagdu nzikha nzikh Mus zǝ Farisakh kǝ kanadi bi, na kur daks da tlǝksa Yazhigǝl tsa ndar bi.
MAT 5:21 Tsǝna tsǝkur a kwarar khai yud kǝ dzidzakh mar kwarne, kǝɗam ba safa itsawar bi, itsera kǝ ude ǝn kǝɗga saf, ka da takara lavud.
MAT 5:22 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, ude nguɗarva rǝv kǝ zǝr bab sar, ka da takara lavud. Tsugun, ude gamp kha niya kǝ zǝr bab sar, da ɓaɓud da tǝvuk li taka lav ya Yakhudakh. Ude ɗakh zǝr bab sar tsugun dǝ dlag, da kǝɗ dagh da kara fay ud.
MAT 5:23 Wirva yan, dǝn bǝdu dǝg tsufa khǝn tǝ vak sadak, da dzamana kha kwarne nǝg dǝge ǝn tǝbur zǝ zǝrbaba gh,
MAT 5:24 bǝga kha dǝg tsufaghen ndan ǝnt vak sadak. Dǝg dǝgal ndan da ɗikva zǝ zǝr babagh. Khalak yan ka saks kha da bǝdu dǝg tsufaghen.
MAT 5:25 Da kǝlga udan ad juguvagh, kujaɗ ɗikfǝkhai kha zin tǝkur ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dǝg, kǝda tsukwa tsukur ǝn tǝ vak takalaven. Da na ba ndǝk yan bi, ka da matlakha zǝ dadak takalav, dadak takalava tsuguna ka ɓǝkha da vak del, tsuguna ka nguɗakhai yud ǝn zaw.
MAT 5:26 Jir ǝn kwara kha kǝ, na ba itar da ɓǝlakhs bǝla bi, kwa pǝlgakha kwaɓ na daghan ai gatakhsud din.
MAT 5:27 A tsǝna tsǝkur a kwaravan kwarne, a ɗuwa man gwaragwar.
MAT 5:28 Ən kwara kura kwara ka kwarne, ude kǝmga dǝg khǝr, audzal ǝn manga gwaragwar zin ǝn rǝvakhuɗ sar.
MAT 5:29 Da di dǝva kafagh ǝn bǝg khan da man khaip, ndǝɗadal ndǝɗa tlǝvarskh. Azǝgha bǝghal ǝn tlǝrna tlepel vǝghagh tǝghǝr kǝɗdagh ɗumba vǝghagh da kar.
MAT 5:30 Da dǝva kafagh ǝn bǝg khan da man khaip, ǝntlars kha tlǝvarskh. Azǝgha bǝghal ǝn tlǝrna tlepel vǝghakh tǝghǝr kǝɗdagh ɗumba vǝghagh da kar.
MAT 5:31 A gwidǝn ud kwara kwara kwarne, ude tǝkaghǝran zǝ nus sar, barari bara kaɗkaɗ tǝkaghǝra tsin.
MAT 5:32 Dǝge ǝn kwara kura ka in kwarne, da tǝkaghǝra udan zǝ nus sar dǝn tǝghǝr kǝ khaipa man gwaragwar bin bi, a ba da man gwaragwar. Itsawar ǝn ɓu nuse a tǝkaghǝra ze zil sar, gwaragwar ǝn manin.
MAT 5:33 Dakhkana a tsǝna tsǝkur a kwarkhai ud kǝ dzidzakh mar kwarne, kǝla ba dǝ waɗe manga kha bi, kwa righanǝf kha waɗe tsa waɗga kha kǝ Dadzikan.
MAT 5:34 Ai dǝge ǝn kwara kura ka in kwarne waɗam ba ɗikiɗiki bi, itsa dǝ gharazhigǝl, wirva vij giɗa Yazhigǝl.
MAT 5:35 Waɗam ba dǝ khay tsugun bi, wirva vak bǝg siga sar kǝ Yazhigǝl, awana tsad Wurshalim wirva in dlǝmdla kǝs zikan kǝ shik.
MAT 5:36 Waɗ ba dǝ ghǝrakh tsugun bi, wirva tǝkh bakha kǝ nandala guj kitakul kǝ maɗakw tsa kǝ lusan bi.
MAT 5:37 Dǝge khwara kǝ kwara tsǝkur in kwarne, ana bi au, da ɓalin sig ǝn mbiyan a so ǝn vake da wurdu yan.
MAT 5:38 Tsǝna tsǝkur a kwarga Yazhigǝl kwarne, da chiɓarnakha di kǝ ud, ka chiɓakhanud diyagh tsǝgun. Da lardarkha tliɗ kǝ ud, ka lakhdalud tliɗa tsǝgun.
MAT 5:39 Ai dǝge ǝn kwara kura ka in kwarne, da mana kurkhai udan ad ghaza pǝlama bi. Da ɗiyakhwal udan ad mekhwpengw ǝn tǝ diwa dǝva kaf, ka gwiyarnǝf khad diwa dǝva dleɓa tsugun.
MAT 5:40 Da kǝlakhghǝr udan ad juguv wirva pǝrɗaghval gabagagh, ka bara kha zǝva khǝɗikana kǝ gabagagh.
MAT 5:41 Da njǝghakhu dadak ndzǝɗan kǝ dǝgal da ǝntla fǝtǝl kitakul, ka dara dǝg kha ǝntla fǝtǝl mits.
MAT 5:42 Da takaɗga udan ad digit ǝn vakagh, barakh. Ude a sagh da takaɗ gǝmau ǝn vakagh tsugun, piyardu bi.
MAT 5:43 Tsǝna tsǝkur a kwarga Yazhigǝl kwarne, waya ad tlǝghǝrwitǝghagh, ɗuda kha dadak dawagh.
MAT 5:44 Dǝge kwara kura ka in kwarne wayam dadak dawur, mana matǝra ɗǝgau kǝ li bakura dlaɗ.
MAT 5:45 Ən tǝ dǝva yan da nǝga kur kǝ zar Dadur ǝn gharazhigǝl, dadake ǝn bǝg fatsi da tǝvǝn tǝghǝr kǝ li kalali zǝ liye kwal kalali, tǝɗadagh ad yu gharazhigǝl tsugun da tǝghǝr kǝ li kanadi zǝ liye kwal kanadi.
MAT 5:46 Da uk liye ǝn way kur way ǝn waya kur, ira kǝ dǝg siga da bakurudi? Itsa liye ǝn dza khadama, ǝn mana ndǝkyan bakh itara?.
MAT 5:47 Da uk zar babakhur ǝn nǝgardi kur, ai, uɗa manga kur mal kǝ yakhayi? Itsa liye kwal tsa Yazhigǝla ǝn mana ndǝk yan bakh itara?
MAT 5:48 Wirva yan reghanyan nǝv giɗur ndǝkve reghan Dadur ǝn gharazhigǝl.
MAT 6:1 Tsukwamana ghǝr, bamaru ba tlǝr kanadiyur kǝ di bi. Wirva da manga kur ndǝk yan, da gǝmadu ba kur dǝg sigur ǝn vak Dadur ǝn gharazhigǝl bi.
MAT 6:2 Wirva yan, da da bǝdu dǝg buti kh, ɓaldu bǝn ghay bi, ndǝk ai ǝn mana mbaɗirakh ǝn gud dzakhav zǝn tǝ ɗulakh bi, wirva kǝ dlǝba tǝra dlǝba tsud. Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, audzala itar ǝn gǝmadu dǝg siga tar.
MAT 6:3 Da ka da bǝdu dǝg buti kur kǝ dadake kwaldin, tsa ba dǝva dleɓagh ad dǝge ǝn mana dǝva kafagh bi.
MAT 6:4 Bǝdu bǝgagha nalnǝgin ɓǝghanyan. Dadaghe ǝn nǝgha nǝgh ad ɗaga dǝge ɓǝghanyan, da bakha dǝg sig.
MAT 6:5 Da da ɗǝgawa kur, manam ba ndǝk mbaɗirakh bi, li way ɗǝgau ǝn vak ghits ǝn gud dzakhava zǝ tuk ɗul ki nǝghatǝra nǝgha kǝ udakh. Jir ǝn kwara kura kǝ, audzala itar ǝn gǝmadu dǝg siga tar.
MAT 6:6 Ai da da ɗǝgawakh, dǝg daks da gud, ka khǝɗardu kh. Ɗǝgawaru ɗǝga kǝ Dadaghe kwal ǝn nǝgha tsud. Dadaghe ǝn nǝgha dǝge manud ɓǝghanyan, da bakha dǝg sig.
MAT 6:7 Da da ɗǝgawa kur, a ɗuwam gwayars kǝ lava zikǝn ndǝk liye kwal tsa Yazhigǝl, liye da ghǝr tsitar ǝn kurana, da gwayars itar kǝ lava zikǝna, ka da tsǝnatru tsǝnud.
MAT 6:8 Manam ba ndǝk itar bi, wirva tsa kǝ Dadur ad dǝge na kur, kǝda da takaɗa takaɗa tsǝkur.
MAT 6:9 Auna ɗule da ɗǝgauda kur. Dadmare ǝn gharazhigǝl, Farghǝr fǝgud kǝ ɗakhaghe chuwaɗaɗ.
MAT 6:10 Tlǝksagha ausǝgin sǝgdagh. Manud ad dǝge ǝn nakh ǝn lard. Ndǝkve ǝn manud ǝn gharazhigǝl.
MAT 6:11 Bakǝnda bǝg dǝg zuwa khan, ndǝkve ǝn bakǝnda kha tsika fatsi.
MAT 6:12 Ɓisa kǝndana kha khepa khǝnd. Ndǝkve ɓisara kǝnda kǝ li mana kǝnda ghaz.
MAT 6:13 Ɓǝla kǝndu ba di daks da dlǝgd bi. Ai kat kǝnd kat ǝn dǝva kǝ wurdu.
MAT 6:14 Da ka ɓisarna kur kǝ li mana kura ghaz, Dadure ǝn gharazhigǝl tsuguna da ɓisa kura ɓis.
MAT 6:15 Ai da ka ɓisarna ba kur kǝ udakh tsugun bi, Dadure tsuguna, na ba da ɓisa kura khaipa khur bi.
MAT 6:16 Dǝn zǝb ndǝl kur, bazamdu ba vakdi ndǝke mana mbaɗirakh bi. Ni itara ǝn bazdu kǝ nǝghda mǝdlara kǝ udakh itar kwarne ǝn zǝɓ ndǝl itar. Kaɗikaɗi ǝn kwara kura kǝ, audzala itar ǝn gǝmadu dǝg siga tar.
MAT 6:17 Ya dǝn zǝɓ ndǝl kh, pardu kha vakdiyagh, masǝm kha wal ǝn ghǝr,
MAT 6:18 ki khek katlga tsud kwarne, ǝn zǝɓ ndǝl kh, uk Dadaghe kwal nǝgha tsud da tsan. Dadaghe ǝn nǝgha dǝge manud ɓǝghanyan, da bakha dǝg sig.
MAT 6:19 Dzakha mara ba lǝman kǝ ghǝrur ǝn lard bi, vake da bazdu terar zǝ kwalavi, zǝ vake da tǝkha gǝlakh kǝ chiɓanan kǝ daks da gǝl.
MAT 6:20 Dzakha mara kǝ ghǝrura ad lǝman ǝn gharazhigǝl, vake kwal da tǝkha kǝ tǝrara zǝ kwalavi kǝ bazdu, zǝ vake kwal tǝkha kǝ gǝl kǝ chiɓanan kǝ daks da gǝl.
MAT 6:21 Wirva vake dǝ lǝmanagha, ǝn vin mǝkǝnagh.
MAT 6:22 Diya in kara kazaza vǝgh, da ka lapi diyagha, ɗaga vǝgha gha ka da nǝga kǝ kheɗeɗ char.
MAT 6:23 Da ka yanga ba diya bi, daghan vǝgha gha da nǝga kǝ gurtl char. Da nala kheɗaɗa vǝghagh kǝ gurtla, ka da zikakhghǝr zika gurtl.
MAT 6:24 Na ude tǝkha kǝ manarkhai kwatnakh kǝ dadmǝgh mits bi, akwa waygan ad fanga, ɗudan ad fang. Bi khǝmbarvan kǝ yana ka nenanan ad yan. Ən manawa ba gatars kǝ Yazhigǝl zǝ kwaɓ tsǝkha bǝrdagha bi.
MAT 6:25 Wirva yan ǝn kwara kura kwara kǝ, dzamam ba safur, zǝ dǝge da zuwa kur zǝ dǝge da khǝɓa kur bi, zǝ kadlange da tala kur kǝ vǝghur bi. A malga bakh safa ad dǝg zuwa? Tsǝguna a malga bakh vǝgh ad kadlange da tala kura?
MAT 6:26 Ən nǝgha bakh kur ɗikakh ǝn pǝdlǝn tǝ gharazhigǝla, na itar ǝn tukha bi, na itar ǝn tsǝg khi bi, naba itar ǝn dza khi da kuvur bi. Sakhkana Dadure ǝn gharazhigǝl ǝn batra dǝg zu. A malga bakh ndangura ad ɗikakh?
MAT 6:27 Warek ǝn kur ǝn tǝ dǝva dǝ ɗangw sar tǝkha kǝ sǝgarghǝr ǝntla sart tetl kǝ safa sari?
MAT 6:28 Ai wuɗek lava tsǝkur ǝn dzamghǝr ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dǝge da tala kuri? Ən nǝgha bakh kur ɗaka kǝ sasikw zǝ firakh ǝn tǝ tǝghala? Na itar ǝn man tlǝr zǝ takhara kadlang kǝ ghǝr tar bi.
MAT 6:29 Sakhkana ǝn kwara kura kwara kǝ, itsa Saluman shik zǝ daghan ndanga sar, a taɓa ba dǝ chaɗfǝkhai ndǝk itsera tar bi.
MAT 6:30 Da ka tǝkha Yazhigǝl kǝ chaɗanǝf sasikw ǝn tǝ tǝghal ndǝk yan, ai khana nǝga, tǝkhula tlǝvdahgud da kara ka ndǝghanud, tǝkh bakh Yazhigǝl kǝ chaɗa kuruf mal kǝ yana? Kuram li khǝtsa fadǝghǝro fǝg.
MAT 6:31 Wirva yana ndiɗam ba kwarne, uɗa da zuwa kiyami? Uɗa da khǝɓa kiyami? Uɗa da tala kiyami?
MAT 6:32 Afke li kwal tsa Yazhigǝl ǝn gat yakhana kǝ digitakh, ai tsa kǝ Dadure ǝn gharazhigǝl kwarne ǝn nagha kur ad yakhana kǝ digitakh daghan.
MAT 6:33 Ai dǝg chaka gatam gata tlǝksa Yazhigǝl zǝ man dǝgakhai ǝn nagha Yazhigǝl, daghan yakhena kǝ digitakh da bakuran ghǝr bǝgud.
MAT 6:34 Wirva yan ndiɗam ba khul bi, wirva khula ǝn saks dǝ dlaɗakh sar. Dlaɗakhe khana a tlakurar kǝ khanen.
MAT 7:1 Bamarghǝr ba dǝ ghaza kǝ itsawar bi, khai kǝ ba kur ghǝr kǝ Yazhigǝl ad ghaz.
MAT 7:2 Ya khulf taka lave manakur kǝ udakh, da taka kura ndǝk yanud. Darame ǝn kurara da kur kǝ udakh, da kura kura din ud.
MAT 7:3 Uɗa kǝ mangan tsǝkha ǝn vaz sasikw ai ǝn di kǝ zǝr babagh, ai nguse ǝn di tsǝkha nga ɗangwa din biyi?
MAT 7:4 Da kwara ndarkha kǝ zǝr babagh kwarne, Ɓakhdal ɓa ka sasikw ǝn di tsǝkh, Ghǝra ghǝragh ngusan di tsǝkhe?
MAT 7:5 Mbaɗirana digi. Ndǝɗadal ndǝɗa ad nguse ǝn di tsa kha ndan, ki zǝɗa nǝgha nǝgha tsǝkha char, kǝ da ndǝɗado sasikw ai ǝn di kǝ sǝkwtagh.
MAT 7:6 Bamara ba dǝgakhe dǝg Yazhigǝl kǝ ghǝd bi, kaɗamardu ba dǝg kwinda chaɗure dzau gan ǝn tǝf kǝ daguwakh bi. Wirva da tǝrkwǝdu tǝrkwa itar, da guyafkhai itar da vakur da vandz kur vandza itar.
MAT 7:7 Ɗawam ɗawa, da bakura bǝgud. Gatam gata da gǝmadu gǝma kur. Dughwam dughwa ghay gud da ngura kura ngurud.
MAT 7:8 Wirva ude takaɗgana da bara bǝgud, ude gatgana da gǝmadu gǝm, tsuguna ude dughgwan ad ghay gud da ngurara ngurud.
MAT 7:9 War ǝn tǝb tsǝkur, kur dadakh, da ka ɗauga zǝr sar ad dǝg zu, ka baran ad kuri?
MAT 7:10 Awana da takaɗga zǝr ad kilf, ka baran ad bubi?
MAT 7:11 Da kure kǝladakha tsa tsǝkur bara dǝgakhe khwarkhwaran kǝ zarur, ngǝɗukw Dadure ǝn gharazhigǝl, afke da bǝdu bǝg ad dǝg khwarkhwaran kǝ udakhe takaɗgan ǝn vak sar.
MAT 7:12 Ɗaga dǝge ǝn nagh kur mana kura mana kǝ udakh ka manatǝra mana ghǝrur, wirva yan dǝge ǝn tuku ndzikha ndzikh Mus zǝ tsagdutsaga tlayangakh Yazhigǝl.
MAT 7:13 Damaks ǝn tǝ dlikhwan na kǝ rang, wirva rangena bang, ɗul daksa tsuguna bang daks da kar. Liye ǝn daks ǝn tǝf tsuguna zikǝn itar.
MAT 7:14 Wirva rang da tǝ ɗul mbǝladu safa kǝ ngǝɗa dlikhw, ɗulen tsuguna dlikhw. Liye ǝn gatars kǝ ɗulen tsuguna na itar zikǝn bi.
MAT 7:15 Tsukwamana ghǝr dǝ tlayang filfilakh liye sakhasaks da vakura ǝn jakva tuwaghakh, ǝn khuɗ tara ndǝk khǝda tǝghalagh itar liye mbatǝra way.
MAT 7:16 Da katltǝr ǝn tǝ ɗule manda itar tlǝr kur. Ən mbǝlo mbǝlakh zǝr inabi ǝn tǝ ǝmdaga? Awana zǝr ghǝdiv ǝn tǝ dzadzǝfa?
MAT 7:17 Ndǝkyan itsera kǝ ufa khwaran ǝn yig zǝr khwaran, ufe bǝzan tsuguna ǝn yig zǝr bǝzan.
MAT 7:18 Ufa khwaran naba da yig zǝr bǝzan bi, ndǝkyan ufa bǝzan tsugun, na ba da yig zǝr khwaran bi.
MAT 7:19 Ɗeghwa ufe kwar nǝg ǝn yig zǝr khwaran, da ǝntlars ǝntlud tlǝvdagh ud da kar.
MAT 7:20 Wirva yan, da tsa diwa vak man tlǝr tar kur ad tlayang filakh.
MAT 7:21 Daghan ba ude ǝn ɗakh ka dǝ Dadzikan, Dadzikan da daks da tlǝksa gharazhigǝl bi. Kwa ude a manga dǝge nagha Dadare ǝn gharazhigǝl.
MAT 7:22 Ai fitsa Taka lava, zikǝn udakhai da kwara ka kwarne Dadzikan, Dadzikan, tsa kwarga bakh kǝnda lave da dzaughǝr ǝn tǝvuk dǝ ɗakhagha? A lakwdu bakh kǝnda shaɗan ǝn ɗakhagha? A manga bakh kǝnda tlǝrakh dǝg japǝr ǝn ɗakhagha?
MAT 7:23 Ka da kwara tǝra kwara ka kwarne, ǝn tsa kura ba ka lingling bi. Tsiyam tsiyan ǝn vakar, kuram li man kǝlad.
MAT 7:24 Wirva yan, ɗeghwa ude a tsǝnga lavaran, mangan tsugun ad tlǝr din, da ndǝk ude kwelemlem ai khǝga fǝtasar ǝn tǝ fǝraɗ.
MAT 7:25 Tǝɗga kǝ yu, ka saudagh rǝkhagw, ka tsiyawo fuɗ sǝgo ka tlǝg mǝghen, a mbǝdga ba tsugun bi, wirva a ndǝravǝn ǝn fǝraɗ.
MAT 7:26 Ɗeghwa ude tsǝna lavaran tsugun kalwala kǝ manaman, da ndǝk dlage ndǝrga fǝtasar ǝn zagh.
MAT 7:27 Tǝɗga kǝ yu, ka saudagh rǝkhagw, ka tsiyawo fuɗ sǝgo ka tlǝg mǝghen, ka mbǝɗgan kwashang kwashang.
MAT 7:28 Audzala kǝ Yasu ǝn kwarakh dǝgakhan, ka ndawatǝref tsagdu lavsar na kǝ dzakhava udakh,
MAT 7:29 a tsagatǝrdu ba ndǝk li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh bi, wirva tsagatǝru ndǝk ude nǝg dǝ ndzǝɗa tsagdu lav.
MAT 8:1 Saudagh kǝ Yasu ǝn tǝ bǝɗar, ka gatars udakh zikǝn.
MAT 8:2 Ka sa dadak madagwilf da tǝvuk sar, kǝlgan ad juguv ka ni, “Dadzikan, da khayanǝfkh tǝkhaha kǝ mbaku fidigiɗ.”
MAT 8:3 Ka talal Yasu ad dǝv sar ka gǝman ad uden, ka ni, “A khayanǝf kǝ, mbumbǝg fidigiɗ.” Ən tǝvin tǝvin ka mbu ǝn tuk fich.
MAT 8:4 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Tsǝna, kwarara ba kǝ itsawar ad dǝge dzaughǝr bi, dǝg da mǝdlara ghǝragh kǝ zil kǝs, bǝdu kha dǝg zaɓa tlatlǝɓ ndǝk vai kwarga ndzikha ndzikh Mus niya. Manga mana ndǝkyan, ki da mǝdla kwarne a mbukha kǝ dlam.”
MAT 8:5 Da kǝ Yasu da Kafarnakhum, ka sasǝg kǝ mal ya tlujiyakh da waksar kǝ takaɗa kwarne,
MAT 8:6 “Dadzikan, zǝr tlǝrar ǝn khǝngan ǝn mǝgh, ǝmtsan tlapǝl vǝgh tsin, ǝn khǝɓ dlaɗ char.”
MAT 8:7 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Da dǝgal ka da mbambǝg.”
MAT 8:8 Ka ngawar khai mal ya tlujiyakh kwarne, “Dadzikan, ǝn tlala ba ka kǝ saks tsǝkha da fǝtara bi. Uk lava da kwarga kha, da mbǝga dad tlǝrar.
MAT 8:9 Wirva ka dǝ ghǝrara ǝn kuskǝ ud kǝ, tsuguna nǝg tlujiyakh ǝn kustsǝk, tǝkhaka kǝ kwarar khai kin, ‘Dǝg dǝgal,’ ka dǝgal, da ka nika kǝ tlǝrna tsugun, ‘Saw,’ ka saks, da ka nika kǝ zǝr tlǝrar, ‘Mana dǝ yan kǝ digit,’ ka mana man.”
MAT 8:10 Tsǝna kǝ Yasu ndǝk yan ka ndawak ni, ka niya kǝ liye gatars gat, “Jir ǝn kwara kura kǝ, ǝn khuɗ kǝ ya Izrail a nǝgha ba ka dadak fadǝghǝro fǝg dǝ ndzǝɗa ndǝk ina bi.
MAT 8:11 Ən kwara kura kwara kǝ, zikǝn li kwal Izrailakh da sǝgo ǝn mbǝrt kǝs zǝ ǝn tǝvak ghǝr, ki da ndzakhgan tsitar zǝ Brakhim zǝ Ishaku zǝ Yakub ǝn tǝ vak khwaɗga ǝn tlǝksa gharazhigǝl.
MAT 8:12 Liye tsa itar ǝn khaitǝra giɗǝn tlǝksa Yazhigǝl, itar udakhe da tlǝv tǝr dagh ud da nikan na kǝ gurtl, vake da tuwa itar da kǝrɗ tliɗ.”
MAT 8:13 Ka nǝv Yasu kǝ mal ya tlujiyakh, “Dǝg dǝgal, wirva fadǝghǝro fǝgagh da mana kha manud.” Ən dǝvǝn dǝva ka mbu zǝr man tlǝr saren.
MAT 8:14 Da kǝ Yasu da fǝta Bitrus, ka nǝghan ad bab nus Bitrus magulaɓ ǝn ndzikǝn ǝn khǝngan.
MAT 8:15 Ka gǝman ad dǝv sar, ka mbu ǝn tuk magulaɓ. Ka tsifa tarkhe ad dǝgzu.
MAT 8:16 Ɓǝlga kǝ khagwa, Ka ɓardǝghǝr udakh ad liye kǝɗtǝr shatan kǝ Yasu zikǝn, uk lava dǝ ghay kalti a kwarga Yasu, ka dzadal ad sǝɗikw bǝzan ǝn vǝgh tsitar, ka mbakhandu tsugun ad liye kwal yanga daghan.
MAT 8:17 A mangan ad ina kǝ righada dǝge tsa kwarga Ishay tlayang kwarne, “In dǝ ghǝr sar kǝ ɓǝf ad kuɗ lapi mar. Ka ɓakiyamghǝr ad kuzakh mar.”
MAT 8:18 Vazga kǝ Yasuwa tsarghǝr dzakhava udakh zikǝna, ka kwarar khai kǝ furakh sar kǝ zǝghva dǝgal da tǝ yan kǝ ghǝdzǝva gadzak dǝlva Urdun.
MAT 8:19 Ka saks kǝ dadak tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus da vak sar kǝ kwarara kwara kwarne, “Malǝma, da gatakhs gata ka tsa da makh.”
MAT 8:20 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Uvakha nǝg fikakh tar, ɗikakhe pǝdlǝn gharazhigǝl tsuguna nǝg itar dǝ fǝtakha tar. Ai Zǝr Uda, na ba dǝ vake da bǝg din ghǝr sar bi.”
MAT 8:21 Ka nǝv tlǝrna fur sar tsin, “Dadzikan, ka daks da khǝɗana dadara ndan.”
MAT 8:22 “Gataks gat, khǝɗa khǝɗa tlamtsakh ad tlamtsakh tar.” Nǝv Yasu tsin.
MAT 8:23 Da kǝ Yasu zǝ furakh sar da peryuwa ka dǝgal tsitar.
MAT 8:24 Ka sugo kǝ zikan kǝ kalangas ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dǝlv, ka farsa daks kǝ ghǝɗkuta yu ǝn dǝlv da peryu. Yasu tsuguna ǝn khǝn khar.
MAT 8:25 Ka dǝgal tsitar da tsiya tsiya kǝ kwarara kwara kwarne, “Dadzikan, Katkiyam kat, da ruwa kiyam.”
MAT 8:26 Ka niya tsitar, “Uɗa lava tsǝkur ǝn gǝdza ndikini? Kuram li khǝtsa fadǝghǝrofǝg.” Ka tsif, tavarghǝr ad di kǝ fuɗǝn zǝ dǝlv, ka ɗiw vake.
MAT 8:27 Ka ndawatrǝf kǝ udakh, avitar, “Khulf ira kǝ ud ini? Zǝva fuɗa zǝ dǝlv ǝn tsǝnaru tsǝni?”
MAT 8:28 Dala kǝ Yasu da tǝ yan kǝ ghǝdzǝva gadzak ǝn tǝ khay kǝs ya Gadarakh, ka sawala ud mits li dǝ sǝɗikw bǝzan ǝn giɗe ngitl, ka gamgitar zin. Na ude dlǝn tǝkha kǝ dal ǝn tǝ yanen kǝ ɗul bi. Wirva nagh bakha jaga tsitar bi.
MAT 8:29 Tǝvin tǝvina ka khula tsitar kwarne, “Zǝr Yazhigǝl uɗa ɗangwa tsǝkha dǝ kǝndǝndi? A sa da bakǝnda dlaɗ nagh kha dla sart kwal sagha?”
MAT 8:30 Ən tǝvuk khǝɗikǝna, nǝg li zighw giɗa dagu.
MAT 8:31 Ka takaɗga sǝɗikw bǝzana khen ad Yasu kwarne, “Da lakundalakh, ka khayakǝndanǝfkh daks da daguwa khan.”
MAT 8:32 Ka niya tsitar, “Iyo, damdǝg.” Ka dǝgala itar, da itar da daguwen. Ka tsiyif giɗa ya daguwen daghan kujaɗkujaɗ, ka ɗaɗara itar dǝga dagh da dǝlv, ruga itar ǝn yu.
MAT 8:33 Ka khwaya kǝ li zighw daguwen, daks da khuɗkǝs ka kwardu lav itar, ǝnt dǝge dzaughǝr dǝ liye dǝ sǝɗikw bǝzan.
MAT 8:34 Ka sawal udakh ǝn khuɗkǝs daghan kǝ gama zǝ Yasu. Nǝgha tsitara, ka takaɗga itar kǝ ɗuwatǝr da kǝs tar tsin.
MAT 9:1 Ka dagh Yasu da peryu, ka darghǝr kǝ dǝlven kǝ daks da kǝs ai ɗakdin.
MAT 9:2 Sa tsitar da khuɗkǝs ka ɓardǝghǝr yakhaya kǝ udakh ad dadak mǝtsa tlapel vǝgh ǝn khǝngan ǝnt khindz. Katlga kǝ Yasu ad fadǝghǝro fǝga tar, ka niya kǝ dadak mǝtsa tlapel vǝghen, “Ndiɗ biya zǝrara, a ɓisakhanud khaipagh.”
MAT 9:3 Tsǝna tsitar yana, ka nǝv chalǝm li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus ǝn tǝb tar, “Ina kǝ uda ǝn nena Yazhigǝl.”
MAT 9:4 Tsa kǝ Yasu ad dǝge ǝn ɗaya itar ghǝr ǝn tǝf, ka niya tsitar, “Uɗa lava tsukur ǝn dzam dǝge ghwaɗghwaɗan ǝn rǝvur ndǝk ini?
MAT 9:5 Ira ngulman ra, ‘A ɓisakhanud khaipakhagha nagha,’ awana, ‘Tsiya dǝg dǝgal khi’?
MAT 9:6 Ai ǝn na ka tsatsǝg tsukur kwarne, ka Zer Ud nǝg ka dǝ ndzǝɗ ǝn lard na kǝ ɓisa khaipakh.” Ka niya kǝ dadak mǝtsa tlapel vǝgh, “Tsiyǝf tsiy, ɓa khindza daks da mǝgh.”
MAT 9:7 Tǝvin tǝvina, ka tsiyif udanena ka daks tsin da fǝta sar.
MAT 9:8 Vazga kǝ dzakhava udakha ndǝkyana ka gǝdzǝf itar, ka ɗabanǝf itar Yazhigǝle bara khulfina kǝ ndzǝɗa kǝ udakh.
MAT 9:9 Ɗuwars kǝ Yasu ad vaken, madǝvin ǝn zu vuk dǝ dǝg, ka nǝghan ad udanen ai ɗakhud dǝ Matiyu, ǝn ndzǝgan tǝvak chau khadam, ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “gataks gat.” Ka tsiyifa gatars.
MAT 9:10 Ən tǝ khal kǝ yan, madǝv Yasu ǝn zu kaf ǝn fata Matiyu, ka saks li chau khadam zǝ li khaipakh zikǝn saks da vak sar ndzakhga itar kǝ zu kaf dagha zǝ furakh sar.
MAT 9:11 Nǝgha kǝ Farisakh ndǝkyan, ka nǝv itar kǝ furakh sar, “Uɗa lava kǝ malǝmura ǝn zu kaf zǝ li chau khadam zǝ li khaipakhi?”
MAT 9:12 Tsǝna kǝ Yasu dina ka ni, “Na li lapi ǝn gat dadak ngura bi, uk liye kwal yang.
MAT 9:13 Dam da tsag dǝge ǝn tuku lavan, ‘Kwiɗkwirva ǝn nak ǝn vakur, dǝg tsufa bi.’ A sau kǝ ɗakh liye man dǝge ǝn nagha Yazhigǝl ba ka bi, a sau kǝ ɗakh li man khaip kǝ.”
MAT 9:14 Fitsa tlǝrna, ka sasǝg kǝ zar ɓǝlakh Yukhan dadak para ud da vak Yasu, ka nǝv itar tsin, “A manga ndar kǝnda zǝ Fariskha ǝn zǝɓ ndǝla, zar ɓǝlagha na ba itar ǝn zǝɓ ndǝl biyi?”
MAT 9:15 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai Yasu kwarne, “Da manawa ndar bazdu rǝv kǝ tsaghwakh zil ghaula, dlaitar dagha zǝ zil ghauli? Ən saks sarte da ɓatǝrvalud ad zǝ zil ghaul. Da zǝɓ ǝn tǝ sarta yan itar ndǝl.
MAT 9:16 “Na ude da ndzǝgharu wilwa lǝgwit kǝ mughura gabag bi, wirva vak ndzǝghena da takwalva, kukha sar tsuguna da mala mala ad ai tsa chak.
MAT 9:17 Na ude da ɗi wilwa yu inabi da mughura mbǝl vigh bi. Itsa ka ɗidaghud, da chaɓa mbǝl vighen, ka da ɗiya yu inabi, mbǝl vighen tsuguna da baz, azǝgha ɗaidagh ud ad wilwa yu inabi da wilwa mbǝl vigh. Wirva yana nabe da bǝghalud ǝmb bi.”
MAT 9:18 Ən tǝghǝr kǝ kwara tǝra yan kǝ lava Yasu ma, ka sasǝg kǝ mal ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ gud dzakhava Yakhudakh, ka kǝlgan ad juguv ǝn tǝvuk sar ka ni, “Amtsǝga dughwar a zulava bi, ausǝg da bo dǝv ǝn tǝf da tsi”
MAT 9:19 Ka tsiyif Yasu zǝ furakh sar, ka gatars itar kǝ udanen.
MAT 9:20 Ka nǝg tlǝrna nus ai manga vǝg kǝlatǝm mits ǝn tukw kuza kǝl vizh, ka sagh du ligsar ka gǝman ad ghay gabag sar.
MAT 9:21 Ni ǝn rǝvakhud sar, “Da gǝma ka itsa gabag sar da mbǝga kǝ.”
MAT 9:22 Gwifkhai kǝ Yasu ka nǝghan, ka ni, “Ndiɗ biya dughwara. Fadǝghǝro fǝgagha kǝ mbakhu.” Ən tǝvin tǝvin ka mbu nusen.
MAT 9:23 Sa kǝ Yasu da fǝta mal ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ gud dzakhava Yakhudakh, ka nǝgha nǝgha tsin liye fǝg fakil zǝ dzakhava udakh ǝn kwara kava ghay sikh sikh sikh.
MAT 9:24 Ka ni, “Tsiyam tsiyǝn van. Amtsǝga ba dughuna bi, ǝn khǝn khara sar.” Ka nenanef itar dǝ ghǝɓas.
MAT 9:25 Ai lakwtǝrdal tsud da mel, ka dagh khutanan ad dǝva dughwen, ka tsiyif.
MAT 9:26 A kwazga laven itsa dǝvar ǝn kǝsen.
MAT 9:27 Ba Yasu ǝn ɗuda vaken ma, ka gatars ngulfakh mits ǝn ɗakha itar dǝ ndzǝɗa kwarne, “Zǝr Doda ziwa kǝndal ziwa.”
MAT 9:28 Da kǝ Yasu da mǝgha ka sagh ngulfakhen da vak sar, ka niya tsitsar, “A fadǝghǝro nagh kur kwarne tǝkhaka kǝ mbakuruwa?” Ka nǝv itar, “Aa, tǝkha kha Dadzikan.”
MAT 9:29 Tǝkhal kǝ yana ka gǝman ad diyakh tar ka ni, “Ən tǝ dǝva dǝ fadǝghǝro fǝgura da mbakura mbǝgud.”
MAT 9:30 Ka ngwarǝf diyakh tar. Ka tǝkhatǝrna Yasu char kwarne, “Kwara mara ba kǝ itsawar ad ina kǝ digit bi.”
MAT 9:31 Ai dala tsitar, ka kwazdu itar ad lava itsa dǝvar ǝn kǝsen.
MAT 9:32 Madǝv itar dǝgal, ka ɓardǝghǝrud ad ude kwal tǝkha kǝ kwarga lav, dadake dǝ sǝɗikw bǝzan ǝn vǝgh sar.
MAT 9:33 Lakwadal tsud sǝɗikw bǝzanen, ine tsa kwar tǝkha kǝ kwarga lav ka farsa kwar lav. A ndawatrǝf kǝ dzakhava udakh ka nǝv itar, “Tsa tapa bud nǝgha khulfinak digit ǝn khaya ya Izrail bi.”
MAT 9:34 Ai ka nǝv Farisakh, “Afke ǝn zaɓado dǝ ndzǝɗa zikan na kǝ mal ya wurdu ad sǝɗikw bǝzanena.”
MAT 9:35 A dakhal Yasu da kǝsakh daghan zǝ gǝdzar kǝsakh, ǝn tsagdu tsag ǝn gud dzakhava Yakhudakh, ǝn tlǝkhdu lav zǝɗan ai tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝksa Yazhigǝl, tsuguna ǝn mbakha udakh zikǝn, zǝ itsera kǝ khulf kuzakh zǝ li kuɗ lapi.
MAT 9:36 “Nǝgha tsin udakh a dzavkhai zikǝn, ka kwiɗ nǝv rǝv tsin, wirva ǝn khǝɓ dlaɗ itar na ude ǝn mǝlatǝru mǝla bi, ngwaɗa tuwaghakh itar kwal nǝg kǝ dadak zighwtǝr zighw.”
MAT 9:37 “Ka niya kǝ furakh sar, zikǝn tsǝg khi, li man tlǝr tsuguna khǝɗikǝn.
MAT 9:38 Wirva yan, takaɗam takaɗa Dadzikan dadake nǝgharu kǝ tlǝr gukhen, kǝ ɓǝlondagh li man tlǝr kǝ tsara khi.”
MAT 10:1 Ka ɗakhga Yasu ad furakh sar kǝlatǝm mits, a batǝran ad ndzǝɗa lakdu itsǝra kǝ siɗikw bǝzan, zǝ mbakha itsera kǝ khulf kuz zǝ liye kwal yan.
MAT 10:2 Auna ɗakhakh dzǝran na kǝ furakh na kǝlatǝm mits. Dǝg chaka, Siman ai ɗakhdud Bitrus zǝ zǝrbab sar Ndros, Yakub zǝr Zabadi zǝ zǝrbab sar Yukhan,
MAT 10:3 Filibus, Bartamawus, Tom, Matiyu dadak chaw khadam, Yakub zǝr Alf, Tladdiyus,
MAT 10:4 Siman ud ya Kanan, Yakhud Iskariyoti dadake bǝdu Yasu kǝ kǝɗgakǝɗ.
MAT 10:5 A ɓǝlatǝrǝf Yasu kǝ dzǝrana kǝ zar ɓǝlakh kǝlatǝm mits, ka tǝkhatǝrna ad lava kwarne, “Damba da vak liye kwal Yakhudakh bi, tsuguna damba da tlǝrna kǝs ya Samariyakh bi,
MAT 10:6 dam da vak udakh ya Izrail liye zaɗgan ndǝk tuwaghakh.
MAT 10:7 Madǝv kur ǝn dǝgal, kwaramatǝra lav Yazhigǝl kwarne, ‘Tlǝksa Ghǝrazhigǝla a khǝrzǝgan.’
MAT 10:8 Mbakhama liye kwal yang, tsiyanǝf kur liye amtsǝgan, mbakhanu kur liye ǝn tukw fich, lakwakh du kur sǝɗikw bǝzanakh ǝn vǝgh kǝ udakh. A bakura butiyud, bǝdu ghǝrura buti.
MAT 10:9 Ɓam ba kwaɓ dawan zǝ shabu zǝ jingal ǝn mbǝlur bi.
MAT 10:10 Ɓam ba jilaɗur bi, tsa zǝ gabag mits bi, tsa kimbak, ɓam ba tsa juguljugulur bi, wirva dadak tlǝra kalkal gǝmadu dǝg siga tlǝr sar tsin.
MAT 10:11 “Itsera kǝ kǝs zǝ gǝdzar kǝsakhe a da kur damb, gatam ga ud charan ai da giɗa kur dagh tangw da da tǝ sarte da tsida kur.
MAT 10:12 Da ka da kur da mǝghen, ka nǝghatǝrdi kur kwarne, ‘gabǝr ǝn tǝghǝr tsǝkur.’
MAT 10:13 Da ka chau kurkhai liye mǝghen, tsukwa gabǝruren ǝn tǝghǝr tsitar, ai da chau kurkhai ba itar bi, ka wura kurva gabǝrur.
MAT 10:14 Ɗaga mǝgha zǝ kǝse kwal chau kurkhai, awa bi kalwal kǝ tsǝn lavur, pangdu kur lagwate ǝn tǝ sigur dǝn sǝgawala kur ǝn kǝsen.
MAT 10:15 Kaɗi ǝn tǝkha kura kǝ, da ziwardal kǝ Sodom zǝ Gomora ud tǝghǝr kǝ kǝsen fitsa takalav.”
MAT 10:16 Ya digiyam, ya ni ɓǝla kura ɓǝla ka ngwaɗa tuwaghakh ǝn tatak ya ghǝda tǝghalakh, wirva yan ɗemekh ni kur ndǝk dǝg vukhakh, tsugun kalali nikur ndǝk kakur.
MAT 10:17 Tsukamana ghǝr kǝ udakh, wirva da lang kur langa itar da vak takalav, tsuguna da dlagha kuru kiɓ itar ǝn gud dzakhavakh tar.
MAT 10:18 Wirvǝn gataks tsǝka kur, da lang kur lang itar da tǝvuk kǝ li man tlǝks ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ tsǝkur zǝ shikakh, wirva ki da kwardu lav zǝɗan tsǝkur ǝn tǝvuk tar zǝn tǝvuk liye kwal Yakhudakh.
MAT 10:19 Da ka da zǝɓ kurdǝghǝr itar da tǝvuk li taka lav, dzamam ba dǝ dǝge da kwara kur bi biya da kwara ndar kur bi. Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sart da bakura bǝg ka dǝ lave da kwara kur.
MAT 10:20 Wirva kuram ba da kwar laven bi, wirva Sǝɗikw Chuwaɗaɗan Dadure ǝn kur, in da kwarado lava sǝgawal ǝn ghayur.
MAT 10:21 Zǝrbab da bǝdu zǝrbab sar kǝ kǝɗa kǝɗa tsud, dad tsuguna da bǝdu ad zǝr sar, zara tsuguna da tsiyara kǝ baba zǝ dad itar, zǝ man dǝgakhai da nala kǝ dlǝva ɗul ǝmtsa tar.
MAT 10:22 Itsawara da nagh kur ba wirva ka bi. Ude bǝga rǝv tangw da tǝ mbasa sar da katakatud.
MAT 10:23 Da ka bakura dlaɗud ǝn mbiyan kǝ kǝs, ka kwaya kur da tlǝrna kǝs, ya kaɗiyǝn ǝn kwara kura kǝ, kǝda ditla ɗaga kǝs ya Izrail tsǝkur, da sosǝg ka Zǝr Ud.
MAT 10:24 Na dadake ǝn tsag digit da mal dadak ai ǝn tsagardu tsaga bi, awana zǝr tlǝre malga dad mǝgh sar bi.
MAT 10:25 Da ka tlakǝnalin kǝ dadak tsag lava kǝ nǝga ndǝk dadak tsagdu lav, zǝr tlǝr tsuguna ndǝk dad mǝghsar. Da ka mal ya wurdu kha nǝv itar kǝ dad mǝghena, da ɗakha dǝ uɗitar ad yakhsari?
MAT 10:26 Wirva yan, gǝdzamtǝr bi, wirva na dǝge khǝmban ai kwal da mǝdlandowal tsud bi, tsuguna na dǝge ɓǝghan kwal da tsatsud bi.
MAT 10:27 Dǝge ǝn kwara kura kǝ ǝn gurtl, kwaram kwar ǝn tǝ fatsi tǝghǝr. Dǝge kwarakh dagh ud da tlim, tlǝkhamdu tlǝkhǝn tǝ mbachar.
MAT 10:28 Gǝdzam ba dǝ liye tǝkha kǝ kǝɗga vǝghur bi, ya tǝkh ba itar kǝ kǝɗga saf bi. Gǝdzam gǝdza Yazhigǝl ai tǝkh kǝ kǝɗga vǝgha zǝ saf tangw da tǝ fay.
MAT 10:29 Mits bakh chughwaghwakh ǝn sukwduwud ǝn tǝ shabu kitakula? Na bai da ɓǝlal itsa kitakul da khay ai kwal da tsa kǝ dadur bi.
MAT 10:30 Afke itsa guj ghǝrura kǝdlana.
MAT 10:31 Wirva yana, gǝdzam bi. Afke a malga kur ad chughwaghwakh zikǝn kǝ ndanga char.
MAT 10:32 Ɗaga ude mǝdla kwarne dǝg sar kǝ ǝn tǝvuk kǝ udakh, ghǝrar tsuguna da mǝdla mǝdla ka kwarne dǝgar ghǝrsar ǝn tǝvuk Dadare ǝn ghǝrazhigǝl.
MAT 10:33 Ɗaga ude bǝga tsuguwar ǝn tǝvuk kǝ udakh, ghǝrar tsuguna da bǝg tsugu kǝn tǝvuk kǝ Dadare ǝn ghǝrazhigǝl.
MAT 10:34 Dzamam ba kwarne gabǝr a ɓadagh ka da lard bi. A so kǝ wirva ɓado gabǝr ba ka bi, ya katsakar.
MAT 10:35 Ya so kǝ, Wusha zǝra zǝ dad sar. Dugh zǝ bab sar tsǝgun. Ghawul tsuguna zǝ dzik sar nus.
MAT 10:36 Dadak mǝgha yakh sar da nǝga kǝ tlǝghum sar.
MAT 10:37 Ude ǝn way bab sar zǝ dad sar mal tsǝk, a tlal ba kǝ nǝga kǝ zǝr ɓǝlara bi. Ude ǝn way zǝr sar awana dugh sar mal tsǝka tsugun, a tlal ba kǝ nǝga kǝ zǝr ɓǝlara bi.
MAT 10:38 Ude ɓǝf ba dǝ ufa khǝrta sar kǝ gataks gata bi, a tlal ba kǝ nǝga kǝ zǝr ɓǝlara bi.
MAT 10:39 Ude ǝn nagh kat safa sar, da bǝgh. Ude kǝɗdu safa sar wirva kǝ, da gǝmadu gǝm.
MAT 10:40 Ɗaga ude a chau kurkhai, ka chau ka yin, ude chau kai tsuguna Dade ɓǝlakondagh a chau gin.
MAT 10:41 Ɗaga ude chauga tlayang Yazhigǝl da chauga kǝ wirve tlayangin. Dǝg sige da baruda, da kalkal zǝ dǝg tlayangen. Ɗaga ude chauga dadak kalali da chauga kǝ wirve dadak kalali yin, dǝg sige da baruda da kalkal zǝ dǝg dadak kalaliyen.
MAT 10:42 Ɗaga ude ǝnkaru itsa kwat yu kitakul ak khǝɗikan ǝn tatak furar wirve furarin, ya jir ǝn kwara kura kǝ, na ba da bǝghǝn dǝg sig sar bi.
MAT 11:1 Udzala kǝ Yasu ǝn tǝkhatǝra lava kǝ furakh sar kǝlatǝm mits, ka ɗuwars ad yanen kǝ vak, tsuguna ka dǝgal tsin da tsagatǝrdu tsaga zǝ tlǝkhatǝra lav Yazhigǝl kǝ dlǝmdla kǝsakhe khǝrza dǝ yanen kǝ kǝs.
MAT 11:2 Tsǝna kǝ Yukhan dadak para ud ǝn zaw ad dǝgakhe tsǝn mana Kristu, ka ɓǝlandal ad chalǝm Zar ɓǝlakh sar da vak sar.
MAT 11:3 Nǝv itar kǝ Yasu, “Kwara kǝnkhe kwar,” “Kha naghek dadake tsǝn kwara Yukhan dadak para ud da sǝgdagh na, nagha da gwit tlǝrna ud sikha khǝkǝndi?”
MAT 11:4 Nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Damaks da kwarara kwara kǝ Yukhan ad dǝge tsǝna kur zǝ dǝge nǝgha kur.
MAT 11:5 Ngulfakha a ngwarǝf di tsitar, ǝn dǝga ghwurɗikakha, li kuza fǝcha a mbakharu fidgiɗ, ǝn tsǝnatsǝna tǝngakh, a gwidǝn tsaya tǝrǝfud kǝ li tsa amtsǝgan, ka kwaratǝra lav zǝɗan ud kǝ talagakh.
MAT 11:6 Dadak bark liye kwal guyakdu lig wirva dǝge ǝn mana kǝ.”
MAT 11:7 Madv zar bǝla Yukhan ǝn daks, ka farsa Yasu kwara tǝra lava kǝ udakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ Yukhan kwarne, “Dala tsǝkur da vak Yukhan ǝn tǝghal, da kuram ǝn kurana wuɗa tsǝn nakur nǝgha nǝghi? A dal da vaz tsǝɓ tsǝɓan kǝ mase ǝn kaɗa fuɗ nagh kur?
MAT 11:8 Tsa dal da vaz uɗa kuri? Ude chaɗfkhai ǝn kadlang khwaran naghf kur? Liye chaɗfkhai ndǝkyana ǝn gidǝn tǝ gǝlvakh shikakh itar fǝka.
MAT 11:9 Kwara make kwar, tsa dal da vaz uɗa kuri? Tlayang nagha? Ndǝk yanen, ai tsuguna a nǝgha tsǝkur dadake a malgan ad Tlayang.
MAT 11:10 Tsa Yukhan dadake tsa vindzava lav ǝn tǝghǝr tsin ǝn kaɗkaɗ kwarne, “ ‘Da ɓǝlaɓǝla ka ad zǝr ɓǝlara kǝ dakho ǝn tǝ vuk. Dadake da ɗikakha ɗul.’
MAT 11:11 Ən tekha kura tǝkha kǝ, na nuse taɓa yig zǝr ai do da tǝ Yukhan dadak para ud dǝ ndanga bi. Ai tsugun, dadake khǝɗikan ǝn tlǝksa gharazhigǝla a malgan ad Yukhan kǝ ndang.
MAT 11:12 Tsif ǝnt sarte tsa kwardu Yukhan dadak para ud ad lav Yazhigǝl tangw da tina kǝ sart. A wushif ghǝr kǝ tlǝksa gharazhigǝl, li tsiyara mǝkǝn kǝ udakha ǝn nagh pǝrd tlǝksa Yazhigǝl itar dǝ ndzǝɗ.
MAT 11:13 Lave a tsagdu nzdikha nzdikh Musa zǝ kaɗkaɗ tlayangakh daghan a kwarga itar lav ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝksen kǝda sǝgdagh kǝ Yukhan
MAT 11:14 Da khayanǝf kur dǝ lav tara, Yukhan ai tsǝn kwarud lavǝn teghǝra, in Ili na tsǝn kwarud da sǝgdagh.
MAT 11:15 Tsǝna dadak tlim ad lave kwarud.
MAT 11:16 “Da kura dǝ war ka udakh zamani? Ghila zar mbisane ǝn giɗǝn te ɓala kasuk ǝn ɗakhva kǝ da man sakw ǝn tatak tar itar zǝ kwar lava kwarne,
MAT 11:17 “ ‘Fakurkhe kǝnda fyakǝla. Kalwala kur kǝ tsug. Fuka kurkhai kǝnda fuk. Kalwala kur kǝ tu.’
MAT 11:18 Sodagh kǝ Yukhana, tsa nabǝn zu dǝg zuwakh zǝ khǝɓ itsera kǝ digitakh bi, ‘Ka sǝɗikw wurdu ǝn vǝghtsino nǝv itar.’
MAT 11:19 Wur sodagh Zer Uda, ǝn zuwa zuwa zǝ khǝɓa khǝɓ, ‘Vaza dǝ udan na. Mbǝlv zǝn ɗayuɗay, zǝ tsaghw li chau khadama zǝ li man khepo nǝv itar.’ Tlǝre ǝn mana udan in da mǝdlan ad kwalemleme a bara Yazhigǝl.”
MAT 11:20 Udakhe ǝn kǝsakhe tsa manakhga Yasu ad dǝg ndawakakh ǝn kǝs tar, a kalwala itar kǝ pǝlghǝr, ka tavatǝrghǝr ad di.
MAT 11:21 Ɗangwa tsǝkur, Korasin. Ɗangwa tsǝkur, Betsaid. Da tsa a manakhgǝn kǝs ya Taya zǝ Sidom ud ad dǝg ndawakhe a manavǝn vakur, tsa pǝlga itar ghǝr gulyan, tsa ɗaiva itar ad Ligwit ngǝz zǝ ɗaiva fǝts ǝn tǝ vǝghakh tar.
MAT 11:22 Ai tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, da ziwardala kǝ udakh ya Taya zǝ Sidon ud tǝghǝr tsǝkur fitsa man taka lav.
MAT 11:23 Kha tsugun Kafarnakhum, da ghǝr tsǝkhǝn kurana da ɓǝkha ɓakhud da gharazhigǝla? Əmma tsǝkhara, da kǝɗkh dagh da vak liye ǝn tǝ fayud. Da tsa mangǝn Sadom ud ad dǝg ndawakakhe tsa mangud ǝn vakur, tsa dla itar sakhkan.
MAT 11:24 Ai tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, da ziwardala kǝ udakh ya Sadom ud tǝghǝr tsǝkur fitsa man taka lav.
MAT 11:25 Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sart a kwarga Yasu kwarne, “Ən kwara kha us ka Dada, Dadzikan dadak gharazhigǝl zǝ khay, wirva a ɓǝgharna kha dǝgakhana kǝ liye kwalemlem zǝ liye ǝn tsa lav, ka mǝdlatǝrankh kǝ zar mbisan liye kwal tsa lav.
MAT 11:26 Khwara Dada, wirva ndǝk yanen kǝ manakhal.
MAT 11:27 “A ba ka Dadar ad digitakh daghan. Na ude tsa Zǝr bi uk Dad, tsuguna na ude tsa Dad bi uk Zǝr, zǝ udakhe a naghga Zǝren tsugun ad mǝdlatǝramǝdl.
MAT 11:28 “Ausǝgam da vakar, daghanure a suvgan dǝ zǝɓ kadlang ɗimɗiman, da bakura fǝtava kǝ.
MAT 11:29 Ɓamǝf ɓa changlagara da tǝ pepur. Tsagam tsagǝn vakar, wirva ka dadak tsukwana ghǝr kǝ man digitakh kǝ, zǝ dadak gulandagh ghǝr kǝ ǝn rǝv, ka da mbǝladu mbǝla kur fǝtava kǝ ghǝrur.
MAT 11:30 Changlagara na ba ɗimɗim bi, kadlangara tsuguna chafchaf.”
MAT 12:1 Ən sartena a dala Yasu dǝgal diwa gukh ǝlkam fitsa fǝtava Yakhudakh. Ndzitǝrǝf kǝ wai kǝ furakh sar, ka farsa itar ad sǝɗ khi ǝlkam kǝ zuwazu.
MAT 12:2 Nǝgha kǝ Farisakh ndǝk yana, ka kwararkhe itar kǝ Yasu kwarne, “Vaz, ǝn man dǝge a gadlga ndzikh zar ɓǝlakhagh fitsa fǝtava Yakhudakh.”
MAT 12:3 Ka nev Yasu tsitar, “A tugwa bakh kur ad dǝge manga Dod mbatǝra kǝ wai zǝ li dǝgakh sara?
MAT 12:4 Ka da da Fǝta Yazhigǝl, ka ɓǝf itar zǝ li dǝga sar ad brudiye kwal kalkal ba zuwa zuwa tsitar bi, uk Zilkǝs kitakul da zuwan.
MAT 12:5 Tsa tugwa bakh kur ǝn ndzikha ndzikh Mus kwarne, Zil kǝsakhkhe ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝla ǝn kǝla ndzikh itar fitsa fǝtav. Tsuguna a nala ba kwarne a manga itar khaip bi.
MAT 12:6 Tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, auna ude a malgan ad Fǝta Yazhigǝl kǝ ndangǝn vana khan.
MAT 12:7 Da tsa katlga kur dǝge ǝn kwara kaɗkaɗ, ai kwarga Yazhigǝl kwarne, ‘Giɗa kwiɗkwiɗǝrǝv ǝn na kǝ, dǝg tsufa bǝn na ka bi.’ Tsa na kur ǝn batǝrghǝr ghaza kǝ li kwal dǝ khaip bi.
MAT 12:8 Wirva yan ka Zǝr Ud, ka Dadmǝgh fitsa fǝtava Yakhudakh.”
MAT 12:9 Ka ɗuwars Yasu ad yanen kǝ vaka, ka dadǝg tsin da gud dzakhava Yakhudakh.
MAT 12:10 Ən gud dzakhvena, nǝg udanen dadak ǝmtsa dǝv, ka ndiɗarwar itar kǝ Yasu kwarne, “A khayanǝf nagh ndzikh ad mba ud fitsa fǝtava?” Nǝv itar kǝ nǝghda mbǝladu ghaza Yasu.
MAT 12:11 Ai ka nditarwal Yasu kwarne, “Da ka nǝg ude dǝ tuwagh ǝn tatakuran, da ɓǝldaghin da fik fitsa fǝtav, atsuk na dadak tuwaghǝn da ɓado ɓa biya?
MAT 12:12 Afka a malga ud ad tuwagh kǝ ndanga char. Wirva yana a khayanǝf ndzikha ad mǝlaru kǝ ud fitsa fǝtav.”
MAT 12:13 Khalak yana ka niya kǝ dadak ǝmtsa dǝven, “Taladala dǝvagh” Ka taladal, ǝn tǝvin tǝvina ka mbu dǝva sar charang, ka nala ndǝk yan kǝ dǝv.
MAT 12:14 Da mbiyanen, ka dǝgal kǝ Farisakh da ɗi dzanak kǝɗ Yasu kǝ ǝmts.
MAT 12:15 Katlga kǝ Yasu ad rajakhadghǝr (ɗayaghǝr) tara, ka ɗudan ad yanen kǝ vak. Ka gatars gata kǝ udakh zikǝn. Ka mbakhatǝru kǝ li kwal tsa yanga daghan.
MAT 12:16 Ka ndǝɗatǝrnǝf ad tlim kwarne, kwarara betar kǝ udakh ad lav ǝn tǝghǝr tsin bi.
MAT 12:17 Dǝge mangin kǝ righanǝf dǝge tsa kwarga Ishay Tlayang. Ai kwarga Ishay kwarne,
MAT 12:18 “Auna zǝr tlǝre a zǝɓǝf kǝ. Ən waya waya kǝ, ai zǝɗaku zǝɗa char. Da bara bǝg ka dǝ Sǝɗikwar. Tsǝguna ka da tlǝkhdu lav ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ taka lav jir kǝ khulf udakh daghan.
MAT 12:19 Na ba da man tsugu zǝ bura bi. Da tsǝna bud lav sar dǝ ndzǝɗ ǝn tǝ ɗulakh ǝn khuɗ kǝs bi.
MAT 12:20 Mbaɗize tsa tǝrɗǝfa, naba da kǝlakǝla bi. Karakazaze tsa dǝm da ǝmtsa, naba da kǝɗakǝɗa bi. Da tǝkhavala tǝkh, akwa nǝghin ad taka lav jir a zugan ad fir.
MAT 12:21 Da bo ghǝr ǝn tǝ ɗakha sar udakh liye kwal tsa Yazhigǝl daghan.”
MAT 12:22 Ka ɓardǝghǝr yakhaya kǝ udakh ad ude ngulf ai ghwirtl da vak Yasu, wirva sǝɗikw bǝzan ǝn vǝgh tsin. Ka mbanu Yasu. Ka farsan ad kwar lav, tsuguna ka nǝgha nǝgh.
MAT 12:23 Ka ndawatǝrǝf kǝ udakh daghan, Ka nǝv itar, “Ara, ina kuda in khǝ Zǝr Doda?”
MAT 12:24 Ai tsǝna kǝ Farisakh ndǝk yana ka nǝv itar, “Afka dǝ ndzǝɗa tsawar bi. Dǝ ndzǝɗa Baalzabul shik ya wurdu, ǝn zaɓakhadowin ad sǝɗikw bǝzan ǝn vǝgh kǝ udakh.”
MAT 12:25 Fatsiye audzala Yasu ǝn tsa dǝge ǝn ɗaya itar ǝn rǝvakhuɗ tar, ka avin tsitar, “Ɗaga tlǝkse a tǝkaghǝran mits, ǝn tlughuma itar ǝn tatak tar, yanen kǝ tlǝksa da ghitsga ba dangar bi. Ɗeghwa kǝsa zǝ mǝghe a tǝkaghǝra mits tsugun, ǝn tlughuma itar ǝn tatak tar, na ba da ghitsa bi.
MAT 12:26 Da ka ǝn zǝɓadal Shatan, Shatan sǝgawal ǝn udakh, afka ǝn gadla dǝ ghǝrsar. Ai da ghitsa ndar tlǝksa sari?
MAT 12:27 Ai da ka dǝ ndzǝɗa Baalzabul ǝn zaɓado ka dǝ sǝɗikw bǝzanakh, ai zar ɓǝlakhura mi? Ən zǝɓtǝrdal dira kǝ ndzǝɗa itari? Ai furakhur da taka kura lav ǝn tǝghǝr kin.
MAT 12:28 Ai daka dǝ ndzǝɗa Sidikw Yazhigǝl ǝn zaɓadal ka ad shatanakh, atsuk a sa tlǝksa Yazhigǝl da tǝghǝr tsǝkur.
MAT 12:29 “A tǝkh bud kǝ da da khutsadala kadlang ǝn mǝgha dadak ndzǝdan bi, khekwa da ndzaɗana ghud ndan, bidǝgud ǝn tǝkha kǝ khutsadala kadlang ǝn fǝta sar.
MAT 12:30 “Ude kwal nǝg zǝ kǝ, atsuk ǝn man tluhguma zǝ kǝ. Ude kwal mǝlaku dǝ dzakha dzakha atsuk ǝn kwazakdu kwaz.
MAT 12:31 Wirva yan, ǝn kwara kura kwara kǝ, da ɓisatra ɓisud kǝ udakh ad itsera kǝ khaip zǝ lav nenakh ai manga itar. Ai tsugun, ude kwarga lava dǝ nen ak Sǝɗikw Yazhigǝl, na bud da ɓisara ɓisa bi.
MAT 12:32 Ɗaga ude kwarga lav nen ǝn tǝghǝr tsǝka Zer Ud, da ɓisara ɓisud. Ai ɗeghwa ude kwarga lav nen ak Sǝɗikw Yazhigǝl, linglinga na bud da ɓisara ɓisa tsa kǝvena tsa da tǝ kwarge da saks bi.”
MAT 12:33 Da nǝgharu kha kǝ uf khwaranyan zǝr khwaran da yigin. Da ka nǝgharu ba kha kǝ uf bi, zǝr bǝzan da yigin. Wirva ufa khwarana ǝn katlǝn tǝ khulf zar sar ud.
MAT 12:34 Kur zar ya pushakhan. Da tǝkh duɗa kur kǝ kwarga lav khwaran fatsiye nguɗiyakh kuri? Afka ǝn khuɗ kǝ dǝgakhe ǝn rǝvakhuɗ ud inǝn sǝgawal ǝn tukw ghay.
MAT 12:35 Ud charana, ǝn zǝɓado ǝn dǝg charane ǝn khuɗ kǝ dǝg charane a bǝgin ǝn rǝvakhuɗ sar. Ud nguɗiya, ǝn zǝɓado ǝn dǝg nguɗi, ǝn khuɗ kǝ dǝg nguɗiye, a bǝgin ǝn rǝvakhuɗ sar.
MAT 12:36 Ən kwara kura kwara kǝ, ɗeghwa kwadlamb ghaye ǝn kwara udakh, da kwara kwara itar dǝge bǝtra da kwar yanen fitsa takalav.
MAT 12:37 Ən tǝ dǝva dǝ lave kwarga kha da mana khud takalav. A bakhghǝr ud ghaza awana dadake kwal dǝ ghaz.
MAT 12:38 Ka kwararkhe yakhaya kǝ li tsagdu ndikha ndikh Mus zǝ Farisakh kwarne, “Malǝm, ǝn na kǝnda mǝdla kǝnda mǝdla tsǝkha ad zikan kǝ dǝg ndawak ai da mǝdla dakha ndzǝɗagh.”
MAT 12:39 Ka niya tsitar, “Udakh li kwargǝna, li kwal fadǝghǝro dǝ Yazhigǝl kur, nguɗiyakh tsugun. Nagha kur ad nǝgha dǝg ndawak ǝn vakar, ai na bud da mǝdla kura mǝdla bi, akwa ndawake ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ Yunan tlayang.
MAT 12:40 Ndǝkve a manga Yunan ad khǝna khǝkerɗ viɗ zǝ fatsi ǝn khuɗ kǝ zikana kǝ kilf, da mana ndǝk yan ka Zǝr Ud ad khǝna khǝkerɗ viɗa zǝ fatsi ǝn mbǝrt kǝ khay.
MAT 12:41 Fitsa takalav da kwara tǝra kwara udakh ya Nineba kǝ li kwargǝn kwarne, a manargan ad khaip. Wirva itar udakh ya Nineba a pǝlga itar ghǝr ǝn tǝ dǝva dǝ lav Yazhigǝle a kwaratǝrkhe Yunan. Ai tsuguna auna ude a malgan ad Yunan dǝ ndzǝɗ ǝn van. Dakhkana a pǝlga ba kur ghǝr bi.
MAT 12:42 Fitsa takalav, da tsiya nuse shik ǝn khay ya Sheba kǝ kwar kwarne udakh kwargǝn a manargan ad khaip. Wirva soghǝr ǝn vak bita char, kǝ tsǝn lav kwalemleme ǝn tsagdu Saluman shik. Ai tsuguna nǝg ude a malgan ad Saluman shik dǝ ndzǝɗ ǝn van.” Dakhkana a pǝlga ba kur ghǝr bi.
MAT 12:43 Da sawala sǝdikw bǝzan ǝn vǝgh kǝ ud, ka gwayav ǝn vakakhe kwal nǝg kǝ yu kǝ mbǝladu vak fǝtava tsin. Ai da ka mbǝladu bin bi,
MAT 12:44 ka ni, da gwiya daks da kwazaghare tsa sawalaka. Da gwiyoghǝrina a tlarghǝr ba kǝ itsawar bi tsuguna tleɗan, a ɗikavana mǝgh.
MAT 12:45 Ka da gwiya dǝgal da khutsado tlǝrna sǝɗikw bǝzanakh uɗif, liye malgan kǝ mbǝrsh. Kǝ daks tsitar kǝ giɗǝmb. Khalakyana, ka da malamala giɗa sare kǝ khal, ade tsa chak kǝ bǝz. Da dzaughǝr ndǝk yan kǝ nguɗi udakh li kwargǝn.
MAT 12:46 Madǝvin ǝn kwar ghay zǝ udakha, ka sasǝg kǝ bab sar zǝ zar babakh sar. Ka ghitsǝga itar ǝn mǝl, ǝn nagh kwar lava itar zin.
MAT 12:47 Ka nǝv tlǝrna ud tsin, “Babagha zǝ zarbabakhagh ǝn ghitsǝn mel, ǝn na kwar lava itar zǝ kha.”
MAT 12:48 Ka ndiɗarwal kǝ dadake tsa kwarkhe kwar, “War babara, zǝ zar babakharenra?”
MAT 12:49 Ka mǝdlarnan ad furakh sar dǝ dǝva ni, “Auna babara zǝ zar babakharǝn tǝ van.
MAT 12:50 Wirva ɗeghwa ude ǝn man dǝge ǝn nagha Dadare ǝn gharazhigǝl kǝ manaman tsin, in zǝr babara, zǝ dugh babara, zǝ babar.”
MAT 13:1 Fitsa vayanena, ka sawala Yasu ǝn mǝghen, dala ka nndzǝgan ǝn tǝ ghay dǝlv kǝ tsagardu kǝ udakh.
MAT 13:2 Dzakhava udakh zikǝn char tsarghǝr itar dingrik. Ka dagh da per yuwa nndzǝgan. Dzakhava udakh tsuguna ghitsga itar ǝn tǝ ghay dǝlv.
MAT 13:3 Ka kwara tǝr khai ad lava dǝ jakva lavakh zikǝn. Ni, “Nǝg dadak gukhen a dala da kwazdu khulf ǝn gukh sar.
MAT 13:4 Madvin ǝn kwazdu khulfa, ka ɓalala yakhay kǝ khuf ǝn tǝ ɗul, ka sa ɗikakha vaɗu itar.
MAT 13:5 Ka ɓalala yakhay kǝ khulfakh ǝn tǝ fǝraɗ vake kwal nǝg khay char. Ka fǝtsawala kujaɗ kujaɗ, wirva khayen ǝn tǝvina naba zikǝn bi.
MAT 13:6 Tǝvga kǝ fatsiya ka ɓayif itar, ka ghulala itar, wirva a dagh ba tlǝl sar char bi.
MAT 13:7 Yakhaya kǝ khulfen tsuguna a ɓalardagh da vake dǝ tak, fǝtsala tsina, ka ɗakalar zǝ tak, ka ɓidzatǝrǝf taken.
MAT 13:8 Yakhaya kǝ khulfakh tsuguna a ɓalal da vake duɓan itar. Ndǝkchiɓ yiga itar zǝr dǝrmǝk dǝrmǝk. Yakhaya kulǝnkwakh kulǝnkwakh. Yakhaya tsuguna kulkhǝkerɗ kulkhǝkǝrɗ.”
MAT 13:9 Ka nǝv Yasu kǝ dǝg mbas, Ɗeghwa ude dǝ tlim tsǝn lava, baru bǝgin tlim.
MAT 13:10 Ka sa furakh Yasu ka nǝv itar tsin, “Uɗa lava tsǝkhǝn kwaratǝra lava tǝ dǝva dǝ jakva lavakhi?”
MAT 13:11 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai kwarne, “A bakura tsǝkurud ndzǝɗa tsa dǝge ɓǝghan ǝn tǝgher kǝ tlǝksa gharazhigǝl. Ai itara a batǝra bud bi.
MAT 13:12 Wirva ɗeghwa ude dǝ digit da banarghǝr bǝgud char, ka da ndaɓai ǝn vak sar zikǝn. Ai ude kwal dǝ digit char, ka da chawarval chawud ngwaɗa khiɗike dinin.
MAT 13:13 Dǝge kǝ mangan ǝn kwara tǝra ka lava dǝ jakvakh in kwarne, “Wirva itsa vazavaza itara ǝn nǝgha ba itar bi. Itsa bǝga itar tlima ǝn tsǝna ba itar bi. Tsuguna ǝn katlanǝf ba itar bi.”
MAT 13:14 Wirva yan lave tsa kwarga Ishay tlayang a righǝf ǝn vak tar. Nǝv Ishay tlayang “Da tsǝnakha tsǝna kur lav, ai da katlga ba kur tsa khǝɗikǝn bi. Uk da ɗema di tsǝkur ǝn tǝf, ai tsuguna da tsa ba kur dǝge ǝmbin bi.
MAT 13:15 Wirva gufǝrva udakhana a ɓengɓengǝf. Ən tsǝna ba tlimakh tar ad lava bi. A khaɗakhardu itar ad diyakh tar. Khek nǝgha nǝgha tsitar dǝ diyakh tar. Khek tsǝna tsǝna tsitar dǝ tlim tar tsǝgun. Wirva nagh ba itar katlgakatlǝn rǝvakhuɗ tar bi. Ka guyoghǝr itar da vakara mbakhatru kǝ.
MAT 13:16 Nǝg bark kǝ diyakhur wirvǝn nǝgha nǝgha kur din. Ndǝk yan tlimakhur tsugun wirvǝn tsǝna tsǝna kur din.
MAT 13:17 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, zikǝn tlayangakh Yazhigǝl, zǝ li kalaliyakh, tsǝn na itar nǝgha dǝge ǝn nǝgha kur. Ai a nǝgha ba itar bi. Zǝ na tsǝna dǝge ǝn tsǝna kur. Ai a tsǝna ba itar bi.”
MAT 13:18 Auna dǝge tuku jakva lav dadak kwazdu khulfen.
MAT 13:19 Da tsǝna kǝ udan ad lavǝn tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝksa gharazhigǝl, ǝn tǝ khalak yana a katlǝga bi, a nala ghila va khulfe a ɓalal ǝn tǝ ɗul. Tsǝnga kǝ udanen ad lav Yazhigǝl, ka sa Shatan, khutsala dǝ khulfe a tukhgud ǝn gufǝrva sar.
MAT 13:20 Khulfakhe balal da tǝ khayen tǝ fǝraɗ, in jakva ude benǝn tsǝna lav Yazhigǝl, ka chauga dǝ khwaɗg.
MAT 13:21 Fatsiye a dagh ba tlǝl sar da khay char bi, baga tsin ad rǝv da tǝ sart khǝɗikǝn. Tsiyif kǝ dlaɗa, zǝ mbakhǝl ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ lav Yazhigǝle tsǝnin, kujaɗ kujaɗ ka mbǝɗgan.
MAT 13:22 Khulfe ɓaldagh da vake dǝ takakh tsugun, itar jakva udakhe tsǝnga lav Yazhigǝl. Ai wirva mbakhǝl nagh dǝg lard zǝ valaval way tluwandal ǝn lard, a gadlarkhe ad ɗaka kǝ khulfen. Khulfen tsuguna a bǝdu bad zǝr bi.
MAT 13:23 Khulfe ɓalal da tǝ vak duɓan tsugun, in jakva ude tsǝnga lav Yazhigǝl katlgan tsugun. A mangan ad tlǝr din, tlǝm gǝmadu ad nuba khulfen. Yakhaya dǝrmǝk dǝrmǝk. Yakhaya kulǝnkwakh kulǝnkwakh. Yakhaya tsuguna kulkhǝkerɗ kulkhǝkǝrɗ.
MAT 13:24 Ka gwidǝn Yasu ad kwara tǝra tlǝrna jakv lav, ni, “ Tlǝksa gharazhigǝla ghila ude tukhga khulf khwaran ǝn gukh sar.
MAT 13:25 Ən tǝ sarte ǝn khǝn khar udakh, ka dala dadak tlǝghum sar ka tukhgan ad khulf dlǝgh ǝn gukh lǝkamen. Ka tǝkaval sar.
MAT 13:26 Ɗakala kǝ lǝkamen yigan ad zǝr. Dlǝghen tsuguna, sawal ǝn khuɗ.
MAT 13:27 “Ka sagh li man tlǝr dadak gukhen da vak sar. Ka nǝv itar tsin, ‘Dadmǝgha, atsuk khulf charan bakh tsa tukhga khǝn gukhaghena? A sawal ndar dlǝgh tsugun ǝn gukheni?’
MAT 13:28 “Ka niya tsitar, ‘Dadak tlughumara kǝ mangain.’ Ka nǝv zar man tlǝrsar tsin. ‘Əna nagh kha dǝgal tsǝkǝnda da ndaɗdu ndaɗa dǝ dlǝghena?’
MAT 13:29 “Ka niya tsitar, ‘Au, wirva nalabin dǝ kur ǝn ndaɗdu dlǝgha, ndǝɗamado ba zǝva lǝkam tsugun bi.
MAT 13:30 A ɗuwam, ɗaka itar dagh zǝ lǝkam, da tǝ sarte da tsǝgdud lǝkam. Ən tǝ sarten da kwaratra ka kǝ li da tsǝgatsǝg, farsafǝg itar ndaɗdu dlǝgh chak, dzanǝf itar, ngwaɗana itar, ndaghana itar. Ka dzanǝf itar lǝkam, ɗiyakdagh ud da kuvurar.’ ”
MAT 13:31 Ka gwidǝn Yasu ad kwaratra tlǝrna jakv lav, ni, “Tlǝksa gharazhigǝl ngwaɗa khulf mastad, ai ɓǝf udanen ka tukhgan ǝn gukh sar.
MAT 13:32 Tsakhǝnmina in khǝɗikan ǝn khulfakh daghan. Ai da fǝtsawalina, ɗakalina, ka in da nǝga kǝ zikan ǝn tatak dǝgakhe ǝn ngaɓ. Da nǝga kǝ ufa zikan, ka da man mǝghakh ɗikakh ǝn tǝ gwalakh sar.”
MAT 13:33 Ka gwidǝn batra tlǝrna jakva lava kǝ Yasu kwarne, “Tlǝksa gharazhigǝla ndǝkva yisti, ai dzǝgǝf nus khǝɗikǝn, kǝ khwaɗum ǝn khǝpi lǝkam daram khǝkǝrɗ, tlǝm tsiyif kǝ khǝpiyen.”
MAT 13:34 A kwara tǝrkhai Yasu ad dǝgakhana daghan kǝ dzakhava udakh dǝ jakva lavakh. Na bǝn kwara tra lava ndǝk yan bi, akwa dǝ jakva lav.
MAT 13:35 Dǝge a manga Yasu a righanǝf ad dǝge tsa kwarga Ishay tlayang. Avin, “Da ngura ghay ka kǝ kwar lava dǝ jakva lavakh. Dǝge tsa ɓǝghanud gul farsafǝg sar kǝ lard, da kwardu kwara kǝ.”
MAT 13:36 Ən tǝ khal kǝ, ɗuwars dzakhava udakh kǝ Yasu, ka da da mǝgh. Ka saks kǝ furakh sar da vak sar. Nǝv itar tsin, “Kwara kǝnkhe kwara dǝge tuku jakva lav dlǝghe a fǝtsal ǝn gukh Lekam.”
MAT 13:37 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai, niya tsitar, “Dadake tukhga khulf khwaran, ka Zǝr Ud.
MAT 13:38 Gukh tsuguna in Lard. Khulf khwarana itar udakhe da daks da tlǝksa Yazhigǝl. Dlǝgh tsuguna itar udakh ya Shatan.
MAT 13:39 Dadak tlughume tukhga dlǝghena in wurdu. Sarta tsǝg khiyena, in fitsa mbasa lard. Li tsǝg khiyena itar zarɓǝlakh Yazhigǝl.”
MAT 13:40 Ndǝkve dzakhud mas kǝ ndǝgha ndǝgh, da ndǝk yan fitsa mbasa lard.
MAT 13:41 Ka Zǝr Ud da ɓǝlondagh ɓǝla ka zarɓǝlakh Yazhigǝlar, kǝ dzakha dzakha tsitar daghan dǝge tsǝn bakh udakh da man khaip, zǝ daghan li tsǝn man nguɗi nguɗi digitakh. Khutstral itar dǝgal ǝn tlǝksar.
MAT 13:42 Ka tlǝvtǝrdagh itar da kara tsakai tsakai, vake da tudai tar dǝ kǝrɗ tliɗ,
MAT 13:43 ǝn tǝ yanen kǝ sart, da wuɗa liye kanadi ngwaɗa fatsi ǝn tlǝksa Dad tar. Ɗeghwa ude dǝ tlim tsǝn lava, baru bǝgin tlim.
MAT 13:44 Tlǝksa gharazhigǝla ghila lemane a ɓǝghanud ǝn gukh, ai mbǝladu udan, ka gwidǝn ɓǝghanan. Wirva khwaɗga, ka dala sakwdu ad dǝgakh sare dinin daghan, ka sukwgan ad yanen kǝ gukh.
MAT 13:45 Dakhkana, tlǝksa gharazhigǝla ghila zǝr kasuke ǝn gat kurakhe ndanga char.
MAT 13:46 Mbǝladu tsin khwaran na kǝ chachaɗ fang, ka dala sakwdu ad dǝgakh sare dinin daghan, ka sukwgan ad ndangan ak chachaɗ kuren.
MAT 13:47 Tsǝguna, Tlǝksa gharazhigǝla ghila sika vai kilfe ɓǝlavdagh da dǝlv, ai viyado ad kilfakh sikh sikh.
MAT 13:48 Righif tsin, ka ndǝɗado udakh da tǝ kalam gǝrdz, ndzakhgud, zaɓadalud khwarkhwaran na kǝ kilf, ɗidaghud da tughub, ka ɗiduwud dǝgal ade kwal khwar.
MAT 13:49 Da nǝga ndǝk yan fitsa mbasa lard. Da sǝgdagh zarɓǝlakh Yazhigǝl da takatak, kǝ zaɓadal nguɗi udakh sǝgawal ǝn li kanadi udakh.
MAT 13:50 Ka da tlǝvtǝrdagh tlǝva itar ad nguɗi udakhen da kara tsakai tsakai, vake da tuwda itar dǝ kǝrɗ tliɗ.
MAT 13:51 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal Yasu, “A katlǝga nagh kur dǝgakhan tsagduwud daghana?” Nǝv itar tsin “Əm” A katlga kǝnd.
MAT 13:52 Ka niya tsitar, “Wirva yan ɗeghwa dadak tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus, ai tsagarduwud kǝ nǝga kǝ zǝr ɓǝla tlǝksa gharazhigǝl, ya ghila dadak mǝghe a dzǝgadal wuliwan zǝ mughuran na kǝ lǝman ǝn vake bǝgdin dǝgakh sar.”
MAT 13:53 Udzala kǝ Yasu ǝn kwarakh inakhan na kǝ jakva lavakhen, ka ɗuwars ad yanen kǝ vak.
MAT 13:54 A do Yasu da kǝs sar. Sa tsin da vaken, ka da da gud dzakhava Yakhudakh, ka farsan ad tsaga tǝrdu tsag kǝ udakh. Ka ndawatǝrǝf kǝ liye a tsǝngan. Avitar ma, “A mbǝladu ǝn vara udan na dina kǝ kwalemlem ra? Tsǝguna a mbǝladu ǝn varin ndzǝɗa man dǝg ndawakakhani?”
MAT 13:55 “Zǝr dadak tsakh mǝgh na baina biya? Bab sar ba Maryam biya? Yakub, Yusuvu, Siman, zǝ Yakhud saghrakh sar baitar kina biya?
MAT 13:56 Daghan dǝghaw babakh sara ǝn giɗǝn vak mar baitar biya? Ai a mbǝladu dǝvarin ad dǝgakhani?”
MAT 13:57 Ka bazala rǝv tsitar, ai nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Itsa dǝvara, nǝg ndanga kǝ tlayang Yazhigǝl. Ai uk ǝn ɗudǝn ǝn kǝs sar zǝ fǝta sarud.”
MAT 13:58 A manga ba dǝ dǝg ndawakakh ǝn vin char bi, wirva kuɗ fadǝghǝro fǝga tar.
MAT 14:1 Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sart, ka tsǝna tsǝna kǝ Khirudus Antifas dadake man tlǝksǝn Galili ad lave ǝn kwara udakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ Yasu.
MAT 14:2 Ka niya kǝ li manara tlǝr, “Afka ina Yukhan dadak para uda. A tsiyavanǝf ǝn ngitl. Yan kǝ mangan nǝg dǝ ndzǝɗa manakh dǝg ndawakakh.”
MAT 14:3 Wirva tsa kwarga Khirudus ad viga Yukhan kǝ kǝɗa da sal, wirva Khirudi nus zǝr bab ghǝrsar Filibus.
MAT 14:4 Wirva tsǝn tǝkhara tǝkha Yukhan gwil yan kǝ Khirudus kwarne, “Kalkal ba pǝrɗ Khirudi tsin kǝ nǝga kǝ nus sar bi.”
MAT 14:5 Tsa khǝnmina tsǝn nagha Khirudus ad kǝɗga Yukhan, ai ka gǝdzgan ad di udakh, wirva a ɓanǝf itar kwarne Yukhana tlayang.
MAT 14:6 Gwiyoghǝr kǝ khǝna vǝge tsa yigdud Khirudusa, ka dzanda dugh Khirudi ad tsugw ǝn tǝvuk kǝ ghulabakhe sawal da vak khwaɗǝg. Tsugwa sarna kǝ zǝɗaru kǝ Khirudus char.
MAT 14:7 Wirva yan, ka manarkhai ad lanji zǝ waɗa kwarne, da barabǝg ad itsauɗa dǝge takaɗgin.
MAT 14:8 Tǝkǝn bab sara, ka shakhanǝf ad dugh sar ad dǝge da kwarin. Ka ni, “Ba ka bǝgud ad ghǝr Yukhan dadak para ud ǝn mbanmban ǝn tǝvana kǝven.”
MAT 14:9 Turug ghǝr kǝ shik, ai wirva waɗe a mangin da nǝga kǝ dǝg zhiru tsin ǝn tǝvuk kǝ ghulabakh sar. Ka kwargan ad barabǝg ad dǝge ǝn naghin.
MAT 14:10 Ka talal ad ghay da gud sala, ǝntladǝghǝr ǝntlud ghǝr Yukhan.
MAT 14:11 Ka ɓardǝghǝrud ghǝr saks ǝn mbanmban, barud kǝ zǝr dughen, khalakyana ka ɓara kǝ bab sar.
MAT 14:12 Ka saks kǝ furakh Yukhan da zǝb gǝdzumba vǝgha sar, ka khǝɗane itar. Ka dǝgal tsitar kwararkhe itar kǝ Yasu.
MAT 14:13 Tsǝna kǝ Yasu ad dǝge dzaughǝr dǝ Yukhan, ka tsiyawal ǝn tǝ vinen ka da da Peryu, ka dǝgal tsin da giɗa tukuɗa sar ǝn vake kwal nǝg kǝ ud. Ai tsǝna kǝ dzakhava udakh kwarne a ɗuda Yasu ad yanen kǝ vak, ka sǝgawal tsitar ǝn kǝsakh, ka dǝgala tsitar dǝ sig da vake dǝ Yasu.
MAT 14:14 Sawala kǝ Yasu ǝn peryu, ka nǝghan ad dzakhava udakh zikǝn. Ka kwiɗ nǝv rǝv tsin, tsuguna ka mbakha tǝru ak li kwal yang ǝn tatak tar.
MAT 14:15 Ɓǝlga kǝ khagw, ka sa furakh sar da vak sar, nǝv itar tsin, “Vakna digi na tsawar bi, tsuguna a ɓǝlga khagw. Ɗuwatǝrs ɗuwa kǝ dzakhava udakhan dǝgal kǝ saku dǝg zuwa tsitar ǝn gǝdzar kǝsakhan.”
MAT 14:16 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Uɗa lava tsitar dǝgal da tlǝrna vaki? Bamatra bǝg ad dǝge da zuwa itar.”
MAT 14:17 Ka ngawarkhe itar kwarne, “Uk ɗumba brudi dliɓa zǝ kilf mits din kǝnd ǝn van.”
MAT 14:18 Ka ni “A nakam.”
MAT 14:19 Ka ndzakhamga ndzakhǝn tǝ dzuɓna niya kǝ udakhen. Ka ɓǝf ad brudina dliɓ zǝ kilfna mits, ka lando dǝ ghǝr da gharazhigǝl, ka kwarara us tsin kǝ Yazhigǝl. Ka kwachanan ad brudiyen baran kǝ furakh sar, ka bara furakh sar tsugun kǝ udakhen.
MAT 14:20 A zuwaru daghan tar, baghala itar. Ka dzakhanǝf furakh sar ad daghan dege tǝmgan. Ka raghanǝf ad tughwbakh kǝlatǝm mits.
MAT 14:21 Ghwalvakhe zuwa a ɓa itar dǝb dliɓ. A tugwana bud nughwasa zǝ zar bi.
MAT 14:22 Mbasu tsitar ma, ka kwara tǝrkhe Yasu kǝ furakh sar kǝ daks da peryu, kǝ dǝgal tsitar ǝn tǝvuk da tǝ tlǝrna ghǝdzǝva gadzak. In tsuguna dlaɓǝn ghits ǝn tǝ vin, kǝ da kwarara kwaza kǝ udakh daks ndan, kǝ dǝgal tsin.
MAT 14:23 Tǝkhal kǝ kwazana dzakhava udakh tsin, ka dugo tsin da tǝ ghuɓ kǝ ɗǝgaw tukuɗa tukuɗ. Ɓǝlga kǝ khagwa, ǝn vin tǝkuɗa sar.
MAT 14:24 Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sarta, bita pǝr yu zǝ ghay gǝrdz. Uk kaɗakaɗa kǝ ghǝɗkuta yu ad pǝr yuwen. Wirvǝn tlǝg tlǝga fuɗ ad pǝr yuwen da tǝlg.
MAT 14:25 Kalkal karfi khǝkǝrɗ dǝ ghǝr kǝdl, ka sagh Yasu da vak furakh sar, ǝn dǝgǝn tǝghǝr kǝ yu.
MAT 14:26 Nǝgha kǝ furakh sarna ad dǝga tsin ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ yuwa, ka gadzǝf itar char. “Ude sawal ǝn tǝ fik,” nǝv itar. Ka khula tsitar wirva gǝdz.
MAT 14:27 Tǝvin tǝvina, ka kwaratǝra lava kǝ Yasu kwarne, “Tukhwamfǝkhe tukha, i ka fǝka, gǝdzmbiya.” Niya tsitar.
MAT 14:28 Ka nǝv Bitrus tsin, “Dadzikan, ai da khin, khaya kanǝf khaya dǝgǝn tǝ ghǝr kǝ yu, kǝ saks da vakagh.”
MAT 14:29 “Ausǝga,” nǝv Yasu tsin. Burkhwit ka tsiyawal Bitrus sǝgawal ǝn peryuwen, ka farsa dǝga tsin ǝn tǝ yu, dǝgal da vak Yasu.
MAT 14:30 Ai vazga tsina a tsiyif fuɗ dǝ ndzǝɗa char, ka gǝdzǝf, ka farsa yu ad ndǝga ndǝg. Ka khula tsin, “Dadzikan katka katka” Niya tsin.
MAT 14:31 Tǝvin tǝvina ka talal Yasu ad dǝv sar, ka viyado sǝgo. Ka niya tsin, “Kha dadak khǝtsa fadǝghǝro fǝg, wuɗa lava kwal khayakǝf tsǝkhi?”
MAT 14:32 Da kǝ Yasu zǝ Bitrus da peryuwa, ka lǝɓukw nǝv fuɗ.
MAT 14:33 Ka ɗabanǝf furakh sare tsǝn Peryu ad Yasu. Ka nǝv itar tsin, “Zǝr Yazhigǝl kha kaɗikaɗi.”
MAT 14:34 Ghǝdzǝvarghǝra tsitar ad dǝlva, ka sa itar da ǝntla khay ya Janisarat.
MAT 14:35 Ai katlga kǝ li kǝsen kwarne, atsuk Yasu, ka ɓal ghay tsitar kǝ kwarara kwara kǝ itsawar ǝntla khaya kǝsen daghan. Khalak yana ka zaɓardǝghǝr udakh kǝsen ad daghan liye kwal yang.
MAT 14:36 Ka tatlga itar, kǝ khaya tǝrnǝf khaya kǝ liye kwal yang kǝ gǝma itsa ghay gabag sar. Daghan li gǝma ghay gabag sara, a mbakhu itar.
MAT 15:1 Dud ǝn kwarina, ka sasǝg kǝ yakhaya kǝ Farisakh zǝ yakhaya kǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzkh Mus ǝn Wurshalim, da vak Yasu. Ka ndiɗarwal itar kwarne,
MAT 15:2 “Uɗa lava kǝ zar ɓǝlakhagh ǝn kala ndzikhe a bǝga dzidzakhǝndi? Wirva na itar ǝn par dǝv kǝda zu kaf ndǝkve tsagdu dzidzakhǝnd bi.”
MAT 15:3 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai Yasu kwarne, “Uɗa lava tsǝkur ǝn kala ndzikha ndzikh Yazhigǝl, uk ǝn gatars kǝ dǝge tsagdu dzidzakhura kuri?
MAT 15:4 Afka nǝv Yazhigǝla, ‘Farghǝrfǝg kǝ dadagha zǝ babagh.’ Tsuguna ni, ‘Itsawar ǝn lakhga dad sar zǝ bab sar, kǝɗgud kǝmts.’
MAT 15:5 Ai ǝn tsagdutsaga kur kwarne, ‘Da nǝg dǝge nagha udan ad mǝlaru mǝla kǝ dad sar zǝ bab sar din, “Ai ka avin tsugun, daghan dǝge tsa da mbǝladu kur ǝn vakar, a barkhe ka kǝ Yazhigǝl.”
MAT 15:6 Wirva yana, atsuk barari ba mǝlaru mǝla kǝ dad bi nikur.’ Wirva yan, a nandal kur lav Yazhigǝl kǝ bat, kǝ nǝghda gatars kǝ ndzikha ndzikhur.
MAT 15:7 Kuram nguɗiyakhan. Kalkal dǝge tsa kwarga Ishay tlayang ǝn tǝghǝr tsukur. Kwarne,
MAT 15:8 “ ‘Udakhanna digi, uk ǝn fakghǝra dǝ ghay itar. Rǝvakhuɗ tara bita zǝ kǝ.
MAT 15:9 Ən ɗaba ka buti itar. Ən tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh udakh itar. Ən dleva lav Yazhigǝl.’ ”
MAT 15:10 Khala kǝ yana, ka ɗakhtǝrkhai Yasu kǝ dzakhava udakh, niya tsitar, “Bambǝg tlim, ka diyarsa kur.
MAT 15:11 Dǝge ǝn da da ghay bǝn naud kǝ kwadlamb ǝn tǝvuk kǝ Yazhigǝl bi. Dǝge ǝn sǝgawal ǝn ghay kǝ dadak sar ǝn nandala kǝ kwadlamb ǝn tǝvuk kǝ Yazhigǝl.”
MAT 15:12 Ka saks kǝ zar bǝlakh sar da vak sar, nǝv itar tsin, “Tsa tsǝkha kwarne a bazala rǝvakhuɗ kǝ Farisakh tsǝnga tsitar lavana kwarga kha?”
MAT 15:13 Ka ngawatǝrkhai Yasu tsitar, “Itsera kǝ ufe Dadar ǝn gharazhigǝl ba kǝ njivgan bi, ka da ndaɗdu ndaɗud kutskuts.
MAT 15:14 Ɗuwamatǝrs ɗu, ngulfakh itar li mǝdlara ɗul kǝ ngulfakh. Daka ngulf ǝn mǝdlara ɗul kǝ ngulfa, afka bǝrdagha tara da mbǝɗa itar dǝgdagh da fika.”
MAT 15:15 Ka nǝv Bitrus tsin, “Kwara kǝnkhai kwara dǝge tuku jakva lavan.”
MAT 15:16 “Atsuk dakhkana ghǝrur tsuguna a katlga ba kur biya?” Nǝv Yasu tsitar.
MAT 15:17 “Ən tsa bakh kur kwarne, ɗeghwa dǝge da da ghay kǝ udan, ǝn dǝgdagh da khuɗ sar, kǝ dǝg mbasa ka da sǝgawal ǝn vǝgh sara?.
MAT 15:18 Ai dǝge sǝgawal ǝn ghaya ǝn sǝgawal ǝn rǝvakhuɗ. In dǝgakhe ǝn naud kǝ kwadlamb ǝn tǝvuk Yazhigǝl.
MAT 15:19 Afke ǝn sǝgawal ǝn rǝvakhuɗ nguɗi nguɗi ɗaya ghǝra. Ndǝk za kǝɗ safa uda, gwaragwara, ǝrɗa, gǝla, dlaghawa fila zǝ bazardu ɗakha kǝ ud.
MAT 15:20 Ina dǝgakhe ǝn naud kǝ kwadlamb ǝn tǝvuk kǝ Yazhigǝl. Ai zu kaf dǝ dǝv kwal paran ǝn tǝ dǝva dǝ ndzikh ba da naud kǝ kwadlamb ǝn tǝvuk kǝ Yazhigǝl bi.”
MAT 15:21 Ɗuwars kǝ Yasu ad yanen kǝ vak, ka dal da ǝntla khaya kǝsakhe khefa dǝ Taya zǝ Sidom.
MAT 15:22 Dzagwdlam, ka sa nusen dugh ya Kanan ǝn giɗǝn khayen da vak Yasu. Ka tuwa tsin kwarne, “Dadzikan, Zǝr Dod, ziwakdal ziw. Ən bara dlaɗ sǝɗikw bǝzan kǝ dughwar char.”
MAT 15:23 A kwararkhe ba Yasu ad tsauɗa kǝ nusen bi. Ka saks kǝ furakh Yasu da takaɗa takaɗ ad Yasu. Nǝv itar tsin, “Lakwars lakw, wirvǝn gatakiyams gat, ǝn mbakiyama mbǝg dǝ tu.”
MAT 15:24 Ka ngawa tǝrkhe Yasu, ni, “Uk a ɓǝlokondagh wirva udakh ya Izraile a zaɗgan ud.”
MAT 15:25 Ai ka saks kǝ nusen da tǝvuk sar, kǝlgan ad juguv. “Dadzikana, mǝlaku mǝla.” Niya tsin.
MAT 15:26 Ka nǝv Yasu kǝ nusen, “Ən manawa ba bǝf ud kaf zara, ka barud kǝ ghǝdakh bi.”
MAT 15:27 Nǝv nusen tsin, “Lave kwarga kha na kalkal Dadzikan. Ai tsuguna, ghǝdakha ǝn zuwa zuwa itar, ad kwacha kafakhe ɓalal ǝn tǝ vǝlengakhe ǝn zuda li mǝghakh ad kaf.”
MAT 15:28 Ka ngawarkhe Yasu, niya tsin, “Awara nusna, fadǝghǝro fǝgagha nǝg dǝ ndzǝɗ, da manakha manud dǝge nakh.” Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sarta, ka mbu dugh sar ǝn tǝvin tǝvin.
MAT 15:29 Ɗuda kǝ Yasu ad yanen kǝ vak, ka dǝgal tsin diwa kalam dǝlva Galili. Khalak yana ka ngalo da tǝ gil nndzǝgan.
MAT 15:30 Ka saks kǝ udakh zikǝn da vak sar. Zaɓardǝghǝr itar dǝ ghurɗikakha, zǝ ngulfakha, zǝ li ǝmtsa kalam vǝgha, zǝ tǝngakha, zǝ chalǝm li kwal yanga zikǝn. Ka bakhga itar ǝn tǝvuk sar. Ka mbakha tru.
MAT 15:31 Ka ndawatrǝf kǝ udakh vazga tsitar ad li kwal tǝkha kǝ kwarga lava ǝn kwarghai itar. Li mǝtsa vǝgha ka a mbakharu, ghurɗikakh ǝn dǝga itar, ngulfakh ǝn nǝgha nǝgha itar. Ka farghǝr itar kǝ Yazhigǝl Izrail.
MAT 15:32 Dud ǝn kwarina, ka ɗakhtǝrkhai Yasu kǝ furakh sar saks da vak sar. Ka niya tsitar, “Ən ziwardal ziwa ka kǝ dlama khan, wirva khǝkǝrɗ khana tsitar ǝn vakar, tsuguna na dǝg zuwun vak tar bi. Nagh ba ka daks tsitar dǝ way bi, wirvǝn tǝkha itar kǝ ɗighǝr khar ǝn tǝ ɗul daks da mǝgh.”
MAT 15:33 Nǝv furakh sar tsin, “Ən tǝghal ndǝkina, da mbǝladu ǝn makiyam ad dǝg zuwe da tǝkhud kǝ batran kǝ udakh pakina ra?”
MAT 15:34 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal Yasu kwarne, “Ngǝrwa brudiye din kur ra?” Ka nǝv itar tsin, “Ɗumba uɗif zǝ mbisan na kǝ kilfakh.”
MAT 15:35 Ka bǝtra kǝ dzakhava udakh kǝ ndzakhga ndzakh ǝn tǝ khay.
MAT 15:36 Ka ɓǝf ad ɗumba brudiyen uɗif zǝ kilfakhen, kwararkhai ad us kǝ Yazhigǝl, ka kwachanǝf, baran kǝ furakh sar. Ka bara furakh sar ad brudiyen zǝ kilfakhen kǝ udakh.
MAT 15:37 Itsawara a zuwa, a baghala itar. Ka dzakhanǝf furakhen ad dǝg zuwe a tǝmgan, tugwǝb uɗif reghan.
MAT 15:38 Udakhe zuwa ruwa, a ɓa itar ghwalvakh dǝb ufaɗ. A kǝdlga bud nughwasa zǝ zara bi.
MAT 15:39 Ən tǝ khal kǝ ɗuwatǝrs ɗuwa kǝ Yasu ad dzakhava udakh, ka da da peryu, ka dǝgal da ǝntla khaya ya Magadan.
MAT 16:1 A sa Farisakha zǝ Sadukiyakh da vak Yasu kǝ nǝghda kurakura tsitar. Ka ndiɗarwal itar kǝ mana tra zikan na kǝ dǝg ndawake da mǝdla din kwarne a saudagh ǝn gharazhigǝl.
MAT 16:2 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai ni, “Da dǝm fatsi da ɓǝl, da ka nǝgha tsǝkur khas khas ǝn tǝ gharazhigǝl, ka nikur, ‘Yauwa, na yu da tǝɗa bi.’
MAT 16:3 Da ka sǝgo gwisǝl zǝ ghabag, da nǝgha tsǝkur khas khas ǝn tǝ gharazhigǝl, lusǝf kes, ka nikur ‘Da tǝɗa yu khan.’ Tǝkha kur kǝ tsan ad dǝgakhe da dzaughǝr ǝn tǝ dǝva dǝ giɗa kǝ fef gharazhigǝl, wur ka tǝkh ba kur kǝ katlga dǝge ǝn tuku jakǝvakh manasar kǝ kwargǝna bi.
MAT 16:4 Udakh kwargǝna li kwal khayanǝf dǝ Yazhigǝl itar, kǝladakh tsugun. Na kur nǝgha dǝg ndawak, ya na bud da mǝdla kura tlǝrna dǝg ndawak bi, akwa dǝg Yunan.” Khalak yana ka ɗuwatǝrs Yasu, dakaval sar.
MAT 16:5 Darghǝra tsitar da tǝ tlǝrna ghǝdzva gadzak dǝlv, ka dzamana furakh sar kwarne a mbitsa tǝrghǝr sǝgawal dǝ brudi.
MAT 16:6 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Ɗem nikur, ya tsukwamana ghǝr dǝ yista Farisakha zǝ Sadukiyakh.”
MAT 16:7 Ka farsa ɗayakavu lav tsitar ǝn tatak tar kwarne, “Wirve a ɓadal ba kiyam ad brudi bi nagh ǝn kwarin adina?”
MAT 16:8 A katlga Yasu ad dǝge tsǝn kwara itar, wirva yana, ka ndiɗatǝrwal kwarne, “Uɗa lava tsǝkur ǝn ɗayakavu lav ǝn tǝbur kwarne, wirva na kur dǝ brudi biyi? Kuram li khǝtsa fadghǝrofǝg.
MAT 16:9 Dakhkana a katlga ba kur biya? A mbitsa kur ghǝrkh sarte tsa baghandala ka udakh dǝb dliɓ (5,000) dǝ ɗumba brudi dliɓa? Tughwb ngǝrwa a dzanǝf kuram ake tǝmgani?
MAT 16:10 Awana ǝn sarte tsa baghandala ka udakh dǝb ufaɗ (4,000) dǝ ɗumba brudi uɗif. Tughwb ngǝrwa a dzanǝf kuram ake tǝmgani?
MAT 16:11 Uɗa kǝ mangan tsǝkur kwal katlgan kwarne ǝn kwara kura lav ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ brudi ba ka biyi? Ən kwara kura kwarne tsukwamana ghǝr dǝ yista Farisakh zǝ Sadukiyakh kǝ.”
MAT 16:12 Ka katlga furakh sar kǝ Yasu kwarne, ǝn kwarǝn tǝghǝr kǝ yiste ǝn ɗiyud ǝn brudi bi. Tsukwamana ghǝr dǝ yisti na tsǝn kwarina, atsuk ǝn kwarǝn tǝghǝr kǝ tsagdutsaga Farisakha zǝ Sadukiyakh.
MAT 16:13 Soghǝr kǝ Yasu da kǝs ya Kesariya Filibiya, ka ndiɗatǝrwal kǝ furakh sar kwarne, “Warek ka Zǝr Ud vek udakh ra?”
MAT 16:14 Ka nǝv itar tsin, “Av yakhaya Yukhan dadak para ud, av yakhaya Ili tlayang, av yakhaya tsuguna Irmi tlayang, awana fang ǝn tatak tlayangakh.”
MAT 16:15 Niya tsitar, “Ai kur ma, warek kavek kuri?”
MAT 16:16 Ka ngawarkhe Siman Bitrus kwarne, “Kha Masikhu, Zǝr Yazhigǝl dadak saf.”
MAT 16:17 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Dadak bark kha Siman zǝr Yukhan, wirva a sakha diwa ud dǝg sig ba ina kǝ jir bi. Dadare ǝn gharazigǝl kǝ kwara khai.
MAT 16:18 Ni ǝn kwarakha kwara kǝ, kha Bitrus, fǝraɗ khǝ, da ɓǝlǝn tǝ kha ka dǝ kur khǝgar, dǝge ǝn tuku kur khǝgena, itar udakhe da fadghǝrofǝg ǝn tǝ kǝ. Ai kwal da tǝkha kǝ ndzǝɗa mǝtsa kǝ manar khai tsauɗ.
MAT 16:19 Da bakha bǝg ka dǝg tusa nga gud tlǝksa gharazhigǝl. Tsugun, ɗeghwa dǝge kwal khayanǝf tsǝkha manaman ǝn lard, nabud da manaman ǝn gharazhigǝl bi. Ɗeghwa dǝge ǝn nakha manaman ǝn lard, da mana ndǝkyan ud ǝn gharazhigǝl.”
MAT 16:20 Ka ndǝɗatǝrnǝf Yasu ad tlim kǝ furakh sar char kwarne, kwarara ba itar kǝ itsawar kwarne ka Masikhu bi.
MAT 16:21 Tsiyif ǝn tǝ yanen kǝ sart, ka farsa Yasu ad kwara tra kwara tsin kǝ furakh sar kwarne, “Barari dǝgal tsin da Wurshalim, kǝ khǝɓ dlaɗakh sikh sikh sikh ǝn dǝv kǝ maludakh zǝ zikzikanakh kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ li tsagdu nzdikha nzdikh Mus. Ka da kǝɗke kǝɗud, fitsa khǝkǝrɗa da tsiyaka tsiyud.”
MAT 16:22 Ka ndǝɗala Bitrus ad Yasu da te kalam, ka farsan ad tavarghǝr di kwarne, “Tsandu tsǝg Yazhigǝl ad yan, Dadzikan. Da dzoghǝr ba yan dǝ kha tsa khǝɗikǝn bi.”
MAT 16:23 Ka gwiyafkhe Yasu ka niya kǝ Bitrus, “Tsiyakval tsiya kha Shatan. Kur khǝtingǝɗ khǝn tǝvukar, wirva ɗaya ɗaya na, ɗaya ghǝr ud dǝg sig, dǝg Yazhigǝl bi.”
MAT 16:24 Ka nǝv Yasu kǝ zar bǝlakh sar, “Ɗeghwa ude nagh gataks gat, barari ɗuda way ghǝrsar tsin. Tsuguna ka ɓǝfin ad ufa khǝrta sar, kǝ gataks gat.
MAT 16:25 Wirva ɗeghwa ude na kat safa sar, da bǝgh. Ai ɗeghwa ude khayanǝf bǝghǝn safa sar wirva kǝ, da mbǝladu mbǝl.
MAT 16:26 Uɗa dǝg sige da gǝmadu udan, da gǝmaduwin dǝgakhe ǝn lard daghan, tsuguna bǝghalǝn safa sari? Uɗa dǝge tǝkha udan kǝ bǝdu kǝ varda safa sari?
MAT 16:27 Da sǝgadagh ka Zǝr Ud ǝn ndanga Dadar zǝ zarɓǝlakhe ǝn gharazhigǝl. Khalak yana, ka da bara dǝg siga sar ka kǝ itsawar, kalkala dǝge a mangin.
MAT 16:28 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, nǝg udakhe ǝn ghitsǝn van, liye kwal da ǝmts, khekwa nǝgha ka itar ka Zǝr Ud, ǝn sǝgdagh ka ndǝk shik.”
MAT 17:1 Tǝkhal kǝ khǝna unkwakh kǝ kwarga kwara kǝ Bitrus kwarne Yasu in Masikhu, ka zǝɓǝf Yasu ad Bitrus, zǝ Yakub, zǝ Yukhan zǝrbab Yakub. Zǝɓtro da tǝ tsǝɓan na kǝ khuɓ. Uk itar kalti ǝn vin.
MAT 17:2 A mbǝɗfǝkhe vǝgh Yasu ǝn di tsitar. Ka wuɗa vakdi sar ndǝk fatsi, tsuguna nala kadlangakh sare a talǝmin kǝ maɗakw tǝl.
MAT 17:3 Ən tǝvin tǝvin, ka nǝgha kǝ zar ɓǝlakhana dǝ Mus tlayang zǝ Ili tlayang ǝn kwar lav itar zǝ Yasu.
MAT 17:4 Ka nǝv Bitrus kǝ Yasu, “Dadzikan, khwaren nǝg kǝnda van. Da khayanǝfkh, da manga mana ka tsikw khǝkǝrɗ ǝn van. Fang tsǝkha, fang kǝ Mus tlayanga, fang kǝ Ili tlayang.”
MAT 17:5 Madǝv Bitrus ǝn kwar lava, ka sodagh ghwike ǝn wuɗ tǝrdlǝm da tǝghǝr tsitar. Khalak yana, ka tsǝna tsǝna tsud ad kwind sǝgawal ǝn ghwiken kwarne, “Zǝraren ǝn waya kǝ, ǝn tsǝn zǝɗa sar ka char. Tsǝna maru tsǝn.”
MAT 17:6 Tsǝna kǝ furakh sar ad yanen kǝ kwinda, ka gǝdzatrǝf char, ka khǝmbga itar da khay.
MAT 17:7 Ka sa Yasu, tapa tǝrkhai avin, “Tsiyamǝf tsi, gǝdzam bi.”
MAT 17:8 Kapanǝf tsitar ghǝra, aghba itsawar ǝn vin bi tǝma Yasu kitakul.
MAT 17:9 Madǝv itar ǝn sǝgadagh ǝn ghuɓen, ka ndǝɗaternǝf Yasu ad tlim kwarne, “Kwarama tra ba kǝ itsawar ad dǝge nǝgha kur bi, khekwa tsiyanǝfud ka Zǝr Ud ǝn ngitl.”
MAT 17:10 Ka ndiɗarwal furakhan na kǝ Yasu kwarne, “Ai uɗa lava kǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus ǝn kwarne, barari khekwa Ili tlayang da farsa sǝgadagh ndan, kǝda sǝgadagh kǝ Masikhuwi?”
MAT 17:11 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai, “Kalkal da sǝgdagh kǝ Ili tlayang, kǝda ɗika itsauɗa kǝ nǝga kalkal ndan.
MAT 17:12 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, audzala Ili ǝn sodagh sǝg, a katlga ba itar kwarne in bi. A manarakhe itar dǝge ǝn nagha reva tar. Da khǝɓa ndǝk yan ka Zǝr Ud tsugun ad dlaɗ ǝn dǝva tar.”
MAT 17:13 Khalak yana ka katlga zar ɓǝlakhana kwarne, atsuk ǝn kwara tra lav ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ Yukhan dadak para ud.
MAT 17:14 Sodagh tsitar ǝn tǝ khuɓen da vake dǝ dzakhava udakh, ka sasǝg kǝ udanen da vak Yasu, kǝlgan ad juguv ǝn tǝvuk sar. Ka ni,
MAT 17:15 “Dadzikan, manga kwiɗkwiɗǝrva zǝraran. Nǝg fuɗ ǝn vǝgh tsin, tsuguna ǝn bara dlaɗ char. Ngǝrwa siga tsin ǝn ɓala dǝgdagh da kar zǝ yu.
MAT 17:16 A ɓala ka da vak zar bǝlakhagha, a piyatǝrwal mbambǝg.”
MAT 17:17 Ka ngawarkhai Yasu kwarne, “Kur udakh kwargǝn, li kwal dǝ fadǝghǝrofǝg, kur mbǝrshakhan. Ki da zulu pak uɗa tsǝka zǝ kuri? Ki da bǝga pak uɗa tsǝka rǝv dǝ kuri? Ɓakdǝghǝr ɓa da van, niya kǝ dad zǝren.”
MAT 17:18 Ka tavarghǝr Yasu ad di kǝ wurduwen, ka sawalǝn zǝren, tǝvin tǝvina ka mbu.
MAT 17:19 Ka saks kǝ furakh Yasu da vak sar ǝn sarte tǝkuɗa sar tsin, ka ndiɗarwal itar, “A piyakǝndǝwala ndar lakwdu wurduweni?”
MAT 17:20 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai Yasu kwarne, “Wirva a khǝtsa fadǝghǝrofǝgur. Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, da tsa nǝg fadǝghǝrofǝgur khǝɗikǝn ndǝk khulf mustad, tǝkha kur kǝ kwararkhe kǝ ghuɓna kwarne, ‘Tsiyin dǝgal van, da tǝ tlǝrna vak’, tsuguna ka da tsi. Na dǝge tǝkha kǝ piyakurwala bi.”
MAT 17:21 “Afka khulf ina kǝ sǝɗikw bǝzana tǝkh ba kǝ sawala bi, khekwa dǝ ɗǝgawa zǝ zǝɓ ndǝl da sǝgawalin.”
MAT 17:22 Dzafkhai kǝ Yasu zǝ furakh sar ǝn ǝntla khaya Galili, ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “A khǝrzǝgud da bǝkdu bǝg ka Zǝr Ud, da dǝva udakh.
MAT 17:23 Da kǝɗ ka kǝɗa itar. Fitsa khǝkǝrɗa ka da tsiya ka tsiyud.” Ka kǝɗatǝrkhe ad vǝgh kǝ furakhna char.
MAT 17:24 Sa kǝ Yasu zǝ furakh sar da kǝs Kafarnakhum, ka saks kǝ li chau khadama Fǝta Yazhigǝl da vak Bitrus, ka ndiɗarwal itar, “Nabakh dadak tsagdu lavur ǝn pǝl khadama Fǝta Yazhigǝla?”
MAT 17:25 Ka ngawar khai Bitrus kwarne, “Ən pǝla pǝlin gǝna.” Da kǝ Bitrus da mǝghen, ka farsa Yasu ad kwarara lav, “Uɗa ɗayaghǝragh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ ndiɗeni? Ən chawun vakǝng shikakh lard na ad khadama lǝman awana khadama gidadi? Ən vak zar tar nagha, ǝn vak kǝstǝlakh khi?”
MAT 17:26 Nǝv Bitrus tsin, “Ən vak kǝstǝlakh.” Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Ai da ndǝkyanin, a mǝdlanan kwarne na zar tar ǝn pela pǝla bi.”
MAT 17:27 “Ai khek bazatǝrdu tsǝki ad rǝva, dǝg dǝgal da tǝ ghay dǝlv, taldagh tala khilga vi kilf da dǝlv. Ka nguranǝf kha ghay kilfe a viga kha chak, da mbǝladu mbǝla kha lotus ai da tlala kǝ pǝl khadamagha zǝ dǝgar. Ɓǝfɓa, pǝla tǝrkhai pǝl.”
MAT 18:1 Ən sartenan, ka sa furakh sar da vak Yasu ka ndiɗarwal itar kwarne, “Warek zikan daghan ǝn tlǝksa gharazhigǝli?”
