MAT 18:2 Ka ɗakhga Yasu ad zǝr khǝɗikan, ka ghitsanan ǝn tǝb tar.
MAT 18:3 Ka ni, “Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, da mbǝɗfǝkhe ba giɗur nala kur ndǝk zar mbisan bi, na kur da daks da tlǝksa gharazhigǝl lingling bi.
MAT 18:4 Itsawar ǝn gulandagh ghǝrsar ndǝk zǝr khǝɗikanǝn, in zikan daghan ǝn tlǝksa gharazhigǝl.
MAT 18:5 “Ɗaga ude chauga zǝr khǝɗikan ndǝk inan wirva kǝ, ka chaukayin.”
MAT 18:6 “Ya digi, ɗeghwa ude a ba ad fang ǝn tatak zar mbisan, liye fadǝghǝro dǝ kǝ, da man khaip. Adara nguɗarǝmud vǝr pǝkhǝn kwind sar, ka tlǝvdagh khud da dǝlve chalangw.”
MAT 18:7 “Ɗangwa kǝ udakhe ǝn lard. Wirva dǝgakhe da bakh udakh da man khaipa, ǝn lard itar. Ya ɗangwa kǝ dadake da saks dǝgakhan ǝn tǝ dǝva din.
MAT 18:8 Da dǝvagha awana sigagh ǝn bǝg khan da man khaip, ǝntlǝdukha, tlǝvars khǝ. Adara daks dǝ dǝv kitakul, awana sig kitakul kha da safa kǝ ngǝɗ, tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝvǝkhǝdagh dǝ dǝvakhagh, awana dǝ sigakhagh bǝrdagh, da kare kwal nǝg ǝn mǝtsa kǝ ngǝɗ.
MAT 18:9 Da wur diyakhagh ǝn bǝg khan da man khaip tsugun, ndǝɗadal kha, tlǝvars khǝ. Adara daks dǝ di kitakul kha da safa kǝ ngǝɗ, tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝvkhǝdagh dǝ di bǝrkǝdagh da kare kwal nǝg ǝn mǝtsa kǝ ngǝɗ.”
MAT 18:10 “Tsukwamana ghǝr, khayamanǝf ba nena itsa fang ǝn tǝɓ kǝ zar mbisana khana bi. Wirvǝn tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, zarɓǝlakh Yazhigǝl tar ai ǝn gharazhigǝl, tsika fatsi ǝn nǝgha nǝgha itar vakdi Dadare ǝn gharazhigǝl.
MAT 18:11 Wirva ka Zǝr Ud a saudagh da kat liye a zaɗgan kǝ.
MAT 18:12 “Uɗa ɗaya ghǝruri? Da nǝg ude dǝ tuwaghakh dǝrmǝk (100), da ka zaɗga kitakul ǝn tǝb tar, nabakhin da ɗuwars kul vaslambaɗ ghǝrf vaslambaɗ (99) nǝn kus kǝ ghuɓe zighwda itara? Kǝ dǝgal da gat kitakule zaɗgana?
MAT 18:13 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, da mbǝladu win ad kitakulen, khwaɗge da manin ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ kitakulǝn, da malamala ad dǝg kul vaslambaɗ ghǝrf vaslambaɗe kwal zaɗgan.
MAT 18:14 Ndǝkyan tsugun, khayanǝf khaya Dadurǝn gharazhigǝl ba zaɗa kǝ itsa fang ǝn tǝb kǝ zar mbisana khana bi.”
MAT 18:15 “Da manakhai sukwtagha ad ghaz, ka dǝgal kha da vak sar, kwarkhekha ghaza sar ǝn tǝbura mits mits. Da tsǝnkhayin, a guyondǝghǝr kha sukwtagh saks.
MAT 18:16 Ai da tsǝnkhe bin bi, ka gwidǝn dǝgala kha da vak sar zǝ ud fang. Wirva a kwarga lav Yazhigǝl kwarne, ‘Itsera kǝ lave a ndazhana ud mitsa zǝ khǝkǝrɗ, a mǝdlanan kwarne lavena jir.’
MAT 18:17 Da kalwalin kǝ tsǝntǝr tsǝn, ka kwararkhe kha ke li gata daghan. Kǝ dǝg mbas, da kalwalin kǝ tsǝn lav li gaten daghan, ka nandala kha ndǝk liye kwal tsa Yazhigǝl, awana ndǝk dadak chau khadam.
MAT 18:18 “Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, daghan dǝge kwal khayanǝf tsǝkur manaman ǝn lard, na bud da manaman ǝn gharazhigǝl bi. Daghan dǝge khayanǝf kur manaman ǝn lard, da mana manud ǝn gharazhigǝl.
MAT 18:19 “Ən gwidǝn kwara kura kwara kǝ, da khayanǝf ud mits ǝn tǝbur ǝn lard, ǝn tǝ ghǝr kǝ dǝge a takaɗga itar, da manatra mana Dadare ǝn gharazhigǝl.
MAT 18:20 Wirva daghan vake dzafkhai ud mitsa zǝ khǝkǝrɗ ǝn ɗakhar, ǝn vak tar kǝ.”
MAT 18:21 Ka sa Bitrus da vak Yasu, ndiɗarwal kwarne, “Dadzikan, da ka manakhaka ghaza sukwtar, sig ngǝrwa da ɓisakhara ki? Sig uɗif nagha?”
MAT 18:22 “Ka ngawar khai Yasu kwarne, uk uɗif siga bi, uɗif uɗif sig kul uɗif.
MAT 18:23 “Wirva yan, da tǝkhud kǝ kurana tlǝksa gharazhigǝl dǝ shike ǝn nagh kǝdla lǝmanakh sare ǝn dǝv kǝ vǝɓakh sar.
MAT 18:24 Farsa kǝ shiken ad kǝdla kǝdla, ka ɓardǝghǝr ud ad ude gatarsin dǝ gǝmaw kwaɓ talenti dǝb kǝlɗǝk (10,000), ai kwal da tǝkha kǝ udanen kǝ pelgan mbasu ba dǝ giɗa sar ǝn lard bi.”
MAT 18:25 “Piyarwala kǝ pǝlapǝl, ka kwarga shik kwarne, sukwamdu sukwa dǝ udanen, zǝ nus sar, zǝ zar sar, zǝ daghan dǝge dinin, kǝ nǝghda pelda gǝmawen din.”
MAT 18:26 “Ka diktliɓ kǝlga vǝɓen ad juguv ǝn tǝvuk kǝ shiken, ǝn takaɗa takaɗa kwarne, ‘Bakai rǝv, da pǝlakha pǝla ka itsauɗ.’
MAT 18:27 Ka ziwardal shiken kǝ vǝɓen, ka ɓǝlars, ɓisarnan ad gǝmawen.
MAT 18:28 “Sawala kǝ vǝɓen ǝn fǝta shiken, papatl ka gamga itar ze tsaghw man tlǝr sare ǝn gatarsin dǝ gǝmaw kwaɓ dinari dǝrmǝk (100), ka vigan ǝn makular, niya tsin, ‘Pǝlakai pǝla gemaware ǝn gatakhs kǝ.’
MAT 18:29 “Ka diktliɓ kǝlga tsaghw man tlǝr sar ad juguv ǝn tǝvuk sar, ǝn takaɗa takaɗa kwarne, ‘Bakai rǝv, da pǝlakha pǝla kǝ.’
MAT 18:30 “Kalwala kǝ ɓisara ɓis, ka ɓal dǝgal da gud sal, khekwa pǝlarkheyin ad gǝmaw saren ndan.
MAT 18:31 Nǝgha kǝ chalǝm zar man tlǝr ad dǝge dzaughǝr, a zǝɗatru ba lingling bi. Ka dala itara, kwararkhe itar kǝ shik, ad dǝge dzoghǝr daghan.
MAT 18:32 “Ka ɓǝlandala shik kǝ ɗakha dǝghǝr vǝɓena tsa chak. Sa tsin, ka nǝv shiken tsin, ‘Kha nguɗi vǝɓǝn. A ɓisakhana ka ad daghan gǝmawe ǝn gatakhs kǝ, wirva takaɗke khǝ.
MAT 18:33 Atsuk ǝn tǝkh ba kha kǝ manga kwiɗkwiɗǝreva tsaghw man tlǝragh, ndǝkve manga ka kwiɗkwiɗa revagh biya?’
MAT 18:34 A bazala rǝv kǝ shik char, ka batrǝm shik ǝn dǝv kǝ li ǝn tuk gud salen, bara bǝg itar dlaɗ, da tǝ sarte da pǝldin ad gǝmaw kwaɓ na daghan.”
MAT 18:35 “Da mana ndǝk yan Dadare ǝn gharazhigǝl, ak itsawar ǝn kur ai kalwala kǝ ɓisara kǝ zǝrbab sar, ǝn revakhuɗ sar.”
MAT 19:1 Udzala kǝ Yasu ǝn kwar dǝgakhana, ka ɗuwars ad ǝntla khaya ya Galili, ka dal da ǝtla khay ya Yakhudi, ai ǝn tǝ ghǝdzǝva gadzak zagh Urdu.
MAT 19:2 Zikǝn udakhe a gatars, ka mbandu ad liye ǝn tukw kuz ǝn vin.
MAT 19:3 Ka saks kǝ yakhaya kǝ Farisakh da vak sar, kǝ nǝghda gat ghaza sar tsitar. Ka ndiɗarwal itar kwarne, “A khayanǝf nagh ndzikh khǝnd ad tǝkaghǝra kǝ ud ze nus sar, ǝn tǝ itsera kǝ dǝge kwal nagha tsina?”
MAT 19:4 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai Yasu kwarne, “Atsuk a tugwa bakh kur ǝn kaɗkaɗ ǝn vake tsǝn kwarin kwarne, dadake tsa vǝrɗtǝrkhe vǝrɗa gul farsafǝga larda, ‘A vǝrɗtǝrkhe kǝ zila zǝ nusa?’
MAT 19:5 A kwarga Yazhigǝl tsugun kwarne, ‘Wirva yan digi, da ɗuwar ɗuwa udan ad dad sar zǝ bab sar kǝ khǝmbarvan kǝ nus sar, kǝ nǝga tsitar bǝrdagh kǝ ud kitakul.’
MAT 19:6 Wirva yana, aghba dlaitar dǝ ud mits bi, a narala kǝ ud kitakul. Wirva yan, dǝge a matlanǝf Yazhigǝl, khayanǝf ba ud ad tǝka tǝka bi.”
MAT 19:7 Ka ndiɗarwal Farisakhen kwarne, “Ai uɗa lava kǝ Mus tlayang a bǝdu ad ndzikha ndzikh kǝ ud kǝ bǝdu kaɗkaɗ tǝkaghǝra zǝ nus sar, kǝ dǝgala tsini?”
MAT 19:8 Ai ka ngawa tǝrkhai Yasu niya tsitar, “A khayakurnǝf Mus tlayang ak tǝkaghǝra zǝ nughwasakhur, wirva ɓengɓeng revakhuɗur kǝ mangan, ai gul ǝn tǝ farsafǝga tsa ndǝk yan bi.
MAT 19:9 Ai ǝn kwara kura kwara kǝ, ɗaga ude tǝkaghǝran zǝ nus sar, da wirva a tlarghǝr ǝn man gwaragwar bud bi, da ɓuwin ad tlǝrna nus tsugun, gwaragwar ǝn manin zǝ nusen.”
MAT 19:10 Ka nǝv furakh sar tsin, “Da ka ndǝk yan giɗǝn tǝb kǝ ud zǝ nus sara, atsuk giɗa kwal nus kaw.”
MAT 19:11 Ai ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Daghan ud bǝn tǝkha kǝ ɓanǝf lava nǝn kwara kur bi, khekwa liye a khayatǝrnǝf Yazhigǝl kǝ nǝga ndǝk yan.
MAT 19:12 Nǝg dǝgakhe da bǝg chalǝm ghwalvakh kwal da zǝɓ nus. Wirva nǝg liye a yakhtǝr khaiyud ndǝk yan. Nǝg liye udakh kǝ natǝrala ndǝk yan. Yakhaya tsuguna itar kǝ nandala ghǝrtar kwal da nǝg da zǝɓ nus, wirva tlǝr tlǝksa gharazhigǝl. Ɗaga ude khayanǝf dǝ lava na, chawin.”
MAT 19:13 Khalak yana, zaɓardǝghǝr yakhaya kǝ udakh ad zar mbisan kǝ Yasu, kǝ nǝghda batǝrghǝr dǝv tsin, kǝ takaɗ Yazhigǝl wirva itar. Ai ka tav di kǝ furakh sar ǝn tǝ li zaɓado zaren.
MAT 19:14 Ka nǝv Yasu kǝ furakh sar, “Ɗuwamatǝrs zar mbisan saks da vakar, tsuwamatra bi. Wirva tlǝksa gharazhigǝla dǝg udakhe ndǝk zar mbisanakhan.”
MAT 19:15 Ka bakhatǝrghǝr ad dǝva, ka takaɗgan ad Yazhigǝl kǝ batǝrghǝr bark, ka dakaval ǝn vin.
MAT 19:16 Dud ǝn manin, ka sa udanen da vak Yasu niya tsin, “Malǝm, uɗa dǝg khwarane barari da mana ka kǝ gǝmadu safa kǝ ngǝɗi?”
MAT 19:17 Nǝv Yasu tsin, “Uɗa lava tsǝkhǝn ndiɗakwala ndiɗ ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dǝge khwarani? Afke uk Yazhigǝl kitakul khwarana. Ai da ka da nakha gǝmadu safa kǝ ngǝɗ, ka tsufanǝf kha ndzikha ndzikh Yazhigǝl.”
MAT 19:18 Ka ndiɗarwal kǝ Yasu, “Irǝn ndzikha ndzikhen ra?” Ka ngawarkhe Yasu, “Kǝɗ ba safa ud bi, a ɗuwa gwaragwar, a ɗuwa man gǝl, a ɗuwa dlǝgh fil,
MAT 19:19 farghǝr fǝg kǝ dadagha zǝ babagh. Tsǝguna waya tlǝghǝr witǝghagh ndǝkve waya kha ghǝragh.”
MAT 19:20 Ka nǝv dakhwal na tsin, “Afka ǝn tsufatsufa ka dǝgakhana daghan. Uɗa kǝ tǝmgan tsǝki?”
MAT 19:21 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Dǝn nakha nǝga tsǝkha kǝ njiva char, dǝg da sakwdu dǝge din kha daghan, tǝkatǝrdukha kǝ talagakh ad kwaɓen. Da mbǝladu mbǝla kha lǝman ǝn gharazhigǝl. Khalak yana, ka saks kha, gatakskh.”
MAT 19:22 Tsǝna kǝ dakhwalen ndǝk yana, ka dǝgal tsin dǝ baza rǝvakhuɗ. Wirva naghbakha tluwandal tsin bi.
MAT 19:23 Ka nǝv Yasu kǝ furakh sar, “Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, da ɗǝmɗǝm kǝ dadak tluwandal daks da gharazhigǝl.
MAT 19:24 Ən gwidǝn kwara kura kwara kǝ, da tsaftsaf kǝ dlugwam daks ǝn tǝ ɗul lipǝr, tǝghǝr kǝ daks kǝ dadak tluwandal da tlǝksa Yazhigǝl.”
MAT 19:25 Tsǝna kǝ furakh sar ndǝk yana, ka a ndawatrǝf char. Nǝv itar, “Da ka ndǝk yanina, ai war da mbǝladu kati?”
MAT 19:26 Ka vaza kǝ Yasu gyer ta titar, ni, “Ən vak uda, ina kǝ digita ǝn manawa bi. Ai ǝn vak Yazhigǝla, ǝn manawa man.”
MAT 19:27 Ka nǝv Bitrus tsin, “Nǝgha, kǝnda kina a ɗuwars kǝnda tsauɗa kǝ gatakhs gat. Ai takina uɗa da mbǝladu kǝndi?”
MAT 19:28 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, sarte da mbǝɗanǝfud ad itsauɗa kǝ wiliw, ka Zǝr Ud da nndzǝgan kǝn tǝ vija tlǝksare ndagan. Kuram liye gataks gat, da nndzǝgan kur ǝn tǝ vijakh man tlǝks kǝlatǝm mits. Da taka tǝra lava kur kǝ mbǝrta ya Izrail na kǝlatǝm mits.
MAT 19:29 Tsuguna itsawar ǝn ɗuda fǝtakha sar, itsa sukwtakh sara, zǝ dǝghaw babagh sar, itsa dad, itsa bab, itsa zila awana nus, itsa zar, awana gukhakh, wirva kǝ. Da mbǝladu mbǝla mal kǝ yan sig dǝrmǝk. Wur tsuguna, da wurawura ad safa kǝ ngǝɗ.
MAT 19:30 Ai tsugun, udakh zikǝn liye ǝn tǝvuk, da nǝga itar kǝ dǝg khal. Liye kǝ khal tsuguna, da nǝga itar kǝ dǝg chak.”
MAT 20:1 “Tlǝksa gharazhigǝla ngwaɗa dadak gukhe a dala pǝrta gǝdl, da gat li da manara tlǝr ǝn gukh inabi sar.
MAT 20:2 Udzala tsitar ǝn khayanǝf lav ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ kwaɓ dinari kitakul, ai da pǝlarud kǝ ud ǝn vak. Ka ɓǝlatǝral dǝgal da man tlǝr ǝn gukh sar.
MAT 20:3 “Manga kǝ karfi vaslambaɗa tǝkǝdl, ka gwidǝn dǝgal tsin. Ka nǝghan ad yakhaya kǝ udakh, ǝn giɗa butbuti ǝn tǝghay kasuk.
MAT 20:4 Ka niya tsitar, ‘Dam dǝgal ghǝrura da man tlǝr ǝn gukh inabiyar. Da pǝla kura pǝla ka dǝge vazga ka khwara kǝ bakura bǝg.’
MAT 20:5 Khalak yana, ka dǝgal tsitar. “Ka gwidǝn dǝgala tsin kǝ fatsi tǝghǝr, zǝn karfi khǝkǝrɗ kǝ khagw, ka kurgan ad gan zitar ndǝkve tsa mangin chak.
MAT 20:6 Dakhkana, ka gwidǝn sǝgawal tsin ǝn tǝ karfi dliɓ, ka tlarghǝr ad yakhaya kǝ udakh, ǝn ghitsa na dǝge ǝn mana itar bi. Ka ndiɗatǝrwal, ‘Uɗa lava tsǝkur birnif ǝn giɗa ǝn van, kwal nǝg kǝ dǝge ǝn manakuri?’
MAT 20:7 “ ‘Wirva na ude bakǝnda tlǝr mana bi,’ nǝv itar tsin. “Ka nǝv dadak gukhen tsitar, ‘Damdǝgal ghǝrur tsugun da gukhar.’
MAT 20:8 “Ɓǝlga kǝ khagwa, ka nǝv dadak gukh kǝ dadak nǝgharu kǝ gukh saren, ‘Ɗakhtǝrkhe ɗakha kǝ li mantlǝren, pǝlatǝrkhekh kwaɓ tar, farsǝf ǝn tǝ li sa kǝ khala, da tǝ li tsa chak.’
MAT 20:9 “Ka saks kǝ li tsa dalǝn karfi dliɓ, itsawar tara a gǝmadu ad dinari kitakul. Ai pǝlarud kǝ ud ǝn vak.
MAT 20:10 Liye tsa farsa man tlǝr chak, da itar ǝn kurana, da pǝlatra mal kǝ chalǝmakhud. Ai itsawar tara a gǝmadu ad dinari kitakul.
MAT 20:11 Chauga tsitar, ka farsa ɗungw tsitar ak dadak gukh.
MAT 20:12 Ən kwar kwarne, ‘Li sawala kǝ khala, uk tlǝr aw kitakul a manga itar. Kǝnde a vakal ǝn man tlǝr, zǝ bǝg rǝv ǝn tǝ dliya fatsi, ka pǝla kǝnda kalkal kha zǝ itar.’
MAT 20:13 “Ka nǝv dadak gukhen kǝ ud fang ǝn tatak tar, ‘Ar tsaghwa, a biɗkurkhe ba ka bi. Tsa khayanǝf bakh kur kwarne, da ba kura kwaɓ dinari kitakule ǝn pǝlarud kǝ ud ǝn vaka biya?
MAT 20:14 Chaukafkhai chawa dǝge dǝgagh, dǝg daksagh. Ka kǝ khayanǝf barabǝg kǝ li sa kǝ khal, kalkal de bakha kǝ.
MAT 20:15 Nakh ka dǝ ndzǝɗa mankafkhe dǝge naghga ghǝrara dǝ dǝge dǝgara? Ən shilga ndar kha man kǝlakhuɗari?’
MAT 20:16 “Wirva yan, udakh zikǝn liye ǝn tǝvuk, da nǝga itar kǝ dǝg khal. Liye kǝ khal tsuguna, da nǝga itar kǝ dǝg chak.”
MAT 20:17 Madǝv Yasu ǝn dǝgo da Wurshalim. Ka ɗakhtǝrkhai ak furakh sar na kǝlatǝm mits da tǝ kalam. Ka niya tsitar,
MAT 20:18 “Nǝgha kina ni dǝgal da Wurshalim kiyam. Vake da bǝkduwud ka Zǝr Ud da dǝva zikzikana kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ malǝmakh li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus. Ka da ǝntlaka lav mǝts itar.
MAT 20:19 Ən tǝ khalak yana, ka da bǝkdu bǝg itar kǝ liye kwal Yakhudakh. Da nena ka nene tar, ka da wadzaku kiɓ itar, ka da khǝrtǝka khǝrta itar tsugun. Ən tǝ fitsa khǝkǝrɗ tsuguna, da tsiya ka tsiyud.”
MAT 20:20 Khalak yana, ka saks kǝ nus Zabadi dǝ zar sar mits da vak Yasu. Kǝlgan ad juguv ǝn tǝvuk Yasu, ka takaɗ digit tsin ǝn vak sar.
MAT 20:21 “Uɗǝn nakhara?” Nǝv Yasu. Ka nǝv nusen kǝ Yasu, “Manakai lanji kǝ zararana mits, tsa ndzǝga itar zǝ khǝn tlǝksagh. Fang ǝn tǝ dǝva kafagha, fang ǝn tǝ dǝva dleɓagh.”
MAT 20:22 Ai ka nǝv Yasu kǝ nusen, “Əntsa ba kur dǝge ǝn takaɗa kur bi. Da tǝkha kur kǝ khǝɓu dlaɗe da khǝɓa ka?” “Da tǝkha kǝnd,” Nǝv itar tsin.
MAT 20:23 Ka nǝv Yasu, “Kaɗikaɗiya da khǝɓa khǝɓa kur dlaɗ, ai giɗǝn tǝ dǝva kafara, zǝ giɗǝn tǝ dǝva dleɓara, na ka dǝ ndzǝɗa zǝɓǝf ude da bara ka yan bi. Ina kǝ vakakha, dǝg liye ɗikatǝrna Dadare ǝn gharazhigǝl wirva itar.”
MAT 20:24 Tsǝna kǝ chalǝm furakh khana kǝlɗǝk ndǝk yana, ka bazdu itar ad rǝv dǝ zar babakhana mits.
MAT 20:25 Ka ɗakhtǝrkhe Yasu daghan tar, ni, “Tsa tsǝkur kwarne shikakh udakhe kwal Yakhudakha, ǝn mǝdlara ndzǝɗǝn itar kǝ udakh tar. Zikzikanakh tar tuguna, ǝn mǝdla ndzǝɗ itar ǝn tǝ ghǝr tsitar.
MAT 20:26 Ya kur tsuguna, nala bin ndǝk yan ǝn tǝbur bi. Ən dleva yan, ɗaga ude ǝn nagh nǝga kǝ zikan ǝn tǝbur, barari tsin nǝga kǝ vǝɓur.
MAT 20:27 Tsugun, ɗaga ude na nǝga kǝ mal ǝn kur, barari tsin nǝga kǝ vǝɓur.
MAT 20:28 Udan na tsuguna, da nǝga ndǝk va kǝ, ka Zǝr Ud, a sodagh kǝ ɗaba udakh kǝ, a so kǝ ɗaba ka ɗaba bud bi. Da bǝdu bǝg ka tsugun ad safar, kǝ kat da udakh zikǝn.”
MAT 20:29 Madǝv Yasu zǝ furakh sar ǝn ɗuwars kǝs Jariko, zikǝn dzakhava udakh ǝn gatatǝrs gat.
MAT 20:30 Ka nǝg ngulfakh mits ǝn nndzǝgan ǝn tǝ kalam ɗul. Tsǝna tsitar kwarne Yasu ǝn dǝgala, ka tlǝkha tsitar kwarne, “Dadzikan, Zǝr Dod, manga kwiɗkwiɗǝrǝvǝnda.”
MAT 20:31 Ka tavdi kǝ chalǝm ǝn tǝb kǝ dzakhava udakh ǝn tǝghǝr tsitar kwarne, “Tǝriɗ nikur.” Ka gwidǝn tlǝkha tsitar char kwarne, “Dadzikan, Zǝr Dod, manga kwiɗkwiɗǝrǝvǝnda.”
MAT 20:32 Ka ghitsǝga Yasu, ka ɗakhtǝrkhai saks, ka sa itar. Niya tsitar, “Uɗǝn na kur mana kura mana tsǝki?”
MAT 20:33 Ka nǝv itar tsin, “Dadzikan, na kǝnda ngwarǝf diyakhǝnd.”
MAT 20:34 Wirva kwiɗkwiɗǝrva, ka gǝma Yasu ad diyakh tar. Tǝvin tǝvina ka nǝgha nǝgha itar. Ka gatars itar.
MAT 21:1 Sa tsitar khefa dǝ Wurshalim, sara da kǝs ya Betafaji, ǝn Ghuɓa Olive. Ka ɓǝlandal Yasu ad furakh sar mits.
MAT 21:2 Niya tsitar, “Damaks da gǝdzar kǝs nǝn tǝvukur. Ba kurǝn daksa, da nǝgha nǝgha kur bab dlingw zǝ gǝlaɓa sar ngwaɗan. Vǝdamatǝrs vǝd, ka ɓakdǝghǝr kur.
MAT 21:3 Da kwara kurkhe udan ad tlǝrna lav, kwararkhe kur kwarne, ‘Dadzikan ǝn naghtǝran.’ Dlaɓ da wura tǝra wura zula khǝɗikǝn.”
MAT 21:4 Ina kǝ dǝge dzoghǝra, a righif dǝge tsa kwarga Ishay tlayang. Ni,
MAT 21:5 “Kwaramatǝra kwara kǝ udakh ya Wurshalim,” “Niya shikur ǝn saks da vakur. Nagh bakh kalali tsin bi, ǝn dǝg ǝn tǝ dlingw, Ən dǝgǝn tǝ gǝlaɓa dlingw.”
MAT 21:6 Ka dǝgal kǝ furakh saren, manga itar ndǝkve tsa kwaratǝrkhe Yasu.
MAT 21:7 Ka ɓadǝghǝr itar dlingwen zǝ zer sar. Ka ɓalakho itar gabagakh tar ǝn titar, in tsuguna dowa nndzǝgan ǝn tǝf.
MAT 21:8 Zikǝn udakhe ɓalakhga gabagakh tar ǝn tǝ ɗul. Ka kalakhga yakhaya tsugun ad tlim uf, ka ɓalakhga itar ǝn tǝ ɗul.
MAT 21:9 Udakhe ǝn tǝvuk sar zǝ liye ǝn gatars gatǝn tǝlga, ka tlǝkha tsitar kwarne, “Bark kǝ Zǝr Dod.” “A ndzawa bark kǝ dadake ǝn sǝgdagh ǝn ɗakha Dadzikan.” “Farghǝrfǝgud kǝ Yazhigǝle ǝn khuɗ kǝ gharazhigǝle chakw.”
MAT 21:10 Da kǝ Yasu da Wurshalima, ka tsiyif mǝkǝn kǝ li kǝsen daghan. Ka ndiɗakave tar kwarne, “Warinena kudra?”
MAT 21:11 Ka nǝv dzakhava udakhen, “ Ina Yasu tlayange ǝn Nazarat ǝn kǝs Galili.”
MAT 21:12 Da kǝ Yasu da Fǝta Yazhigǝl, lakwtǝrdu kǝ li dzawa zǝ li sakw digit ǝmb. Ka khambanǝf ad vǝlenga li mbaɗu kwaɓ. Ka khambanan ad vak ndzakhgan li sakwdu takalamasar.
MAT 21:13 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “A vindzavan ǝn kaɗkaɗ Yazhigǝl kwarne, ‘Da ɗakh mǝgharud, mǝghe da ɗǝgawud ǝmb.’ Ai a nandala kur kǝ vak ɓǝghava sǝnkarakh.”
MAT 21:14 Ka saks kǝ ngulfakh zǝ ghwirɗikakh da vak sar ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝl, ka mbakhatru.
MAT 21:15 Zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus, nǝgha tsitar ad dǝg ndawakakhe a mangin. Tsuguna, tsǝna tsitar ad tlǝkh kǝ zar ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝl kwarne, “Bark kǝ Zǝr Dod.” Ka bazala rǝv tsitar.
MAT 21:16 Ka ndiɗarwal itar kǝ Yasu, “Ən tsǝna tsǝna kha dǝge ǝn kwara zara na kina?” Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Ən tsǝna tsǝna ka gǝn. Atsuk a taɓa bakh kur tugwado tugw ǝn vindzan na kǝ lav Yazhigǝl kwarne, “ ‘A batrǝm ǝn ghai kǝ zara zǝ vunjakh ka de mbaɗkhambaɗ.’ ”
MAT 21:17 Ka ɗuwatǝrs ǝn vin. Sawala, ka dal da kǝs ya Betani. A khǝnal ǝn vin.
MAT 21:18 Ngurga kǝ kǝs, madvin ǝn saks da Wurshalim, ka ndzikǝnǝf way.
MAT 21:19 Nǝgha tsin ufa ghǝdiven ǝn tǝ kalam ɗul, ka dal da vak ufen, na dǝge mbǝladuwin ǝn tǝf bi, uk tlim sar. Ka niya kǝ ufen, “Aghba kha da yig zǝr kǝ ngǝɗa bi.” Tǝvin tǝvina ka ghulkavala ufen.
MAT 21:20 Nǝgha kǝ furakh sar ndǝk yana, ka ndawatrǝf char. “Uɗa lava kǝ ufa ghǝdivena ghulkavala gujaɗ ndǝk ini?” Nǝv itar.
MAT 21:21 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai Yasu, ni, “Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, da nǝg kur dǝ fadǝghǝrofǝg, tsuguna a bǝga ba kur tsugu tsa khǝɗikǝn bi, da tǝkha kur kǝ mangan mal kǝ dǝge a manarkhe ka kǝ ufa ghǝdivǝn. Tsugun, da tǝkha kur kǝ kwarkhai kǝ gil zikan kwarne, ‘Tsiyin tǝvan, ɓǝlvǝdagh ɓǝla da dǝlv.’ Ka da dzoghǝr dzǝg ndǝk yan.
MAT 21:22 Da fadǝghǝro kur, ɗaga dǝge takaɗga kur ǝn vak Yazhigǝl ǝn ɗǝgau, da mbǝladu mbǝla kur.”
MAT 21:23 Sa kǝ Yasu da Feta Yazhigǝl, madvin ǝn tsagdutsag, ka sasǝg kǝ zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ malakh tar kǝ dlamakh da vak sar. Ka nǝv itar, “Ən mana dira kǝ ndzǝɗa kha dǝgakhani? Tsuguna war kǝ bakhena kǝ ndzǝɗi?”
MAT 21:24 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai Yasu kwarne, “Ghǝrara tsugun khine da ndiɗakurwala ndiɗa kǝ. Da ngawake kur ndiɗar, ghǝrar tsuguna, da kwara kura kwara ka ad ndzǝɗakhe ǝn manakh da ka dǝgakhan.
MAT 21:25 A so dǝvara ndzǝɗe ǝn parada Yukhan dadak para ud ad udi? A so ǝn vak Yazhigǝle, awana a so ǝn vak ud khi?” Ka farsa tsugu tsitar ǝn tatak tar, kwarne, “Da ka ǝn vak Yazhigǝla nikiyam, ka da ndiɗa kiyamwal ndiɗa kwarne, ‘Ai uɗa lava tsukur kwal fadǝghǝro dini?’
MAT 21:26 “Ai daka ǝn vakuda nikiyam, ǝn gǝdza kiyam kǝ dǝge da mana kiyama udakh. Wirva a fadǝghǝro udakh daghan kwarne tlayang Yukhan.”
MAT 21:27 Ka ngawarkhai itar kǝ Yasu kwarne, “Ən tsa ba kǝnda bi.” Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Ai na ghǝrara da kwara kura khulf ndzǝɗe ǝn manakha ka dǝgakhana bi.”
MAT 21:28 “Uɗǝn ɗaya kur ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ ina kǝ lavi?” Ai ǝn kwarin kwarne, nǝg udanen mits zar ghwalvakh tsin. Ka dǝgal tsin da vak malan, niya tsin, “Zǝrara, dǝg dǝgal da mantlǝr ǝn gukh inabi khan.”
MAT 21:29 Ka niya tsin, “ ‘Na kǝn dǝgal bi,’ Ai kǝ khala ka ɗayanan ad ghǝra, ka dǝgal tsin.”
MAT 21:30 “Dǝgal kǝ daden da vak yan kǝ zǝr sar, kwararkhai ndǝkve tsa kwarar khaiyin kǝ dǝg chak. Ka ngawarkhai zǝr saren kwarne ‘Aya dada, da dǝgal kǝ,’ Ka dal ba tsugun bi.”
MAT 21:31 “Ən tǝb tar na mitsa, war kǝ manga dǝge na dad tarni?” “Dadake tsa chak na,” Nǝv itar. Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar “Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, li chau khadama zǝ garnakakh, itar da dagh da tlǝksa Yazhigǝl tǝghǝr kǝ tsǝkur.
MAT 21:32 Wirva a sodagh Yukhan da mǝdla kura ɗul kanadi, a fadǝghǝro ba kur din bi. Ai li chau khadama zǝ garnakakh, a fadǝghǝro itar din. Tsakhǝnmin nǝgha tsǝkur ndǝk yan, a mbǝɗanǝf ba kur rǝvura ka fadǝghǝro kur din bi.
MAT 21:33 “Bambǝg tlim kǝ tsǝn tlǝrna jakva lava tsugun. Nǝg udanena, a njavgan ad gukh inabi. Tsarghǝran dǝ ghǝrgh, tǝfgan ad fike da pǝrtsin ad yu inabi ǝmb. Ɗikanan ad tsǝɓana kǝ vak, ki dǝgo kǝ dadak uf chau kǝ nǝgharu kǝ gukh. Ka batrǝm ad gukh inabi ǝn dǝv kǝ yakhay, kǝ nǝgharu nǝgha tsitar. Khala kǝ yana, ka dal da tlǝrna khaye bit.
MAT 21:34 Manga kǝ sarta tsǝg zar inabi, ka ɓǝlanǝf ad zar man tlǝr sar, da vak li batrǝmin ad gukh inabi ǝn dǝv tar. Kǝ chawardǝghǝr dleva dǝg sar, ak zar inabiyen.
MAT 21:35 “Tǝkǝn liye nǝgharu kǝ gukhen, ka vaitǝrkhai itar kǝ zar man tlǝr saren. Mbakǝn itar dǝ kǝɗa kǝ yan. Kǝɗga itar ad yan kǝ mǝts. Laiga itar ad yan dǝ kurakh, ka amtsǝgan.
MAT 21:36 Ka gwidǝn dadak gukhen ad ɓǝla tlǝrna zar man tlǝr sar mal ke tsa chak. Ka gwidǝn manarkhai li nǝgharu kǝ gukhen, ndǝkve tsa manarkhai itar kǝ li tsa chak.
MAT 21:37 Kǝ dǝg mbasa, ka ɓǝlanǝf dadak gukhen ad zǝr sar dǝgal da vak tar. Avin, ‘Na tsugu bi, da farghǝrfǝg itar kǝ zǝrar.’
MAT 21:38 “Nǝgha kǝ li nǝgharu kǝ gukhen ad zǝren, ka nǝv itar ǝn tǝb tar, ‘Auna dadake da wur gukhen ǝn saks. Kǝɗyamga kǝɗ. Dǝgakhe da wurina, nǝgin kǝ dǝg mar.’
MAT 21:39 Ka viga itar, tlǝvars itar da tilg lingwa gukh Inabi, kǝɗga itar.
MAT 21:40 “Ka nǝv Yasu, da soghǝr dadak gukh na ma, ka uɗa da manarin kǝ li nǝgharu kǝ gukheni?”
MAT 21:41 Ka nǝv itar tsin, “Da khǝdztǝr khǝdza kǝ nguɗiyakhen ǝn tǝ ɗule kwal khwara kǝ vaz. Ka da bara kǝ yakhay ad nǝgharu kǝ gukhen. Liye da bakhara dlǝva dǝg sar, ak zar inabi ǝn sarta tsǝga tsǝg.”
MAT 21:42 Nev Yasu Tsitar “Atsuk a taɓa bakh kur tugwado tugw ǝn vindzan na kǝ lav Yazhigǝla? Ai kwarin, “ ‘Kure a ɗuda li khǝga kǝ man tlǝr din. In kǝ nala kǝ kure, a khutanan ad khǝg. Ina kǝ digita tlǝr Yazhigǝl, tsuguna dǝg ndaw ndawan ǝn diyakh mar.’ ”
MAT 21:43 “Wirva yan, ǝn tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, da chawa chawud tlǝksa Yazhigǝl ǝn vakur. Da bara kǝ udakhe da man dǝg khwaranakh ai da yara zǝre da dlayaru kǝ tlǝksa Yazhigǝl.
MAT 21:44 Ɗaga ude da ɓǝlo da tǝ kuren, da kala khwetl khwetl. Ude da ɓǝlo kurna da tǝf tsugun, da pǝkha pǝkha kurɗik ndǝk khǝpi.”
MAT 21:45 Tsǝna kǝ zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ Farisakh ad yan kǝ jakva lavakhe kwargin, ka katlga itar kwarne ǝn kwarǝn tǝghǝr kǝ tsitar ad lavan.
MAT 21:46 A gatga itar ɗul kǝ viyavi. Ai ǝn gǝdza itar kǝ dlamakh. Wirva a fadǝghǝro udakh daghan kwarne tlayang Yasu.
MAT 22:1 A gwidǝn Yasu ǝn kwara tǝra lav dǝ jakva, ni,
MAT 22:2 “Tlǝksa gharazighǝla ngwaɗa shike, a ɗikarnan ad khwaɗga sǝba kǝ zǝr sar.
MAT 22:3 Ka ɓǝla tǝrǝf kǝ zar man tlǝr sar, kǝ dǝgal da kwara tǝra kǝ udakhe tsa ɓalgin. Ka kalwal itar kǝ sausǝg.
MAT 22:4 “Ka gwidǝn ɓǝlatǝrǝf kǝ tlǝrna zar man tlǝr sar kwarne, ‘Kwarama tǝrkhai kwara kǝ liye tsa ɓalgud kwarne, Niya audzala kǝn takhga dǝg zu, a kharga ka kawakh, zǝ kawakh gude tsa ngalgud wulǝklǝk. Itsauɗa audzandalud. Ausǝgam da vak sǝb.’ ”
MAT 22:5 “Li tsa ɓalgud da vak khwaɗgen, na ɗangwa tsitar dǝ ɓalen bi. Yana dakaval da gukh, yan tsuguna dakaval da man kasukw sar.
MAT 22:6 Yakhaya tsuguna, ka vaige tar liye tsa ɓǝla tǝrǝfuden, ka mbatǝre tar dǝ dlaɗ char, ka khadztǝr khai itar.
MAT 22:7 Ka kǝɗga rǝvakhuɗ ad shik char. Ka ɓǝlanǝf ad tlujiyakh sar, dǝgal da khǝdz liye tsa khǝdzga zar man tlǝr sar. Ka ndǝghǝrs itar kǝs tar.
MAT 22:8 “Tǝkhal kǝ yana, ka niya kǝ zar man tlǝr sar, ‘Audzandalud ɗikana dǝg zuwa khwaɗga sǝb. Ai liye tsa ɓalguda, a dlai ga ba itar tsugun kǝ saks bi.
MAT 22:9 Wirva yan, gatamars kǝ ghay baramakh, ɓalamga ɓal itsǝra kǝ ude a gamga kur zin, kǝ saks da vak kwaɗgen.’
MAT 22:10 Zar man tlǝren tsuguna, ka dǝgala tsitar kǝ baram kǝ baram. Ka dzakhadǝghǝr itar ad daghan udakhe a gamge tar zitar, zǝ liye njivva, zǝ liye kwal njiv. A righǝf vak kwaɗgen dǝ ghulabakh char.
MAT 22:11 “Ka sa shik da vaz liye tsa ɓalgin, ka nǝgh nǝgha tsin ad udanen, ai kwal talǝm gabag khwaɗga sǝben.
MAT 22:12 Ka niya kǝ udanen, ‘Tsaghw, a sa ndar kha da vana kwal talǝm gabag khwaɗga sǝbi?’ Ka piyarwala dǝg kwar.
MAT 22:13 “Ka nǝv shik kǝ zar man tlǝr sar, ‘Ndzaɗamarna dǝva zǝ sig, tlǝvamars tlǝva dǝgal da mel, vake dǝ gurtl. Vake da tudin dǝ kǝrɗ tliɗ.’
MAT 22:14 “Zikǝn liye ɗakhtǝrkhai ud, ai khǝɗikǝn liye dzaravan.”
MAT 22:15 Dud ǝn kwarina, ka dala Farisakh kǝ ɗaya kavu lav ngara dlǝgd kǝ Yasu, kǝ viyaviya tsitar, ǝn tǝ dǝva dǝ dǝge da kwarin.
MAT 22:16 Ka ɓǝlanǝf itar furakh tar, dagha zǝ udakhe khayanǝf dǝ man tlǝksa Khiridus, da vak sar. Ka nǝv itar, “Malǝm, tsa tsǝkǝnda kwarne ud jir khǝ, ǝn tsagdu lav Yazhigǝl kha kalkal. Wirva yakitakw ud ǝn vakagh. Na khǝn gǝdz kwarara lava kǝ ud, itsa ndar zika sar bi.
MAT 22:17 Kwara kǝnda kwar, da khǝn vazana, kalkal nagh pǝlara khadam tsǝkǝnda kǝ Kaisar, zikan kǝ Shik ǝn Roma, kalkal ba khi?”
MAT 22:18 Ai Yasu tsuguna, tsa tsin kǝlade ǝn rǝvakhud tar. Ka ndiɗatǝrwal, “Kur nguɗiyakh, uɗa lava tsǝkur ǝn na ngaka dlǝgdi?
MAT 22:19 Mǝdla maka kwaɓen ǝn pǝl da kur khadamen.” Ka ɓardǝghǝr itar ad kwaɓ dinari.
MAT 22:20 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal, “Vakdiying zǝ ɗakhǝng ǝn tǝfi?”
MAT 22:21 Ka ngawar khai itar kwarne, “Dǝg Kaisar.” Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Bamara bǝg kǝ Kaisar ad dǝg Kaisar. Bara kur kǝ Yazhigǝl ad dǝg Yazhigǝl.”
MAT 22:22 Tsǝna tsitar ndǝk yana, ka ndawatǝrǝf char. Ka ɗuwars itar, dakaval itar.
MAT 22:23 Fitsa va yanen, tǝkǝn Sadukiyakh li kwarne na tsiyin ngitl bi, sagh itar da vak Yasu dǝ ndiɗ.
MAT 22:24 Ka nǝv itar, “Malǝm, a kwarga Mus kwarne, da ǝmtsǝga ude kwal yiga zǝr dǝ nus sar, barari wura wura kǝ zǝr bab sar ad nus saren, ki yakhar khai zara tsin.
MAT 22:25 Neg sukwtakh uɗif ǝn tǝbǝnd. Ɓu kǝ zǝr chak ad nus, ka amtsǝgan kwal zar, ɗuwardan ad nus sar kǝ saghǝr sar ai ǝn gatars gat.
MAT 22:26 A dzogher ndǝk yan kǝ dǝg mits, a yiga ba dǝ zǝr din bi. Ndǝk yan zǝva kǝ dǝg khǝkǝrɗ, tangw da tǝ dǝg uɗif, a yiga ba itar zara din bi.
MAT 22:27 Kǝ dǝg mbasa, ka ǝmtsǝga nusen.
MAT 22:28 Fitsa tsiyin ngitla, da nǝga kǝ nus warin ǝn tǝb kǝ udakhana uɗifi? Fatsi daghan tara a zǝɓaruwi?”
MAT 22:29 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai Yasu, “A zaɗga kur char. Wirvǝn tsa ba kur vindzan na kǝ lav Yazhigǝl bi. Tsuguna, ǝn tsa ba kur ndzǝɗa Yazhigǝl bi.
MAT 22:30 Fitsa tsiyin ngitla, na dǝɗungw da zǝɓ nus bi. Tsuguna na bud da bǝdu dugh kǝ sǝba bi. Da ngwaɗa zarɓǝlakh Yazhigǝl ǝn gharazhigǝl itar.
MAT 22:31 Ən tǝghǝr kǝ fitse da tsida tlamtsakh ǝn ngitla, a tugwa bakh kur dǝge a kwara kur khai Yazhigǝla? A vindzavan kwarne,
MAT 22:32 ‘Ka Yazhigǝl Ibram. Ka Yazhigǝl Ishaku. Ka Yazhigǝl Yakub?’ A mǝdlanan kwarne Yazhigǝl tlamtsakh ba ka bi, Yazhigǝl liye dǝ safa kǝ.”
MAT 22:33 Tsǝna kǝ dzakhava udakh ndǝk yan, ka ndawatǝrǝf, wirva tsagdutsaga saren.
MAT 22:34 Tsǝna kǝ Farisakh kwarne a bǝlaterghǝr Yasu ak Sadukiyakh, ka dzafkhai itar ǝn vak kitakul.
MAT 22:35 Fang a tǝb kǝ li wagayal ǝn tsa ndzikha ndzikh Mus, ka kurakura tsin dǝ ndiɗ.
MAT 22:36 “Malǝm, ira kǝ ndzikh ǝn ndzikha ndzikh Yazhigǝle a maltǝr khai kǝ yakhaya daghani?”
MAT 22:37 Ka ngawar khai Yasu kwarne, “ ‘Waya dǝ Dadzikan Yazhigǝl gha, dǝ rǝvakhuɗagha daghan, dǝ safagha daghan, zǝ ɗayaghǝragha daghan.’
MAT 22:38 Ina dǝg chak, in tsugun kǝ maltǝr khai kǝ yakhaya daghan.
MAT 22:39 Dǝg mits kǝ ndzikhe a malgan ad yakhaya kǝ ndzikha ndzikhakhen tsuguna, ngwaɗa dǝg chak ghǝrsar. ‘Waya dǝ udakh daghan ndikve ǝn wayakha ghǝragh.’
MAT 22:40 Daghan dǝge a vindzavan ǝn ndzikha ndzikh Mus, zai in kaɗkaɗakh tlayangakh Yazhigǝl, a ghitso ǝn tǝ ndzikha ndzikhakhana mits itar.”
MAT 22:41 Dzafkhai kǝ Farisakh ǝn tǝ dǝva kitakw, ka ndiɗatǝrwal Yasu,
MAT 22:42 “Uɗa ɗayaghǝrur ǝn tǝ dǝva dǝ Kristuwi? Zǝr warek kini? “Zǝr Dod,” nǝv itar.
MAT 22:43 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal Yasu, “Uɗa lava kǝ Dod tsugun ǝn tǝ dǝva dǝ Sǝɗikw Yazhigǝl ǝn ɗakhin dǝ Dadzikani? Wirva nǝv Dod,
MAT 22:44 “ ‘Dadzikan Yazhigǝl. Niya kǝ Dadzikan nar. Ndzǝga ndzǝg ǝn tǝ dǝva kafar. Akwa bars ka ad tlǝghumakhagh. Ən kuskǝ ɗǝgaɗǝgagh.’ ”
MAT 22:45 “Da ka ǝn ɗakha dǝ ‘Dadzikan,’ Dod ad Kristu, ai da nala ndar, Kristu kǝ zǝr sari?”
MAT 22:46 Na ude ngawar khai bi. Ve tsǝn tǝ yanen kǝ khǝna, na dla ude sigwif kǝ ndiɗarwal ndiɗa bi.
MAT 23:1 Ka nǝv Yasu kǝ dzakhava udakh zǝ furakh sar.
MAT 23:2 “Liye tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh zǝ Farisakh, ǝn man tlǝr tsagdu ndzikha ndzikhe tsǝn mana Mus itar.”
MAT 23:3 “Wirva yan, tsǝnamaru tsǝna kǝ ɗaga dǝge kwara kurkhai itar. Ai gatamars ba kǝ dǝge ǝn mana itar bi. Wirva na itar ǝn man dǝge ǝn tsagdu itar bi.
MAT 23:4 Bakhatro itar kadlang ɗimɗiman kǝ udakh, ai kwal tǝkha kǝ ud kǝ kapanǝf. Ai itar dǝ ghǝr tar, nugw ba itar itsa kǝ barva zǝr dǝv kǝ mǝlaru kǝ kapa kapa kǝ udakh bi.”
MAT 23:5 “Daghan tlǝre ǝn mana itara, ǝn mana kǝ nǝghda nǝgha nǝgha kǝ udakh itar. Ən ngwaɗa zikzikan na kǝ vindzan na kǝ lav Yazhigǝl ai mbǝghga itar, kǝ nguɗǝn tǝ vakdi tar zǝn tǝ dǝva tar. Tluzhe ǝn tukw ghai gabagakh tara, tsǝɓanyan mal kǝ dǝg udakh.”
MAT 23:6 “Zik gat vij ndzakhgan khwarkhwaran tsitar ǝn vak man khwaɗǝg. Zǝ vak ndzakhgan khwaran ǝn gud dzakhava Yakhudakh.
MAT 23:7 Zǝ gat nǝghatǝrdi nǝgh dǝ fatǝrghǝrfǝg tsud ǝn kasuk. Zǝ ɗakhtǝr ɗakha dǝ ‘Malǝm.’
MAT 23:8 “Ya kur dǝgi, ɗakh kur bud dǝ ‘Malǝm’ bi. Wirva Malǝmura kitakul, tsuguna daghan nura sukwtakh kur.
MAT 23:9 Ɗakham ba dǝ itsawar dǝ ‘dad’ ǝn larda nabi. Wirva uk kitakul Dadure ǝn gharazhigǝl.
MAT 23:10 Ɗakh kur bud dǝ mal bi. Wirva kitakul Malur in Kristu.
MAT 23:11 Dadake in zikan daghan ǝn tatakur, barari nǝga tsin kǝ dadak mana kura tlǝr.
MAT 23:12 Ɗaga ude a fǝrghǝr kǝ ghǝrsar, da gulandagh gulud. Ude a gulandagh ghǝrsar tsuguna, da fǝrghǝrfǝg ud.
MAT 23:13 “Ɗangwa tsǝkur, li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh zǝ Farisakh, kur li valdu ghǝrur. Khǝdardu kur ɗul daks da tlǝksa gharazhigǝl kǝ udakh. Kura a da ba kur bi, tsuguna a khayarnǝf ba kur kǝ liye ǝn na daks kǝ daks bi.
MAT 23:14 “Ɗangwa tsǝkur, li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh zǝ Farisakh, kur li valdu ghǝrur. Ən zawakh dǝgakh widgakh kur. Ən tǝ khala kǝ yana, ǝn zulu zula kur ǝn ɗǝgau, wirva ki nǝgakura nǝga tsud. Wirva yan, taka lave da mana kuruda da malamala dǝ dǝg udakh char.
MAT 23:15 “Ɗangwa tsǝkur, li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh zǝ Farisakh, kur li valdu ghǝrur. Wirvǝn ɗitsagharghǝr kǝ ɗǝlvakh kur, zǝ khay kǝsakh wirva ki gǝmadu dadak pǝlghǝr kitakul kǝ gatars kǝ Yazhigǝlur. Khala kǝ khayanǝf khaya tsin, ka da nanadala nǝg kur, kǝ dadake tlayga daks tsin da kara fay, mal tsukur sig mits.
MAT 23:16 “Ɗangwa tsǝkur, ngulfakh li ndaɗ ngulfakh. Ən kwara kwara kur kwarne, ‘Ɗaga ude a waɗgan dǝ Fǝta Yazhigǝl, barari ba tsin man dǝge waɗgin da manamana bi. Ai tsugun, ɗaga ude a waɗgan dǝ vǝrshakanǝv ai ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝlen, barari tsin man dǝge a waɗgin da manaman.’
MAT 23:17 Kur dlagakhan ngulfakh. Irek ndanganra, vǝrkashanǝve, awana Fǝta Yazhigǝle a nandala ad vǝrkashanǝv kǝ chuwaɗaɗ khi?
MAT 23:18 Nikur tsugun, ‘Ɗaga ude a waɗgan dǝ vak sadak, barari ba tsin man dǝge waɗgin da manamana bi. Ai tsugun, da ka waɗgin dǝ dǝg tsuf, barari tsin man dǝge a waɗgin da manaman.’
MAT 23:19 Kur ngulfakhan. Irek ndanganra, dǝg tsufa nagha, awana vak sadake a nandala ad dǝg tsuf kǝ chuwaɗaɗ khi?
MAT 23:20 Wirva yana, itsaware waɗgan dǝ vak sadak, a waɗgan dǝ vak sadak zǝ dǝge ǝn tǝf daghan.
MAT 23:21 Tsugun, ɗaga ude waɗgan dǝ Fǝta Yazhigǝl, a waɗgan dǝ Fǝta Yazhigǝlen, zǝ Yazhigǝl ai nzǝgan ǝn ǝmb.
MAT 23:22 Ɗaga ude a waɗgan dǝ gharazhigǝl, a waɗgan dǝ vij man tlǝksa Yazhigǝl, a waɗgan tsugun dǝ dadake ǝn nndzǝgan ǝn tǝ vij man tlǝksen.
MAT 23:23 “Ɗangwa tsǝkur, li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh zǝ Farisakh, kur li valdu ghǝrur. Ən bǝdu bǝg kur ad zak chachakuram, zǝ tlim dǝg ɗalakhur. Ai ka ɗuwar kur man zik zikan kǝ dǝgakhe ǝn nagha ndzikha ndzikh Yazhigǝl kǝ manaman. Zik zikan na kǝ dǝge ǝn nagha ndzikha ndzikh ad manaman tsukur in kwarne, man jir ǝn itsauɗ, mǝdla kwiɗkwiɗǝrv, khayanǝf khay ǝn digitakh. Itar dǝge tsa khwara manamana tsǝkur, zǝ kwal ɗuda manakh yakhin bi.
MAT 23:24 Kur ngulfakh li mǝdlara ɗul kǝ ngulfakh. Ən ɗizdu ɗiza kur kusingakh, ai tsuguna, ka ndǝg dlǝgwam kur.
MAT 23:25 “Ɗangwa tsǝkur, li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh zǝ Farisakh, kur li valdu ghǝrur. Li pardu lig kwat hǝb yu, zǝ kwat zu kaf, ai ǝn rǝvakhuɗura, reghan kur dǝ dǝgakhe a khwatsga kur ǝn vak udakh dǝ ndzǝɗ, zǝ nagh ghǝr tsugun.
MAT 23:26 Kur ngulf ya Farisakh. Famarsa paradu khuɗ kwat hǝɓ yu, zǝ kwat zu kaf, ǝn tǝ khal kǝ yana, ka da chuwaɗaɗ zǝva lǝgsar.
MAT 23:27 “Ɗangwa tsǝkur, li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh zǝ Farisakh, kur li valdu ghǝrur. Ngwaɗa ngitlakhe a masar vud ɓǝgan na kǝ wal, ai da khwara kǝ vaza dǝ lǝgan, ai ǝn khuɗ khuɗa, uk tlatlakh zǝ ruta digitakh.
MAT 23:28 Ndǝk yan ghǝrur tsugun ǝn tǝ ɓal. Dǝn vaz kur vaza udakh, li kanadi kur ǝn tǝvuk Yazhigǝl. Ai du khuɗan tsuguna, reghan kur dǝ man dǝgakh valdu ghǝrur zǝ kǝladakh.
MAT 23:29 “Ka zu vuk kǝ Yasu dǝ kwar kwarne, Ɗangwa tsǝkur, li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh zǝ Farisakh, kur li valdu ghǝrur. Wirva khakhga kur ngitlakh tlayangakhe tsa dur. Ka ɗikakhga kur ad dǝg chaɗakhe da dzamatǝr dud kǝ li tsa manga kanadiyakh.
MAT 23:30 Afkur tsugun, da tsa tlǝm kǝnda ǝn sarta dzidzakhǝnd, tsa na kǝnda da bǝg dǝv zitar ǝn khǝdz tlayangakh Yazhigǝl bi.
MAT 23:31 Ən tǝ dǝva dǝ lavur a mǝdlanan kwarne, zar ya udakhe tsa kaɗakhga tlayangakh Yazhigǝl kur.
MAT 23:32 Dam da mbasana nguɗi nguɗi dǝgakhe tsa farsa ndzidzakhur.
MAT 23:33 “Kur bubakh, kur zar ya kukhukhwakh. Da ngikha ndar kur ǝntla lave da mana kurud kǝ daks da kara fayi?
MAT 23:34 Wirva yana, ǝn ɓala kura ɓala kǝ ad tlayangakh Yazhigǝl, zǝ li kwalemlem, zǝ liye ǝn tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus. Ka da kaɗakaɗa kur yakhaya. Khǝrtga kur yakhay. Dlagha tǝrkhai kur kǝɗa tsugun kǝ yakhay ǝn gud dzakhavur. Ən gatatǝrs gata kur kǝ kǝsa kǝs, ǝn batra dlaɗ.
MAT 23:35 Da ɓǝlondagh ɓǝla ka ad udakhan, wirva viz li kalali, liye khǝdzavan ǝn lardǝn, kǝ wurakurǝm da kwindur. Farsǝn tǝ viz Habil dadak kalali, kakh da tǝ viz Zakari zǝr Bereki. Ai kǝɗga kur ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝl ǝn tǝvǝgh kǝ vak ndǝgha dǝg tsuf.
MAT 23:36 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, daghan ina kǝ digitakh, da dzoghǝr dzǝg dǝ udakh kwargǝn.”
MAT 23:37 “Udakh ya Wurshalim, udakh ya Wurshalim, kur li khǝdz tlayangakh Yazhigǝl. Liye ǝn lay liye a ɓǝlondaghud da vakur. Ngǝrwa siga tsǝka nagh dzakha kura dzakh, ngwadai dzakha ghwachik ad zar sar ǝn kus kǝ kudlǝbsari? Da mbiyanena kalwal kur.
MAT 23:38 Auna tǝkhina, a ɗuwakurdud fǝtur, nala kǝ kwazagh.
MAT 23:39 Ni ǝn kwara kura kwara kǝ, farsǝn tǝkhina, da aghba kur da nǝghakan bi, akwa sarte da kwara kur kwarne, ‘Bark kǝ dadake ǝn sǝgdagh ǝn khuɗ kǝ ɗakha Dadzikan.’ ”
MAT 24:1 Sawal kǝ Yasu ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝl madvin ǝn dǝg, ka sa furakh sar da vak sar. Ka ndǝɗga itar ghǝr sar, ka mǝdlara itar Fǝta Yazhigǝle a khǝgud.
MAT 24:2 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal kwarne, “Nǝgha tsǝkur ina kǝ khǝgakha? Ai ǝn tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, na itsa kitakul kǝ kure da ɗudud ǝn tǝ tlǝrna bi. Daghana da khatdu khatud.”
MAT 24:3 Madǝv Yasu ǝn nndzǝgan ǝn tǝ khuɓa Olive, ka sa furakh sar da vak sar tukuɗa tar. Ka ndiɗarwal itar. “Kwara kǝnda kwar, da dzoghǝr yawa yakhana daghani? Tsuguna da zǝk ndǝk uɗa, da katlda kǝnda sarta guyo guyagha, zǝ mbasa lardi?”
MAT 24:4 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai Yasu kwarne “Ya tsǝkwamana ghǝr, valkurdu ba itsawar bi.
MAT 24:5 Wirva zikǝn li da sosǝg ǝn ɗakhar da kwara kwara itsawar tar kwarne, itar Kristu. Da valduvala itar udakh zikǝn.
MAT 24:6 Da tsǝna tsǝna kur lav ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ pǝgakh, zǝ lavakh wuleng wuleng ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ pǝgakh. Ya gǝdzam bi, wirva barari dzoghǝr dzǝg tsin ndǝkyan. Ai mbasa sara a sa ba ndan bi.
MAT 24:7 Tlǝrna khaya da darghǝr dǝg kǝ tlǝrna khay. Tlǝrna shik tsugun da darghǝr dǝg kǝ tlǝrna shik dǝ pǝg. Da nǝg way, zǝ mbǝɗa pǝgdǝmakh ǝn tlǝrna vakakh.
MAT 24:8 Daghan ina kǝ digita, farsafǝg sar kǝ dlaɗ, ngwaɗa farsa ɓis tatǝrs yiga kǝ nus.
MAT 24:9 “Da vi kur viya itar, bǝkurdu itar kǝ li da bakura mbakhǝl, kǝɗ kurkhai itar. Daghan udakh ǝn larda, da ɗukurd khai ɗuwa itar wirva ɗakhar.
MAT 24:10 Ən tǝ yan kǝ sart, zikǝn li da guyardu lǝg kǝ fadǝghǝrofǝg. Da sakwdu sukwtakh tar itar kǝ tlǝrna udakh. Tsuguna da naghva ba itar bi.
MAT 24:11 Da zikǝn tlayanga filfilakh da sakhgawal kǝ valakhdu udakh zikǝn.
MAT 24:12 Wirva sǝgva kǝladakh, wayve ǝn manakava udakha da zang.
MAT 24:13 Ai itsawar ǝn bǝga rǝv da tǝ mbas, da kata katud.
MAT 24:14 Tsuguna da kwardu kwarud ina kǝ lav zǝɗa kǝ tsǝn, ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝksa gharazhigǝl, itsa dǝvar ǝn lard. Ki da nǝga kǝ shid kǝ itsera kǝ mbǝrtakh ǝn lard daghan. Tǝkhal kǝ yana, ka da saks mbasa sar.
MAT 24:15 “Wirva yan, da ka nǝgha tsǝkur dǝg dzadle a kwarga Daniyal tlayang, ǝn ghitsǝn tǝ vakvak Chuwaɗaɗan ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝl, (dakake ǝn tugwado lavana katlga katlin dǝge tukuwin).
MAT 24:16 Ghalak liye ǝn ǝntla khay ya Yakhudi, khwaya itar dǝgo da ghuɓakh.
MAT 24:17 Ya ude nndzǝgan ǝn tugwud tsuguna, ya so ɓin da zǝɓ dǝge ǝn khud mǝgh bi.
MAT 24:18 Ude ǝn gukh tsuguna, ya guyo bin saks da zǝɓ nura sar bi.
MAT 24:19 Ya ɗangwa kǝ nǝghwase dǝ khuɗ, zǝ liye dǝ zǝr ǝn tǝ tukw dǝv, ǝn tǝ yanen kǝ sart.
MAT 24:20 Kwam ɗǝgau, dzoghǝr ba khwayana ǝn sarta fagh bi, awana fitsa ngiya bi.
MAT 24:21 Yǝn tǝ yanen kǝ sarta, da nǝg dlaɗ char, khulfe kwal taɓa tsuɗ manaman. Gwil farsa vǝrɗ lard, tangw da tina kǝ sart. Aghbud da gwidǝn man khulf sar kǝ yanen bi.
MAT 24:22 “Da tsa khǝtsana bud ad khǝnakhen bi, tsa na ud dǝg sige da tǝma dǝ safa bi. Ai wirva li dzǝran na kǝ udakh Yazhigǝl, da khǝtsa khǝtsa Yazhigǝl ad khǝnakhen.
MAT 24:23 Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sart, da ka nǝv itar tsǝkur, ‘Vaza, auna Kristu ǝn van’ awana, ‘A niya ǝn vin’ ya khayamanǝf bi.
MAT 24:24 Wirva Kristu filfilakh zǝ tlayang filfilakh da sakhgawal itar. Da manakh zik zikan na kǝ jakvakh, zǝ zik zikan na kǝ dǝg ndawakakh itar kǝ valdu udakh. Da tsa tǝkhin kǝ manawan, da valdu vala itar zǝva liye a dzǝrtǝkhai Yazhigǝl.
MAT 24:25 Tsǝnam tsǝna, a kwara kur khai ka, kǝda saks kǝ sart.
MAT 24:26 “Wirva yan, da ka kwara kur khe itar kwarne, ‘Ani ǝn tǝghal,’ a ɗuwam dǝgal da vinen. Awana, ‘Aunin ǝn khuɗan kǝ gud ɓǝghan,’ ya famadǝghǝro bi.
MAT 24:27 Ndǝkve ǝn tsuwaɗa wuɗ ad gharazhigǝl, sǝgo ǝn mbǝrt kǝ kǝs da tǝ vakghǝr, da dzoghǝr ndǝk yan sǝgdaghara ka Zǝr Ud.
MAT 24:28 Ɗaga vake dǝ ǝmtsa digitakh, ǝn vin ǝn dzakhava gumbakh.
MAT 24:29 “Ən dǝvǝn dǝv, ǝn tǝ khal kǝ khǝna dlaɗakhen, “ ‘Ka da nǝga fatsi kǝ gurtl. Tǝl tsuguna naba da kheɗaɗ bi. Kwadladlakh tsuguna ka da ɓaloɓalǝn Sǝgadagh ǝn gharazhigǝl. Da gǝdiya gǝdyud ad ndzǝɗakhe Ən fǝf gharazhigǝl.’ ”
MAT 24:30 “Da mǝdlo ǝn tǝ yanen kǝ sart jakva Zǝr Ud ǝn tǝ fef gharazhigǝl. Ɗaga mbǝrt udakhe ǝn lard tsugun, da tuwa itar wirva ruwa udakh. Da nǝgha nǝgha itar Zǝr Ud ǝn sǝgadagh ǝn ghwik, dǝ ndzǝɗa zǝ ndanga char.
MAT 24:31 Da bǝlondagh ɓǝla ad zarɓǝlakh sar, kǝ fǝg dǝro ɗakh ǝn tuwa char. Da dzakha dzakha itar ad dzǝran na kǝ udakh sar, ǝn tǝ kalam lard daghan. Tsiyif ǝn tǝ yan kǝ kalam lard, da tǝ yan.
MAT 24:32 “Tsagam tsaga digit ǝn vak ufa ghǝdiv. Da farsin ɗidu tlim kǝ ɗado wilwa tlim, ǝn tsatsǝg kur kwarne a khǝrzǝga vi.
MAT 24:33 Ndǝk yan tsugun, da nǝgha tsǝkur dǝgakhana daghan. Da tsa tsǝg kur kwarne, a khǝrzǝgan, ǝn tǝ ghay gud.
MAT 24:34 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, udakh kwargǝn, da ruga ba itar bi, khekwa dzoghǝr dǝgakhana daghan.
MAT 24:35 Gharazhigǝl zǝ khaya da nige tar. Ai lave ǝn sǝgawal ǝn ghayara na bai kwal da regha bi.”
MAT 24:36 “Ai na ude tsa khǝna zǝ sarte da dzoghǝr dǝgakhan na bi. Itsa zarɓǝlakhe ǝn gharazhigǝl, itsa Zǝren, uk Dad kitakul ǝn tsan.
MAT 24:37 Ndǝkve tsa manavin ǝn sarta Nuhu, da dzoghǝr ndǝk yan, ǝn tǝ sarte da sǝgdagh ka Zǝr Ud.
MAT 24:38 Ən khǝna khen kǝda saks kǝ ǝrkhagw, ǝn zuwazu, zǝ khǝɓakhǝɓ udakh. Ən sǝbado sǝbud nus, ǝn sǝbdu sǝbud dǝghaw dǝgal, da tǝ sarte a dagh Nuhu daks da gakhunda peryu.
MAT 24:39 Ən tsa ba itar dǝge da dzoghǝr dzǝg bi, ba sa kǝ ǝrkhagwa ndǝtru daghan. Da nǝga ndǝk yan sǝgdaghara ka Zǝr Ud.
MAT 24:40 Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sart, ud mits da man tlǝr ǝn gukh, da ɓaɓud kitakula, ɗuwars ud kitakul.
MAT 24:41 Nughwasa mits da pǝkha itar ǝn tǝ vǝr, da ɓaɓud kitakula, ɗuwars ud kitakul.
MAT 24:42 “Wirva yana, ɗikamfǝkhe ɗik, da tsa ba kur sarte da sǝgdagh Dadzikan nura bi.
MAT 24:43 Ya dǝgi, katlamga katla din. Da tsa tsatsǝg dadak mǝgh ad sarte da saks gǝl da fǝta sar kǝviɗ, tsa na ba da khǝn khar bi. Tsuguna, tsa da khayanǝf ba daks kǝ gǝl da fǝta sar bi.
MAT 24:44 Wirva yan, barari tsǝ ghǝrur tsǝgun, kǝ giɗa ɗem. Wirva da sǝgdagh ka Zǝr Ud ǝn tǝ sarte kwal kurga tsǝkur.
MAT 24:45 “War zǝr man tlǝre njiv, zǝ khiɗanyan tsǝgun, ai bǝga dad mǝgh sar, kǝ nǝgharu kǝ yakhaya kǝ zar man tlǝr sar, kǝ batra dǝg zuwa tar tsin ǝn tǝ kalkala sart, kwal mbitsana tsini?
MAT 24:46 Da dadak bark yan kǝ zǝr mǝghe da sa dad mǝgh sar, ka tlarghǝr ǝn man tlǝre tsa barud.
MAT 24:47 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, dad mǝgh na, da barǝmbǝg kǝ zǝr tlǝren ad daghan dǝgakh sar kǝ nǝgharu nǝgha tsin.
MAT 24:48 Da ka dǝg charan ba zǝr tlǝren bi, ka niya kǝ ghǝrsar, ‘Dad mǝghara da zulu zula kǝ saks.’
MAT 24:49 Ka farsa mbatltǝr mbatla tsin kǝ liye ǝn mane tar tlǝr dagh. Ka zuwazu zǝ khǝɓakhǝɓa tsin zǝ li khaɓ digit.
MAT 24:50 Ka da saks dad mǝgh sar kǝ zǝr tlǝren, ǝn tǝ khǝne kwal kurga tsin, zǝ sarte kwal tsa tsin.
MAT 24:51 Ka da ngadla ngadla dad mǝgh sarna dǝ kiɓ. Dǝge da dzoghǝr dǝ liye valdu ghǝr tar da ndǝk yan kǝ ghǝr sar. Ən tǝ vake da tuda udakh dǝ kǝrɗ tliɗ.
MAT 25:1 “Ən tǝ sarte da sǝgdagh ka Zǝr Ud, tlǝksa gharazhigǝl da kura dǝ dugh mbǝlakh kǝlɗǝkud. Li zǝɓarǝf karakazaz tar kǝ dǝgal da gam zil ghaul.
MAT 25:2 Dliɓ ǝn tǝb tara dlagakh, dliɓ tsuguna li khiɗan.
MAT 25:3 Dlagakhena a ɓarǝf ad karakazaz tar, a ɓǝf ba itar wal bi.
MAT 25:4 Li khiɗanakhena a ɓarǝf ad wal ǝn khatakwakh tar zǝ karakazaz tar.
MAT 25:5 Zil ghaulena a sa ba dura bi, daghan tara a mbatǝra khar, ka kaɗ tǝrkhe khar.
MAT 25:6 “Ən tǝb viɗ char, ka tsǝna tsǝna tsud ɗakha kwarne, ‘Auna zil ghaul, ausǝgam sǝgawal da gamagam.’
MAT 25:7 “Ka tsayif dugh mbǝlakhen daghan. Ka ɗikanǝf itar ad karakazazkh tar.
MAT 25:8 Ka nǝv dlagakhana kǝ li khiɗan, ‘Chiɗa makǝndu chiɗa walur, wirva karakazazǝnda da ǝmts.’
MAT 25:9 “Ka nǝv itar, ‘Au, da tlakiyamal ba tsǝkǝnda zǝ kur bi. Damdǝgal da vak li sakwdu wal, kǝ sukwaru sukwa tsǝkur kǝ ghǝrur.’
MAT 25:10 “Madǝv dlagakhen ǝn tǝ ɗul dǝgal da sukw walen, ka soghǝr zil ghaul. Dugh mbǝlakhe a ɗikfekhaya, ka dara zǝ zil ghaul da vak khwaɗga sǝb. Ka khǝɗarduwud gud.
MAT 25:11 “Kǝ khala ka sasǝg kǝ dlagakhen. ‘Dadzikan, Dadzikan, ngura kǝnda ngura gud,’ nǝv itar.
MAT 25:12 “Ka ngawa tǝrkhai zil ghaul kwarne, ‘Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, ǝn tsakura ba ka bi.’
MAT 25:13 “Wirva yan, ɗem nikur, wirvǝn tsa ba kur ad khǝna awana sarte da sǝgdagh ka Zǝr Ud bi.
MAT 25:14 “Tsugun, da kura tlǝksa gharazhigǝlud dǝ ude da dǝgal da tlǝrna vak. Ka ɗakhgan ad zar tlǝr sar, ka batrǝm ad lǝmanakh sar ǝn dǝv tar, kǝ nǝgharu nǝgha tsitar.
MAT 25:15 Ka baran ak itsawar ad kalkal ndzǝɗa sar. Ak yan fanga, baran ad talenti dliɓ. Ak tlǝrna baran ad talenti mits. Ak tlǝrna tsuguna, baran ad talenti kitakul. Ka dǝgala sar tsin.
MAT 25:16 Dadake tsa chauga talenti dliɓǝna, ǝn tǝvin tǝvin, ka dǝgal tsin da mbǝɗa dǝv dǝ kwaɓ sar. Ka mbǝladu ad tlǝrna talenti dliɓ ǝn tǝghǝr.
MAT 25:17 Ndǝk yan ak dadake tsa chauga talenti mits. Ka mbǝladu ad tlǝrna talenti mits ǝn tǝghǝr.
MAT 25:18 Ai dadake tsa chauga talenti kitakulǝn, ka dǝgala tsin, tǝfgan ad fika, ɓǝghanan ad kwaɓ dadmǝgh saren.
MAT 25:19 “Ən tǝkhal kǝ zulu zula tsin, ka sasǝg kǝ dadmǝgh taren, kǝ kwarara dǝge a manga itar dǝ kwaɓakhen.
MAT 25:20 Ka zǝghvoghǝr zǝr tlǝre tsa chauga talenti dliɓna da tǝvǝgh tsin. Ka ni, ‘Dadmǝgh, talenti dliɓ a baka khǝ, auna kwaɓe tsa baka khǝ. A mbǝladu ka ad yu talenti dliɓ ǝn tǝghǝr tsugun.’
MAT 25:21 “Ka nǝv dadmǝgh sar tsin, ‘Dakhwal khǝ, zǝr tlǝr charan zǝ dadak khuta lanjikh. A manga kha dǝ jir ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ digit khǝɗikǝn. Da bǝg kha bǝga ka kǝ dadak nǝgharu kǝ digitakh zikǝn. Ausǝg da khwaɗga zǝ kǝ.’
MAT 25:22 “Ka zǝghvoghǝr zǝr tlǝre tsa chauga talenti mits da tǝvǝgh tsin. Ka ni, ‘Dadmǝgh, talenti mits a baka khǝ. Auna kwaɓe tsa baka khǝ. A mbǝladu ka ad yu talenti mits ǝn tǝghǝr tsugun.’
MAT 25:23 “Ka nǝv dadmǝgh sar tsin, ‘Dakhwal khǝ, zǝr tlǝr charan zǝ dadak khuta lanjikh. A manga kha dǝ jir ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ digit khǝɗikǝn. Da bǝg kha bǝga ka kǝ dadak nǝgharu kǝ digitakh zikǝn. Ausǝg da khwaɗga zǝ kǝ.’
MAT 25:24 “Ka zǝghvoghǝr zǝr tlǝre tsa chauga talenti kitakul da tǝvǝgh tsin. Ka ni, ‘Dadmǝgh, tsa tsǝka kwarne bǝza manva zǝ khǝ. Ən tsǝg khikh ǝn vake kwal tukhga tsǝkh, zǝ udz digit ǝn vake kwal kwazdu tsǝkha ad khulf.
MAT 25:25 Wirva yana, a gǝdzǝf kǝ, a dala ka ɓǝghana ka ad kwaɓagh ǝn khay. Auna dǝge dǝgagh.’
MAT 25:26 “Ka ngawar khai dadmǝgh saren kwarne, ‘Kha nguɗi zǝr tlǝr, mandǝlgh tsǝgun. Tsa tsǝkha kwarne ǝn tsǝg khi kǝn vake kwal tukhga tsǝka? Zǝ udz digit ǝn vake kwal kwazdu tsǝka khulfa?.
MAT 25:27 Afke tsa bake kha dǝ kwaɓar ǝn bank, vake ǝn ɗidud kwaɓ. Da tsa soghǝr ka, tsa ka chauga ka dǝ yu ǝn tǝghǝr.
MAT 25:28 Wirva yan, ka gwiyavǝkhe da vak udakhe ǝn vin, ka niya tsitar, chawamarval chaw ad talenti kitakulen, ka bara kur kǝ dadake dǝ talenti kǝlɗǝk.
MAT 25:29 Itsawar ai nǝg dǝ digit, da banarghǝr bǝgud, ka da ngǝrsh digit ǝn vak sar. Ude naba din tsugun bi, ngwaɗa khǝɗike dinin, da pǝrɗarval pǝrɗud.
MAT 25:30 Ai ina kǝ nguɗi zǝr tlǝrǝn, tlǝvam dagh tlǝva da nikyen na kǝ gurtl. Vake ǝn tuwud dǝ kǝrɗ tliɗ.’ ”
MAT 25:31 “Sarte da sǝgdagh Zǝr Ud ǝn ndanga sar, zǝ zarɓǝlakh Yazighǝle ǝn gharazhigǝl. Ka da nndzǝgan ǝn tǝ vǝja man tlǝksa sar.
MAT 25:32 Daghan mbǝrt udakh ǝn lard da dzakhavǝn tǝvuk sar. Ka da taka taka ad udakh, ngwaɗe ǝn taka dadak zighwa ad tuwaghakh zǝ waghakh.
MAT 25:33 Ka da bǝga bǝga ad tuwaghakh ǝn tǝ dǝva kaf sar, ka waghakh tsuguna ǝn tǝ dǝva tleɓ sar.”
MAT 25:34 “Ka dǝge da kwaratǝra shik ak li ǝn tǝ dǝva kaf sar, ‘Ausǝgam kur li ba kur ghǝr Dadar ad bark, wuramuwur ad tlǝkse a ɗika kur nud gwil sarta vǝrɗ lard.
MAT 25:35 Ən sarte tsǝn ndzika waya, ka ba ka kur dǝg zu. Ndzikǝf kǝ ndǝl, ka ba ka kur yu khǝɓ. Ən sarte tsa ghwulab kǝ, chaw ke kur da fǝtur,
MAT 25:36 Na ka dǝ dǝg nguɗa bi, ba ka kur dǝg nguɗ. Tsǝn yanga ba ka bi, ka nǝghakdi kur. Tsǝn gud sal kǝ, sa kur da nǝghakdi nǝgh.’
MAT 25:37 “Ka da ngawara ngawa li kanadi kwarne, ‘Dadzikan, tsa nǝgha kha yawa kǝnda ǝn ɓis way, ka bakha kǝnda dǝg zuwi? Yawa nǝgha kha kǝnda kǝɗkhe ndǝl, ka bakha kǝnda yu khǝɓi?’
MAT 25:38 Yawa a nǝgha kha kǝnda ghwulab, ka chaw khe kǝnda da fǝtǝndi? Yawa nǝgha kha kǝnda kwal dǝg nguɗ, tsuguna bakha kǝnd ad dǝg nguɗi?
MAT 25:39 A nǝgha kha yawa kǝnda kwal yanga, awana ǝn gud sal, ka dal kǝnda da nǝghakh di nǝghi?
MAT 25:40 “Ka da ngawa tǝra ngawa shik kwarne, ‘Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, itsauɗa a manar khai kur kǝ sukwtakharan liye khǝtsala ndanga tar char, a manake tsǝka kur.’
MAT 25:41 “Ka da niya kǝ li ǝn tǝ dǝva tleɓ sar, ‘Tsiyam tsiyin vakar, kur liye tlap kurkhai Yazhigǝl. Damaks da kare kwal da ǝmtsa kǝ ngǝɗ. Ai ɗikarna ghud kǝ Shaɗan zǝ zarɓǝlakh sar.
MAT 25:42 Sarte tsa ndzika way, a ba ka ba kur dǝg zuwa bi. Ən sarte tsa ndzika ndǝl, a ba ka ba kur yu khǝɓa bi.
MAT 25:43 Ən sarte tsa ghulab kǝ, a chaw kai ba kur da fǝtakhur bi. Na ka dǝ dǝg nguɗa bi, a ba ka ba kur dǝg nguɗa bi. Sarte kwal tsa yanga tsǝk, tsuguna tsǝn ǝn gud sal kǝ, a nǝghakdi ba kur bi.’ ”
MAT 25:44 “Ka da ngawara ngawa itar kwarne, ‘Dadzikan, tsa nǝgha kha yawa kǝndǝn ndzikha waya zǝ ndǝli? Tsa nǝgha kha yawa kǝnda man ghulaba ghulabi? Tsuguna yawa nǝgha kha kǝnda kwal yanga, zǝn sarte tsǝn gud sal khǝ, kwal mǝlakhu tsǝkǝndi?’
MAT 25:45 “Ka da ngawa tǝra ngawa shik kwarne, ‘Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, itsauɗa dǝge kwal manar khai tsǝkur kǝ sukwtakharan liye a khǝtsala ndanga tar char, ka kwal mǝlaku tsǝkur.’
MAT 25:46 “Ka da bǝg tǝr bǝgud da dlaɗe kǝ ngǝɗ, li kanadi tsuguna da daks da safa kǝ ngǝɗe tar.”
MAT 26:1 Udzala kǝ Yasu ǝn kwaratǝra lavakhan na daghan, ka niya kǝ furakh sar.
MAT 26:2 “Tsa tsǝkur kwarne khwaɗga ɗitsaɗits tǝghga khǝna mits, da bǝdu bǝgud ad Zǝr Ud kǝ khǝrtakhǝrt.”
MAT 26:3 Tǝkǝn zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ malanakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ udakh, dzafkhai itar ǝn fǝta zikan na kǝ zil kǝs, ai ɗakhud dǝ Kayaf.
MAT 26:4 Ka ngakhanǝf itar ɗule da vida itar Yasu bǝghanyan, kǝɗa itar.
MAT 26:5 Ka nǝv itar, “Yin tǝ sarta khwaɗga ɗitsaɗitsa bi, ki khai kǝ da tsiya kǝ mǝkǝn kǝ udakh, kǝ tsiya ngǝji.”
MAT 26:6 Ən sarte tsǝn Betani Yasu, ǝn fǝta Siman ai tsa ndzikǝn fǝch.
MAT 26:7 Madǝv Yasu ǝn zu kaf, ka sasǝg kǝ nusen da vak sar, dǝ wal bǝtbǝtan, ai dǝ kwaɓ char righan ǝn khatakw. Ka ɗiyaro ǝn tǝ ghǝr.
MAT 26:8 Nǝgha kǝ furakh sar ndǝkyan, a bazatǝrdu ad rǝv. Ka nǝv itar, “A bazdu kǝ uɗud ad ina ni?”
MAT 26:9 “Azǝgha tsa sukwdu ud ad walǝn tǝ kwaɓ zikǝn, ka batrud ad kwaɓ sar kǝ talagakh.”
MAT 26:10 Tsa kǝ Yasu ad dǝge ǝn kwara itar, ka ndiɗatǝrwal kwarne, “Uɗa lava tsǝkur ǝn njǝgharu kǝ nusni? Ai dǝge a manakai yina dǝg khwaran.
MAT 26:11 Itsera kǝ khǝna dagha kur zǝ talagakh, ai ka, da dagh ba kiyam zǝ kur itsera kǝ khǝna bi.
MAT 26:12 Wal na ɗiyakdaghin, a manga kǝ ɗika ka vǝgh, kǝ khǝɗa ka khǝɗ.
MAT 26:13 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, itsa da kwardu ǝn varud lav zǝɗa kǝ tsǝna nǝn, ǝn lard daghan, dǝgǝn na manga nusna da kwardu kwarud ki da dzama da dzam.”
MAT 26:14 Fang ǝn tǝb kǝ kǝlatǝm mits, ai ɗakha sar Yakhud Iskariyoti, dal da vak zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh
MAT 26:15 ka niya tsitar, “Uɗa da ba ka kur, da sukwakurdu ka dǝ Yasuwi?” Ka kǝdlana itar ad kwaɓ dawan kulkhǝkǝrɗ, ka bara itar.
MAT 26:16 Tsiyif ǝn tǝ yanen kǝ sarta, ka farsa Yakhud ad tsakwaɗ ɗule da batǝrduwin ad Yasu.
MAT 26:17 Fitsa chak kǝ zu brudiye kwar yisti, ka sa furakh Yasu da vak Yasu, ndiɗarwar itar kwarne, “Ən varǝn nakha da ɗikakhana kǝnda vak zu kaf ɗitsaɗitsi?”
MAT 26:18 Ka niya tsitar, “Dam dǝgal da vak udanen ǝn dlǝmdla kǝs, kwararkhai kur kwarne, ‘A khǝrzǝga sartar, da zuwun fǝta ka kaf khwaɗga ɗitsaɗitsa zǝ furakhar.’ ”
MAT 26:19 Ka manga furakhen ndǝkve kwara tǝrkhai Yasu, ka ɗikanǝf itar ad kaf ɗitsaɗitsen.
MAT 26:20 Ɓǝlga kǝ khakhugw, ka ndzǝga Yasu zǝ furakh sar kǝlatǝm mits kǝ zu kaf.
MAT 26:21 Madǝv itar ǝn zu kaf, ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, kitakul ǝn kur, da sukwdu sukw.”
MAT 26:22 Ka bazala rǝv tsitar char. Ka farsa itar ad ndiɗarwar ndiɗa dǝ fang fang kwarne, “Ka nagh Dadzikana?”
MAT 26:23 Ka ngawga Yasu kwarne, “Ude ǝn zuwa kǝnda kaf ǝn kwat kitakul zin, in da sukwdu.
MAT 26:24 Da ǝmtsa ndǝkve a kwarga kaɗkaɗ Zǝr Ud. Ai ya ɗangwa kǝ ude da sukwdu Zǝr Ud. Adara tsa kǝ yanen kuda, tsa yiga bud bi.”
MAT 26:25 Ka nǝv Yakhud dadake da sukwdu sukw, “Malǝma, ka nagha?” Ka ngawarkhai Yasu, “An, audzala khǝn kwarga kwar.”
MAT 26:26 Madǝv itar ǝn zu kaf, ka ɓǝf Yasu ad brudi, udzala tsin ǝn kwarara us kǝ Yazhigǝl, ka kwachanan. Batran kǝ furakh sar, niya tsitar, “Vǝgharen, chawam chaw, zuwam zu.”
MAT 26:27 Ka ɓǝf ad kwate dǝ yu inabi, udzala tsin kwarara us kǝ Yazhighǝl, ka batran, niya tsitar, “Khǝɓam khǝɓ daghan nura.
MAT 26:28 Ina vizhare a righanǝf ad wilwa lanji Yazhigǝl. Ai da ɗiduwud wirva udakh zikǝn. Wirva ki ɓisa da khaipakh.
MAT 26:29 Ən kwara kura kwara kǝ, aghba ka da khǝɓ yu inabi bi, akwa sarte da khǝɓa ka wilwa yu inabi zǝ kur ǝn tlǝksa Dadar.”
MAT 26:30 Ka ɓǝlga Yasu zǝ furakh sar ad ndus. Khalak yana, ka sawal itar, ka dal itar da tǝ ghuɓe dǝ ufakh Oliv.
MAT 26:31 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Ən khuɗ viɗ khan, daghanura da khwaya kur dǝgal, da ɗukda ɗuwa kur. Ngwaɗe vindzan kwarne, “ ‘Da kǝɗga kǝɗa kad dadak zighw, Giɗa tuwagha da kwaza itar.’
MAT 26:32 Ai ǝn tǝ khal kǝ tsiyakǝf tsiya tsud ǝn ngitl, kǝn da dala tǝghǝr tsǝkur da khaya Galili.”
MAT 26:33 Ka ngawar khai Bitrus, “Itsa kwazga itar daghan, ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dǝge da dzoghǝr dǝ khǝ, na ka da khwaya dǝgala, ɗuwakhs ka lingling bi.”
MAT 26:34 Ka nǝv Yasu kǝ Bitrus, “Ən tǝkha kha tǝkha kǝ, ǝn khuɗ viɗ khan, kǝda wuga kǝ ghwachik, da bǝg tsugu tsakatsǝg kha sig khǝkǝrɗ.”
MAT 26:35 Ka nǝv Bitrus tsin, “Itsa da ǝmtsa kǝ, na ka da bǝg tsugu tsakhatsǝg bi.” A kwarakhga ndǝkyan chalǝm furakh sar daghan.
MAT 26:36 Ka dal Yasu dagha zǝ furakh sar da tǝ vaken ai ɗakhdud Getsemani. Ka niya tsitar, “Ndzamga ndzǝg ǝn van, dǝgal da ɗǝgau ǝn tǝ vin.”
MAT 26:37 Ka dala zǝ Bitrus zǝ zar ya Zabadi na mits. Ka dzoghǝr bazala rǝv zǝ dzamghǝr tsin.
MAT 26:38 Ka niya tsitar, “Rǝvara righan da baza rǝv, ai da tǝgh kǝ kǝɗkai. Giɗam giɗa ǝn van, ndzamga ndzǝg, ǝn gwitagwita zǝ kǝ.”
MAT 26:39 Dal tsin da tǝvuk khǝɗikǝn, ka khǝmbǝgan dǝ khuɗ khuɗ, ka ɗǝgau tsin, ni, “Dadara, da tǝkhin kǝ manawan, ɓakghǝr ɓa ad ina kǝ dlaɗ. Tsakhǝnmina, dǝge ǝn naka ba da manud bi, khekwa dǝge ǝn nakha da manud.”
MAT 26:40 Guyoghǝr tsin da vak furakh sar, ka tlatǝrghǝr ǝn khǝn khar. Ka niya kǝ Bitrus, “Atsuk tǝgh bakh kur khǝkarɗ daghur kǝ manga ɗǝm zǝ ka, kǝ dǝg aw kitakul biya?
MAT 26:41 Ɗem nikur zǝ ɗǝgau, ki khek da ɓǝla tsǝkur da dlǝgd. A khayanǝf sǝɗikw, ma vǝgha lǝɓukw.”
MAT 26:42 Ka gwidǝn dǝgal tsin da ɗǝgau kǝ dǝg mits, ni, “Dadara, da ka ǝn manawa ba ɓakghǝra inen kǝ tlaɗ bi, ba ka khǝɓa khǝɓa kǝ. Manud dǝge ǝn nakh.”
MAT 26:43 Gwiyoghǝr tsin saks da vak furakh sar, ka tlatǝrghǝr ǝn khǝn khar, wirva khar ǝn di tsitar char.
MAT 26:44 Ka gwidǝn ɗuwatǝrs Yasu, dala kǝ dǝg khǝkǝrd da ɗǝgau, ǝn gwayars kǝ lav kitakul.
MAT 26:45 Ka gwidǝn guyoghǝr da vak furakh sar, ka niya tsitar, “Dlakh kur ǝn khǝn khar zǝ fǝtava? Vazam vaz, a sagh sarte da bǝdu wud Zǝr Ud, da dǝv kǝ li khaipakh.
MAT 26:46 Tsiyam tsi, ndziyam dǝgal. Auna khǝrzǝga dadake da sukwdu sukwa saks da van.”
MAT 26:47 Madǝv Yasu dlǝn kwar lav, tǝkǝn Yakhud ai kitakul ǝn tǝɓ kǝ kǝlatǝm mits, a sagh dǝ dzakhava udakh zikǝn. Khwatan katsakarakh zǝ yaghwatakh ǝn dǝvakh tar kǝ udakhen. Zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ malanakhe ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ udakh kǝ ɓǝlatǝrǝf.
MAT 26:48 Yakhud dadak sukwdu sukwena, audzala kǝbitstǝr khai kǝbitsa kǝ dzakhava udakhen kwarne, “Dadake da bruwa ka, in udanen, viyam vi.”
MAT 26:49 Ka sagh Yakhud ger da vak Yasu, niya tsin, “Malǝm, ndzǝga ndzǝg gabǝr ǝn tǝghǝr tsǝkha.” Ka ɗuts khǝpangwang sar tsin.
MAT 26:50 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Tsaghwa mana dǝge a ɓǝkhdǝghǝr.” Ka zǝghvoghǝr udakhen, ka viga itar Yasu. Ka khutana itar char.
MAT 26:51 Ka fang ǝn tǝb kǝ liye dagh zǝ Yasu, ndǝɗadal ad katsakar sar. Ka tsaɓgan ad vǝɓ zikan na kǝ zil kǝs, ka ǝntlardu ad tlim.
MAT 26:52 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Bǝmbǝg ad katsakaragh da kumbǝgh sar.” Ɗaga liye udzǝva dǝ katsakar, da ǝmtsǝn tukw katsakar itar.
MAT 26:53 “Da khǝn kurana tǝgh bakh ka kǝ tatlaga Dadar kǝ mǝlaku mǝla? Ən dǝvǝn dǝva ka ɓǝlokandagh ad zar ɓǝlakh sar mal kǝ dǝb ǝnkwakh ǝnkwakh sig kǝlatǝm mits (6,000 x 12) kǝ tlujiyakha?
MAT 26:54 Ai da ka takaɗga ka kǝ mǝlaku mǝl, da righa ndarud vindzan na kǝ lav Yazhigǝle tsa kwargin kwarne, barari tsin dzoghǝr dzǝg ndǝkyani?”
MAT 26:55 Ka nǝv Yasu kǝ dzakhava udakhe a sa da viya vi, “A sawala dǝ katsakar zǝ yaghwatakh kur kǝ da vika viya ngwaɗa sǝnkara? Itsera kǝ khǝna kǝn ndzǝgan ǝn tsagdutsag ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝl, a vikai ba kur bi.
MAT 26:56 Ai daghan dǝgakhana dzoghǝra, a manga kǝ righada dǝge vindzga tlayangakh Yazhigǝl ǝn kaɗkaɗud.” Ka khwayala furakh sar daghan, ɗuwars itar.
MAT 26:57 Liye tsa viga Yasu, ka ɓal itar da fǝta Kayaf, zikan na kǝ zil kǝs. Li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh zǝ malanakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ udakh audzala itar ǝn dzafkhai dzǝg ǝn vin.
MAT 26:58 Bitrus tsuguna an gatatǝrsk kǝ bit, tangw da tǝ gǝlvakh zikan na kǝ zil kǝs. Da tsina, ndzǝgan zǝ li uf udakh kǝ vaz ɗule da mbasda dǝge da dzoghǝr dzǝg.
MAT 26:59 Zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ daghan li taka lav, ǝn gat udakhe da ǝntlarva lav fila fila itar ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ Yasu, kǝ nǝghda kǝɗa kǝɗa tsitar.
MAT 26:60 Itsa kitakula a mbǝladu ba itar bi, tsakhǝnmina zikǝn udakhe a sarawal kǝ ngatlarva fil. Kǝ dǝg mbasa ka sawala ud mits,
MAT 26:61 Ka nǝv itar, “Nǝv udanǝn, ‘Tǝkha ka kǝ khǝtana Fǝta Yazhigǝl, ndǝrga kǝn khǝna khǝkǝrɗ.’ ”
MAT 26:62 Ka tsiyif zikan na kǝ zil kǝs, ka niya kǝ Yasu, “Na kha dǝ dǝge tǝkha kha kǝ kwargan ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ lave ǝn kwarud ǝn tǝghǝr tsǝkha?”
MAT 26:63 A mbǝɗa ba Yasu ad khay bi. Ka nǝv zikan na kǝ zil kǝs tsin tsǝgun, “A takaɗ khe ka, a dzakhǝf ka dǝ Yazhigǝl dadak saf, kwara kǝnda kwar, da kha Kristu, Zǝr Yazhigǝl.”
MAT 26:64 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “An kalkal ndǝkve kwargakh.” Ai ǝn kwara kura kwara kǝ, tsiyif tǝkhǝn, da nǝgha nǝgha kur Zǝr Ud ǝn ndzǝgan ǝn tǝ dǝva kaf Dadak Ndangan daghan, tsuguna ǝn sǝgdagh ǝn ghwik ǝn gharazhigǝl.
MAT 26:65 Ka kwakhdu zikan na kǝ zil kǝs ad katlang sar, ka ni, “A nenenan ad Yazhigǝl, wirva yan, uɗa dla lava tsǝkiyam ǝn gat tlǝrna shidakhi? Tǝkhina a tsǝna tsǝkur ad nena Yazhigǝle a mangin.
MAT 26:66 Uɗa ɗayaghǝruri?” Ka ngawa tsitar kwarne, “Khwaran sara kǝɗgud.”
MAT 26:67 Ka tafarve tar ad shaghwvai ǝn tǝ vakdi, ka kǝɗǝf itar. Chalǝmakh tsuguna ɗayarwar itar mekhwpeng.
MAT 26:68 Ən kwar kwarne, “Kwara kǝnda kwar, kha Kristu, dadake barghǝr Yazhigǝl ad dǝv, war kǝ kǝɗkhǝfi?”
MAT 26:69 Ən tǝ sarta yayena, ǝn ndzǝgan Bitrus ǝn tǝ gǝlvagh mǝghen, ka sasǝg kǝ dugh kuɗig mǝghen da vak sar, ka ni, “Fang ghǝragha ǝn tǝb kǝ liye zǝ Yasu ud Galili nǝ”
MAT 26:70 Ka bǝgan ad tsugu tsa Yasu ǝn tǝvuk tar daghan. Ka ni, “Ən tsa ba ka dǝge ǝn kwara kha lavǝn tǝghǝr bi.”
MAT 26:71 Ka dala Bitrus da tǝ ghay rang, ka nǝgha nǝgh kǝ tlǝrna dugh kuɗig, ka niya kǝ udakhe ǝn ghitsǝn vin, “Ina kǝ uda, dagh itar zǝ Yasu ud ya Nazarat.”
MAT 26:72 Ka gwidǝn bǝg tsugu tsin, zǝva waɗa tsin kwarne, “Ən tsa ba va ka dǝ udan na bi.”
MAT 26:73 Zula khǝɗikǝn, ka sasǝg kǝ li ǝn ghitsǝn vinen da vak Bitrus. Ka nǝv itar tsin, “Kaɗkaɗiya ghǝragha fang khǝn tǝb tar, wirva ghaye ǝn kwara kha, in kǝ mǝtlakhai.”
MAT 26:74 Ka farsa Bitrus ad tlap ghǝrsar, zǝva waɗa tsin kwarne, “Ən tsa ba ka dǝ udan na bi.” Tǝvin tǝvin ka wuga kǝ ghwachik.
MAT 26:75 Ka dzamana Bitrus ad lav ai tsa kwararkhe Yasu kwarne, “Kǝda wuga kǝ ghwachik, da bǝg tsugu tsatsǝgarakh sig khǝkǝrɗ.” Ka dal da mel, ka tuwa tsin char.
MAT 27:1 Pǝrta kǝdl, daghan zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ malanakhe ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dlam, ka ɗayakavu itar dzanak kǝ kǝɗ Yasu.
MAT 27:2 Ka ngwuɗana itar, bo itar ǝn tǝvuk, ɓala itar da vak Bilatus Gwumn.
MAT 27:3 Vazga kǝ Yakhud dadake sukwdu Yasu kwarne a tǝkavarna lav ǝmtsa kǝ Yasu, ka bazala rǝv tsin dǝ dǝge a mangin. Ka sa da vak zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ malanakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dlam, guyatǝrnǝf ad kwaɓ dawan kulkhǝkǝrɗǝn.
MAT 27:4 Ni, “A manga ka khaip, kǝ sukwdu dadake kwal dǝ ghaz.” Ka nǝv itar, “Uɗa ɗangwundi? Ya ɗangwa yan.”
MAT 27:5 Ka ɗiyars ad kwaɓ dawanen ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝl, sawala, dakavala, ka khǝrtgan ad ghǝrsar.
MAT 27:6 Ka khutsanǝf zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakhen ad kwaɓen. Ka nǝv itar, “Kalkal ba ɗiga kwaɓ na tsud, ǝn vake ɗidud kwaɓ Fǝta Yazhigǝl bi. Wirva kwaɓ vizhinen.”
MAT 27:7 Ka ɗayakavu itar dzanak, ka sugwa itar vak dadake ndar dǝg ndǝr dǝ kwaɓen. Ki da nǝga tsin kǝ giɗengitl kǝstǝlakh.
MAT 27:8 Wirva yan, sakhkana ǝn ɗakha kǝ yanud ad vaken dǝ Vak Vizh.
MAT 27:9 Wirva yan, a righif lave tsa kwarga Rimi tlayang. Kwarne, “Ka ɓǝf itar kwaɓ dawan kulkhkǝrɗen, gane tsa kurga udakh ya Izrail kǝ pǝlapǝl ǝn tǝghǝr tsin.
MAT 27:10 Sukgwa itar vak dadak ndar dǝg ndǝr dǝ kwaɓen, ndǝkve tsa kwarakhai Yazhigǝl Dadzikan.”
MAT 27:11 Madǝv Yasu ǝn ghitsǝn tǝvuk kǝ Bilatus Gwumn, ka ndiɗarwar Gwumn kwarne, “Kha nagh shik ya Yakhudakha?” Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “An, kalkal a kwargakh.”
MAT 27:12 Ai kwarakhga kǝ zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ malanakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dlam, ad lav ghaze a ǝntlarva itar, a mbǝɗa ba dǝ ghay bi.
MAT 27:13 Ka nǝv Bilatus tsin, “A tsǝna bakha daghan lavakhan na ngatlakhvuda?”
MAT 27:14 A mbǝɗa ba Yasu ad itsauɗa bi. Itsǝn tǝghǝr kǝ kitakul kǝ lavakhe a ǝntlarva itar bi. A ndawanǝf ad Gwumn char.
MAT 27:15 Ən te itsera kǝ sarta khwaɗga fuɗkǝs ɗitsa ɗits, a kuyala Gwumn ǝn ɓalars dadak khaip kitakul sǝgawal ǝn gud sal. Ai naghga dlamakh ad ɓǝlars ɓǝl.
MAT 27:16 Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sart, nǝg udanen ai tsaghud, a ɗǝmal ǝn gud sal, ɗakha sara Barabas.
MAT 27:17 Dzafkhai kǝ udakha, ka ndiɗatǝrwar Bilatus kwarne, “War na kur ɓǝlakurnars ɓǝla tsǝki? Yasu Barabase, nagha Yasu ai ǝn ɗakhdud dǝ Kristu khi?”
MAT 27:18 A ndiɗga Bilatus ad ndiɗa na ndǝkyan, wirva tsatsin kwarne, a bǝdu itar ad Yasu ǝn dǝv sar kǝ wirva shilga.
MAT 27:19 Uk yan fang bi, madǝv Bilatus ǝn ndzǝgan ǝn tǝ vij taka lav, ka ɓǝlanǝf nus sar ad ud dǝ lava kǝ kwararkhai kwara kwarne, “Ɗuwars ɗuwa kwar lav ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dadake kwal khaipǝn. Wirva a mbaka dlaɗ char, ǝn tǝghǝr kina kǝ ud khan ǝn suwan.”
MAT 27:20 Tǝkǝn zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ malanakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dlam, shakhanǝf itar udakh kǝ kwar kwarne, ɗuwars ɗuwud Barabas, ka kǝɗguɗ Yasu.
MAT 27:21 Ka gwidǝn ndiɗatǝrwal Bilatus kǝ dzakhava udakh. “Warek ǝn tǝb tar ǝn nakur ɓǝlakurnars bǝla tsǝki?” Nǝv itara, “Barabas.”
MAT 27:22 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal Bilatus kwarne, “Ai uɗa da mana ka dǝ Yasu ai ɗakhud dǝ Kristuwi?” Nǝv itar daghana, “Khǝrtǝga khǝrtud.”
MAT 27:23 Ka ndiɗatǝrwar Bilatus kwarne, “Wirva uɗi? Uɗa dǝg bǝzane a mangini?” Ka sǝga ɗichaw kǝ udakh kwarne, “khǝrtǝga khǝrtud.”
MAT 27:24 Vazga kǝ Bilatus aghba dǝge tǝkhin kǝ mangan bi, tsugun a katlgan kwarne udakha ǝn tsikwva kǝ tsiya gadl. Ka ǝnkǝf ad yu, pargan ad dǝvakhsar ǝn tǝ vuk dzakhava udakh. Ka ni, “Na vizh ina kǝ ud ǝn kwindara bi. Ya ɗangur yan.”
MAT 27:25 Ka ngauga udakhen daghan kwarne, “Nalnǝg vizh sar ǝn kwindǝnda zǝ kwinda zarakhǝnd.”
MAT 27:26 Ka ɓǝlatǝrnars ad Barabas. Ən tǝkhal kǝ ba udakh tsin kǝ wadzaru kiɓ kǝ Yasu, ka bǝdu kǝ khǝrtga khǝrt.
MAT 27:27 Ka ɓalɓa kǝ tlujiyakh Gwumna Bilatus ad Yasu da tǝ gǝlvagh Gwumn, daghan tlujiyakhe ǝn dakwalen tsuguna a tsarghǝr itar.
MAT 27:28 Sakhardo itar kadlang, ka talarǝm itar shalaraz, khulf katlang shikakh.
MAT 27:29 Mbusaga itar dzakw man tlǝks dǝ tak, barǝm itar ǝn ghǝr. Ka ba itar da khuta gulv man tlǝks ǝn dǝva kaf sar. Khala kǝ yana ka kalaga itar juguv ǝn tǝ vuk sar, ka tsafatsafa tsitar, ka nǝv itar, “Dǝg safagh da tǝ uragh, Shik ya Yakhudakh.”
MAT 27:30 Tafarava itar shaghwvai da tǝ vǝgh. Ka chawarvar itar yaghwat man tlǝksen, dlaghar khai itar kǝɗa din ǝn ghǝr tsǝgun.
MAT 27:31 Udzal tsitar ǝn tsafatsafa, ka sakhardu itar gabag man tlǝkse tsa talarǝm itar. Ka talarǝm itar katlangakh sar. Ka ɓǝlando itar ǝn tǝvuk, ka ɓala itar kǝ wirva khǝrta khǝrt.
MAT 27:32 Madǝv itar ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dǝga, ka gamga itar zǝ ud ya Sayirin, ɗakha sara Siman. Ka barghǝr itar dǝ ndzǝɗ ad zǝɓ ufa khǝrte da khǝrtdud Yasu.
MAT 27:33 Sara da vake ǝn ɗakhud dǝ Golgot (dǝge ǝn tukuwina in, vak tlatl ghǝr).
MAT 27:34 Ən vin a bara itar yu inabi laɓan dǝ dǝg ɗekhɗekhan. Tapana tsina, ka kalwal kǝ khǝɓakhǝɓ.
MAT 27:35 Ən tǝkhal kǝ khǝrtǝga khǝrta tsitar ǝn tǝ ufa khǝrt, ka man tsats tsitar ki da taka gabagakh sar.
MAT 27:36 Ən tǝkhal kǝ yana, ka ndzakhga itar ǝn tǝ vin kǝ ufauf.
MAT 27:37 Ka tsakhga itar ad ghaza sare ǝn kwara itar, ǝn tǝ vakghǝr sar kwarne, “INA YASU, SHIK YA YAKHUDAKH.”
MAT 27:38 Khǝrtga itar tsugun ad sǝnkarakh mits ǝn tǝvǝgh kǝ Yasu. Fanga ǝn tǝ dǝva kaf tsin, yan tsuguna ǝn tǝ dǝva dleɓ sar.
MAT 27:39 Udakhe ǝn dǝgal, ka tsafatsafa itar ad Yasu, ka kaɗaghǝr itar.
MAT 27:40 Ka nǝv itar, “Khai ǝn kwarne tǝkhakha kǝ khǝtana Fǝta Yazhigǝl, ka gwiɗǝn ndǝrgakhǝn tǝ khǝna khǝkǝrɗ. Ai kata dǝ ghǝragh. Da Zǝr Yazhigǝl khǝ, sodagh sǝg ǝn tǝ ufa khǝrtan.”
MAT 27:41 Ndǝkyan tsugun kǝ zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus, zǝ malanakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dlam, ka tsafatsafa tsitar kwarne,
MAT 27:42 “A katgan ad yakhai, in tsuguna a piyarwal kat ghǝr sar. Shik ya Izrail bakhini? Sodagh sǝgin ǝn tǝ ufa khǝrtana tǝkhin, ka fadǝghǝro kǝnda din.
MAT 27:43 A bo dǝ ghǝr ǝn tǝ Yazhigǝl. Ai katga kata Yazhigǝlen tǝkhin, dǝn wayawayin. Wirva Zǝr Yazhigǝl ka ni.”
MAT 27:44 Ndǝkyan sǝnkarakh ai khǝrt tǝrkhai ud dagh, ghǝrtar tsuguna kwarar khai itar lav bǝzan.
MAT 27:45 Ən tǝ fatsi tǝghǝr, ka khǝɗardu ngurtl ad khaya kǝsen daghan, tangw da tǝ karfi khǝkǝrɗa khakhug.
MAT 27:46 Ən tǝ kalkala karfi khǝkǝrɗa khahughen, ka tlǝkha tsin char kwarne, “Elo, Elo, lama sabaktani?” Dǝge ǝn tukuwina in, “Yazhigǝla, Yazhigǝla, a ɗukǝdai ndar kha ndikini?”
MAT 27:47 Chalǝm udakhe ǝn ghitsǝn tǝvin, tsǝna tsitar ad inen, ka nǝv itar, “Ina kǝ uda, ǝn ɗakh Ili Tlayang.”
MAT 27:48 Ən dǝvǝn dǝva, ka khwayala fang ǝn tǝb tar, ɓadǝghǝr ad zǝr ndǝma ndǝm, luɓanan ǝn yu Inabi kwarekrekan. Siɓau ǝn tǝ yaghwat, ka talaro kǝ Yasu kǝ ɗutsaɗuts.
MAT 27:49 Ka nǝv chalǝmakh, “A ɗuwaman ndan, nǝgha nǝgha kiyam ndan patak da sǝgadagh Ili da katakat.”
MAT 27:50 Ka gwidǝn Yasu ǝn tlǝkha char, ka ɗi safa tsin, ɓawala safa sar.
MAT 27:51 Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sart, lǝgwit ghay gud ai ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝla tiɗǝm mits, tsif ǝn tǝ vak ghǝr kakh da tǝ khay. Khay tsuguna a giɗikǝfkhai, tiɗakhǝm kurakh.
MAT 27:52 Ka chaɓga ngitlakha ngwarǝf itar. Zikǝn udakh ya Yazhigǝle tsa rugana, a tsayatǝrǝfud dǝ saf.
MAT 27:53 Sakhawal itar ǝn ngitlakh tar. Ən khal kǝ tsif tsiya kǝ Yasu ǝn ngitl, ka dal itar da Wurshalim, chuwaɗaɗan kǝ dlǝmda kǝs. A mǝdlawa itar kǝ udakh zikǝn.
MAT 27:54 Nǝgha kǝ zikan kǝ tluji zǝ chalǝm tlujiyakhe ǝn uf Yasu ad mbǝɗa pǝgdǝm zǝ daghan dǝgakhe dzoghǝr, a gadzǝf itar char. Ka nǝv itar. “Zǝr Yazhigǝl ina kaɗi kaɗi.”
MAT 27:55 Nǝg chalǝm nughwaskh zikǝn tsugun ǝn vinen, ǝn vaza vaza kǝ bit. Liye tsa gatars kǝ Yasu gwil sǝgawal ǝn Galili, ǝn nǝgharu nǝgha itar.
MAT 27:56 Ən tǝb tara nǝg Maryam ǝn kǝs ya Magdal, zǝ Maryam bab Yakub zǝ Yusuvu, zǝ nus Zabadi.
MAT 27:57 Ɓǝlga kǝ khakhug, ka sa ud ya Armati, dadak tluwadal, ɗakha sara Yusuvu. In tsuguna fura Yasu.
MAT 27:58 Ka da da vak Bilatus shik da takaɗ tluvǝgha Yasu. Ka kwara tǝrkhai Bilatus ad bara tluvǝgha Yasu tsud kǝ Yusuvu.
MAT 27:59 Ka ɓǝf Yusuvu ad tluvǝgha Yasu, mbusanǝm ǝn wilwa lapin.
MAT 27:60 Ka khǝnanan Yusuvu ǝn gitl sare tsa khuradalin ǝn khurzǝzǝ. Ka tlǝgaru ad kur zikan, ka tǝkaval.
MAT 27:61 Maryam ǝn kǝs ya Magdal, zǝ tlǝrne ai ɗakhdud dǝ Maryam ǝn ndzǝgan itar ǝn vin, ǝn vaza ger da tǝ ngitlen.
MAT 27:62 Tǝkǝdla sar kǝ fitsa fǝtav, ka dala zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ Farisakh da vak Bilatus.
MAT 27:63 Nǝv itar, “Dǝg safagh da tǝ uragh, a dzamana kǝnda ad sarte tsa dla dadak valdu udakh na dǝ saf, kwarne, ‘Fitsa khǝkǝrɗa da tsiya ka dǝ saf.’
MAT 27:64 Wirva yan, babǝg ad udakh kǝ uf ngitlen char tangw da tǝ khǝna khǝkǝrɗ. Ki khek dǝgal kǝ furakh sar da gǝl tluvǝgh sar, kwarar khai itar kǝ udakh tsugun kwarne, ‘A tsiyif ǝn ngitl.’ Ya valdu udakhe kǝ dǝg mbas, da malamala dǝ dǝg chak kǝ bǝz.”
MAT 27:65 Ka nǝv Bilatus tsitar, “Khutsamǝf tlujiyakh, dam da ufaufa ad ngitlen, khalavuwa tǝkhur.”
MAT 27:66 Ka dǝgala itar kǝ gadlara gǝma gǝma kǝ itsawar ad ngitlen, ǝn tǝ dǝva dǝ tsakhga jakva ndzǝɗa shik ǝn tǝ kur ghay ngitlen. Tsuguna ka ba itar tlujiyakh kǝ ufauf.
MAT 28:1 Ən tǝkhal kǝ fǝtav, tǝkǝtlapǝrt fitsa tugwa chak kǝ kasuk, Maryam ǝn kǝs ya Magdal zǝ tlǝrne ai ɗakhdud dǝ Maryam, dala itar da nǝgha ngitl.
MAT 28:2 Kǝda dǝgal tsitar, a mangud mbǝɗa pǝgdǝm, wirva zǝrɓǝla Dadzikan a sodagh ǝn gharazhigǝl, tlǝgarwar ad kur ǝn tukw ngitlen, ka ndzo ǝn tǝf.
MAT 28:3 Da nǝgha tsǝkha ǝn wuɗa tsuwaɗaɗ, katlangan vǝgha sar tsuguna til ndǝk chachaɗ.
MAT 28:4 Nǝgha kǝ li ufa ngitlen, a gǝdzǝf itar char, ka tǝga vǝgh tsitar. Mbaɗakhga itar da khay ngwaɗa ǝmtsa udakh.
MAT 28:5 Ai ka nǝv zǝrɓǝla Yazhigǝlen kǝ nughwasakhen, “Gǝdzam bi, tsatsǝka Yasu ǝn gata kur, ai tsa khǝrtavan.
MAT 28:6 Aghbǝn vana bi, a tsif ndǝk vai tsa kwargin. Ausǝgam nǝghama nǝgha vakai tsa khǝnganin.
MAT 28:7 Damdǝgal kujaɗ kujaɗ, kwarama tǝrkhai kwar kǝ furakh sar kwarne, ‘A tsiyif ǝn ngitl. Kǝvena ǝn tǝvukur in da dal tsukur da Galili. Da nǝghǝn vin kur.’ Tsǝnam tsǝn, niya audzal kǝn kwarakur khai kwar.”
MAT 28:8 Ka ɗuwars itar ad vak ngitl kujaɗ kujaɗ, dǝ gǝdza zǝ khwaɗga char. Khwayala itar da kwarara kwara kǝ furakh sar.
MAT 28:9 Dzagwdlam ka tlatǝrghǝr Yasu kǝ nughwasakhen, ka niya tsitar, “Gabǝr ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ tsǝkur.” Ka zǝghvoghǝr itar da vak sar, khwtana itar ǝn tǝ sigakh sar, ka ɗabanǝf itar.
MAT 28:10 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Gǝdzam bi. Dam da kwarara kǝ zar babakhar dǝg itar da Galili, ǝn vin da nǝghaka itar.”
MAT 28:11 Madv nughwasakhen ǝn tǝghǝr dǝga tar, chalǝm kǝ li uf ngitlen dagh itar daks da dlǝmdla kǝs, ka tugwarkhai itar ak zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh ad ɗaga dǝgakhe a dzoghǝr.
MAT 28:12 Dzafkhai zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ malanakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ udakh ɗaya kavu itar lavakh ǝn tǝb tar kwarne, batǝra bǝg itar kwaɓ kǝ tlujiyakhna zikǝn.
MAT 28:13 Nǝv itar kǝ tlujiyakhen, “Dǝge da kwara kur, ‘Furakh sar kǝ sa kǝviɗ kǝ gǝlalgǝl, madv kǝnd ǝn khar.’
MAT 28:14 Da dagh lavana da tlim kǝ Gumn, da kwarara lava kǝnd kwarne na ghazur bi, wirva yan na dǝge da gǝma kuran bi.”
MAT 28:15 Ka chauga tlujiyakh ad kwaɓen, manga itar ndǝkve tsa kwara tǝrkhai yud. Ina kǝ lava sakhkana, dla Yahudakh ǝn kwarakha kavu kwar ǝn tǝb tar.
MAT 28:16 Ka dǝgala kǝ furakhan na kǝlatǝm kitakw da Galili, do itar da ghuɓe tsa kwara tǝrkhai Yasu.
MAT 28:17 Nǝgha tsitara, ka ɗabanǝf itar, ai yakhaye ǝn tǝb tar a khayanǝf ba itar kwarne patak in bi.
MAT 28:18 Ka sa Yasu khǝrzha ditar, ka ni, “Ɗaga nɗzǝɗe ǝn gharazhigǝl zen lard, a baka tsǝkud.
MAT 28:19 Wirva yan, dam da nandal udakh ǝn lard daghan kǝ nǝga kǝ furakhar. Paratǝra para kur ǝn ɗakha Dada, zǝ Zǝra, zǝ Sǝɗikw Yazhigǝl.
MAT 28:20 Ka tsagatǝrdu tsaga kur, kǝ tsǝnaru kǝ ɗaga dǝgakhai a kwarakur khai kǝ. Da dagha ka zǝ kur tsika fatsi, tangw da tǝ mbasa lard.”
MAR 1:1 Auna ɗule a farsud kwar lav zǝɗan ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ Yasu Kristu, Zǝr Yazhigǝl.
MAR 1:2 A farsud ndǝkve a vindzgud ǝn kaɗkaɗ Ishay tlayang kwarne, “Da ɓǝla ɓǝla ka dǝ zǝr ɓǝlar, sadaghin ǝn tǝvuk tsǝkh, dadake da ɗika ɗul wirvakh.”
MAR 1:3 “Udanen ǝn kwar lav dǝ ndzǝɗ ǝn tǝghal kwarne, ‘Ɗikamarna ɗul kǝ Dad Zikan, nandal kur ɗul sar ger.’ ”
MAR 1:4 Ka mǝdlawala Yukhan dadak para ud ǝn tǝghal, ǝn kwardu lav kwarne pǝla udakh ad ghǝr, paratǝralud, ɓisatǝrna Yazhigǝl tsugun ad khaipakh tar.
MAR 1:5 Daghan udakhe ǝn ǝntla khaya ya Yakhudi zǝ udakh ya Wurshalim a dalar da vak sar, ǝn kwarakh khaipakh tar itar. In tsuguna ka paratǝral ǝn zagh ya Urdu.
MAR 1:6 A talǝm Yukhan ad gabage a manava dǝ guj dlǝgwam, nguɗan sambal ǝn tǝ khukw tsin, dǝg zuwa sar tsuguna, tsǝvakwa zǝ yu mame ǝn tǝghal.
MAR 1:7 A kwara tǝrkhai ad lav Yazhigǝl kwarne, “Nǝg dadake da sǝgadagh ǝn tǝ tǝlg tsǝk, ai malke kǝ ndang. Ai kwal tǝkha tsǝka kǝ ɓukgan kǝ vǝda zaw kimbak sar bi.
MAR 1:8 A para kurar ka dǝ yu, in tsuguna da para kura dǝ Sǝɗikw Yazhigǝl.”
MAR 1:9 Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sarta ka tsiyif Yasu sǝgadagh ǝn kǝs Nazarat ai ǝn khaya Galili, ka parandal Yukhan ǝn zagh Urdu.
MAR 1:10 Madǝv Yasu ǝn sǝgawal da tǝghay gǝrdz, ka nǝghan ad gharazhigǝl a ngurǝf, ka sodagh Sǝɗikw da tǝghǝr tsin ndǝk takalamasar.
MAR 1:11 Ka tsǝnud kwind ǝn gharazhigǝl kwarne, “Kha Zǝrar, ǝn way kha waya kǝ. Ən tsǝn zǝɗa ka char.”
MAR 1:12 Ən tǝvin tǝvina, ka ɓala Sǝɗikw da tǝghal.
MAR 1:13 Ən tǝghalena khǝna kul ufaɗ kǝ Shatan uk ǝn kura kur. Ən giɗa zǝ dǝg tǝghalakh itar ǝn vin. Ka nǝgharu Zar ɓǝlakh Yazhigǝl ǝn vin.
MAR 1:14 Ən tǝkhal kǝ nguɗana Yukhan tsud ǝn gud sal, ka tsiyif Yasu, dal da Galili, ǝn kwardu lav Yazhigǝl ai zǝɗanyan.
MAR 1:15 Ən kwar kwarne “A sagh sart, tlǝksa Yazhigǝla a ghǝrzgan. Pǝlam pǝla ghǝr, tsuguna fadǝghǝro kuram ǝn tǝ lav zǝɗan nǝn.”
MAR 1:16 Madǝv Yasu ǝn dǝgal ǝn tǝ kalam zagh Galili, ka nǝghan ad Siman zǝ saghǝr sar Ndros, ǝn ɗi sik vay kilf itar da dǝlv, wirva li vay kilf itar.
MAR 1:17 Ka nǝv Yasu, “Ausǝgam, gatamaks gat, da nakura kǝ li da ɗakhado udakh ka da vak Yazhigǝl.
MAR 1:18 Ən dǝvǝn dǝva, ka ɗuwars itar sika vay kilf tar, ka gatars itar.
MAR 1:19 Daga tsin da tǝvuk khǝɗikǝn, ka nǝghan ad yakhaya kǝ zarbabakh mits tsugun, Yakub zǝ Yukhan zar Zabadi ǝn peryu. Ən ɗika sik vay kilf itar.
MAR 1:20 Ən dǝvǝn dǝva ka ɗakh tǝrkhai, ka ɗuwars itar ad dad tar Zabadi ǝn peryu, zǝ zar tlǝr sar, gatars itar.
MAR 1:21 Ka dagh Yasu zǝ furakh sar da Kafarnakhum. Sa kǝ fitsa ngiya ya Yakhudakh, dagh Yasu da gud dzakhava Yakhudakh. Ka farsa tsagatǝrdu tsag.
MAR 1:22 A ndawatǝrǝf tsagdu tsaga sar kǝ udakh, wirva a tsagatǝru ad lava ndǝk ude dǝ ndzǝɗ, ndǝk liye ǝn tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh bi.
MAR 1:23 A zulava bi, ka sasǝg kǝ udanen ai nguyanǝf sǝɗikw bǝzan da vak dzakhava Yakhudakh. Ka tlǝkha tsin kwarne,
MAR 1:24 “Uɗa ɗangwa tsǝkha dǝ kǝnda, Yasu ud ya Nazarati? A sa da khǝdz kǝnd khǝdza nagh kha? Tsakha tsǝka, kha Chuwaɗaɗan ai ɓǝlandagh Yazhigǝl.
MAR 1:25 Ka tavarghǝr Yasu ad di kǝ sǝɗikw bǝzan kwarne, “Tǝriɗ nǝkh, sawal sǝg ǝn vǝgh kǝ udan.”
MAR 1:26 Ka gǝɗikanǝf sǝɗikw bǝzan na dǝ yanen kǝ ud. Ka khula, sawal ǝn vǝgh tsin.
MAR 1:27 Daghan udakhe ǝn vin, a ndawatǝrǝf char. Ən ndiɗakava tsitar kwarne, “Uɗe neni? Wilwa tsagdu tsaga nagha? Udan na ǝn tsagdu tsaga dǝ ndzǝɗ. Zǝ batǝrghǝr bǝg tsin kǝ sǝɗikw bǝzanakh, kǝ tsǝnaru kǝ lav sar.
MAR 1:28 Ən dǝvǝn dǝva ka kwazga lavǝn tǝghǝr tsin, ǝn khaya Galili daghan.
MAR 1:29 Uk sawal sǝg tsitar ǝn gud dzakhava Yakhudakha, ka dagh Yasu zǝ Yakub zǝ Yukhan ger da fǝta zai Siman zǝ Ndros.
MAR 1:30 Bab nus Simana, ǝn khǝngan ǝn tuk magwǝlaɓ. Kujaɗ kujaɗa ka kwarar khai itar kǝ Yasu ad lav ǝn tǝghǝr tsin.
MAR 1:31 Ka dagh da vak sar, ka khutanan ǝn tǝ dǝv kǝ mǝlaru kǝ tsiya tsi. Tǝvin tǝvina, ka mbu ǝn tuk magwǝlaɓ, ka tatǝr khai ad dǝgway.
MAR 1:32 Kǝ khagw fitsa yanen, ɓǝldagh kǝ fatsi. Ka zaɓardǝghǝr udakh ad daghan liye kwal yang, zǝ liye ngwiyanǝf sǝɗikw bǝzan.
MAR 1:33 Ka dzafkhai udakhe ǝn khuɗ kǝs daghan ǝn tǝghay rang.
MAR 1:34 Ka mbakhatǝru Yasu kǝ udakh zikǝn, liye dǝ kuzakh sikh sikh sikh. Ka dzǝtǝrdal kǝ wurduwakh zikǝn. Ai a ɓǝlatǝrna ba dǝ kwal lava kǝ wurduwakhen bi. Wirva tsa tsitar khulfira kǝ ud Yasu.
MAR 1:35 Pǝrta kǝdla, ǝn sarta warkhamen, ka tsiyif Yasu, ɗuwars ad mǝgh, ka dala da vake kwal nǝg kǝ itsawar, ka ɗǝgau.
MAR 1:36 Simana, zǝ liye ǝn dǝga itar dagh, a dalar da gat Yasu.
MAR 1:37 Tlarghǝr tsitara, “Udakh daghana ǝn gatkha gata” Nǝv itar tsin.
MAR 1:38 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai Yasu, “Dziyamal da tlǝrna gǝdzar kǝsakhe khef, ki da kwardu lav Yazhigǝl tsǝkǝn vin. A sodagh kǝ wirva yan kǝ.
MAR 1:39 Ka gwayafkhai ǝn khuɗ kǝ Galili daghan, ǝn kwardu lav Yazhigǝl ǝn gud dzakhava Yakhudakh, zǝ dzatǝrdu wurduwakh ǝn vǝgh kǝ udakh.
MAR 1:40 Ka sasǝg kǝ ude dǝ kuza fǝch da vak Yasu, kǝlgan ad juguv kǝ takaɗa takaɗ, “Da khayanǝf khǝ, tǝkha kha kǝ ghuɓkay tsǝrdlak.”
MAR 1:41 Ka kwiɗ nǝv rǝv kǝ Yasu. Talala dǝ dǝv sara ka gǝman ad udanen. Ka ni, “A khayanǝf kǝ, ghuɓfǝkhay ghuɓa tsǝrdlak”
MAR 1:42 Ən dǝvǝn dǝva ka ghuɓfǝkhay tsǝrdlak ǝn tukw fǝchen.
MAR 1:43 Ka tǝkharna Yasu ad lava char, daksa niya tsin.
MAR 1:44 “Kwarara ba ak itsawar ad dǝge dzoghǝr bi. Dǝg dǝgal, mǝdlara mǝdla ghǝragh kǝ zil kǝs. Ka bǝdu kha dǝg tsufe kwarga ndzikha ndzikh Mus, wirva ghuɓe a ghuɓkhayud. Ki tsatsǝg kǝ itsawar kwarne a ghuɓkhayud.
MAR 1:45 Ai udanen tsuguna, uk dǝgal ǝn kwardu kwara tsin ad dǝge a manar khai Yasu. A ɓǝghana ba dǝ itsauɗa bi. Wirva yana, ka aghba Yasu tǝkha kǝ dagh da khuɗ kǝs ǝn di kǝ ud bi. Khalak yana ka giɗkavǝn vakakhe kwal nǝg kǝ ud. Dakhkana ka dla udakh ǝn saghgawala da vak sar itsa dǝvar.
MAR 2:1 Khal kǝ khǝna khǝɗikǝna, ka gwidǝn dagh Yasu da Kafarnakhum. Ka tsǝna udakh kwarne a sagh da mǝgh.
MAR 2:2 Ka dzafkhai udakh dingǝrik, kwal dla kǝ vake a tǝmgan, itsǝn tǝ ghay rang. Ka kwaratǝra lav Yazhigǝl tsin.
MAR 2:3 Ka ɓardǝghǝr chalǝm udakh ufaɗ, ad dadak mǝtsa tlepel vǝgh.
MAR 2:4 Fatsiye piyatǝrwal daks din da vak Yasu, wirva dzakhava udakh. Ka pǝsdu itar ghǝr gud kalkal dǝ vake din Yasu. Pǝsdu tsitara, ka taldagh itar ad dadak mǝtsa tlepel vǝghen ǝn khǝngan ǝn tǝ khindz, da tǝvuk Yasu.
MAR 2:5 Nǝgha kǝ Yasu ad fadǝghǝrofǝga tar, ka niya kǝ dadak mǝtsa tlepel vǝghen, “Zǝrara, a ɓisakhanud khaipakhagh.”
MAR 2:6 Nǝg li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus ǝn ndzǝgan ǝn tǝvin, ǝn ɗayakava ghǝr itar ǝn revakhuɗ tar.
MAR 2:7 “Uɗa lava kǝ udan nǝn kwar yan kǝ lava ndǝkyani? Ən nena Yazhigǝl. Warek tǝkha kǝ ɓisana khaipakh da na Yazhigǝl kitakul biyi?”
MAR 2:8 Tǝvin tǝvina tsa kǝ Yasu ad dǝge ǝn ɗaya itar ǝn rǝvakhuɗ tar. Ka niya tsitar, “Uɗa lava tsukur ǝn ɗayakava ina kǝ dǝgitakh ǝn rǝvakhuɗuri?
MAR 2:9 Ira kujaɗan kǝ manara? ‘Kǝ kwar kwarne, a ɓisakhanud khaipakhaghe,’ Awana, ‘Tsiyif tsiya, ɓa dǝ khindzagha kwa dǝga khi?’
MAR 2:10 Ai ǝn na ka tsatsǝg tsukur kwarne, Zǝr Uda nǝg dǝ ndzǝɗa ɓisara khaipakh kǝ udakh ǝn lardǝn.” Ka niya kǝ dadak mǝtsa tlepel vǝghen,
MAR 2:11 “A kwarakhai kǝ, tsiyif tsi, ɓa dǝ khindzagh dǝg daks da mǝgh.”
MAR 2:12 Ka tsiyif, ɓǝf ad khindza sar ka dǝgal, ɗaga udakh tsuguna ǝn vazavaz. Ina kǝ dǝgita a ndawatǝrǝf kǝ udakh daghan, ka mbaɗ Yazhigǝl itar, ǝn kwar kwarne, “A tapa bakǝnda nǝgha dǝgit ndǝk ina bi.”
MAR 2:13 Ka gwidǝn Yasu dǝgal da tukw ghay dǝlv. Ən sakha saks udakh zikǝn da vak sar, in tsuguna ǝn tsagatǝrdu tsag.
MAR 2:14 Madǝvin ǝn dǝg, ka nǝgha nǝgha tsin ad Lawi zǝr Half ǝn ndzǝgan ǝn gud chaw khadam. Nǝv Yasu tsin, “Tsiyif tsiya, gataks gat.” Ka tsiyif Lawiya, gatars.
MAR 2:15 Madǝv Yasu zǝ furakh sar ǝn zu kaf ǝn fǝta Lawi. Nǝg chalǝm udakhe ghǝr tar tsuguna li man khaip ndǝk li chaw khadam, ǝn zu kaf itar dagh. Wirvǝn gatars gata khutsa khutsa udakh.
MAR 2:16 Nǝgha kǝ yakhaya kǝ Farisakh li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus, ad Yasu ǝn zu kaf zǝ li khaipakh, zǝ li chaw khadam liye ghǝrtara li khaip. Ka ndiɗarwal itar kǝ furakh sar kwarne, “Uɗa lava tsin ǝn zu kaf zǝ li chaw khadam zǝ liye ghǝrtara li khaipi?”
MAR 2:17 Tsǝna tsin ad yan, ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Liye yanga bǝn gat dadak ngura bi, akwa liye kwal yang. A so da ɗagh li kanadi baka bi, ai li khaipakh.”
MAR 2:18 Furakh Yukhan zǝ dǝg Farisakh ǝn zǝɓ ndǝl itar. Ka sa chalǝm udakha, ka ndiɗarwal itar kǝ Yasu, “A sa ndar furakh Yukhan zǝ dǝg Farisakh ǝn zǝɓ ndǝl itara, ai furakhagha naba itar biyi?”
MAR 2:19 Ka nggauga Yasu kwarne, “Da mana ndar tsaghwakh zil ghaul ad ndǝl, dla itar dagha zǝ zil ghauli? Ən manawa bi. Fatsiye dla zil ghaul dagha zitar, na itar da zǝɓ ndǝl bi.
MAR 2:20 Da saks sarte da ɓatǝrvalud zil ghaul ǝn vak tar, ǝn tǝ yanen kǝ sart da zǝɓa itar ndǝl.
MAR 2:21 “Na ude ǝn ndzǝgharu wilwa kachakach kǝ mughura gabag bi. Da mangud ndǝkyan, ka da mǝɗukwa wilwan sǝgawal ǝn tǝ mughuran, ka da kukhwa mal kǝ ai tsa chak.
MAR 2:22 Tsuguna na ude ǝn ɗi wilwa yu inabi da mughuran kǝ mbǝl vighakh bi. Da mangud ndǝkyana, ka da chǝɓ chǝɓa yu inabi ad mughur mbǝl vighakhen, yu inabi zǝ mbǝl vighakhena, bǝrdagha tara da bǝghud ǝmb. Ən manawa bi, khekwa wilwa yu inabi ǝn ɗiyud ǝn wilwa mbǝl vighakh.”
MAR 2:23 Fitsa tlǝrn kǝ kasukw nggi, madǝv Yasu zǝ furakh sar ǝn dǝgal diwa gukh lǝkam. Madǝv itar ǝn dǝgal, ka farsa furakh sar ad kwakhu ghǝr lǝkam.
MAR 2:24 Nǝgha kǝ Farisakh ndǝk yan, ka ndiɗarwar itar kwarne, “Uɗa lava tsitar ǝn man dǝge kwal kalkal fitsa nggiyi?”
MAR 2:25 Ka nggawa tǝrkhai kwarne, “A tugwa bakh kur dǝge a manga Doda? Ndzikǝnǝf kǝ way zǝ liye ǝn dǝga itar dagh, tsuguna ǝn nagha itar digita?
MAR 2:26 Ən kwarga Abiyat zikan na kǝ zil kǝs. Dagh Dod da fǝta Yazhigǝl, ka zu ad brudiye a bandalud, ai kalkal ba zuwa zuwa kǝ itsawar bi. Uk zil kǝsakh kalti ǝn zuwan. Ka baran kǝ tsaghwakh sar kǝ zuwa zuwa tsitar.
MAR 2:27 Ka niya tsitar, a barkhai kǝ udud ad fitsa nggi, a vǝrɗava ba ud wirva kǝ fitsa nggiya bi.
MAR 2:28 Wirva yan, Zǝr Ud, in Dad Zikan, in Dad Zikan fitsa nggiya tsugun.
MAR 3:1 Fitsa tlǝrn tsuguna, a da Yasu da gud dzakhava Yakhudakh. Ka nǝg udanen dadak mǝtsa dǝv ǝn vinen.
MAR 3:2 Ən tǝb kǝ udakhe ǝn vin, nǝg liye ǝn gat ɗule da vide tar Yasu dǝ ghaz. Ka vaza vaza tsitar ɗem, tsaghe da mbambǝgin ad udanen fitsa nggi.
MAR 3:3 Nǝv Yasu kǝ dadak mǝtsa dǝven, “Tsiyif tsi, ausǝg, ghitsga ghits ǝn van.”
MAR 3:4 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal Yasu kwarne, “Ira dǝge khwara kǝ mana mana fitsa nggiyi? Man dǝg khwarane, awana dǝg bǝzan khi? Kat safa fitsa nggiye, awana kǝɗga dǝ kǝɗa khi?
MAR 3:5 Ka vazakh tǝrkhai dǝ bazarǝv, wirva ɓengɓeng rǝve din itar. Ka niya kǝ udanǝn, “Taladal dǝvagh.” Ka taladal, tǝvin tǝvina ka mbu dǝv sar ndiɗ.
MAR 3:6 Nǝgha kǝ Farisakh ndǝkyan, ka dǝgal tsitar da ɗembar lava zǝ liye tlǝkhara lǝg kǝ Khiridus, ad ɗule da kǝɗ da itar Yasu.
MAR 3:7 Ka sawal Yasu zǝ furakh sar ǝn tǝb kǝ udakh, dǝgal da tǝ ghay dǝlv, zikǝn udakhe ǝn khaya Galili a gatars.
MAR 3:8 Tsǝna kǝ udakh ad lav ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dǝgakhe ǝn manin daghan. Zikǝn udakhe ǝn ǝntla khaya ya Yakhudi, Wursalim, zǝ ǝntla khaya ya Edom, zǝ li khǝdzǝva gadzak zagh Urdu, zǝ udakh ya Taya zǝ Sidon, a sawal da vak sar.
MAR 3:9 Wirva zika udakha, ka kwarar khai Yasu kǝ furakh sar, kǝ ɗikarna khǝɗikan na kǝ peryu, ki khek tlǝgars kǝ udakh.
MAR 3:10 Wirva a mbakhatǝru kǝ udakh zikǝn. In kǝ mangan kǝ liye tukw kuzakh ǝn tlagǝva daks da gǝmagǝm.
MAR 3:11 Itsǝn nǝghǝn vara sǝɗikw bǝzan ad Yasu, ka mbaɗa itar ǝn tǝvuk sar, zǝ tuwa tsitar kwarne, “Kha Zǝr Yazhigǝl.”
MAR 3:12 Ka tǝkhatǝrnan chara, kwarara bai tar kǝ udakh ad lavǝn tǝghǝr tsin bi.
MAR 3:13 A do Yasu da tǝ kalam ghuɓ, ka ɗakh tǝrkhai kǝ liye ǝn naghin, ka sagh itar da vak sar.
MAR 3:14 A dzǝrgan ad ud kǝlatǝm mits, ki nǝga kǝ dzǝran na kǝ furakh sar. Kǝ giɗa tsitar dagh, kǝ ɓalatra ɓal dǝgal da kwardu lav Yazhigǝl.
MAR 3:15 Mbǝladu itar ndzǝɗa dzado wurduwakh.
MAR 3:16 Yakhana udakh kǝlatǝm mitse a dzǝrgin. Siman (ai barvin ɗakh Bitrus).
MAR 3:17 Yakub zǝr Zabadi zǝ saghǝr sar Yukhan (ai batǝrvin ɗakh Buwarnajis, in kwarne “Zar ya fit”).
