MAR 3:18 Chalǝmakh tsuguna itar, Ndros, Filibus, Bartalamaus, Mat, Tom, Yakub zǝr Half, Taddiyus, Siman ude nagh ba gwiya kǝ khaya sar da tǝlg bi.
MAR 3:19 Zǝ Yakhuz Iskariyoti, dadake a bǝdu Yasu.
MAR 3:20 Ən tǝkhal kǝ yana, ka dagh Yasu da tlǝrna mǝgh. Ka sa dzakhava udakh zikǝn da vak sar. Wirva yan, in zǝ furakh sar, a mbǝlatǝru ba ɗul zu kaf bi.
MAR 3:21 Tsǝna kǝ yakhtar ad in, ka dǝgal tsitar da ɓadoɓ. Da itar ǝn kurana, ba kǝɗǝf ghǝr tsin.
MAR 3:22 Yakhaya kǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus liye sodagh ǝn Wurshalim, ǝn kwar kwarne, “Ba’alzabul shik ya wurduwakh ǝn man tlǝks din. In tsugun kǝ bara ndzǝɗa lakwdu wurduwakh ǝn vǝgh kǝ udakh.”
MAR 3:23 Ka ɗakh tǝrkhai Yasu da vak sar, ka farsa kwaratǝra lava tsin dǝ jakǝva lavakh. “Da lakwa ndar Shatan ad Shatani?
MAR 3:24 Da tǝkaghǝra tlǝks mits. Tǝkhakh yan kǝ tlǝks kǝ ghitsgana?
MAR 3:25 Da tǝkaghǝra udakhe ǝn mǝgh mits. Da tǝkha yan kǝ mǝgh kǝ ghitsgan?
MAR 3:26 Da ka ǝn man tlughuma Shatan dǝ ghǝr sar, a tǝkana ba dǝ ghǝra sar kina biya? Da tǝkha kǝ ghitsgan dǝ ndzǝɗa? A sagh ba mbasa sar kina biya?
MAR 3:27 Nǝg ude tǝkha kǝ dagh da fǝta ude dǝ ndzǝɗa kǝ khuts kadlang sara? Khekwa ndzaɗana bakhin ndan kǝda khuts katlang sar tsin ǝn fǝta sara?
MAR 3:28 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, tǝkhud kǝ ɓisatǝrna daghan khaipakh tar kǝ udakh, zǝ ɗaga tsafa tsafe a manarkhai itar kǝ Yazhigǝl.
MAR 3:29 Ai daka tsafanǝfin ad Sǝɗikw Yazhigǝl, na bud da ɓisara ɓisa kǝ ngǝɗa bi.”
MAR 3:30 Dǝge kǝ ba da kwar yana, wirva a kwarga itar kwarne, “Nǝg dǝ sǝɗikw bǝzan ǝn vǝgh sar.”
MAR 3:31 Ka sagh zarbabakh Yasu zǝ bab sar da vak Yasu. Ghitsge tar ǝn mel, ka ɓǝlanǝf itar ad ud daks da ɗakhatra Yasu.
MAR 3:32 Nǝg dzakhava udakh a tsarghǝran, ka kwararkhai itar kwarne, “Babagha zǝ zarbabakhagh ǝn mel itar, ǝn na nǝgha kha nǝgha itar.”
MAR 3:33 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal Yasu kwarne, “War babara zǝ zarbabakhari?
MAR 3:34 Ka vazatǝrvala kǝ liye ǝn ndzǝgan, liye tsarghǝran, ka ni, “Auna babara zǝ zarbabakhar.
MAR 3:35 Ɗaga ude ǝn man dǝge ǝn nagha Yazhigǝl, in zǝrbabara, dughwbabara, zǝ babar.”
MAR 4:1 Fitsa tlǝrna, ka dala Yasu da tǝghay dǝlv, ka gwidǝn farsa tsagatǝrdu tsaga tsin kǝ udakh. Dzakhava udakhe a tsarghǝrana zikǝn itar char. Wirva yana, ba da tsin da peryuwa ndzǝgan ǝmb. Dzakhava udakh daghan tsuguna ǝn ghitsǝn tǝghay gǝrdz.
MAR 4:2 A tsagatǝrdu ad dǝgitakh zikǝn dǝ jakva lavakh. Ka niya tsitar,
MAR 4:3 “Bambǝg tlim, tsǝnam tsǝn, dadak wusa a dala da tukhǝn gukh sar.
MAR 4:4 Madǝvin ǝn kwazdu khulfa, yakhaya ɓalal da tǝ ɗul, ka sa ɗikakha vaɗu itar.
MAR 4:5 Yakhaya tsuguna ɓalala da tǝ vake dǝ jajǝrkh, vake kwal dǝ khay char. Ka fǝtsawal itar kujaɗ kujaɗ, wirva vakena na khay chara bi.
MAR 4:6 Tǝvga kǝ fatsiya, ka ɓayandal ad khiyakhen, ka ghulala itar. Wirva tlǝla tara, a dagh ba da khay chara bi.
MAR 4:7 Yakhaya kǝ khulf tsuguna, ɓaldagh itar da tak. Ka ɗakala takena, ɓidzatǝrǝf. Ka yiga ba itar zǝr bi.
MAR 4:8 Yakhaya kǝ khulf tsuguna, ɓalala itar da tǝ dǝlɓ. Fǝtsawala tsitara, ka ɗakala itar, yiga itar zǝr ndǝkchiɓ. Yakhaya yige tar zǝr kulkhǝkǝrɗ kulkhǝkǝrɗ. Yakhaya tsuguna kulunkwakh kulunkwakh. Yakhaya tsuguna dǝrmǝk dǝrmǝk.”
MAR 4:9 A mbasana Yasu ad kwar lav sar dǝ kwarne, “Ɗaga ude dǝ tlǝm tsǝn lava, tsǝnin.”
MAR 4:10 Madǝv Yasu ǝn ndzǝgan tukuɗa tukuɗa, furakh sar na kǝlatǝm mits, zǝ liye a tsarghǝran, ka ndiɗarwal itar ad dǝge ǝn tuku jakva lavakhen.
MAR 4:11 Ka niya tsitar, “Kura a khayakurnǝfud ad tsa ɓǝghan na kǝ dǝge tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝksa Yazhigǝl. Ak yakhaye kwal nǝg ǝn kura, itsauɗa ǝn kwaratǝrǝn jakva lavud.
MAR 4:12 Ki zǝɗa, “ ‘Ən vaza vaza itara, ǝn nǝgha ba itar bi, zǝn tsǝna tsǝna itara, ǝn diyarsǝf bai tar bi Ki khek katlga tsitar, pǝlga itar ghǝr, ɓisatǝrna Yazhigǝl ad khaipakh tar.’ ”
MAR 4:13 Tsuguna ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Ai da katlga ba kur ad dǝge ǝn tuku inana kǝ jakva lava bi, ai da katla ndar kur ad dǝge ǝn tuku tlǝrna jakva lavakhi?
MAR 4:14 Auna dǝge ǝn tuku jakva lavan. Khulfe a kwazdu dadak tukha, in lav Yazhigǝl.
MAR 4:15 Khulfakhe a ɓalal da tǝ ɗul, ǝn mǝdla jakva udakhe a tsǝna lav Yazhigǝl. Ba itar ǝn tsǝna lavana, ǝn dǝvǝn dǝva, ka sagh Shatana khutsala dǝ lave ǝn rǝvakhuɗ tar.
MAR 4:16 Khulfe a ɓalala da tǝ jajǝrkh, ǝn mǝdla jakva udakhe a tsǝna lav Yazhigǝl, ka chauge tar kujaɗ kujaɗ, dǝ khwaɗǝg tsugun.
MAR 4:17 Fatsiya a tsǝga ba itar ad tlǝl bi, uk da zulu da tǝ sart khǝɗikǝn itar. Da ka sagh dlaɗa awana mbakhǝl, kǝ wirva fadǝghǝro dǝ lav Yazhigǝl, ka gwiyal itar da tǝlg kujaɗ kujaɗ.
MAR 4:18 Khulfe a ɓaldagh da tak, ǝn mǝdla jakva udakhe a tsǝna lav Yazhigǝl.
MAR 4:19 Ai wirva puta giɗǝn larda, zǝ valdu ghǝr gat tluwandala, zǝ nagh dǝgakh lard sikh sikh sikh, ka ɓidzanǝf ad laven. Ka na dǝge ǝn tukuwin bi.
MAR 4:20 Khulfe ɓalal ǝn tǝ vak duɓan, ǝn mǝdla jakva udakhe a tsǝna lav Yazhigǝl, chauge tar, mangga itar tlǝr din. Ka yige tar zǝr, kulkhǝkǝrɗ kulkhǝkǝrɗ. Yakhaya, kulunkwakh kulunkwakh. Yakhaya tsuguna, dǝrmǝk dǝrmǝk, ak khulfe a kwazduwud.
MAR 4:21 Ka zuvuk Yasu dǝ kwarne, “Ən vǝdza kara kazaz khud ka barsud ǝn kus kǝ gagaya? Awana ǝn kus kǝ pin khǝngana? Nabakhud ǝn bǝga bǝg ǝn vak bǝgan sara?
MAR 4:22 Dǝge ɓǝghanud, da ɓadala ɓud da tǝ ɓal. Dǝge kwargud bǝghanyan, da ɓado ɓud da tǝ ɓal.
MAR 4:23 Ude dǝ tlim tsǝn lava, tsǝnin.”
MAR 4:24 Ka kwara tǝrkhai tsugun kwarne, “Bamaru tlim kǝ dǝge ǝn tsǝna kur. Darame ǝn kuradakha dǝgit kǝ udakh din, din da kura kha dud. Da gwidǝn kurakha dinud mal kǝ yan.
MAR 4:25 Ude dina, da banargher bugud zikǝn. Ude kwal dina, ngwaɗa khǝɗike dinin, da chawarval chawud.”
MAR 4:26 Ka nǝv Yasu tsugun, “Nggwaɗe na tlǝksa gharazhigǝl. Nggwaɗa ude a kwazdu khulf ǝn gukh.
MAR 4:27 Khana zǝ tǝkhul, ǝn fǝtsa khulfena ka ɗak. In tsuguna ǝn tsa ba dǝ ɗule ǝn fǝtsda khulfen zǝ ɗaka bi.
MAR 4:28 Khayen dǝ ghǝr sar ǝn bǝgan ad khulfen da fǝtsa, zǝ ɗaka, sǝkhadal ad ghǝr, ka yigan ad zǝr.
MAR 4:29 Ba dǝgwayen ǝn tǝkhala tǝkh, ka da zǝɓ gidz kǝ da tsǝga tsǝg, wirva a tlala sarta tsǝg khi.”
MAR 4:30 Ka nǝv Yasu tsugun, “Uɗa da kwara kiyami? Da kura dǝ uɗa kiyam ad tlǝksa Yazhigǝli? Awana, ira kǝ jakva lave da kurada kiyam mana sari?
MAR 4:31 Nggwaɗa khulf mastad, ai khǝɗikan ǝn daghan khulfakhe ǝn tukhud ǝn lard.
MAR 4:32 Dǝmbiyanen, da tukhgud, ǝn ɗaka mal kǝ dǝgakhe ǝn wusud ǝn nggaɓ. Ən bakh gwal char, ai da tǝkha ɗikakh kǝ ndzǝgan ǝn kus kǝ sǝɗikw sar.
MAR 4:33 Dǝ khulf ina kǝ jakva lavakh zikǝn, a kwara tǝrkhai Yasu ad lava Yazhigǝl kǝ udakh. Kalkal ɗule da katlda itar.
MAR 4:34 Na dǝge a kwara tǝrkhayin kwal dǝ jakva lava bi. Ən sarte da tukuɗa tukuɗa itar zǝ furakh sar, ǝn kwaratra kwara dǝge ǝn tuku laven.
MAR 4:35 Ɓǝlga kǝ khagw fitsa yanen, ka nǝv Yasu kǝ furakh sar, “Dziyamal da tǝ yan kǝ ghǝdzǝva gadzak.”
MAR 4:36 Ɗuwars itar ad dzakhava udakh, ka dagh furakh sar da peryuwe ǝn ndzǝgan Yasu ǝmb. Nǝg tlǝrna peryuwakh tsugun zitar.
MAR 4:37 Ka soghǝr zikan kǝ fuɗ char ǝn yuwen, ǝn tlǝga tlǝga ghǝɗkuta yuwa ad peryuwen. Ən daks yu da peryu, tǝmga khǝɗikǝn kǝ righa righ.
MAR 4:38 Ən khǝnkhar Yasu ǝn tǝlg kǝ peryu, ka bo ad ghǝr sar ǝn tǝ dǝg ɓǝl ghǝre kurɓǝt. Ka tsiyanǝf furakh sar, ka ndiɗarwal itar kwarne, “Malǝma, na ɗangwa tsǝkha itsa ndǝkiyamu yuwa, ǝmtsǝga kiyam biya?
MAR 4:39 Ka tsiyif ǝn khar, tavarghǝr ad di kǝ fuɗen. Ka niya kǝ ghǝɗkuta yu, “Ghitsga ghits.” Ka ghitsga fuɗen. Ka ɗiw nǝv vaken.
MAR 4:40 Ka niya kǝ furakh sar, “Uɗa lava tsukur a gǝdzǝf ndǝkyani? Sakhkana na kur dǝ fadǝghǝrofǝg biya?”
MAR 4:41 Ka gǝdzǝf itar char. Ka ndiɗakava tsitar kwarne, “Khulf ira kǝ ud ineni? Zǝva, fuɗa zǝ ghǝɗkutayuwa ǝn tsǝnaru tsǝn kǝ lav sari?”
MAR 5:1 13 A dala Yasu zǝ furakh sar, da tǝ ghǝdzǝva gadzak dǝlva khaya Garasinakh.
MAR 5:2 Uk sawala sǝg kǝ Yasu ǝn peryuwa, ka sawala udanen ai ngwiyanǝf sǝɗikw bǝzan ǝn giɗe nggitl, kǝ gama zin.
MAR 5:3 Yanen kǝ uda ǝn giɗǝn giɗe nggitl, na ude dla tǝkha kǝ nggwaɗanan, tsa dǝ tsǝrvayu bi.
MAR 5:4 Wirva tsǝn nggwaɗa nggwaɗud ǝn tǝ sigakh sar, zǝ dǝvakh sar dǝ tsǝrvayu. Ən nggadla nggadla dǝ tsǝrvayu. Zǝ kǝla dǝg tuse ǝn tǝ kwinda siga sar. Na dadak ndzǝɗe tǝkha kǝ payana bi.
MAR 5:5 Viɗa zǝ fatsi tsin ǝn giɗǝn nggitl, zǝn tǝ ghuɓ. Ən khula, zǝ khara vǝgha sar tsin dǝ kurakh.
MAR 5:6 Nǝgha tsin Yasu kǝ bit, ka tsiyif dǝ khway, kǝlgan ad juguv ǝn tǝvuk sar.
MAR 5:7 Ka khula tsin char, ni, ‘Yasu, Zǝr Yazhigǝl Ndanggan, uɗa ɗangwa tsǝkha dǝ ki? A takaɗkhai ka dǝ ɗakha Yazhigǝl, baka ba dǝ dlaɗ bi.’
MAR 5:8 A kwargan ndǝkyan, wirva audzala Yasu ǝn kwarar khai kwara kwarne, “Kha sǝɗikw bǝzan, ausǝg sǝgawal ǝn udan.”
MAR 5:9 Ka ndiɗarwal Yasu kwarne, “War ɗakhaghi?” Ka nggawar khai kwarne, “Ɗakhara Ghamag, wirva zikǝn kǝnd.” ...
MAR 5:10 Ka gwidǝn tǝkhaval kǝ takaɗ Yasu tsin char, khek lakwtǝrdu tsin sǝgawal ǝn ǝntla khayen.
MAR 5:11 Nǝg giɗa daguwakh ǝn zighw ǝn tǝ kalam ghuɓ.
MAR 5:12 A takaɗga wurduwakh ad Yasu, kwarne, “Khaya kǝndanǝf khaya, daks da daguwakhin.”
MAR 5:13 Ka khayatǝrnǝf, ka sawal sǝɗikw bǝzanakhen, ka dagh itar da daguwakh. Giɗa daguwakhena a ɓa itar dǝb mits. Ka ɗaɗardagh itar dǝgdagh diwa tsǝɓan na kǝ ghay gǝrdz, ka ɓaldagh itar da yuwa, ruga itar.
MAR 5:14 Ka khwaya li zighw daguwakhen daks da khuɗ kǝsa, zǝ gǝdzar kǝsakh, kwarar khai itar kǝ udakh ad dǝge dzoghǝr. Ka sawala udakhen, dala itar da vaz dǝge dzoghǝr.
MAR 5:15 Sa tsitar da vak Yasu, ka nǝgha itar ad dadake tsa ghamag sǝɗikw bǝzanakh ǝmb, ǝn ndzǝgan. Dǝ gabag ǝn tǝvǝgha sar, zǝn mǝkǝn sar khwaranyan. Ka gǝdzǝf udakhen.
MAR 5:16 Liye tsa nǝghan dǝ diyakh tar ad dǝge a dzoghǝr, uk kwara khatra kwara tsitar kǝ udakh, ad dǝge a dzoghǝr dǝ dadake tsa ghamag sǝɗikw bǝzanakh ǝn vǝgh sar, zǝ daguwakhen.
MAR 5:17 Ka farsa udakhen ad takaɗ Yasu, kǝ ɗuwatǝrda khay tar tsin.
MAR 5:18 Madǝv Yasu ǝn daks da peryuwen, ka takaɗga ude tsa ghamag sǝɗikw bǝzan ǝn vǝgh sar ad Yasu, kǝ khayarnǝf dǝgal tsin dagh.
MAR 5:19 Ai ka khayarnǝf ba Yasu bi. Ən dleva yan, ka niya tsin, “Dǝg daks da mǝgh, da vak yakhur, kwara tǝrkhai kwara ad zik zikan na kǝ dǝgakhe a mana khai Dad Zikan, zǝ kwiɗkwiɗǝrve mana khayin.”
MAR 5:20 Wirva yan, ka tǝkaval sar, ka gwayava tsin ǝn Dikapolis, kǝsakh kǝlɗǝk, ǝn kwarakhdu dǝge a manar khai Yasu. A ndawatǝrǝf, kǝ daghan liye a tsǝnan.
MAR 5:21 Gwiyoghǝr kǝ Yasu saks da tǝ ghǝdzva gadzak dǝlve tsa dinin, ǝn peryu. Ka tsarghǝra dzakhava udakh zikǝn. Madǝvin tlaɓ ǝn tǝ kalam ghǝdzva gadzaka,
MAR 5:22 ka nǝg udanen kitakul ǝn tǝb kǝ zikan ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ gud dzakhava Yakhudakh, ɗakhasara Yayirus ka sa. Nǝgha tsin Yasu, ka sagha kǝlgan ad juguv ǝn tǝvuk sar.
MAR 5:23 A takaɗgan char, ‘‘Khǝɗikan na kǝ dughwara ǝn yanga bi, da mǝts. Tatl ausǝg da bo dǝvagh ǝn tǝf, kǝ mbandu mbǝg tsǝkh, khek ǝmtsǝga tsin.”
MAR 5:24 Ka dala zǝ Yasu. Ka gatatǝrs dzakhava udakh zikǝn, ka ɓidzanǝf itar. ...
MAR 5:25 Ka nǝg nusen ǝn vin, ai a zulavan ǝn kǝl vizh vǝg kǝlatǝm mits.
MAR 5:26 A khǝɓu a dlaɗ char ǝn vak gat nggur, ǝn vak li bǝdu nggur. Kǝɗgan ad khalavuwa dǝge dinin. Dǝmbiyanena, a mbu bi. Ən mbǝra dǝ mbǝra kuzen.
MAR 5:27 Ka tsǝna nusen ad lavǝn tǝghǝr kǝ Yasu, ka sasǝg tsin shuwakh ǝn tǝb kǝ udakh diwa lǝg Yasu. Ka gǝman ad gabag Yasu.
MAR 5:28 Wirva a ɗayandagh ǝn rǝvakhuɗ sar kwarne, “Da gǝma ka itsa gabag sara, da mbǝga kǝ.”
MAR 5:29 Tǝvin tǝvina ghitsga kǝl vizh sar. A tsǝnan ǝn vǝgh sar kwarne a mbu.
MAR 5:30 Tǝvin tǝvina ka tsǝna Yasu ad sǝgawala kǝ ndzǝɗ ǝn vǝgh sar, a manggan ad tlǝr. Gwiyafkhaya ka ndiɗatǝrwal kǝ dzakhava udakhen kwarne, “War kǝ gǝma gabagari?”
MAR 5:31 Ka nǝv furakh sar, “Ən nǝgha nǝgha kha dzakhava udakh ǝn tlagva kǝ ɓidza kha ɓidza ndikina, ka ndiɗ kwarne war kǝ gǝmakan nikha?”
MAR 5:32 Ka ɓalakh di kǝ Yasu, kǝ vaz ude kǝ gǝman.
MAR 5:33 Fatsiye a audzal nus na tsa dǝge a dzoghǝr dina, ka saks tsin da kǝl juguv ǝn tǝvuk Yasu. Ən tǝga vǝgh sar dǝ gǝdz, ka kwar khai ad khalavuwa jir.
MAR 5:34 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Dughwara, fadǝghǝrofǝga kǝ mbakhu. Dǝg daks dǝ lapi, a mbu khǝn tukw kuzagh.”
MAR 5:35 Madǝv Yasu dlǝn kwar lava, ka sagh yakhaya kǝ udakh ǝn fǝta Yayirus, mal ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ gud dzakhava Yakhudakh. Nǝv itar tsin, “A mǝtsga dughwagh, uɗa dla dǝg njǝgharu njǝgha tsǝkha kǝ malǝmi?
MAR 5:36 A baru ba Yasu ad tlim kǝ lave a kwarga itar bi. Ka niya kǝ Yayirus, “Gǝdz biya, fadǝghǝrofǝg bakh.”
MAR 5:37 A khayanǝf ba Yasu ad gatars gata kǝ itsawar bi, uk Bitrus, zǝ Yakub zǝ zǝrbab sar Yukhan.
MAR 5:38 Tsugwa tsitar ǝn fǝta mal ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ gud dzakhava Yakhudakh, ka nǝgha nǝgha kǝ Yasu ad yakhaya kǝ udakh ǝn tuwa, yakhaya tsuguna ǝn khul.
MAR 5:39 Dagh da vak tar, ka ndiɗatǝrwal kwarne, “Uɗa lava tsukur ǝn tuwa zǝ khula ndikini? A mǝtsga ba dughw na ndan bi, ǝn khǝnkhar.”
MAR 5:40 Ka ghuɓasa ghuɓasa tsitar dǝ nen. Ka lakwtǝral kǝ udakh daghan dǝgal da mel. Ka daks tsin zǝ dad dughwen, zǝ bab sar zǝ furakh sar na khǝkǝrɗ, da vake din dughwen. ...
MAR 5:41 Khutana tsin dǝva dughwen, ka niya tsin, “Talita kumi.” In kwarne, “Zǝr dughwa, ǝn kwara kha kwara ka, tsiyif tsi.”
MAR 5:42 Tǝvin tǝvin ka tsiyif zǝr dughwen, ka farsa dǝga tsin ǝn tǝb tar. Dughwena, khi kǝlatǝm mits tsin. Ina kǝ digita a nala kǝ dǝg ndawak tsitar.
MAR 5:43 A ndǝɗatǝrna Yasu ad tlim chara, kwarne, tsǝna ba itsawar ad lavǝna bi. Ka gwidǝn kwara tǝrkhai kwarne, bara bǝg itar dǝg zuwa kǝ dughwen.
MAR 6:1 A ɗuda Yasu ad yanen kǝ vaka, a gwiya da kǝs sar. Dala furakh sar zin.
MAR 6:2 Sa kǝ fitsa nggi, ka farsan ad tsagdutsag ǝn gud dzakhava Yakhudakh. Ɗaga liye a tsǝnan ad tsagdutsaga sar, a ndawatǝrǝf. Ka ndiɗa tsitar, “A mbǝladu ǝn ma udan na ad dǝgakhani? Khulf ira kǝ kwelemlem a barud ndikini? Vaza dǝ khulf dǝg dawakakhe ǝn manin. ...
MAR 6:3 Dadak tsakh mǝgh na ba ina biya? Maryam bakh Bab sara? Saghǝrakh sar bakh Yakub, zǝ Yukhan, zǝ Yakhuda, zǝ Simana? Saghǝrakh sar bakh dǝghawakhan ǝn giɗǝn vakmara? Ka chauga ba itar bi.
MAR 6:4 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Na tlayangge kwal dǝ ndanga bi, uk ǝn kǝs sar, zǝn tǝb kǝ jib sar, zǝ li fǝta sar.”
MAR 6:5 Wirva yan, a mangga ba dǝ dǝg ndawak ǝn vin bi, uk dǝv a bakhowin ǝn tǝ chalǝm liye kwal yang, a mbakhatru.
MAR 6:6 Kuɗ fadǝghǝrofǝg tara, a nala kǝ dǝg ndawak tsin. Ka dakhgal tsin da tsagdu lav Yazhigǝl ǝn gǝdzar kǝsakh sikh sikh sikh. ...
MAR 6:7 Ka ɗakhgan ad furakh sar kǝlatǝm mits, kǝ ɓǝlatra ɓǝla dǝ mits mits. Ka batran ad ndzǝɗ ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ sǝɗikw bǝzanakh.
MAR 6:8 Ka tǝkhatǝrnan kwarne, a ɗuwam zǝɓ itsa uɗa kǝ dǝgal uk gulv. A ɗuwam ɓǝ dǝg zuwa, itsa jilaɗ, zǝ kwaɓ ǝn mbǝlur.
MAR 6:9 Talǝm kur kimbak. Talam tala gabag, ɓamba tlǝrna gabag bi.
MAR 6:10 Itsera kǝ mǝgh ǝn dagh kur, ndzamga ndzǝg ǝn vin, da tǝ sarte da ɗuwars kur kǝsen.
MAR 6:11 Ɗaga vake kwal chaukur khai tsud, awana kwal tsǝnakuru tsud. Da da ɗuwars ɗuwa kur ad yanen kǝ vak, ka pangdu kur ad lagwat ǝn tǝ sigur. Ki nǝga tsin kǝ shid ǝn tǝghǝr tsitar, kwarne da takatra lava Yazhigǝl.
MAR 6:12 Ka dala itar, ka kwardu lava tsitar kwarne, pǝla udakh ad ghǝr.
MAR 6:13 A lakwadal itar ad wurduwakh ǝn vǝgh kǝ udakh zikǝn, a masar khai itar wal kǝ liye kwal yanga zikǝn, ka mbakhatru itar.
MAR 6:14 A tsǝna Khiridus shik ad dǝge a dzoghǝr, wirva a kwazga ɗakha Yasu itsa dǝvar. Nǝv chalǝm kǝ udakha, Yukhan dadak para ud kǝ tsiyif ǝn nggitl. Yan kǝ manggan nǝg dǝ ndzǝɗa manakh dǝg ndawakakh.
MAR 6:15 Av yakhaya, udan na ‘Ili.’ Av chalǝmakh tsuguna ‘Ina tlayang, ndǝk fang ǝn tǝb kǝ tlayangakhe tsa ndur.’
MAR 6:16 Tsǝna kǝ Khiridus ad yan, ka ni, “Yukhane a ǝntlargǝr ka ghǝr a tsiyanǝfud ǝn nggitl.”
MAR 6:17 Wirva Khiridus dǝ ghǝrsar tsa ba dǝ yakhaya kǝ udakh da vi Yukhan, kǝ nguɗa nguɗa tsud, bǝmud ǝn gud sal. A mangan ad ina kǝ wirva Khirudi nus zǝr dad sar Filibus, ai pǝrɗuwin kǝ nǝga kǝ nus sar.
MAR 6:18 Wirvǝn tsǝn kwarakhara kwara Yukhan kǝ Khiridus, kwarne, “Kalkal ba pǝrɗ nus zǝr dadagh tsǝkha kǝ nǝga kǝ nusagh bi.”
MAR 6:19 A bazardu lavan ad rǝv kǝ Khirudi tsuguna a mbitsana bi. Wirva yan, ka tsǝn nagha dǝ kǝɗga Yukhan. A gǝmadu ba dǝ ɗul bi.
MAR 6:20 Wirvǝn gǝdza gǝdza Khiridus ad Yukhan, a khayanǝf ba gǝma gǝma kǝ itsauɗa bi. Wirva tsatsin kwarne, Yukhana dadak kanadi zǝ chuwaɗaɗa rǝv. Itsǝra kǝ sarte ǝn tsǝna Khiridus ad kwar lava kǝ Yukhan, ka ndzikǝn ndziya char. Tsakhǝnmina, zǝɗa tsin tsǝn lav sar.
MAR 6:21 Kǝ dǝg mbasa ka gǝmadu Khirudi ad ɗul. Fitsa dzama khǝna yiga sar kǝ Khiridus. Ka ɓalga Khiridus ad zik zikan na kǝ udakh sar, zǝ zik zikan na kǝ tlujiyakh sar, zǝ malanakh kǝs ya Galili.
MAR 6:22 Sagh kǝ dughw Khirudi da vak khwaɗǝg, tsugwa tsin, ǝn tǝvuk kǝ Khiridus zǝ ghulabakh sar, ka zǝɗatǝru tsugwen. Ka nǝv shik kǝ dughwen, “Takaɗa dǝ itsauɗǝn nakhǝn vakar, da bakha bǝg kǝ.” ...
MAR 6:23 A waɗar khai Khiridus kǝ dughw na kwarne, “Itsauɗǝn takaɗgakha da bakha bǝg kǝ, itsa tǝkanud ǝntla khaye ǝn mana ka tlǝksa sar mits.”
MAR 6:24 Ka dala dughwena, ndiɗarwal kǝ babsar, “Uɗa da ɗawaki?” Ka niya tsin, “Ghǝr Yukhan dadak para ud.”
MAR 6:25 Ka gwiyal kujaɗ kujaɗ da vak shik. Takaɗgan kwarne, “Ən naka baka bǝg tsǝkha ghǝr Yukhan dadak para ud ǝn tǝ play tǝkhin tǝkhin.”
MAR 6:26 Tsǝna kǝ shik ad yan, ka bazala rǝv tsin char. Wirva waɗe a zugin, zǝ zhiruwe da khǝɓin ǝn tǝvuk kǝ ghulabakh sar, nagh ba dǝ kǝla lanji sar bi.
MAR 6:27 Ka ɓǝlanǝf ad fang ǝn tǝb kǝ tlujiyakh sar, dǝgin dǝgal da ɓardǝghǝr ghǝr Yukhan. Ka dala tlujiyena, ǝntlardǝghǝr ad ghǝr Yukhan ǝn gud sal.
MAR 6:28 Ɓadǝghǝr ad ghǝren ǝn tǝ play. Baran kǝ dughwen, ka ɓara dughwen kǝ bab sar.
MAR 6:29 Tsǝna kǝ furakh Yukhan ad yana, ka sagh itara da zǝb gǝdzumba vǝgha sar, ka ba itar ǝn ɗungwe khurzǝz.
MAR 6:30 Dzǝran na kǝ furakh kǝlatǝm mits ai tsa ɓǝlatǝr ndalin, a sara da vak sar. Kwarar khai itar daghan dǝgakhe manga itar, zǝ dǝgakhe tsagardu itar kǝ udakh.
MAR 6:31 Wirva zikǝn udakh ǝn sǝgawalina ǝn daksin, itsa sarta zu kafa a gǝmadu bai tar bi. Ka niya furakh sar, “Ausǝgam, na dziyamal da tlǝrna vake kwal nǝg kǝ itsawar, fǝtavkhai kiyam.”
MAR 6:32 Ka dagh itar da peryu, dala itar tukuɗa tukuɗa, da vake kwal nǝg kǝ itsawar.
MAR 6:33 Ən sarte tsǝn dǝgal itar, zikǝn udakhe a nǝghatǝran, ka katlga itar kwarne itar ǝn dǝgal. Ka khwaya kǝ udakh zikǝn ǝn khuɗ kǝs dǝgal dǝ sig diwa kalam zagh, ka itar kǝ dala chak tǝghǝr kǝ Yasu zǝ furakh sar.
MAR 6:34 Sawala kǝ Yasu ǝn peryuwen, ka nǝghan ad dzakhava udakh char. Kwiɗ nǝv rǝv tsin, wirva nggwaɗa tuwaghakhe kwal nǝg kǝ dadak zighw itar. Ka farsa tsagatra dǝgitakh sikh sikh sikh tsin.
MAR 6:35 Dǝm kǝ fatsi da ɓǝla, ka sagh furakh sar, ka nǝv itar tsin, “Vak na, na itsawar bi, tsuguna a dǝm fatsi da ɓǝl.
MAR 6:36 Ɓǝlatǝrs ɓǝla kǝ udakhan na daks, da khuɗ kǝsakh zǝ gǝdzar kǝsakhe khef ǝn van, kǝ sǝku dǝg zuwa tsitar kǝ ghǝrtar.”
MAR 6:37 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai Yasu kwarne, “Bamatra bǝg kur dǝge da zuwa itar.” Ka nǝv itar tsin, “Ina da nagha dǝ kwaɓ tǝl ǝntla vǝg, kǝ dadak man baryam. Dǝg kǝnda dǝgal da kǝɗ kwaɓ pakyan ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ brudi, kǝ batra kǝ zuwa zuwa nikha?
MAR 6:38 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal, “Ngǝrwa ɗumba brudi din kuri? Dam da nǝgha nǝgh.” Dala tsitar da nǝgha nǝgha, kwarar khai itar, kwarne, “Brudi dliɓ zǝ kilf mits.”
MAR 6:39 Ka bǝtra Yasu kǝ furakh sar, babǝg itar udakh da ndzakhga ndzakha kǝ dakwala kǝ dakwal, ǝn tǝ dzuɓ.
MAR 6:40 Ka ndzakhga itar kǝ dakwala kǝ dakwal. Yakhaya kǝ dakwala, dǝrmǝk, yakhaya tsuguna kuldlǝɓ.
MAR 6:41 Ka ɓǝf Yasu ad ɗumba brudiyen dliɓ zǝ kilfen mits. Kapanan ad ghǝra, vazo da gharazhigǝl, kwarar khai ad usus kǝ Yazhigǝl. Ka kalanan ad ɗumba brudiyakhen, baran kǝ furakh sar, kǝ takara kǝ udakh. Takatǝr khai ad kilfakhen mits na kǝ udakh daghan.
MAR 6:42 Itsawara a zu, a bagharal daghan.
MAR 6:43 Ka dzakhanǝf furakh sar ad tughub kǝlatǝm mits, kǝ kala brudiya zǝ kilfe tǝmgan.
MAR 6:44 Zika ghwalvakhe zuzuwa dǝb dliɓ.
MAR 6:45 Ən dǝvǝn dǝv, ka kwarar khai Yasu kǝ furakh sar, daks da peryu kǝ dǝgal tsitar da tǝ ghǝdzǝva gadzak kalam Betsed. In tsuguna da ɓǝlatǝrs kǝ udakh ndan.
MAR 6:46 Ən tǝ khal kǝ ɓǝlatǝrs ɓǝla tsin daksa, ka do da tǝ kalam ghuɓ kǝ ɗǝgau.
MAR 6:47 Ɓǝlga kǝ khagwa, tsǝn tǝb kǝ dǝlv peryu, in tsuguna tsa tukuɗa tukuɗ ǝn tǝ bǝɗar.
MAR 6:48 Ka nǝghan ad furakh sar ǝn khǝɓ dlaɗ wiya peryu, wirva zika fude ǝn gwiyatra da tǝlg. Dǝm kǝ kǝs da ngura, ka dala da vak tar, ǝn dǝgǝn tǝghǝr kǝ yu, vadge da dǝgala fǝt.
MAR 6:49 Nǝgha tsitar ǝn dǝgǝn tǝghǝr kǝ yuwa, ba ude a sawal ǝn tǝ fik nǝv itar. Ka khula tsitar.
MAR 6:50 Wirva daghan tara a nǝgha tsitar, ka gǝdzǝf itar char. Kujaɗ kujaɗa ka kwaratǝr khai ad lava kwarne, “Khǝna mana khǝna rǝvur, ka fǝka. A ɗuwam gǝdz.” ...
MAR 6:51 Ka dagh da peryu ǝn vak tar, ka lǝɓga fuɗen. A ndawatǝrǝf char.
MAR 6:52 Wirva a katlga ba itar ad dǝge ǝn tuku baghandala ud dǝb dliɓ na bi. Wirva dǝkdǝk rǝva tar.
MAR 6:53 Darghǝra tsitar kǝ dǝlva, ka tsugwa itar ǝn kalam khaya ya Janisarat. Ka nguɗana itar ad peryuwen ǝn tǝ ghay gǝrdz.
MAR 6:54 Sawala tsitar ǝn peryu, tǝvin tǝvina, ka katlga udakh ad Yasu.
MAR 6:55 Ka khwaya udakhen daks da khuɗ kǝsakh daghan. Ən zaɓado liye kwal yang itar ǝn tǝ pinakh tar, da ɗaga vake da tsǝne tar din Yasu.
MAR 6:56 Itsa dal dǝvarin, ǝn gǝdzar kǝsakh, zǝ dlǝmdla kǝsakh, awana mǝghakhe ǝn khuɗ tǝghal, ǝn khana liye kwal yanga udakhen ǝn tǝ ɓala ɓal. Ən tatl Yasu itar kǝ khayatǝrnǝf kǝ liye kwal yang, kǝ gǝma itsa ghai gabag sar. Daghan liye a gǝmana a mbakharu.
MAR 7:1 Farisakha zǝ yakhaya kǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus, ai sarawal ǝn Wurshalim. Dzafkai itar ǝn vak Yasu.
MAR 7:2 Ka nǝgha itar ad yakhaya kǝ furakh Yasu, ǝn zu kaf itar kwal parga tsitar ad dǝv ndǝke tsagdu dzidzakh tar.
MAR 7:3 Wirva Farisakha zǝ Yakhudakh daghan, na itar zu kaf kwal parga tsitsar dǝv ndǝke tsagatǝrdu dzidzakh tar bi. Wirvǝn tsufada ndzikha ndzikh dzidzakh tar itar.
MAR 7:4 Da sa itar ǝn kasuk, na itar ǝn zu kaf bi, akwa pardu itar dǝv ndǝke tsagatǝrdu dzidzakh tar. Ən tsufa tsufa itar ad yakhaya kǝ ndzikha ndzikh tar ai wuru itar zikǝn. Ndǝk zai pardu kwat khǝɓ yu, shakakh, zǝ shugudakhe mangud dǝ vǝrshakanvǝ, zǝ vak zu kafakh tar.
MAR 7:5 Wirva yan, ka ndiɗarwal Farisakhen zǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikhen kǝ Yasu, “Uɗa lava kǝ furakhagh kwal nǝg ǝn gatars kǝ ndzikha ndzikh dzidzakhǝnd, kǝ zu kaf tsitar kwal par dǝv ndǝkve tsagdu dzidzakhǝndi?”
MAR 7:6 Ka nggawa tǝrkhai Yasu, ‘Kalkal lav tlayang tlayange tsa kwarga Ishay ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ tsukur kur mbaɗirakh. Ndǝke vindzanin kwarne, ‘ “Udakhan na uk ǝn fakghǝr dǝ ghay itar, rǝvakhuɗ tara bita zǝ kǝ.
MAR 7:7 Ən ɗabaka buti itar, ǝn tsagdu ndzikha ndzikhe a bǝga ud itar vadge ndzikha ndzikhe a bǝga Yazhigǝl.’
MAR 7:8 Ɗuwars kur gatars kǝ ndzikha ndzikh Yazhigǝl, ǝn gatars kǝ ndzikha ndzikh dzidzakhur kur.”
MAR 7:9 Ka zu vuk tsin dǝ kwar kwarne, “Nǝg kur dǝ khiɗa ɗuda ndzikha ndzikh Yazhigǝl, kǝ wirva tsuf tsagdutsagur.
MAR 7:10 Wirva kwarga Mus kwarne, ‘Fargǝrafǝg kǝ dadagha zǝ babagh, ɗaga ude kwarga lav bǝzan ǝn tǝ dad sar awana bab sar, ka kǝɗgud.’
MAR 7:11 Ai ǝn kwara kwara kur kwarne, da ka nǝv udan kǝ bab sar awana dad sar, dǝge tsa da mǝlakuru ka din, audzala kǝn barkhai kǝ Yazhigǝl. A manga ba dǝ khaip bi.
MAR 7:12 Wirva yan, a khayarnǝf ba kur kǝ ud ad mǝlaru kǝ dad sara zǝ bab sar bi.
MAR 7:13 Tǝ dǝva dǝ yan, a nandala kur lav Yazhigǝl kǝ bat, wirva ndzikha ndzikhakh dzidzakhure ǝn tsagardu kur kǝ zarur. Ən manakha mana kur digitakh zikǝn ndǝkva dǝgakhen.
MAR 7:14 Ka gwidǝn Yasu ad ɗakhga dzakhava udakh, ka ni, “Tsǝnam ka tsǝna itsawar, diyarsǝf kur ad inan.
MAR 7:15 Na dǝge ǝn ba udan da ghay sar, ai da nan kǝ kwadlamb ǝn tǝvuk kǝ Yazhigǝl bi. Akwa dǝge ǝn sǝgo ǝn khuɗ sar da nan kǝ kwadlamb, ǝn tǝvuk kǝ Yazhigǝl.
MAR 7:16 Ɗaga ude dǝ tlim tsǝn lav, tsǝnin ad lavan.
MAR 7:17 Ən tǝkhal kǝ tǝkaghǝra tsin zǝ dzakhava udakh, ka dagh da mǝgh. Ka ndiɗarwal furakh sar ad dǝge ǝn tuku jakva lavan.
MAR 7:18 Ka niya tsitar, “Atsuk a katlga bakh ghǝrura? Ən tsa bakh kur kwarne dǝge ǝn ba udan da ghay sar bǝn na ud kǝ kwadlamb ǝn tǝvuk kǝ Yazhigǝl biya?
MAR 7:19 Wirvǝn nabǝn daks da rǝvakhuɗ bi ǝn dǝgdagh da khuɗ, khalakyan ka sǝgawal ǝn vǝgh. (Lav Yasu ǝn tǝ vana, a mǝdlanan kwarne, itsera kǝ dǝg zuwa chuwaɗaɗ kǝ zuwazu.)
MAR 7:20 Ka zu vuk tsin dǝ kwar lav kwarne, ‘Dǝge sǝgo ǝn khuɗ kǝ uda ǝn nan kǝ kwadlamb ǝn tǝvuk kǝ Yazhigǝl.
MAR 7:21 Wirvǝn rǝvakhuɗ ud ǝn sǝgo nguɗi nguɗi ɗayaghǝrakh, ai bǝgan da man dǝgakhe kwal khwar, ndǝk zai garnak, gǝl, zǝ kǝɗ safa ud.
MAR 7:22 Gwaragwar, khuwa, kǝlada, valdu ud, kuɗ bǝg zhiru, shilga, bazdu ɗakha ud, nagh ghǝr, zǝ dlǝgǝr dlag.
MAR 7:23 Daghan dǝg nguɗi nguɗiyakhan, ǝn sǝgo ǝn khuɗ kǝ ud, tsuguna in ǝn nan kǝ kwadlamb ǝn tǝvuk kǝ Yazhigǝl.”
MAR 7:24 Ka ɗuda Yasu ad vaken, dagh da ǝntla khaya Taya zǝ Sidon. Ka dagh da mǝghen, tsuguna ǝn nagh ba tsatsǝg ak itsawar bi, dǝmbiyanena, a ɓǝghafkhai bi.
MAR 7:25 Uk tsǝna tsǝna kǝ nuse ǝn kǝɗa shatan ad dughw sar ad lavǝn tǝghǝr kǝ Yasu, ka sagha kǝlgan ad juguv ǝn tǝvuk sar.
MAR 7:26 Nusen tsuguna liye kwal Yakhudakh. A yavǝn Finiki ǝntla khaya ya Suri. Ka tatl Yasu tsin kǝ ɓardal wurdu sǝgawal ǝn vǝgh kǝ dughw sar.
MAR 7:27 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Ɗuwaks ɗuwa bara bǝg ka dǝg zuwa kǝ zaren (Yakhudakh) ndan, wirva kalkal ba ka ɓatǝrvalud dǝg zuwa zara, ka liyarduwud kǝ ghǝdakh bi.”
MAR 7:28 Ka nǝv nusen, “Ai ndǝk yan Dad Zikan, ai ghǝdakha ǝn vaɗuvaɗa itar ad kwacha kafakhe a ɓalal ǝn tǝ vǝlang zu kaf zar.”
MAR 7:29 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Wirva lavana a kwargakh, gwiya daks da mǝgh, a tǝkaghǝra wurdu zǝ dughwagh.”
MAR 7:30 Ka wura da mǝgh, tlarghǝr kǝ dughw sar ǝn khǝngan ǝn tǝ pin, audzala wurduwen ǝn dala dǝg ǝn vǝgh sar.
MAR 7:31 Ka ɗuwars Yasu ad kǝs ya Taya, ka dal da dǝlva Galili, diwa Sidon zǝ Dikapolis (kǝsakh kǝlɗǝk).
MAR 7:32 Ka ɓardǝghǝr yakhaya kǝ udakh ad tǝnge dlakh kwar ghay tsin, ka tatl Yasu tsitar kǝ barghǝr dǝv tsin, ki mbǝga tsin.
MAR 7:33 Tǝkhal kǝ ɗakhga tsin udanen ǝn tǝb kǝ dzakhava udakh da tǝ kalam. Ka ba Yasu ad wirik dǝv sar da tlim kǝ tǝngen, ka tǝfaw ad shaghwvai ǝn tǝ zǝr dǝv sar, ka gǝman ad rikha udanen din.
MAR 7:34 Ka lando Yasu ad ghǝr da gharazhigǝl, ka gǝlf niya zikzik, ka niya tsin, “Iffata” Dǝge ǝn tukuwina in kwarne “Ngurǝf ngur.”
MAR 7:35 Kwarga tsin ndǝkyan, ka ngurǝf tlim udanen. Ka tasla nǝv rikh sar a vǝdgan, ka farsa kwar lava tsin khwaraniyan.
MAR 7:36 Ka ndǝɗatǝrnǝf Yasu ad tlim kwarne, kwarara ba itar kǝ itsawar ad dǝge a dzoghǝr bi. Itsera kǝ sart ǝn kwargin kwarne kwar ba itar bi, ka zu vuk dǝ kwardu laven itar.
MAR 7:37 Dǝgǝn na mangina a ndawatǝrǝf kǝ udakh char. Ka nǝv itar, “A mangan ad itsauɗa kalkal. A ba dǝ tǝngakh, da tsǝna lav. Liye kwal tǝkha kǝ kwarga lava, ka kwar lava.”
MAR 8:1 Ən khǝnakhena, ka gwidǝn dzafkhai udakh zikǝn da vak Yasu. Fatsiye a mbasu dǝg zuwa tar, a ɗakhga Yasu ad furakh sar da vak sar. Ka ni,
MAR 8:2 “Ən man kwiɗkwiɗǝrv udakhana kǝ, khǝkǝrɗ khana tsitar zǝ kǝ, kǝvena na dǝge da zuwa itar bi.
MAR 8:3 Da ɗuwatǝrs ka daks da mǝgh dǝ way, da mbaɗa itar ǝn tǝ ɗul, wirva chalǝm tara a sara kǝ bit.”
MAR 8:4 Ka nǝv furakh sar tsin, “Ai da mbǝladu ǝn varud ad dǝg zuwa zikǝn ǝn khuɗ tǝkhal na ndǝkin, ai da bagha tǝra bagha kǝ udakhan na daghani?”
MAR 8:5 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal Yasu, “Ngǝrwa brudiye din kuri?” Ka nggawar khai itar kwarne, “Uɗif.”
MAR 8:6 Ka kwara tǝrkhai kǝ udakh kǝ ndzakhga ndzakh ǝn tǝ khay. Ɓǝf tsin brudina uɗif, ka kwar sus tsin kǝ Yazhigǝl, kalanan, baran kǝ furakh sar kǝ takatǝra taka kǝ udakhen. Ka manga furakhen ndǝkyan.
MAR 8:7 Nǝg itar dǝ mbisan na kǝ kilfakh khǝɗikǝn tsugun. Ka kwarar khai dǝ sus kǝ Yazhigǝl, kǝ wirva kilfakhen tsugun. Kwara tǝrkhai kǝ furakh sar kǝ takardu taka tsitar kǝ udakh, ad kilfakhen tsugun.
MAR 8:8 Azu udakh baghala itar. Tǝkhal kǝ zuzuwa tsitara, dzakhanǝf furakh sar ad tughub uɗif ake tǝmatǝru kǝ udakh.
MAR 8:9 Tsa ghwalvakh dǝb ufaɗ ǝn vinen. Tǝkhal kǝ ɓǝlatǝrs bǝla tsin daks,
MAR 8:10 tǝvin tǝvina ka dagh da peryu zǝ furakh sar, da ǝntla khay Dalmanut.
MAR 8:11 Ka sagh yakhaya kǝ Farisakh da vak Yasu, farsa itar man tsugu zǝ zin. Ən gat mǝdlatra dǝg ndawak itar. Kǝ mǝdla kwarne, a khayanǝf Yazhigǝl din.
MAR 8:12 Ka safa tsin gǝlf dǝ ndzǝɗ, ni. “Uɗa lava kǝ udakh kwargǝn ǝn ndiɗ dǝg ndawaki? Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, na dǝg ndawake da mǝdlatrud bi.”
MAR 8:13 Khalak yana, ka ɗuwatǝrs, ka gwiya da peryu. Dal da tǝ tlǝrna ghǝdzǝva gadzak.
MAR 8:14 A mbitsa tǝrghǝr zǝɓ brudi kǝ furakh Yasu, uk brudi kitakul ǝn peryuwen.
MAR 8:15 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Tsukwamana ghǝr dǝgi, ɗem nikur kǝ yista Farisakh zǝ dǝg Khirudus.”
MAR 8:16 Ka farsa itar ad kwarakava lav ǝn tatak tar kwarne, “Wirva na brudi ǝn vak mar bi, in kǝ mangan kǝ kwar ina tsin.”
MAR 8:17 Tsa kǝ Yasu ad lave ǝn kwara itar. Ka ndiɗatǝrwal, “Ən kwara kǝ uɗa kur kwarne nakur dǝ brudi biyi? Sakhkana a katlga ba kur biya? Tsuguna, a diyarsǝf ba kur biya? Uɗa lava kǝ rǝvura dlaɓ dǝkdǝki?
MAR 8:18 Nǝg kur dǝ diyakh, uɗa lava tsukur kwal ǝn nǝgha nǝghi? Nǝg kur dǝ tlimakh, uɗa lava tsukur kwal ǝn tsǝna tsǝni? A dzamana bakh kura.
MAR 8:19 Ən sarte tsa kalanaka brudi dliɓ, kǝ udakh dǝb dliɓ, ngǝrwa tughubakh, ake tǝmgan a dzakhanǝf kuri?” Ka nǝv itar, “Kǝlatǝm mits.”
MAR 8:20 “Ən sarte tsa kalanaka brudi uɗif, kǝ udakh dǝb ufaɗ, ngǝrwa tughubakh, ake tǝmgan a dzakhanǝf kuri?” Ka nǝv itar, “Uɗif.”
MAR 8:21 Ka niya tsitar, “Dambiyanena, dla kur kwal katlgana?”
MAR 8:22 Sa tsitar da Betsaid, ɓadǝghǝr yakhaya kǝ udakh ad ngulf da vak Yasu. Ka takaɗ Yasu tsitar kǝ gǝma gǝma tsin, kǝ mbambǝg tsin.
MAR 8:23 Ka khutanan ad ngulfen ǝn tǝ dǝv, ndaɗal da tǝlg kǝs. Tǝfara tsin shaghwvay da di kǝ udanǝn, baw ad dǝv sar ǝn tǝf. Ka ndiɗarwal, “Ən nǝgha nǝgha kha digita?”
MAR 8:24 Ka lando ngulfen ad ghǝr, ni, “Ən nǝgha nǝgha ka udakh, ai ǝn vastra ngwaɗa ufakhe ǝn gwayava kǝ.”
MAR 8:25 Ka gwidǝn bo Yasu ad dǝv sar ǝn tǝ di udanen. Ngwarǝf di sar charang. Ka farsan ad nǝgha vak tsugun. Ka nǝghan ad itsauɗa chaɗaɗ.
MAR 8:26 Ka ɓǝlars Yasu daks da mǝgh, ka kwar khai tsugun, “A ɗuwa daks diwa khuɗ kǝs.”
MAR 8:27 A ɗuwars Yasu zǝ furakh sar ad kǝs Betsaid, da itar da gǝdzar kǝsakh ǝn khaya ya Kaisari Filibi. Madǝv itar ǝn dǝga, ka ndiɗatǝrwal kǝ furakh sar, “Warek ka vek udakhi?”
MAR 8:28 Ka nǝv itar tsin, “Av yakhaya Yukhan dadak para ud khǝ. Av yakhay Ili khǝ. Av yakhaya tsuguna kha fang ǝn tǝb kǝ tlayanggakhe tsa dur.”
MAR 8:29 Ka niya tsitar, “Ai kur ma? Warek ka vek kuri?” Ka nggawar khai Bitrus kwarne, “Kha Kristu.”
MAR 8:30 Ka ndǝɗatǝrnǝf Yasu ad tlim, kwarara ba itar kǝ itsawar ad lavǝn tǝghǝr tsin bi.
MAR 8:31 Ən tǝkhal kǝ yan, ka farsa Yasu ad tsagatǝrdu tsaga kǝ furakh sar kwarne, “Ka Zǝr Ud, da khǝɓa khǝɓa ka dlaɗ char sikh sikh sikh. Malanakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ udakh, zǝ zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh, da ɗukda ɗuwa itar. Da kǝɗ kai kǝɗud, ǝn tǝ fitsa khekǝrɗa da tsiya kǝn nggitl.
MAR 8:32 A kwara tǝrkhai ad ina kǝ lav ǝn ɓal a ɓǝghana bi, ka ndaɗala Bitrus ad Yasu da tǝ kalam, ka farsa tavarghǝr di tsin.
MAR 8:33 Ai guyafkhai kǝ Yasu, ka vazgan ad chalǝm furakh sar. Ka tavarghǝr ad di kǝ Bitrus, “Tsiya dǝgal ǝn tǝvǝgh tsǝka kha Shatan, rǝvagha a khayanǝf ba dǝ dǝge ǝn nagha Yazhigǝl bi, ǝn khaya dǝge ǝn nagha ud dǝg sig.”
MAR 8:34 Ka ɗakhga Yasu ad dzakhava udakh zǝ furakh sar da vak sar. Ka ni, “Ɗeghwa ude ǝn na nǝga kǝ furara, akwa ɗudin ghǝr sar, ɓǝfin ufa khǝrta sar, ka gataks in.
MAR 8:35 Wirva ɗeghwa ude ǝn na kat safa sar, da bǝghǝmb. Ai ɗeghwa ude ǝn bǝdu safa sar wirva kǝ, zǝ kǝ lav Yazhigǝl, da gǝmadu gǝma dǝ safa kǝ ngǝɗ.
MAR 8:36 Khwara ndǝk uɗa da gǝmadu udan ad digit daghan ǝn lard, ai ka bǝghalǝn safa sari?
MAR 8:37 Uɗǝn da bǝdu udan kǝ dleva safa sari?
MAR 8:38 Itsawar ǝn man zhiruwar, zǝ zhiru kwardu lavar, ǝn nguɗi nguɗi kwargǝn, ka Zǝr Uda, da man zhiru sar kǝn sarte da sǝgadagh kǝn ndanga Dadar, dagha zǝ zar ɓǝla Yazhigǝl.”
MAR 9:1 Ka zu vuk tsin dǝ kwar kwarne, “Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, nǝg yakhayin ghitsǝn van, na itar da mǝtsa bi, akwa nǝgha itar ad tlǝksa Yazhigǝl, ai da mǝdlo dǝ ndzǝɗ.”
MAR 9:2 Ən tǝkhal kǝ khǝna ǝnkwakha, ka dal Yasu zǝ Bitrus, zǝ Yakub, zǝ Yukhan, ka ɓǝtǝro dugo da tǝ ghuɓe tsǝɓanyan, vake uk itar tukuɗa tar. Ən tǝ vina ka mbǝɗfkhai vǝgha sar ǝn tǝvuk tar.
MAR 9:3 Gabag sara a nala kǝ maɗakw til ǝn wuɗ char ǝn zǝɓara di kǝ ud. Na dadak ghuɓ kadlang ǝn lard ai da tǝkha kǝ ghuɓgan da tǝ maɗakw sar bi.
MAR 9:4 Dzagwdlam, ka mǝdlawala Ili tlayang zǝ Mus tlayang, ǝn kwar lava itar zǝ Yasu.
MAR 9:5 Ka nǝv Bitrus kǝ Yasu, “Malǝm, khwarenǝn vana kǝnd. Manga mana kǝnd ad tsikw khǝkǝrɗ, fang tsǝkha, fang kǝ Musa tlayang, fang kǝ Ili tlayang.”
MAR 9:6 Ən tsa ba dǝ dǝge da kwarin bi, wirva khǝkǝrɗ dagha tara a gǝdzǝf itar char.
MAR 9:7 Ka sadagh ghwikwa, khǝmbatǝrghǝr. A tsǝna tsud lavǝn ghwik kwarne, “Zǝraren, ǝn waya waya kǝ. Tsǝnamaru tsǝn.”
MAR 9:8 Ɓalakhga tsitar ad diya, a gwidǝn ba itar nǝgha itsawar bi, uk Yasu.
MAR 9:9 Madǝv Yasu zǝ furakh sar ǝn sǝgdagh ǝn ghuɓ, ka ndǝɗatǝrnǝf Yasu ad tlim kwarne, kwarara ba itar kǝ itsawar ad dǝge a nǝgha itar bi. Akwa tsiyakǝfud ka Zǝr Ud ǝn nggitl.
MAR 9:10 Wirva yana, ka ɗu itar ad laven ǝn khuɗ tar. Ən ɗaya kava ɗaya itar ǝn tǝb tar kwarne, “Uɗa dǝge ǝn tuku tsiyin nggitle a kwarga Yasuwi?”
MAR 9:11 Khalak yana, ka ndiɗarwal itar kǝ Yasu kwarne, “Uɗa lava kǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh ǝn kwarne, khekwa Ili tlayang da sodagh chak kǝ Kristuwi?”
MAR 9:12 Ka nggawa tǝrkhai Yasu kwarne, “Barari Ili tlayang da sodagh chak, kǝ ɗika itsauɗ, kalkal ndǝke ǝn naghud. Wirva yan, ai uɗa lava tsin vindzan kwarne, da khǝɓ khǝɓa Zǝr Ud ad dlaɗ char zǝ ɗuda duwa tsudi?
MAR 9:13 Ai ǝn tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, audzal Ili tlayang ǝn sodagh sǝg. A manarkhai udakh ad ɗaga dǝge ǝn nagha rǝva tar. Ndǝkve vindzanin ǝn kaɗkaɗ lav Yazhigǝl ǝn tǝghǝr tsin.”
MAR 9:14 Gwiyoghǝr kǝ Yasu zǝ furakhna khǝkǝrɗ da vak furakhe tsa tǝmgan, ka nǝgha itar ad dzakhava udakh a tsatǝrghǝran kǝ furakhen. Li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus tsuguna, ǝn manakava tsugu zitar.
MAR 9:15 Ba uk nǝgha nǝgha kǝ dzakhava udakh ad Yasu, ka a ndawatǝrǝf char, ka khwaya tsitar da gama gam.
MAR 9:16 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal Yasu kǝ furakh sar kwarne, “Tsugu uɗǝn mana kur zǝ itar ra?”
MAR 9:17 Ka nggawar khai udanen ǝn tǝb kǝ dzakhava udakh kwarne, “Malǝma, a ɓakhdǝghǝr ka zǝrar ai dǝ sǝɗikw bǝzan ǝn vǝgh tsin, ai gadlarkhai ad kwar ghay.
MAR 9:18 Itsǝra kǝ sart ǝn tsukwarghǝrin, ka tlǝvarghǝr da khay. Ka sǝgawala kubǝn ghay tsin, ka kǝrɗ tliɗ tsin, ghulala jigh. A takaɗga ka furakhagh kǝ lakwadal sǝɗikw bǝzan ǝn vǝgh sar, ai a piyatǝrwal.”
MAR 9:19 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Kur udakh kwargǝn, li khǝtsa fadǝghǝrofǝg. Da zulu pak uɗa kǝn giɗa zǝ kuri? Da zulu pak uɗa kǝn bǝg rǝv dǝ kuri? A nǝgham zǝren da vakar.”
MAR 9:20 Ka ɓardǝghǝr itar zǝren. Nǝgha kǝ sǝɗikwen ad Yasu, kujaɗ kujaɗa, ka tatǝg tsin ad zǝren, ka ɓǝlal zǝren da khay. Ka kuɗmbǝl kuɗmbǝl dǝva tsin ǝn tǝ khay, dǝ kubǝn ghay.
MAR 9:21 Ka ndiɗarwar Yasu kǝ dad zǝren, “Yawa farsin manara mani?” Ka nggawar khai dad zǝren kwarne, “Gwil ǝn zara tsin.” ...
MAR 9:22 Ka zu vuk tsin dǝ kwar lav, ngǝrwa sig tsin ǝn tlavarghǝr tlava da kar zǝ yu kǝ kǝɗga kǝɗ. Da nǝg dǝge da tǝkha kha kǝ mangan, ziwa kǝndalakh, mǝlakǝndu khǝ.”
MAR 9:23 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin. “Uɗa lava tsǝkhǝn kwar kwarne, da da tǝkha khi? Itsauɗa ǝn manawa mana kǝ dadake a fadǝghǝro.”
MAR 9:24 Tǝvin tǝvina ka nǝv dad zǝren, “A fadǝghǝro kǝ. Mǝlaku mǝla kǝ sǝgakarghǝr fadǝghǝro fǝgar.”
MAR 9:25 Nǝgha kǝ Yasu ǝn saks dzakhava udakh da vak sar dǝ khway, ka tavarghǝr ad di kǝ sǝɗikw bǝzanen. Ka ni, “Kha sǝɗikw bǝzan, khe ngǝdlarkhai kwar ghay kǝ zǝrǝn. Ən kwara kha kwara kǝ, sawal sǝg ǝmb, aghba khǝn da damb bi.”
MAR 9:26 Ka khula kǝ sǝɗikw bǝzanen, gwidzanǝfa, ka sawal ǝn vǝgh sar. Ka khǝnga zǝren ǝn khay ndǝk mǝtsa ud. Wirva yan, nǝv udakh zikǝn, “Amtsǝgan.”
MAR 9:27 Ka khutana Yasu ad dǝv zǝren, tsiyanǝf, ghitsgan ǝn tǝ siga sar.
MAR 9:28 Da kǝ Yasu da mǝgh, ka ndiɗarwal furakh sar ɓǝghaniyan, “Uɗa lav a piyakǝndwal ɓadal sǝɗikw bǝzaneni?”
MAR 9:29 Ka nggawa tǝrkhai Yasu kwarne, “Khulfina kǝ sǝɗikw bǝzan na, uk ɗǝgawa kalti ǝn ɓado.”
MAR 9:30 Ka ɗuwars Yasu zǝ furakh sar ad vaken, dala itar, dǝgal diwa khaya Galili. Nagh ba Yasu ad tsatsǝg kǝ itsawar ad vake din itar bi,
MAR 9:31 wirvǝn tsagatǝrdu tsaga kǝ furakh sar. Ka niya tsitar, “Da bǝkdu bugud, ka Zǝr Ud da dǝv kǝ udakh. Ka da kǝɗka kǝɗa itar kǝ ǝmts, ǝn tǝ fitsa khǝkǝrɗa, da tsiya kǝn nggitl.”
MAR 9:32 Ai a katlga ba itar ad tsagdu tsaga sar na bi. A ndiɗarwal ba itar tsugun bi. Wirvǝn gǝdza gǝdza itar.
MAR 9:33 A sa Yasu zǝ furakh sar da Kafarnakhum. Da kǝ Yasu da mǝgh, ka ndiɗatǝrwal kǝ furakh sar, “Uɗa tsǝn kwara kava kur ǝn tǝ ɗuli?”
MAR 9:34 Ai ka ndzǝga itar tǝriɗ, wirva tsǝn kwara kava kwara itar ǝn tǝb tar, ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ, warek zikan daghan ǝn tǝb tar.
MAR 9:35 Ka ndzǝga Yasu, ɗakhgan ad furakh sar kǝlatǝm mits, niya tsitar, “Ɗeghwa ude ǝn na nǝga kǝ dǝg chak, barari tsin nǝga kǝ dǝg ngiɗangiɗ, nalin kǝ dadak manara tlǝr kǝ itsawar.”
MAR 9:36 Ka ɓadǝghǝr ad zǝr khǝɗikan ghitsanan ǝn tǝb tar, ka ɓǝlarghǝr ad dǝv sar, ka niya tsitar,
MAR 9:37 “Itsawar ǝn chauga zǝr khǝɗikan ndǝk inan ǝn ɗakhar, ka chaukayin. Dadake chaukaya, ka kitakul ba chaukayin bi, zǝva dadake a ɓǝlokondagh a chaugin.
MAR 9:38 Ka nǝv Yukhan, “Malǝm, nǝgha tsǝkǝnda udanen ǝn ɓado sǝɗikw bǝzan ǝn vǝgh kǝ udakh ǝn ɗakhagh. Ka gadlar khai kǝnd, wirva na ba zǝ kiyam bi.”
MAR 9:39 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Gadlamara bi. Wirva na ude ǝn man dǝg ndawak ǝn ɗakhara, tǝvin tǝvin tsuguna ka kwar lav bǝzan ǝn tǝghǝr tsǝka bi.
MAR 9:40 Wirva ude kwal man tlughuma dǝ kiyama dǝg mar.
MAR 9:41 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, ɗaga ude ǝn kakuru yu itsǝn kwat khǝɗikan, wirva a fadǝghǝro kur ǝn tǝ ka, ka Kristu. Naba da bǝghǝn dǝg siga sar tsa khǝɗikǝn bi.
MAR 9:42 Ɗeghwa ude a ba fang ǝn tǝb kǝ zar mbisan nan, liye fadǝghǝro ǝn tǝ kǝ da man khaip, a dara nguɗarǝmud zikan na kǝ vǝr ǝn kwind, kǝɗ daghud da dǝlv.
MAR 9:43 Da dǝva ǝn bǝgkhan da man khaip, ǝntlars ǝntla dǝgal. Adara da dǝ dǝv kitakul kha da vake da mbǝladu kha safa kǝ ngǝɗ, tǝghǝr kǝ daks tsǝkha dǝ dǝv mits da kara tsakaitsakai.
MAR 9:44 [Vake, “ ‘Kwaɗe ǝn zutǝr zuwa naba itar ǝmtsa bi. Karen tsuguna da tǝkh bud kǝ kǝɗgan bi.’]
MAR 9:45 Da ka sigagh ǝn bǝgkhan da man khaip, ǝntlars ǝntl. Azǝgha da ghurɗik kha da vake da mbǝladu kha safa kǝ ngǝɗ, tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝvkhǝdaghud dǝ sigakh mits da kara tsakaitsakai.
MAR 9:46 [Vake, “ ‘Kwaɗe ǝn zutǝr zuwa naba itar ǝmtsa bi. Karen tsuguna da tǝkh bud kǝ kǝɗgan bi.’]
MAR 9:47 Da ka diyagh ǝn bǝgkhan da man khaip, ndǝɗdu khǝ. Azǝgha da dǝ di kitakul kha da tlǝksa Yazhigǝl, tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝvǝghǝdaghud dǝ diya mits da kara tsakaitsakai.
MAR 9:48 Vake, “ ‘Kwaɗe ǝn zutǝr zuwa naba itar ǝmtsa bi. Karen tsuguna da tǝkh bud kǝ kǝɗgan bi.’]
MAR 9:49 Da chuwaɗa chuwaɗud ad itsawar dǝ kar, ndǝkve ǝn chuwaɗud dǝg tsufa dǝ tlugul.
MAR 9:50 Tlugula khwar, da tǝkaghǝrin dǝ nashnasha sara, da gwiyondǝghǝr ndarud ad nashnasha sari? Nalnǝg giɗura zǝ tlǝrur ndǝk tlugul. Tsuguna, ka giɗa gabǝr kur ǝn tǝbur.”
MAR 10:1 Ka ɗuwars Yasu ad yanen kǝ vak, ka dal da ǝntla khaya Yakhudi, zǝ ghǝdzǝva zagha Urdun. Ka gwidǝn sawala dzakhava udakh da vak sar. A tsagatǝrdu ndǝkve a kwiyalin.
MAR 10:2 Ka saks kǝ yakhaya kǝ Farisakh da kura kura dǝ ndiɗ. Ka ndiɗarwal itar, “Kalkal nagh tǝkaghǝra kǝ udan zǝ nus sara?”
MAR 10:3 Ka niya tsitar, “Uɗa tǝkha kurna Musi?”
MAR 10:4 Ka nǝv itar tsin, “A khayarnǝf Mus ad vindzara kaɗkaɗ pǝcha sǝba kǝ ud, kǝ lakwars lakwa dǝgal.”
MAR 10:5 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Tsa wirva ɓengɓeng rǝvakhuɗur, tsa vindza kurkhai Mus adina kǝ ndzikh.”
MAR 10:6 “Ai gwil farsa vǝrɗ lard, ‘A vǝrɗtǝrkhai Yazhigǝl kǝ zila zǝ nus.’
MAR 10:7 Wirva yan, ka da ɗuwars udan ad dadsar zǝ babsar kǝ khǝmbarva kǝ nus sar.
MAR 10:8 Ka mits dagha tara da nǝga kǝ vǝgh kitakul. Aghba itar mits bi, anala kǝ vǝgh kitakul itar.
MAR 10:9 Wirva yan, dǝge audzala Yazhigǝl ǝn matlanǝf matla, tǝka ba udan bi.”
MAR 10:10 Gwiyoghǝr tsitar saks da mǝgh, ka ndiɗarwar furakh sar kǝ Yasu ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ tǝkaghǝren.
MAR 10:11 Ka nggawa tǝrkhai Yasu, “Ɗeghwa ude tǝkaghǝra zǝ nus sar, ka zǝɓu ad tlǝrna nus, gwaragwar ǝn manin zin.
MAR 10:12 Ai da ka tǝkaghǝra nus zǝ zil sar, ka zǝɓuwin tlǝrna zil, gwaragwar ǝn manin zin.
MAR 10:13 Tsǝn zaɓakhado zar mbisan udakh da vak Yasu, kǝ bakhatǝrghǝr dǝv tsin, kǝ batǝrghǝr bark. Ai ka tavatǝrghǝr furakh sar ad di kǝ zaren.
MAR 10:14 Vazga kǝ Yasu ad dǝge a mangga furakh sar, ka bazala rǝv tsin. Niya tsitar, “Ɗuwamada ɗuwa zar mbisan saks da vakar, gadlamatra bi. Wirva tlǝksa Yazhigǝla, dǝg khutsak tar.
MAR 10:15 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, itsawar kwal khayanǝf dǝ tlǝksa Yazhigǝl, ndǝkve a khayanǝf zar mbisan, a tǝkh ba kǝ da da tlǝksa Yazhigǝl bi.”
MAR 10:16 Ka tsakwatrǝf dǝ fang fang, ɓalatǝrghǝr ad dǝv, ka batǝrghǝr ad bark.
MAR 10:17 Tsif kǝ Yasu da ɗuwars yanen kǝ vak, ka khwayoghǝr udanen da vak sar, kǝlgan ad juguv ǝn tǝvuk sar. Ka ndiɗarwal kwarne, “Malǝm charan, uɗa da mana ka kǝ gǝmadu safa kǝ ngǝɗi?”
MAR 10:18 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Uɗa lava tsǝkhǝn ɗakhka dǝ charani? Na ud charan bi, uk Yazhigǝl kitakul.
MAR 10:19 Tsa tsǝkha dǝ ndzikha ndzikhen, ai kwarne, ‘Kǝɗ ba safa bi. Man ba gwaragwar bi. A ɗuwa man gǝl. Man ba shida dǝge kwal nǝgha tsǝkha bi. Biɗ ba dǝ ud bi. Farghǝra fǝg kǝ dadagha zǝ babagh.’ ”
MAR 10:20 Ka nǝv daghwalen tsin, “Malǝm, gwil ǝn zara tsǝka ǝn tsufa tsufa ka dǝgakhan na daghan.”
MAR 10:21 Ka vazga Yasu dǝ vaza waiv. Niya tsin, “Digit kitakul kǝ khǝtsakhu. Daks sakwdu sakwa daghan dǝge din khǝ, batra kha kwaɓ sar kǝ talagakh. Ka da gǝmadu gǝma kha tluwandal ǝn gharazhigǝl. Tǝkhal kǝ yana ka gataks khǝ.”
MAR 10:22 Tsǝna kǝ dakhwalen ad lave kwarga Yasu, ka bazala rǝv tsin. Tǝkavala dǝ baza rǝv, wirva nǝg lǝman tsin char.
MAR 10:23 Ka vazakhga Yasu ad furakh sar, ka niya tsitar, “Da bǝza daks kǝ dadak tluwandal da tlǝksa Yazhigǝl.”
MAR 10:24 A ndawatǝrǝf kǝ furakh sar, tsǝna tsitar ad lave kwargin. Ai ka nǝv Yasu tsugun, “Zar mbisan nakhar, bǝza daks kǝ ud da tlǝksa Yazhigǝl.
MAR 10:25 Da lakhlakh kǝ dlǝgwam daks ǝn tǝ ɗul lipǝr, tǝghǝr kǝ daks kǝ dadak tluwandal da tlǝksa Yazhigǝl.”
MAR 10:26 Tsǝna kǝ furakh sar ad laven, ka gwidǝn ndawatǝrǝf char. Ka nǝv itar ǝn tǝb tar, “Ai da ka ndǝkyanina, war da gǝmadu safa nǝn vak Yazhigǝli?”
MAR 10:27 Ka vaztǝrkhai Yasu, ka ni, “Ən vak ud dǝg siga ǝn manawa bi, ai ǝn vak Yazhigǝla itsauɗa ǝn manawa man.”
MAR 10:28 Ka nǝv Bitrus tsin, “Ai kǝnda ma, a ɗuwars kǝnda itsauɗa a gatakhs kǝnd.”
MAR 10:29 Ka nggawa tǝrkhai Yasu, “Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, na ude a ɗuwars fǝta sara, itsa zarbabakh sara, zǝ dǝghaubabakh sar, zǝ bab sar, itsa dad sar, itsa zar sar, awana gukhakh sar, wirva ka, zǝ lav zǝɗan tsugun,
MAR 10:30 ka piyarwala gǝmadu dǝg siga sar sig dǝrmǝk dǝrmǝk ǝn kwargǝna bi. Da gǝmadu gǝma dǝ mǝghakha, zǝ zarbabakh, zǝ dǝghaubabakh, zǝ babakh, zǝ zar, zǝ gukhakh. Gǝmadu yaken tsuguna khekwa dǝ dlaɗ. Ən kwarge da saks, da gǝmadu gǝma ad safa kǝ ngǝɗ.
MAR 10:31 Wirva zikǝn liye tsa dǝg chaka, da nǝga itar kǝ dǝg khal. Liye dǝg khal tsuguna, itar da nǝga kǝ dǝg chak.”
MAR 10:32 Ən tǝghǝr kǝ ɗul dǝgo da Wurshalim Yasu zǝ furakh sar, Yasu ǝn mǝlatra vuk. Lave tsa kwarga Yasu, ǝn ndawatra ndawa kǝ furakh sar, ka liye ǝn gatatǝrs gata tsuguna ǝn gǝdza itar. Ka gwidǝn ndǝɗtǝraga Yasu kǝ furakh sar na kǝlatǝm mits da tǝ kalam, ka kwara tǝrkhai ad dǝge da dzoghǝr din.
MAR 10:33 Ka ni, “Tǝkhina ǝn dǝgo da Wurshalim kiyam, da bǝdu bǝgud Zǝr Ud da dǝv kǝ zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh. Da ǝntlara lav ǝmtsud. Ka da barǝm bǝg itar ǝn dǝv kǝ liye kwal Yakhudakh.
MAR 10:34 Da nenenena itar, zǝ tafarva shaghwvai. Wadzaru itar kiɓa, zǝ kǝɗga kǝɗa tsitar. Ən tǝkhal kǝ khǝna khǝkǝrɗa da tsi.
MAR 10:35 Ka sagh Yakuba zǝ Yukhan zar ya Zabadi da vak Yasu. Ka nǝv itar, “Malǝm, ǝn na kǝnda mana kǝndkhe kha ɗaga dǝge a takaɗga kǝnd.”
MAR 10:36 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal Yasu, “Uɗǝn nagh kur mana kurkhai mana tsǝki?”
MAR 10:37 Ka nggawar khai itar, “Khaya kǝndanǝf khaya ndzǝga ndzǝg tlǝrna udǝnd ǝn tǝ dǝva kafagh, tlǝrna udǝnda tsuguna ǝn tǝ dǝva dleɓagh, ǝn sarte da sǝgdagh khǝn ndangagh.”
MAR 10:38 Ai ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Ən tsa bakur dǝge ǝn takaɗa kur bi, da tǝkha kur kǝ khǝɓga dlaɗe da khǝɓa ka? Awana da khayanǝf khaya khǝ kur ad mana kura para tsud dǝ khulf pare da manakuda?”
MAR 10:39 Ka nggauga itar, “Da tǝkha kǝnd,” Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Da tǝkha kur kǝ khǝɓga dlaɗe da khǝɓa kǝ, parakuralud dǝ khulf pare a parakadud. ...
MAR 10:40 Ndzǝgan ǝn tǝ dǝva kafara zǝ dǝva dleɓara, na ka dǝ ndzǝɗa bǝdu bǝg bi. Yan kǝ vakakha dǝg liye audzalud ǝn ɗikatǝrna ɗik.
MAR 10:41 Tsǝna kǝ chalǝm furakh kǝlɗǝk ad yan kǝ lav, ka bazala rǝv tsitar ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ Yakub zǝ Yukhan.
MAR 10:42 Ka ɗakh tǝrkhai Yasu da tǝ dǝva kitakw, ka ni, “Tsa tsukur liye a bǝgud kǝ man tlǝks ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ liye kwal Yakhudakh, ǝn mǝdlatra tlǝks itar kǝ udakh tar. Zik zikanakh tar tsuguna ǝn mǝdlatra ndzǝɗe tar.
MAR 10:43 Da ndǝkyan bǝn tǝbura bi. Ai ɗaga ude ǝn nagh nǝga kǝ zikan ǝn tǝbur, barari tsin nǝga kǝ dadak mana kura tlǝr.
MAR 10:44 Tsugun ɗaga ude ǝn nagh nǝga kǝ mal ǝn tǝghǝr tsukur, barari tsin nǝga kǝ dadak mana tlǝr kǝ itsawarur.
MAR 10:45 Wirva itsa ka Zǝr Uda dǝ ghǝrar, a sodagh ba kǝ wirva ɗaba ka ɗaba tsud bi. Ai a sodagh kǝ ɗaba udakh kǝ, zǝ bǝdu safara tsǝka kǝ kat da udakh daghan.
MAR 10:46 Khalak yana, ka sagh Yasu zǝ furakh sar da Yariko. Madǝv Yasu zǝ furakh sar zǝ dzakhava udakh zikǝn, ǝn ɗuwars khuɗ kǝs, ka nǝg ngulfen ɗakha sara Batamawus (dǝge ǝn tuku Batamawus na, “Zǝr Timawus.”) Ən ndzǝgan ǝn tǝ kalam ɗul ǝn takaɗ.
MAR 10:47 Tsǝna tsin kwarne, Yasu ud Nazarat ǝn dǝgal, ka farsa tlǝkha tsin kwarne, “Yasu Zǝr Dod, ziwakdal ziw.”
MAR 10:48 Zikǝn liye tavarghǝr di kwarne, “Tǝriɗ nikh.” Ai ka gwidǝn tlǝkha tsin char, ǝn kwar kwarne “Zǝr Dod, ziwakdal ziw.”
MAR 10:49 Ghitsga Yasu, ka ni, “Ɗakhamakdǝghǝr ɗakh.” Ka ɗakhga itar ad ngulfen. Ka nǝv itar tsin, khǝnana rǝvagh, “Tsiyiftsi, ǝn ɗakha ɗakh.” ...
MAR 10:50 Ka tlǝvars ad lǝgwit sar da tǝ kalam. Ɗǝkut niya ghǝdzǝvǝf, khwayal da vak Yasu.
MAR 10:51 Ka ndiɗarwal Yasu, “Uɗǝn nakha manakha mana tsǝki? Ka nggawar khai ngulfen, “Malǝm, ǝn na ka nǝgha nǝgh.”
MAR 10:52 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “Dǝg dǝgal, fadǝghǝrofǝgagh kǝ mbakhu.” Tǝvin tǝvina ka ǝn nǝgha nǝgh. Ka gatars kǝ Yasu dǝgal.
MAR 11:1 Sa kǝ Yasu zǝ furakh sar khef dǝ Wurshalima, da da dlǝmdla kǝs Betfaji zǝ Betani, ǝn tǝ ghuɓa Olive. Ka ɓalanǝf ad furakh sar mits.
MAR 11:2 Niya tsitar, “Damdǝgal da gǝdzǝr kǝsin ǝn tǝvukur. Ba kur ǝn daksa, da nǝgha nǝgha kur gǝlaɓa dlingw ngguɗan ǝn vin, ai kwal taɓa tsud ngala ngal. Vǝdamadǝghǝr vǝd saks da van.
MAR 11:3 Itsawar ǝn ndiɗakurwal, kwarne, ‘Uɗa lava tsukur ǝn zǝɓ gǝlaɓa dlingwna? Nikur tsina, ‘Dad Zikan ǝn naghan, da guyondǝghǝr guya zula khǝɗikǝn.’ ”
MAR 11:4 Ka dala itar, tlarghǝr itar ad gǝlaɓa dlingwen nguɗan ǝn tǝ ghay rang da tǝ baram. Da itar ǝn vǝdavǝda,
MAR 11:5 ka ndiɗatǝrwal liye ghits ǝn tǝ vin, kwarne, “Uɗa lava tsukur ǝn vǝda dlingw ni?”
MAR 11:6 Ka nggawa tǝrkhai itar ndǝkve tsa kwara tǝrkhai Yasu, ka ɗuwatǝrs udakhen dǝgal dǝ dlingw.
MAR 11:7 Ɓadǝghǝr tsitsar gǝlaɓa dligwen da vak Yasu, ka ɓalo itar lǝgwitakh tar da tǝf, ka ndzo Yasu ǝn tǝf.
MAR 11:8 Zikǝn udakhe a ɓalga lǝgwitakh tar ǝn tǝ ɗul, yakhaya tsuguna a ɓalakhga itar tlim ufakhe tsa patsadǝghǝr itar ǝn tǝghal.
MAR 11:9 Liye ǝn tǝvuk sara zǝ liye gatars gatǝn tǝlg, ǝn ɗichau itar kwarne, “Bark kǝ Zǝr Dod” “Bark kǝ dadake ǝn saks ǝn ɗakha Dad Zikan”
MAR 11:10 “A ndzawa bark kǝ tlǝksa Dad mar Dod ai da saks” “Bark kǝ Yazhigǝl ai ǝn gharazhigǝl”
MAR 11:11 Sa kǝ Yasu da Wurshalima, ka da da Fǝta Yazhigǝl. Ka vazarvala kǝ itsauɗ, fatsiye tsatsin kwarne a sawal ba dura bi, ka dal da Betani zǝ furakh sar kǝlatǝm mits.
MAR 11:12 Tǝkǝtla sar, madv Yasu zǝ furakh sar ǝn ɗuda Betani. Ka ndzikǝnǝf way kǝ Yasu.
MAR 11:13 Ka nǝgha Yasu ad ufa ghǝdiv ngudǝv kǝ bit, ka dǝgal tsin da vaza zǝr ǝn tǝf. Da tsǝn da tǝ vǝgh, na dǝge a mbǝladuwin ǝn tǝ bi, uk mas, wirva sarta yig zǝr ba yanen kǝ gǝdiv bi.
MAR 11:14 Ka nǝv Yasu kǝ ufa ghǝdiven, “Na ude da gwidǝn zu zǝr ufagh bi.” A tsǝna kǝ furakh sar ad dǝge kwargin.
MAR 11:15 Da kǝ Yasu zǝ furakh sar da Wurshalim, ka da Yasu da fǝta Yazhighǝl. Ka farsan ad lakw li sakw digita zǝ li dzaw ǝn vin. Ka tlagars ad vǝleng li mɓaɗdu kwaɓ, zǝ vǝleng li sakwdu takalamasar.
MAR 11:16 Ka gadlarkhai ad zǝɓ itsauɗ kǝ udakh dǝgal diwa Fǝta Yazhigǝl.
MAR 11:17 Ka farsa tsagatǝrdu lava tsin kǝ udakh, ni, “Vindzan ǝn kaɗkaɗ lav Yazhigǝl kwarne, ‘Fǝtara da ɗakha dǝ vak ɗǝgawa kǝ daghan kǝsakhud. Ai tsuguna ka nandal kur kǝ vak ɓǝghava sǝnkarakh.’ ”
MAR 11:18 Tsǝna kǝ zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh ad yan, ka gat ɗul kǝɗ Yasu tsitar kǝmts. Wirvǝn gǝdza gǝdza itar, wirva ɗeghwa dzakhava udakh a batra tsagdutsaga sar ad ndawak.
MAR 11:19 Ɓǝlga kǝ khagwa, ka sawala Yasu zǝ furakh sar ǝn dlǝmdla kǝsen.
MAR 11:20 Tǝkǝdla pǝrt, madv Yasu zǝ furakh sar ǝn dǝgal. Ka nǝgha nǝgha tsitar ufa ghǝdive tsa tlapga Yasu a ghulal tangw da tǝ tlǝl.
MAR 11:21 Ka dzamana Bitrus, niya kǝ Yasu, “Malǝm, vaza dǝ ufa ghǝdive tsa tlapgakh a ghulkaval.”
MAR 11:22 Ka nggawa tǝrkhai Yasu kwarne, “Famadǝghǝrofǝg dǝ Yazhigǝl.”
MAR 11:23 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ. Itsawar ǝn kwarar khai kǝ ghuɓ nǝ, ‘Dǝg dǝgal, tlǝvdagh tlǝva ghǝra da dǝlv.’ Da bǝga bin dǝ tsugu ǝn rǝvakhuɗ sar bi, a fǝdghǝro tsugun ǝn tǝ dǝge kwargin da dzoghǝr ndzǝg, da manara manud.
MAR 11:24 Wirva yan, ǝn kwara kura kwara kǝ, itsauɗa ǝn takaɗga kur ǝn ɗǝgau, famadǝghǝro fǝg nggwaɗa gǝmadu kur. Da nǝga kǝ dǝgur.
MAR 11:25 Da ghitsaga kur kǝ ɗǝgau, da ka nǝg ude a khutana kur ǝn khuɗur, ɓisatǝrna kur. Ki ziɗa ɓisa kura ɓisa kǝ Dadur ai ǝn gharazhigǝl ad khaipakhur.
MAR 11:26 Ai da ka ɓisana ba kur bi. Ndǝkyan kǝ Dadar ai ǝn gharazhigǝl na ba da ɓisa kura khaipakhur bi.
MAR 11:27 Ka guyoghǝr Yasu zǝ furakh sar da Wurshalim, madv Yasu ǝn gwayav ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝl. Ka sa zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh, zǝ malakha ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dlam da vak sar.
MAR 11:28 Ka nǝv itar tsin, “Ən mana dǝ ira kǝ ndzǝɗakha dǝ dǝgakhani? War kǝ bakha ndzǝɗa man dǝgakhani?”
MAR 11:29 Ka nggawa tǝrkhai Yasu kwarne, “Da ndiɗakurwal ndiɗa ka digit kitakul. Da nggawake kur, ka da kwara kura kwara kǝ ad khulf ndzǝɗe manda ka dǝgakhan.
MAR 11:30 Kwarama ke kwar, para ude tsǝn mana Yukhan, a so ǝn gharazhigǝle awan ǝn vak ud khi?”
MAR 11:31 Ka kwara kava kwara tsitar ǝn tar kwarne, “Da ka ǝn ghǝrazhigǝla, nikiyam,’ Da ndiɗakiyamwal ndiɗa kwarne, ‘Uɗa lava tsukur kwal fadǝghǝro dini?’
MAR 11:32 ‘Da ka ǝn vak uda, nikiyam,’ Ən gǝdza kiyam kǝ udakh, wirva itsawara a khayanǝf kwarne, Yukhana tlayang Yazhigǝl.
MAR 11:33 Ka nggawar khai itar kǝ Yasu, “Ən tsa bakǝnda bi.” Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Na ghǝrar ǝn kwara kura khulf ndzǝɗe ǝn manakha da ka dǝgakhan na bi.”
MAR 12:1 Khalakyana, ka farsa Yasu ad kwaratra lava dǝ jakva lav, ni, “Nǝg udanen a tukhgan ad inabi ǝn gukh sar. Ka tsarghǝran dǝ ghǝrgh. Tǝfgan ad fik pǝrts yu inabiyen, ndǝrar khai ad vak uf chaw kǝ dadak uf gukhen. Ən tǝkhal kǝ yana, ka bǝdu ad mbucha gukhen kǝ yakhaya kǝ li wus, ka dakaval da tlǝrna vak.
MAR 12:2 Sa kǝ sarta tsǝg inabi, ka ɓǝlandal ad zǝr tlǝr sar da vak li wus gukhen, kǝ chawardǝghǝr tleva sar ǝn gukhen.
MAR 12:3 Ka vige tara, mbakǝn itar dǝ kǝɗ. Ɓǝlars itar dǝgal dǝ dǝv dliɓ.
MAR 12:4 Ka ɓǝlanǝf ad tlǝrna zǝr tlǝr sar da vak tar, kǝɗǝf itar ǝn ghǝr, ka tsafanǝf itar.
MAR 12:5 Ka gwidǝn ɓǝlanǝf ad tlǝrn zǝr tlǝr, ka kǝɗga itar. Ka gwidǝn ɓǝlanǝf ad yakhaya tsugun zikǝn, mbakǝn itar kǝ yakhay dǝ kǝɗ, kǝɗga itar chalǝm kǝmts.
MAR 12:6 “Tǝma ud fang a tǝmgan kǝ ude da ɓǝlin, in zǝr sar ai ǝn wayin. Ka ɓǝlandal kǝ dǝg mbas, ni, ‘Da farghǝrfǝg itar kǝ zǝrar.’
MAR 12:7 “Ka kwarakav khai li wus gukhen ǝn tǝb tar, ‘Auna makajen. Ausǝgam, kǝɗyamga kǝɗ, dǝg wura sara da nǝga kǝ dǝgmar.’
MAR 12:8 Ka viga itar ad zǝr saren kǝɗge tar. Ka tlǝval itar da tǝlg ghǝrgh ad tluvǝgha sar.
MAR 12:9 “Uɗa da mana dadak gukh kini? Da saks da khadz li tsa wus gukhen, ka da batra kǝ tlǝrna udakh ad gukh inabiyen.
MAR 12:10 Atsuk a tugwa bakh kur vindzan na kǝ lav Yazhigǝl ai ǝn kwar kwarne, “Kure a ɗuda li khǝg, in kǝ nala kǝ kur khǝga khwaran.
MAR 12:11 Dad Zikan kǝ mangga yan, A nala kǝ dǝg ndawak ǝn diyakh mar tsugun.’ ”
MAR 12:12 Ka gat ɗul vi Yasu kǝ zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh, wirva tsa tsitar kwarne ǝn tǝghǝr tsitar a kwarga Yasu ad jakva laven. Ai ǝn gǝdza itar kǝ dzakhava udakh, ka ɗuwars itara, dakaval itar.
MAR 12:13 Ən tǝkhal kǝ yana, ka ɓǝlandal itar ad chalǝm Farisakh zǝ udakh ya Khiridus da vak Yasu, ki zǝɗa viya vi ǝn tǝ dǝva dǝ lave da kwarin.
MAR 12:14 Ka sa itar da vak Yasu, nǝv itar tsin, “Malǝm, tsa tsǝkǝnda kwarne dadak jirkh. Itsawar wikitakw ǝn vakagh. Na khǝn bǝg ghal ǝn udakh bi. Ən tsagdu lav Yazhigǝle jir kha kǝ udakh. Kalkale, awana kalkal bakh pǝlara khadam tsǝkǝnda kǝ Kaisari?
MAR 12:15 Pǝla nagh kǝnda pǝl bakh kǝndi? Wirva tsa kǝ Yasu kwarne mbaɗirakh itar. Ka ndiɗatǝrwal ni, “Uɗa lava tsukur ǝn na nggaka dlǝgdi? A nakam kwaɓ dawanen nǝgha nǝgha kǝ” ...
MAR 12:16 Ɓardǝrghǝr itar ad kwaɓen, ka ndiɗatǝrwal, “Vakdiya zǝ ɗakhǝng inǝn tǝfi?” Ka nǝv itar, “Dǝg Kaisar.”
MAR 12:17 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Bamara bǝg kǝ Kaisar ad dǝg Kaisar, kǝ Yazhigǝl tsugun ad dǝg Yazhigǝl.” Ka a ndawatǝrǝf.
MAR 12:18 Ka tǝkǝn Sadukiyakh, liye ǝn kwar kwarne na tsiyǝn nggitl bi, sara da vak Yasu dǝ ndiɗ.
MAR 12:19 Nǝv itar, “Malǝm, a vindza kǝnd khai Mus kwarne, da mǝtsǝga zǝrbab sar kǝ udan ɗuwars ad nusar kwal zǝr. Barari wura wura kǝ zǝrbab sar ad widǝgen, kǝ yarkhai zar kǝ zǝrbab saren.
MAR 12:20 Ai nǝg zǝrbabakhen uɗif. Ka ɓu dǝg chak ad nus mǝtsgan kwal zar.
MAR 12:21 Ka ɓu dǝg mits ad widǝgen. Ka mǝtsǝga ghǝr sar tsugun, kwal zǝr. Ndǝkyan kǝ dǝg khǝkhǝrɗ tsugun.
MAR 12:22 Ndǝkvayan kǝ uɗif dagha tar, na ai yakhga zara bi. Kǝ dǝg mbasa, ka mǝtsǝga nusen.
MAR 12:23 Kina fitsa tsiyen nggitla da nǝga kǝ nusǝngini, fatsiye uɗifdagh tara a zǝɓaruwi?”
MAR 12:24 Ka nggawa tǝrkhai Yasu, ni, “A zaɗga ba kur bi, fatsiye ǝn tsa ba kur ad kaɗkaɗ lav Yazhigǝla awana ndzǝɗa Yazhigǝl bi.
MAR 12:25 Da tsiyifud ǝn nggitla, na lav zǝɓ nus zǝ bǝdu sǝba bi, da nǝga ndǝk zar ɓǝla Yazhigǝl ǝn ghǝrazhigǝl itar.
MAR 12:26 Ai ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ tsiyen nggitla, a tugwa bakh kur ǝn kaɗkaɗe vindzga Mus? Ən tǝghǝr kǝ lave kwararkhai Yazhigǝl ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ ndǝgha kar ǝn suya? ‘Ai ka Yazhigǝl Brahim, zǝ Yazhigǝl Ishaku, zǝ Yazhigǝl Yakub kǝ.’
MAR 12:27 Yazhigǝl tlamtsakh ba ka bi, dǝg liye dǝ safa kǝ. A mangga kur tleɓ”
MAR 12:28 Fang ǝn tǝb kǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikhe ǝn vak tar, ǝn tsǝnatǝrval tsǝna ad bǝg tsuguwe ǝn mane tar, ka katlgan kwarne a nggawa tǝrkhai Yasu khwaraniyan. Ka ndiɗarwal, “Ən tǝb kǝ ndzikha ndzikh daghan, ira khwaran ǝmbi?”
MAR 12:29 Ka nggawar khai Yasu, kwarne, “Ai khwaran na kǝ ndzikha, in ‘Tsǝnam tsǝn, Udakh ya Izrail. Yazhigǝl Dad Zikan mara, Dad Zikan kitakul.
MAR 12:30 Waya dǝ Dad Zikan Yazhigǝlagh dǝ rǝvakhuɗagh daghan. Dǝ vǝgha daghan. Dǝ mǝkǝnagh daghan. Zǝ ndzǝɗagh daghan.’
MAR 12:31 Dǝg mitsa in kwarne, “Waya dǝ tlǝghǝrwitǝghagh ndǝkva ghǝragh.’ Na ndzikha ndzikhe malgan ad yakhana bi.”
MAR 12:32 Ka nǝv dadak tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh, kǝ Yasu, “Kalkal dǝge a kwargakha,” uk Yazhigǝl kitakul na tlǝr bi uk inen.
MAR 12:33 Waya dǝ Yazhigǝlen dǝ rǝvagha daghan, zǝ mǝkǝnagh daghan, zǝ daghan ndzǝɗagh, zǝ way tlǝghǝrwitǝghagh ndǝkva ghǝragh. In khwaran tǝghǝr kǝ bara digit kǝ Yazhigǝl zǝ dǝg tsuf.”
MAR 12:34 Vazga kǝ Yasu a nggawar khai kwelemlem, ka niya tsin, “Bita bakh dǝ tlǝksa Yazhigǝl bi.” Ən tǝkhal kǝ yana, na ude a gwidǝn ndiɗarwal bi.
MAR 12:35 Madv Yasu ǝn tsagdutsag ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝl, ka ndiɗa tsin kwarne, “Uɗa lava kǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh ǝn kwar kwarne Kristuwa Zǝr Dodi?
MAR 12:36 Wirva Dod dǝ ghǝr sar, ǝn tǝ dǝva dǝ Sǝɗikw Yazhigǝla, a kwargan kwarne, “ ‘Nǝv Dad Zikan kǝ Dad Zikanar. “Ndzǝga ndzǝg ǝn tǝ dǝva kafar khekwa ba ka dǝ li dawagh ǝn kus kǝ sigagh.” ’
MAR 12:37 Dod dǝ ghǝr sara ǝn ɗakha dǝ ‘Dad Zikan.’ Ka da nǝga ndarin kǝ zǝr sari? Zikǝn dzakhava udakh ǝn tsǝn kǝn tsǝna dǝ khwaɗg.
MAR 12:38 Madv Yasu ǝn tsagdutsaga, ka ni, “Tsukwamana ghǝr dǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh, li way gwayava dǝ zikzikan kǝ gabag. Ən nagha itar naghatǝrdi nagh zǝ fatǝrghǝrfǝg ǝn tǝ ɓala kasuk.
MAR 12:39 Zǝ batra vǝj khwaran ǝn gud dzakhava Yakhudakh, zǝ vak khwaran ǝn vak khwadg.
MAR 12:40 Ən biɗ widǝgakh itar diwa zu dǝgakh tar. Ən zulu zula itar ǝn ɗǝgau, kǝ nǝghatra nǝgha tsud. Khulf yan kǝ udakha da manatra taka lavud char, mal kǝ dǝg yakhaya kǝ udakh.
MAR 12:41 Ən tǝkhal kǝ yana, ka ndzǝga Yasu khefa dǝ vake ǝn bǝduwud ad dǝg buti, ǝn vaz ɗule ǝn ɗida dzakhava udakh ad kwaɓ tar da vake ǝn bǝduwud ad dǝg buti. Zikǝn tluwandalakhe bakhdagh ad kwaɓ tar ɗǝmbǝr.
MAR 12:42 Ai ka sa widǝge talag, ka bǝdagh ad kalami vǝrshakanv mits, ai kwal do dat kwaɓ kitakul.
MAR 12:43 Ka Dakhga Yasu ad furakh sar da vak sar, ka ni, ǝn tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, kwaɓe a bǝdagh widǝg na da dǝg ɗi dǝg buti na, a malgan ad dǝg itsawar daghan.
MAR 12:44 Wirva daghan tara khǝɗikǝn a bǝdu itar ǝn zika dǝge din itar. Ai widǝg na ǝn talag sar a bǝduwin ad ɗaga dǝge dinin.
MAR 13:1 Madv Yasu ǝn sǝgawal ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝla, ka nǝv fang ǝn tǝb kǝ furakh sar tsin, “Malǝm, vaza dǝ ɗigan kurakhana zǝ khwara khǝgakhan.”
MAR 13:2 Ka ngawar khai Yasu kwarne, “Nǝgha tsǝkha adina kǝ khǝgakhana? Na bai da ɗuɗud ǝn tǝ vavak sar bi. Itsera tara da ndaza ndazud.”
MAR 13:3 Madv Yasu ǝn giɗǝn tǝ ghuɓa Oliv, ger dǝ Fǝta Yazhigǝl, ka sa Bitrus, zǝ Yakubu, zǝ Yukhan zǝ Ndros da vak Yasu ɓǝghanyan.
MAR 13:4 Ka nǝv itar, kwara kǝnda kwar, da dzoghǝr yawa ina kǝ digitakhi? Tsugun da zǝk ndǝk uɗa dǝge da nǝghud da da dzoghǝr dǝgakhana daghani?”
MAR 13:5 Ka ngawa tǝrkhai Yasu kwarne, “Ɗem nikur khayamanǝf ba valkurdu udan bi.
MAR 13:6 Da saks udakh zikǝn ǝn ɗakhar ǝn kwarne ka Yasu. Tsuguna, da valdu vala itar udakh zikǝn.
MAR 13:7 Da tsǝna kur lav ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ pǝga zǝ wilenga sar kǝ pǝg, gǝdzam bi. Wirva barari dzoghǝr dzǝg kǝ yakhen kǝ digitakh. Ai mbasa sara a sa ba ndan bi.
MAR 13:8 Kǝsa da tsiyara tsiya kǝ tlǝrna kǝs. Tlǝksa da kǝl ghum itar ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ tlǝrna tlǝks. Da man mbǝɗa pǝgdǝmud ǝn vakakh sikh sikh sikh. Da nǝg way tsugun. Daghan yakhana kǝ digitakha, ndazhazha sar bi, farsafǝg sar kǝ dlaɗ.
MAR 13:9 Ka tsukwana kur ghǝr. Da ɓǝkur ɓa itar da vak takalav, zǝ kǝɗ kur kǝɗǝn ǝn vak dzakhava Yakhudakh. Da ɓǝkur ɓud da tǝvuk kǝ maludakh zǝ shikakh wirva ɗakhar, ki kwaratra lav zǝɗan tsukur ǝn tǝvuk tar.
MAR 13:10 Ai kǝda saks kǝ mbasa sara, barari kwardu lav zǝɗan na tsud chak kǝ daghan udakh.
MAR 13:11 Itsa yau ǝn vai kur khai itar zǝ ɓǝkur ɓa da vak taka lav, dzamam ba dǝge da kwara kur bi. Kwaram kwara ba kur dǝge a sakura da mǝkǝnur ǝn tǝ sarten. Wirva kur bǝn kwar lava bi, Sǝɗikw Yazhigǝl ǝn kwaran.
MAR 13:12 “Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sarta, da bǝdu zǝrbab ad zǝrbab sar kǝ mǝts, dad tsugunsa da bǝdu bǝg ad zǝr sar. Zara tsugun da tsiyara tsiya tar kǝ yakh tar, zǝva kǝɗtǝr kǝɗa tsitar kǝmts.
MAR 13:13 Da nagh kur ba itsawar wirva ka bi. Ai ɗaga ude a bǝgan ad rǝv da tǝ mbasa, da mbǝladu mbǝla dǝ kat.
MAR 13:14 “Da nǝgha nǝgha kur dǝg dzadlakhe, ǝn bazdu Fǝta Yazhigǝl, zǝ udakhe ǝn nenanen, ǝn ghitsǝn tǝ vakvake tsa kalkal ba ghitsa tsin bi, (dakake ǝn tugwado lavana katlga katlin dǝge tukuwin). Ka liye ǝn ǝntla khay ya Yakhudi, barari khwaya tsitar dǝgo da ghuɓakh.
MAR 13:15 Ude ǝn ndzǝgan ǝn tǝ ghǝr gud tsuguna, ya so ɓin sǝgadagh da zǝɓ itsauɗ dǝgal ǝn khud mǝgh bi.
MAR 13:16 Ude ǝn gukh tsuguna, ya guyo bin saks da zǝɓ nura sar bi.
MAR 13:17 Da nǝg dlaɗ kǝ nǝghwase dǝ khuɗ, zǝ liye dǝ zǝr ǝn tǝ tukw dǝv, ǝn tǝ yanen kǝ sart.
MAR 13:18 Kwam ɗǝgau, dzoghǝr ba khwayana ǝn sarta fagh bi.
MAR 13:19 Yǝn tǝ yanen kǝ sarta, da nǝg dlaɗ char, khulfe kwal taɓa tsuɗ manaman. Gwil farsa vǝrɗ lard, tangw da tǝ ina kǝ sart. Aghbud da gwidǝn man khulf sar kǝ yanen bi.
MAR 13:20 “Da tsa khǝtsana bud ad khǝnakhen bi, tsa na ud dǝg sige da tǝma dǝ safa bi. Ai wirva li dzǝran na kǝ udakh Yazhigǝl, da khǝtsa khǝtsa Yazhigǝl ad khǝnakhen.
MAR 13:21 Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sarta, da ka nǝv udan tsukur, ‘Vaza, auna Kristu ǝn van’ awana, ‘A niya ǝn vin’ ya khayamanǝf bi.
MAR 13:22 Wirva Kristu filfilakh zǝ tlayang filfilakh da sakhgawal itar. Da manakh zik zikan na kǝ jakvakh, zǝ zik zikan na kǝ dǝg ndawakakh itar kǝ valdu udakh. Da tsa tǝkhin kǝ manawan, da valdu vala itar zǝva liye a dzǝrtǝkhai Yazhigǝl.
MAR 13:23 Wirva yana, ɗem nikur, a kwara kur khai ka itsauɗǝn sart.
MAR 13:24 Ən tǝ yanen kǝ khǝnakha, ǝn tǝkhal kǝ dzoghǝr dzǝg kǝ dlaɗakhen, “ ‘Ka da nǝga fatsi kǝ gurtl. Tǝl tsuguna naba da kheɗaɗ bi.
MAR 13:25 Kwadladlakh tsuguna ka da ɓaloɓalǝn Sǝgadagh ǝn tǝ fef gharazhigǝl. Da gǝdiya gǝdyud ad ndzǝɗakhe Ən fǝf gharazhigǝl.’ ”
MAR 13:26 “Da mǝdlo ǝn tǝ yanen kǝ sart jakva Zǝr Ud ǝn tǝ fef gharazhigǝl, ǝn sǝgadagh ǝn ghwik, dǝ ndzǝɗa zǝ ndanga char.
MAR 13:27 Da bǝlondagh ɓǝla dǝ zarɓǝlakh sar, kǝ dzakha dzǝran na kǝ udakh sar, ǝn tǝ kalam lard daghan. Tsiyif ǝn tǝ yan kǝ kalam lard, da tǝ yan kǝ kalamakh.
MAR 13:28 “Tsagam tsaga digit dǝ ufa ghǝdiv. Da farsin ɗidu tlim kǝ ɗado wilwa tlim, ǝn tsatsǝg kur kwarne a khǝrzǝga vi.
MAR 13:29 Ndǝk yan tsugun, da nǝgha tsukur dǝgakhan ǝn dzoghǝr dzǝg. Tsa tsukur kwarne, a khǝrzǝgan, ǝn tǝ ghay gud.
MAR 13:30 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, udakh kwargǝn, da ruga ba itar bi, khekwa dzoghǝr dǝgakhana daghan.
MAR 13:31 Gharazhigǝl zǝ khaya da nige tar. Ai lave ǝn sǝgawal ǝn ghayara na bai kwal da righa bi.”
MAR 13:32 “Na ude ǝn tsa khǝna zǝ sart bi, itsa zarɓǝlakhe ǝn gharazhigǝl, itsa Zǝren, uk Dad kitakul ǝn tsan.
MAR 13:33 Ɗem nikur, ɗikfǝkhe kur, wirvǝn tsa bakur sarte da sǝgadaghin bi.
MAR 13:34 Ndǝk ude da dǝgal da tlǝrna kǝs. Madvin ǝn ɗuwada mǝgha, batrǝm ad tlǝr ǝn dǝv kǝ li man tlǝr sar. Ka kwarar khai ak itsera kǝ zǝr tlǝr ad tlǝre da manin, ka kwarar khai kǝ dadake ǝn uf mǝgh ad giɗa ɗem.
MAR 13:35 Wirva yan, ɗem nikur, wirvǝn tsa bakur sarte da guyo dad mǝgh bi. Itsa kǝ khakhuga awana ǝn tǝb viɗ, itsa tǝkǝdla pǝrt awana kǝ fatsi tǝghǝr.
MAR 13:36 Da soghǝrin dzagwdlam, tlakurghǝr bin ǝn khǝnkhar bi.
MAR 13:37 Dǝge ǝn kwara kura ka, ǝn kwarara kǝ itsawar kǝ. Ɗem nikur.
MAR 14:1 Tǝmga khǝna mits kǝ khwaɗga ɗitsaɗits ai ǝn kwarud dǝ khwaɗga brudiye kwal yist. Ka gat ɗul vi Yasu kǝ zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh ɓǝghanyan, kǝ kǝɗa kǝɗa kǝmts.
MAR 14:2 Ai ka nǝv itar, “Na kiyam da viya viya fitsa khwaɗga bi, wirva da tsiya gadla udakh.”
MAR 14:3 Madv Yasu ǝn kǝs Betani, ǝn zu kaf ǝn fǝta Bitrus ai tsa ndzikǝn fǝch. Ka saks kǝ nusen dǝ wal bǝtbǝtan ǝn khatakw ai dzaw gan ǝn tǝf. Ka nguranǝf ad khatakwa, ka ɗiyarǝm ad wal bǝtbǝtanen ǝn ghǝr kǝ Yasu.
MAR 14:4 Ka bazala rǝv kǝ chalǝm udakhe ǝn vin. Ka nǝv itar kǝ itsawar, “Uɗa lava tsin ǝn bazdu wal bǝtbǝtan ai dzaw gan ǝn tǝf ndǝkini?
MAR 14:5 Azǝgha tsa sukwdu ud, tsa gǝmaduwud kwaɓ mal kǝ kwaɓe ǝn pǝlarud kǝ dadak tlǝr ǝn vǝg, ka batrud ad kwaɓ sar kǝ talagakh.” Ka tavarghǝr itar di kǝ nusen char.
MAR 14:6 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, a ɗuman ad nusǝn “Uɗa lava tsukur ǝn njǝgharu njǝghi? A manakai ad dǝg khwaran.
MAR 14:7 Tsika fatsiya da kur zǝ talagakh. Tǝkha kur kǝ mǝlatru ǝn tǝ itsera kǝ sarte ǝn na kur. Ai ka, da dagh ba kiyam zǝ kur tsika fatsi bi.
MAR 14:8 A mangan ad khalavuwa dǝge a mangin. A ɗiyo ad wal bǝtbǝtan an tǝ vǝghar, ki da ɗika kǝ khǝɗa ka da khǝɗ.
MAR 14:9 Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, itsa da kwardu ǝn varud lav zǝɗa kǝ tsǝna nǝn, ǝn lard daghan, dǝgǝn na manga nusna da kwardu kwarud ki da dzama da dzam.”
MAR 14:10 Ka dala Yakhuda Iskariyoti kitakul ǝn tǝb kǝ furakh Yasu kǝlatǝm mits, da vak zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, kǝ batǝrdu Yasu.
MAR 14:11 Tsǝna tsitar ad yana ka zǝɗatru char. Ka manarkhai itar lanji da bara kwaɓ. Ka farsa Yakhud ad gat ɗule da batǝrduwin ad Yasu.
MAR 14:12 Fitsa chak kǝ zu brudiye kwal yisti, fitsa khǝr mbaklak khwaɗga ɗitsaɗits. Ka ndiɗarwar furakh sar kǝ Yasu, kwarne, “Ən varǝn nakha da ɗikakhana kǝnda vake da zu dakha kaf ɗitsaɗitsi?”
MAR 14:13 Ka ɓǝlanǝf Yasu ad furakh sar mits, niya tsitar, “Dam daks da dlǝmdla kǝs, da gama kur zǝ ude ǝn ɓa shuguda yu. Gatams gat.
MAR 14:14 Da daghin da mǝgh, ka nikur kǝ dadak mǝgh, nǝv malǝm, “Mǝdla kǝnda mǝdla dǝ gude da zudin kaf ɗitsaɗitsa zǝ furakh sar’
MAR 14:15 Da mǝdlakura mǝdla dǝ zikan kǝ gud lind, ai udzalud ɗikana ɗika kǝ khwaɗg. Ɗikama kiyamana dǝg zuwun vin.”
MAR 14:16 Ka dala furakhen da dlǝmdla kǝsa, tlarghǝr itar kǝ digitakh, ndǝkve tsa kwara tǝrkhai Yasu. Ka ɗikana itar ad dǝg zuwa khwaɗga ɗitsaɗits.
MAR 14:17 Ɓǝlga kǝ khagwa, ka sagh Yasu zǝ furakh sar kǝlatǝm mits da mǝghen.
MAR 14:18 Madv itar ǝn zu kaf, ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Ən tǝkha kura tǝkha kǝ, kitakul ǝn kur, ai ǝn zuwa kaf zǝ kǝ, da bǝkdu bǝg.”
MAR 14:19 Ka bazala rǝv tsitar char. Ka nǝv itar tsin dǝ kitakw kitakw, “Ka nagha?”
MAR 14:20 Ka nggauga Yasu kwarne, “Kitakul ǝn kur kǝlatǝm mits na, ude ǝn zuwa kǝnda kaf ǝn kwat kitakul.
MAR 14:21 Da ǝmtsa Zǝr Ud ndǝkve a vindzǝgud ǝn tǝghǝr tsin. Ai ya ɗangwa kǝ ude da bǝdu Zǝr Ud. Adara tsa yiga bu dǝ yanen kǝ ud bi.”
MAR 14:22 Madv itar ǝn zu kaf, ka ɓǝf Yasu ad brudi, kwarar khai ad us kǝ Yazhigǝl, ka kwachanan. Batran kǝ furakh sar, niya tsitar, “Chawam chaw, vǝgharen.”
MAR 14:23 Ka ɓǝf ad kwate dǝ yu inabi, kwarar khai dǝ us kǝ Yazhighǝl. Ka batran, daghan tara ka khǝɓaru.
MAR 14:24 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Ina vizhar dǝg lanji, ai ɗiduwud kǝ wirva udakh zikǝn.”
MAR 14:25 Ən kwara kura kwara kǝ, aghba ka da khǝɓ yu inabi bi, akwa sarte da khǝɓa ka tlǝrna wilwan sar kǝ yu inabi ǝn tlǝksa Yazhigǝl.”
MAR 14:26 Ɓǝlga kǝ Yasu zǝ furakh sar ad ndusa. Ka sawal itara, dal itar da tǝ ghuɓ Oliv.
MAR 14:27 Ka nǝv Yasu tsitar, “Daghanura da khwaya kur dǝgal, da ɗukda ɗuwa kur. Wirva vindzan kwarne, “ ‘Da kǝɗga kǝɗa kad dadak zighw, Giɗa tuwagha da kwaza itar.’
MAR 14:28 Ai ǝn tǝkhal kǝ tsiyif tsiya tsǝkǝn ngitl, kǝn da dala tǝghǝr tsukur da khaya Galili.”
MAR 14:29 Ka nǝv Bitrus kǝ Yasu, “Itsa kwazga itar daghan, na ka da ɗuwakhs ɗuwa bi.”
MAR 14:30 Ka nǝv Yasu kǝ Bitrus, “Ən tǝkha kha tǝkha kǝ, ǝn khuɗ viɗ khan, kǝda wuga kǝ ghwachik sig mits, da bǝg tsugu tsakatsǝg kha sig khǝkǝrɗ.”
MAR 14:31 Ka gwidǝn Bitrus ad khwarar kwara kwarne, “Itsa da ǝmtsa ki dagh, na ka da bǝg tsugu tsakhatsǝg bi.” A kwarakhga ndǝkyan chalǝm furakh sar daghan.
MAR 14:32 Ən tǝkhal kǝ yana, ka dala Yasu dagha zǝ furakh sar da tǝ vaken ai ɗakhdud Gatsamani. Ka niya tsitar, “Ndzamga ndzǝg ǝn van, dǝgal da ɗǝgawa kǝ.”
MAR 14:33 Ka ɗaghga Yasu ad Bitrus, zǝ Yakub, zǝ Yukhan dǝgal dagha zin. Ka soghǝr bazala rǝv zǝ dzamghǝr kǝ Yasu.
MAR 14:34 Ka niya tsitar, “Rǝvara righan da baza rǝv, ai da tǝgh kǝ kǝɗkai. Giɗam giɗa ǝn van, ɗem nikur.”
MAR 14:35 Dal tsin da tǝvuk khǝɗikǝn, ka khǝmbǝgan dǝ khuɗ khuɗ, ka ɗǝgawa tsin kwarne, da tǝkhin kǝ manawan, ɓakghǝr ɓud ad ina kǝ sarta dlaɗ.
MAR 14:36 Ka ni “Dada, itsauɗa ǝn manawa man ǝn vakagh. Tsa ɓakghǝra kha dǝ ina kǝ dlaɗ. Tsakhǝnmina, dǝge ǝn na ka ba da manud bi, ai dǝge ǝn nakh.”
MAR 14:37 Guyoghǝr kǝ Yasu da vak furakh sarna khǝkǝrɗ, ka tlatǝrghǝr ǝn khǝn khar. Ka niya kǝ Bitrus, “Siman ǝn khǝn khar kura? Atsuk tǝgh bakh kur kǝ manga ɗǝm, kǝ dǝg aw kitakula?
MAR 14:38 Ɗem nikur zǝ man ɗǝgau, ki khek da ɓǝla tsukur da kura. Sǝɗikwa, ǝn nagha dǝ man tlǝr kwaran, ma vǝgha a khǝtsaru ndzǝɗ.”
MAR 14:39 Ka gwidǝn dala da ɗǝgau kǝ dǝg mits, ka gwayars kǝ ɗǝgawe tsa chak.”
MAR 14:40 Gwiyoghǝr tsin saks da vak furakh saren, ka tlatǝrghǝr ǝn khǝn khar, wirva khar ǝn di tsitar char. Wirvǝn tsa ba itar ad dǝge da kwarara itar bi.
MAR 14:41 Ka dala, gwiyoghǝr kǝ dǝg khǝkǝrɗ da vak furakh saren, ka niya tsitar, “Dlakh kur ǝn khǝn khar zǝ fǝtava? A tlal, vazam vaz, a sagh sarte da bǝduwud Zǝr Ud, da dǝv kǝ li khaipakh.
MAR 14:42 Tsiyam tsi, ndziyam dǝgal. Auna dadake da bǝkdu bǝg a sagh.”
MAR 14:43 Madv Yasu dlǝn kwar lav, ka sagh Yakhud ai kitakul ǝn tǝɓ kǝ kǝlatǝm mits, dagha zǝ dzakhava udakh zikǝn. Khwatan katsakarakh zǝ yaghwatakh ǝn dǝvakh tar. Zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ malanakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ udakh kǝ ɓǝlatǝrǝf.
MAR 14:44 Yakhud dadak bǝdu bǝgena, audzala kǝbits tǝrkhai kǝbitsa kǝ dzakhava udakhen kwarne, “Dadake da bruwa ka, in udanen, viyam viyǝn dǝgala, khutana kur char.”
MAR 14:45 Sa tsitara, ka dala Yakhud ger da vak Yasu. Ka ni, “Malǝm, ka bru Yasu tsin.
MAR 14:46 Ka viga udakhen ad Yasu. Khutana itar char.
MAR 14:47 Ka ndǝɗadal fang ǝn tǝb kǝ liye ǝn ghitsgan ǝn vin ad katsakar sar. Ka tsaɓgan ad vǝɓ ndangan kǝ zil kǝs, ǝntlardu ad tlim.
MAR 14:48 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal Yasu, kwarne, “Sǝnkarakh khǝka, ǝn sǝgawal kur dǝ katsakarakh zǝ yaghwatakh da vika viya?
MAR 14:49 Tsika fatsi da ka zǝ kur ǝn tsagdutsag ǝn Fǝta Yazhigǝl, a vikai ba kur bi. Ai manava kǝ righda dege a vindzgud ǝn kaɗkaɗ Yazhigǝl.”
MAR 14:50 Ka khwayala furakh sar daghan, ɗuwars itar.
MAR 14:51 Ka nǝg dakhalen a gatars kǝ Yasu, na gabag ǝn tǝvǝgh tsin bi, uk lǝgwit khǝngan. Tsǝn nagha itar ad viya vi,
MAR 14:52 ka ngǝdlgan ǝn vak tar. Khwayal dǝgal kwal kadlang ǝn tǝ vǝgha sar.
MAR 14:53 Ən tǝkhal kǝ viga viya kǝ dzakhava udakhen ad Yasu, ka ɓal itar da vak ndangan kǝ zil kǝs. Ka dzafkhe zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh, zǝ malanakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ udakh zǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh ǝn vak kitakul.
MAR 14:54 A gatars Bitrus kǝ Yasu tsugun kǝ tsub, tangw da tǝ gǝlvakh ndangan kǝ zil kǝs. Ka ndzǝgan ǝn vin da zǝ li uf udakh, ǝn ɗir kar.
MAR 14:55 Zik zikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ daghan li taka lav, ǝn gat udakhe da ǝntlarva lav fila fila kǝ Yasu itar, kǝ nǝghda kǝɗga kǝɗa tsitar. Ai ka mbǝladu ba itar bi.
MAR 14:56 Tsakhǝnmina zikǝn udakhe a sarawal kǝ ngatlarva fil. Ai fila tara a dzǝf bǝn tǝ dǝva kitakw bi.
MAR 14:57 Ka tsiyif yakhaya kǝ udakh, ka kwarga itar ina kǝ fil ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ Yasu.
MAR 14:58 “A tsǝna tsǝkǝnda ina kǝ ud ǝn kwar kwarne, ‘Tǝkha ka kǝ khǝtana Fǝta Yazhigǝl nǝ ai ndǝrga udakh. Ka ndǝrga ka tlǝrn ǝn khǝna khǝkǝrɗ. Ai ud ba da ndǝran bi.’ ”
MAR 14:59 Tsakhǝnmina, fila tara dzǝf bǝn tǝ dǝva kitakw bi.
MAR 14:60 Ka tsiyif ndangan kǝ zil kǝs ǝn tǝvuk tar. Ka ndiɗarwal kǝ Yasu kwarne, “Na kha dǝ lave tǝkhakha kǝ kwargan ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ lave ǝn kwara itar ǝn tǝghǝr tsǝkha?”
MAR 14:61 A mbǝɗa ba Yasu ad khay bi. Ka gwidǝn ndiɗarwal ndangan kǝ zil kǝs kǝ Yasu tsugun, “Kha khǝ Kristu, Zǝr Yazhigǝl dadak barka?”
MAR 14:62 Ka nǝv Yasu tsin, “An nǝv Yasu, da nǝgha nǝgha kur Zǝr Ud ǝn ndzǝgan ǝn tǝ dǝva kaf Dadak Ndangan daghan, zǝ sǝgdagh ǝn ghwik ǝn gharazhigǝl.”
MAR 14:63 Ka kwakhdu ndangan kǝ zil kǝs ad katlang sar. Ka ndiɗatǝrwal, “Uɗa dla lava tsǝkiyam ǝn gat tlǝrna shidakhi?
MAR 14:64 “A tsǝna tsukur ad nena Yazhigǝle a mangin. Uɗa ɗayaghǝruri?” Ka nǝv itar, “Khwaran sara kǝɗgud.”
MAR 14:65 Ka tafarva chalǝm udakh ad shaghwvai kǝ Yasu, mbusar khai itar ad vak di, ka kǝɗǝf itar. Ka nǝv itar, “Kwara kǝnda lav tlayang tlayang, war kǝ kǝɗfǝkhe?” Ka ɓala li uf udakha, ka kǝɗǝf itar.
MAR 14:66 Ən tǝkhal kǝ yana, madv Bitrus ǝn ndzǝgan ǝn tǝ gǝlvagh mǝghen, ka sagh dugh kuɗig ndangan kǝ zil kǝs da tǝ gǝlvaghen.
MAR 14:67 Nǝgha tsin ad Bitrus ǝn ɗir kar, ka vazarvar char. Ka ni “Ghǝragha da kur zǝ Yasu ud Nazarat nǝ.”
MAR 14:68 Ka bǝg tsugu tsin. Ka ni, “Ən tsa ba ka dǝge ǝn kwara kha lavǝn tǝghǝr bi.” Ka dala da tǝ ghay rang.
MAR 14:69 Ka gwidǝn nǝgha nǝgh kǝ dugh kuɗigen ad Bitrus ǝn vin, ka niya kǝ udakhe ǝn ghitsǝn vin tsugun, “Ina kǝ uda, kitakul ǝn li dagha zǝ in.”
MAR 14:70 Ka gwidǝn bǝg tsugu kǝ Bitrus. Zula khǝɗikǝna, ka nǝv liye ǝn ghitgan ǝn tǝvǝgh kǝ Bitrus, “Kaɗkaɗiya ghǝragha fang khǝn tǝb tar, wirva ud ya Galili khǝ.”
MAR 14:71 Ka farsa Bitrus ad tlap ghǝr sar, zǝva waɗatra waɗa tsin kwarne, “Ən tsa ba ka dǝ udan nǝn kwara kur lavǝn tǝghǝr bi.”
MAR 14:72 Tǝvin tǝvin ka wuga ghwachik kǝ dǝg mits. Ka dzamana Bitrus ad lave tsa kwararkhe Yasu, kwarne, “Kǝda wuga kǝ ghwachik kǝ dǝg mitsa, da bǝg tsugu tsatsǝgarakha sig khǝkǝrɗ.” Ka tuwa tsin char.
MAR 15:1 Pǝrta kǝdl, zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ malanakh ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh, zǝ daghan malanakhe ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dlam, ka ɗaykavu itar dzanak. Ka nguɗana itar Yasu, ɓala itar da tǝvuk kǝ Bilatus.
MAR 15:2 Ka ndiɗarwal Bilatus kwarne, “Kha nagh shik ya Yakhudakha?” Ka nggawar khai Yasu kwarne, “An ndǝkve kwargakh.”
MAR 15:3 Ka kwarakh lavakhe a ngatlarva udakh kǝ Yasu, a zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh.
MAR 15:4 Ka gwidǝn ndiɗarwal Bilatus kǝ Yasu kwarne, “Na khǝn mbǝɗa ghay ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dǝgakhe a ngatlakhve tara?
MAR 15:5 Ai tsuguna a gwidǝn ba Yasu mbǝɗa ghay bi, ka ndawanǝf ad Bilatus.
MAR 15:6 Dǝge a kuyala shik ǝn mana man ǝn sarta khwaɗga ɗitsa ɗits. Ən ɓǝlars ud kitakul ǝn gud sal, ai ɗauga udakh kǝ ɓǝlars ɓǝl.
MAR 15:7 Ən tǝ yanen kǝ sarta nǝg udanen ɗakha sar Barabas nguɗan ǝn gud sal, dagha zǝ li tsaya gadle, kǝɗga ud ǝn sarte tsa tsiyanǝf itar gadl.
MAR 15:8 Sa kǝ dzakhava udakha, ka farsa itar ad takaɗ Bilatus, kǝ ɓǝlatǝrnars ud kitakul ǝn gud sal ndǝkve tsa kuyalin.
MAR 15:9 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal Bilatus kwarne, “Ən na nagh kur ɗuwakurnǝs ka dǝ shik ya Yakhudakha?”
MAR 15:10 Tsa kǝ Bilatus kwarne wirva silg a bardǝghǝr zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh ad Yasu da vak sar.
MAR 15:11 Ai ka shakanǝf zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh ad udakh kǝ kwar kwarne, ɓǝlars ɓǝlin Barabas, ǝn dleva Yasu.
MAR 15:12 Ka gwidǝn ndiɗatǝrwal Bilatus kwarne, “Ai uɗa da mana ka dǝ ude ǝn ɗakha kur dǝ shik ya Yakhudakhi?
MAR 15:13 Ka tlǝkha tsitar kwarne, “Khǝrtga khǝrtud.”
MAR 15:14 Ka ndiɗatǝrwal Bilatus, “Wirva uɗi? Uɗa ghaze manggini?” Ka gwidǝn tlǝkha tsitar kwarne, “Khǝrtga khǝrtud.”
MAR 15:15 Fatsiye ǝn nagh ba Bilatus ad bazatǝrdu rǝv bi, ka ɓǝlatǝrnars ad Barabas. Ən tǝkhal kǝ ba udakh tsin da dlagharu kiɓ kǝ Yasuwa, ka batran kǝ khǝrtga khǝrta tsitar.
MAR 15:16 Ka ɓala tlujiyakh ad Yasu da tǝ gǝlvakh Gumn ai ǝn ɗakhdud (Firitoriyum.) Ka dzanǝf itar dakwal tlujiyakh daghan.
MAR 15:17 Ka talarǝm itar gabag shalaraz ndǝkva dǝg shikakh. Faɗarkhai itar ad dzakw tak, ka barǝm itar ǝn ghǝr.
MAR 15:18 Ka farsa itar ad nǝghardi nǝgha kwarne, “Dǝg safagh da tǝ uragh, shik ya Yakhudakh.”
MAR 15:19 Ka farsa itar dlaghara yaghwat ǝn ghǝr, tafarve tar shaghwvai. Kalga itar juguv ǝn tǝvuk sar, ǝn manara ɗaba nen itar.
MAR 15:20 Udzala tsitar ǝn manara nena, ka sǝkhardo itar ad gabag shalaraz ai tsa talarǝm itar, ka talarǝm itar ad gabag sar. Ka ɓala itar da mel kǝ khǝrta khǝrt.
MAR 15:21 Madv itar ǝn tǝghǝr kǝ dǝga, ka gamga itar zǝ udanen ǝn dǝgal ɗakha sar Siman, ud ya Sayirin, dad Alekzanda zǝ Rufus ǝn saks ǝn dlǝdla kǝs. Ka barghǝr itar zǝɓ ufa khǝrt Yasu.
MAR 15:22 Ka ɓala itar ad Yasu da tǝ vaken ǝn ɗakhdud dǝ Golgot, (“Dǝge ǝn tukuwin in kwarne, “Vak tlatl ghǝr”).
MAR 15:23 Ka bara itar ad yu inabi laɓan dǝ mur. Ai ka kalwal kǝ khǝɓa khǝɓ.
MAR 15:24 Ka khǝrtge tar. Ka taku itar gabag sar ǝn tatak tar, ka tlǝv tsats tsitar ǝn tǝf kǝ nǝghda dǝge da gǝmadu itsawar.
MAR 15:25 Ən tǝ kalkal karfi vaslambaɗ tǝ kǝdl a khǝrtga itar Yasu.
MAR 15:26 Vindzga itar ad lav file a ngatlva itar ǝn tǝ vak ghǝr tsin kwarne, “SHIK YA YAKHUDAKH.”
MAR 15:27 Ka khǝrtga itar sǝnkarakh mits zin. Fang ǝn tǝ dǝva kaf sar, fang tsuguna ǝn tǝ dǝva dleɓ sar.
MAR 15:28 Ina righa sar kǝ lav tlayang tlayang ai ǝn kwar kwarne, “A tǝgwanǝfud ǝn liye mangga khaz.”
MAR 15:29 Udakhe ǝn dǝgala, tsǝn kwarakh lav nen itar, ǝn ngǝts ghǝr itar, ǝn kwar kwarne, khe da khǝtana Fǝta Yazhigǝl, ka ndǝrga khǝn khǝna khǝkǝrɗ.
MAR 15:30 Kata dǝ ghǝragh dǝ sǝgadagh ǝn tǝ ufa khǝrt.
MAR 15:31 Ndǝkiyan tsugun a nenena zikzikan na kǝ zil kǝsakh zǝ li tsagdu ndzikha ndzikh Mus ad Yasu ǝn kwar kwarne, “A katgan ad yakhay, a tǝkh ba kǝ katga ghǝr sar bi.
MAR 15:32 Da ka Kristuwin kaɗi, sodagh sǝgin ǝn tǝ ufa khǝrta na tǝkhin, ki da nǝgha nǝgha tsǝkǝnda, ka khayanǝf kǝnd.” Sǝnkarakhe khǝrtǝgud zina, ghǝtar tsuguna a kwarar khai itar lav ɗekh ɗekhan.
MAR 15:33 Ən tǝ fatsi tǝghǝr, ka khǝɗaru gurtl ad khay daghan, tangw da tǝ karfi khǝkǝrɗ kǝ fatsi khakhug.
MAR 15:34 Ən tǝ kalkal karfi khǝkǝrɗena, ka tlǝkha kǝ Yasu dǝ ndzǝɗa char, kwarne, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabaktani?” (Dǝge ǝn tukuwin in, Yazhigǝlara, Yazhigǝlara, a ɗukde ndar kha ndikini?”
MAR 15:35 Tsǝna kǝ yakhaya kǝ udakh ǝn ghitsǝn tǝvin ad yan. Ka nǝv itar, tsǝnam tsǝn, ǝn ɗakh Ili tlayang.”
MAR 15:36 Ka kwayala fang ǝn tǝb tar, ka lubanan ad soso dǝ yu inabi kwarekrekan, siɓo ǝn tǝ uf, ka talaro kǝ Yasu kǝ khǝɓa khǝɓ. Ka ni, ɗuwama da ɗuwa ndan, wazyam vaz, ma sǝgadagh Ili tlayang da zǝɓadagh zǝɓ.”
MAR 15:37 Ka tlǝkh kǝ Yasu dǝ ndzǝɗa char, ka gǝlf niya ɗiga safa sar kǝ dǝg mbas, ka mǝtsgan.
MAR 15:38 Ka kukhum lǝgwit ghay gude Fǝta Yazhigǝl mits, tsiyif tǝ vak ghǝr da tǝ khay.
MAR 15:39 Nǝgha kǝ tlujiye ǝn ghitsǝn tǝ vin ad mǝtsa Yasu, ka ni, “Kaɗiya, udan na Zǝr Yazhigǝl.”
MAR 15:40 Ghitsga yakhaya kǝ nǝghwasa kǝ bit ǝn vazavaz. Ən tǝb kǝ li khitsena nǝg Maryam Magdali, zǝ Maryam bab Yakub ai khǝɗikan, zǝ Yusuvu, zǝ Salomi.
MAR 15:41 Yakhana kǝ nǝghwas ai tsa gatars kǝ Yasu saks ǝn ǝn Galili, ǝn nǝgharu nǝgh. Zikǝn nǝghwas a sara zin ǝn Wurshalim, ǝn vin tsugun.
MAR 15:42 Daghan ina kǝ digita a dzoghǝr ǝn tǝ fitsa ɗika digitakh kǝ udakh. Khǝna kǝda fitsa nggi. Ɓǝlga kǝ khagw
MAR 15:43 Ka sa udanen ai ɗakha sara Yusuvu ud ya Arimati. Kitakul ǝn li taka lav, ghǝr sara kitakul ǝn tǝb kǝ liye ǝn gwit tlǝksa Yazhigǝl. Ka da da vak Bilatus kwal dǝ gǝdz kǝ takaɗ tlu vǝgh Yasu.
MAR 15:44 Ka ndawanǝf ad Bilatus tsǝna tsin kwarne a mǝtsga Yasu. Ka ɗakhgan ad tlujiyen kǝ ndiɗarwal ndiɗa kwarne, kaɗi nagh a mǝtsga Yasuwa?
MAR 15:45 Ndazhana tsin ǝn tǝ ghay kǝ tlujna, ka baran ad tlu vǝgh Yasuwen kǝ Yusuvu.
MAR 15:46 Ka sukwadǝghǝr Yusuvu ad lǝgwit kǝlpakan, zǝɓadagh ad tlu vǝgha Yasu ka mbusanan ǝn kǝlpakanen, ka bǝm ǝn nggitle a tǝfgud ǝn khurzǝz. Ka tlǝgadagh ad gil, khǝɗaru ad nggitlen.
MAR 15:47 A nǝgha kǝ Maryam Magdali, zǝ Maryam bab Yusuvu ad vake bava tlu vǝgh Yasu.
MAR 16:1 Ən tǝkhal kǝ khǝna fitsa fǝtav. Ka sukwadǝghǝr Maryam Magdali, zǝ Maryam bab Yakub, zǝ Salomi, ad tǝrshin bǝtbǝtan kǝ masara kǝ vǝgha Yasu.
MAR 16:2 Pǝrta kǝdl fitsa khǝna dǝg chak kǝ fǝtav, dǝ gwisǝl, madv itar dǝgal da vak nggitla.
MAR 16:3 Ka ndiɗakava tsitar ǝn tǝbtar kwarne, “Ware kǝ da tliga kiyamdu kur ǝn tuk nggitleni?”
MAR 16:4 Ai vazo tsitar dǝgo, ka nǝgha itar kuren, na bakha kǝ zika bi, a audzalud ǝn tlǝgarwal tlǝg.
MAR 16:5 Da tsitar da nggilten. Ka nǝgha nǝgha tsitar dakhwal zeren ǝn ndzǝgan ǝn tǝ kalam dǝva kaf ǝn lǝgwit maɗakw. Ka gǝdzif itar.
MAR 16:6 Ka niya tsitar, “Gǝdzam bi. Ən gat Yasu ud Nazarat kur, ai khǝrtavan. A tsiyif aghbǝn vana bi. Nǝghama nǝgha vake tsa khǝnanud.
MAR 16:7 Ai damdǝgal kwaramar tǝrkhai kwara kǝ furakh sar zǝ Bitrus, ‘In da dala tsitar da Galili. Da nǝghan vin itar, ndǝkve tsa kwara tǝrkhayin.’ ”
MAR 16:8 Ka khway tsitar dǝgal ǝn nggitlen, dǝ gǝdzǝf ǝn tǝga vǝgh titar. A kwararkhai bai tar dǝge dzoghǝr kǝ itsawar bi, wirvǝn gǝdze tar.
MAR 16:9 Tsiyif kǝ Yasu ǝn nggitl tǝkǝdla pǝrt fitsa khǝna fǝtav. Ka mǝdlawal chak kǝ Maryam Magdaliye, a zǝɓardalin sǝɗikw bǝzan uɗif ǝn vǝgh.
MAR 16:10 Ka dala kwara tǝrkhai kǝ furakh sar, zǝ liye baza rǝva zǝ tu.
MAR 16:11 Tsǝna tsitar kwarne a tsiyif Yasuwa, tsuguna a nǝgha tsin, ka a fadǝghǝro ba itar bi.
MAR 16:12 Ən tǝkhal kǝ yana, ka mǝdlawala Yasu kǝ furakh sar mits ǝn tlǝrna jakv, madv itar ǝn dǝgal da dlǝmdla kǝs.
MAR 16:13 Guyaghǝr tsitar, ka kwarar khai itar kǝ chalǝmakh tar. Ai ghǝr tar tsuguna a khayanǝf ba itar bi.
MAR 16:14 Ən tǝkhal kǝ yana, ka soghǝr Yasu kǝ furakh sarna kǝlatǝm kitakw, madv itar ǝn zu kaf. Ka tavatǝrghǝr ad di wirva kuɗ fadǝghǝrofǝg tar, zǝ ɓengɓeng ghǝre a kalwal itara kǝ fadǝghǝrofǝg dǝ lave a kwara tǝrkhai liye tsa nǝghan ǝn tǝkhal kǝ tsiya sar.
MAR 16:15 Ka niya tsitar, “Damdǝgal da lard daghan, kwaramdu lav zǝɗan kǝ daghan ud dǝg sig.
MAR 16:16 Ɗaga ude fadǝghǝro, parandalud, da gǝmadu gǝma dǝ saf. Ai ɗaga ude kwal fadǝghǝro, da tǝkara lavud.
MAR 16:17 Auna dǝgakhe da mana liye fadǝghǝro dǝ kǝ, ai da mǝdla fadǝghǝrofǝg tar. Da zaɓado zaɓe tar sǝɗikw bǝzan ǝn ɗakhar, da kwar lav itar dǝ ghay tlǝrna kǝs.
MAR 16:18 Da zǝɓa zǝɓe tar bub dǝ dǝvakh tar, ai da ka khǝɓu itar ngura, na dǝge da manatǝrin itsa khǝɗikǝn bi. Da bakhatǝr ghǝr bakha itar dǝv kǝ udakh kwal yanga, tsuguna da mbǝga itar.”
MAR 16:19 Ən tǝkhal kǝ kwara tǝrkhai kwara kǝ Dad zikan Yasu ad ɗaga lavakhana kǝ furakh sar. Ka ɓo dǝgo da gharazhigǝl, ndzǝgan ǝn tǝ dǝva kaf Yazhigǝl.
MAR 16:20 Ka dala furakh sar da kwardu lav Yazhigǝl itsa dǝvar. Dad zikan tsuguna ka a mǝlatru, a ndazhana kwarne kwardu lav tara jir, tǝ dǝva dǝ dǝg ndawakakhe a mange tar.
